/**
 * Checks for a 'prebuild' hash in the URL on page load.
 * If found, decompresses the data and merges it into the initial buildState.
 * @returns {boolean} - Returns true if a prebuild hash was handled, otherwise false.
 */
const handlePrebuildState = () => {
  if (window.location.hash && window.location.hash.startsWith('#prebuild=')) {
    console.log('%c[Builder] Found #prebuild hash in URL.', 'color: #03a9f4; font-weight: bold;');
    const encodedData = window.location.hash.substring(10);
    history.replaceState(null, document.title, window.location.pathname + window.location.search);

    try {
      const decodedDataString = decodeURIComponent(encodedData.replace(/\+/g, ' '));
      console.log('[Builder] Decoded Data String:', decodedDataString);

      if (!decodedDataString || decodedDataString.trim() === '{}') {
        console.warn("Pre-build data from URL was empty ('{}'). Ignoring. Check product page Liquid template.");
        return false;
      }
      
      const prebuildState = JSON.parse(decodedDataString);
      console.log('[Builder] Parsed Pre-build State Object:', prebuildState);

      if (prebuildState && (prebuildState.selections || prebuildState.startComponent)) {
        if (prebuildState.selections && prebuildState.selections.step1) {
            buildState.ridingStyle = prebuildState.selections.step1.ridingStyle || null;
            buildState.ridingStyleDisplay = prebuildState.selections.step1.ridingStyleDisplay || null;
            buildState.buildType = prebuildState.selections.step1.buildType || null;
        }
        if (prebuildState.selections && prebuildState.selections.step2) {
          // [DEBUG] Log the state of specs BEFORE the assignment
          console.log('%c[DEBUG] buildState.specs BEFORE assignment:', 'color: #orange;', JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(buildState.specs)));
          console.log('%c[DEBUG] Incoming prebuildState.selections.step2:', 'color: #orange;', prebuildState.selections.step2);

          if (Array.isArray(prebuildState.selections.step2.brakeStyle)) {
            prebuildState.selections.step2.brakeStyle = prebuildState.selections.step2.brakeStyle[0];
          }
          Object.assign(buildState.specs, prebuildState.selections.step2);

          // [DEBUG] Log the state of specs AFTER the assignment
          console.log('%c[DEBUG] buildState.specs AFTER assignment:', 'color: #00A36C;', JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(buildState.specs)));
        }
        if (prebuildState.startComponent) {
          buildState.startComponent = prebuildState.startComponent;
        }
        
        console.log("Pre-build state successfully loaded. Final buildState:", buildState);
        
        updateStep1VisualFeedback();
        validateStep1();

        return true;
      } else {
        console.warn("Parsed pre-build data was invalid. Ignoring.");
        return false;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to parse pre-build state from URL hash:', error);
    }
  }

  return false;
};

/**
 * Gathers all unique masterVariantGids from rim rules and fetches their prices in a single API call.
 */
async function cachePreconfiguredPrices() {
   if (allRimProductsCache.length === 0) {
        console.log("cachePreconfiguredPrices: Rim cache is empty, cannot fetch prices.");
        return;
    }

    const uniqueVariantGids = new Set();
    allRimProductsCache.forEach(rim => {
        if (rim.preconfiguredRules && rim.preconfiguredRules.length > 0) {
            rim.preconfiguredRules.forEach(rule => {
                if (rule.masterVariantGid) {
                    uniqueVariantGids.add(rule.masterVariantGid);
                }
            });
        }
    });

    const gidsToFetch = Array.from(uniqueVariantGids);
    if (gidsToFetch.length === 0) {
        return;
    }

    console.log(gidsToFetch);

    const query = `
      query getVariantPrices($ids: [ID!]!) {
        nodes(ids: $ids) {
          ... on ProductVariant {
            id
            price { amount }
          }
        }
      }
    `;

    try {
        const data = await storefrontApiQuery(query, { ids: gidsToFetch });
        if (data && data.nodes) {
            data.nodes.forEach(variantNode => {
                if (variantNode && variantNode.price) {
                    preconfiguredPriceCache[variantNode.id] = parseFloat(variantNode.price.amount) * 100;
                }
            });
        }
        console.log(preconfiguredPriceCache);
    } catch (error) {
    }
}


// --- Spacing Normalization Helper ---
// This ensures "12x148mm" matches "12×148mm" (multiplication sign) 
// and ignores extra spaces or capitalization.
const normalizeSpacing = (str) => {
    if (!str) return "";
    return str.toString()
        .replace(/[\u00D7\u2715]/g, 'x') // Replace multiplication signs (×) with regular x
        .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')           // Collapse multiple spaces into one
        .trim()
        .toLowerCase();
};

    // --- START: WHEEL WEIGHT CALCULATION ENGINE ---

/**
 * Performs the geometric spoke length calculation. Ported from spoke-calculator.js.
 * This version is for weight estimation and does not account for stretch.
 * @param {object} params - Object containing all geometric parameters.
 * @returns {number} The calculated geometric spoke length in mm.
 */
function calculateGeometricSpokeLength(params) {
    // Destructure all required variables from the params object
    const { hubType, crossPattern, spokeCount, erd, hubFlangeDiameter, flangeOffset, spOffset = 0, hubSpokeHoleDiameter = 2.6 } = params;

    // Ensure all critical numbers are valid before proceeding
    if ([crossPattern, spokeCount, erd, hubFlangeDiameter, flangeOffset].some(val => typeof val !== 'number' || isNaN(val))) {
        console.warn("calculateGeometricSpokeLength: Missing critical geometric data.", params);
        return 0;
    }

    let effectiveCrossPattern = crossPattern;
    // Straight pull hubs effectively add a half-cross to the geometric pattern
    if (hubType === 'Straight Pull' && crossPattern > 0) {
        effectiveCrossPattern += 0.5;
    }

    const angle = (2 * Math.PI * effectiveCrossPattern) / (spokeCount / 2);
    const term1 = Math.pow(flangeOffset, 2);
    const term2 = Math.pow(hubFlangeDiameter / 2, 2);
    const term3 = Math.pow(erd / 2, 2);
    const term4 = 2 * (hubFlangeDiameter / 2) * (erd / 2) * Math.cos(angle);

    const geometricLength = Math.sqrt(term1 + term2 + term3 - term4);

    let finalLength;
    if (hubType === 'Classic Flange' || hubType === 'Hook Flange') {
        finalLength = geometricLength - (hubSpokeHoleDiameter / 2);
    } else { // Straight Pull
        finalLength = geometricLength + spOffset;
    }
    return finalLength > 0 ? finalLength : 0;
}

/**
 * Extrapolates the weight of a single spoke based on its calculated length.
 * @param {number} baseWeightG - The manufacturer's weight for a reference spoke (in grams).
 * @param {number} calculatedLengthMm - The actual length needed for the wheel.
 * @param {number} [baseLengthMm=260] - The length of the reference spoke (e.g., 260mm).
 * @returns {number} The extrapolated weight for one spoke of the calculated length.
 */
function extrapolateSpokeWeight(baseWeightG, calculatedLengthMm, baseLengthMm = 260) {
    if (!baseWeightG || !calculatedLengthMm || baseLengthMm === 0) {
        return 0;
    }
    // Simple ratio calculation: (actual length / base length) * base weight
    return (calculatedLengthMm / baseLengthMm) * baseWeightG;
}

function isLacingPossible(spokeCount, crossPattern) {
    if (crossPattern === 0) return true;
    if (!spokeCount || spokeCount < 4) return false;
    const angleBetweenHoles = 360 / (spokeCount / 2);
    const lacingAngle = crossPattern * angleBetweenHoles;
    return lacingAngle < 90;
}

/**
 * Determines the cross pattern for weight estimation.
 * Defaults to Radial (0) for Front Rim Brake wheels.
 */
function getEstimatedCrossPattern(hubProduct, hubVariantData, spokeCount, position, brakeStyle) {
    if (!hubProduct || !spokeCount) return 3; // Fallback

    const lacingPolicy = hubProduct.hub_lacing_policy?.value;

    // PRIORITY 1: Manual Override Field (Respects your specific hub settings first)
    if (lacingPolicy === 'Use Manual Override Field') {
        const manualCross = hubVariantData?.hub_manual_cross_value?.value;
        if (manualCross) return parseFloat(manualCross);
    }

    // PRIORITY 2: Specific Lacing Policies
    if (lacingPolicy === 'Force 2-Cross for 28h Only' && spokeCount === 28) return 2;
    if (lacingPolicy === 'Force 3-Cross for 28h Only' && spokeCount === 28) return 3;
    if (lacingPolicy === 'Force All as 2-Cross') return 2;

    // PRIORITY 3: Front Rim Brake Default (RADIAL - ONLY for low spoke counts)
    // We only assume Radial if it's a front wheel, rim brake, and 24 holes or less.
    const numericSpokeCount = parseInt(spokeCount);
    if (position === 'Front' && brakeStyle === 'Rim Brake' && numericSpokeCount <= 24) {
        return 0; 
    }

    // PRIORITY 4: Standard / No Policy -> Calculate Max Possible
    const possibleCrosses = [4, 3, 2, 1, 0];
    for (const cross of possibleCrosses) {
        if (isLacingPossible(spokeCount, cross)) {
            return cross;
        }
    }

    return 3; // Final fallback
}
// --- END: WHEEL WEIGHT CALCULATION ENGINE ---

/**
 * Calculates total weight including Valves, Tape, and dynamic Spoke calculations.
 * Also updates the Spoke UI text with the calculated values.
 */
function calculateTotalEstimatedWeight() {
    const TAPE_WEIGHT_G = 10;
    const weights = { front: 0, rear: 0, total: 0 };
    const { components, buildType, specs } = buildState;
    
    // Debug Groups help keep console clean
    // console.groupCollapsed("⚖️ Weight Calc Detail"); 

    const positionsToCalculate = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToCalculate.push('Front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToCalculate.push('Rear');

    for (const position of positionsToCalculate) {
        const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
        let positionWeight = 0;

        const rim = components[`${posLower}Rim`];
        const hub = components[`${posLower}Hub`];
        const nipples = components[`${posLower}Nipples`];
        const valves = components[`${posLower}ValveStem`];
        const spokeCount = specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`] ? parseInt(specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`], 10) : 0;

        // 1. Add Component Weights
        positionWeight += rim?.weight_g || 0;
        positionWeight += hub?.weight_g || 0;
        positionWeight += valves?.weight_g || 0; // Valve Weight

        if (rim && buildState.tubelessTapeInstalled) {
            positionWeight += TAPE_WEIGHT_G;
        }

        if (nipples?.weight_g && spokeCount > 0) {
            positionWeight += nipples.weight_g * spokeCount;
        }
        if (position === 'Rear' && components.rearComponentFreehub) {
            positionWeight += components.rearComponentFreehub.weight_g || 0;
        }

        // 2. Calculate Spokes
        const spokes = components[`${posLower}Spokes`];
        let displaySpokeText = null;

        if (spokes?.weight_g && rim && hub && spokeCount > 0) {
            const hubProduct = allHubProductsCache.find(p => p.id === hub.productId);
            // Use Variant ERD if available, else Product ERD
            const erd = rim.rim_erd ? parseFloat(rim.rim_erd) : NaN;
            
            const pcdL = hubProduct?.hub_flange_diameter_left ? parseFloat(hubProduct.hub_flange_diameter_left) : NaN;
            const pcdR = hubProduct?.hub_flange_diameter_right ? parseFloat(hubProduct.hub_flange_diameter_right) : NaN;
            const flangeL = hubProduct?.hub_flange_offset_left ? parseFloat(hubProduct.hub_flange_offset_left) : NaN;
            const flangeR = hubProduct?.hub_flange_offset_right ? parseFloat(hubProduct.hub_flange_offset_right) : NaN;
            
            const hasAllGeoData = !isNaN(erd) && !isNaN(pcdL) && !isNaN(pcdR) && !isNaN(flangeL) && !isNaN(flangeR);

            if (hubProduct && hasAllGeoData) {
                const hubVariantData = hubProduct.variants.find(v => v.id === hub.variantId);
                const hubTags = hubProduct.tags || [];
                const hubType = hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull') ? 'Straight Pull' : (hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') ? 'Hook Flange' : 'Classic Flange');
                const crossPatternToUse = getEstimatedCrossPattern(hubProduct, hubVariantData, spokeCount, position, specs.brakeStyle);
                
                const spOffsetL = hubVariantData?.hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_left ? parseFloat(hubVariantData.hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_left) : 0;
                const spOffsetR = hubVariantData?.hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_right ? parseFloat(hubVariantData.hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_right) : 0;
                const avgPCD = (pcdL + pcdR) / 2;
                const avgFlangeOffset = (flangeL + flangeR) / 2;
                const avgSpOffset = (spOffsetL + spOffsetR) / 2;
                
                const estimatedLength = calculateGeometricSpokeLength({
                    hubType: hubType, crossPattern: crossPatternToUse,
                    spokeCount: spokeCount, erd: erd, hubFlangeDiameter: avgPCD, 
                    flangeOffset: avgFlangeOffset, spOffset: avgSpOffset,
                    hubSpokeHoleDiameter: parseFloat(hubProduct.hub_spoke_hole_diameter) || 2.6
                });

                if (estimatedLength > 0) {
                    const singleSpokeWeight = extrapolateSpokeWeight(spokes.weight_g, estimatedLength);
                    const totalSpokeWeight = singleSpokeWeight * spokeCount;
                    positionWeight += totalSpokeWeight;
                    
                    // --- CHANGED: Only showing Weight, NO LENGTH ---
                    displaySpokeText = `Wt: ${Math.round(totalSpokeWeight)}g`;
                } else {
                     // Fallback
                     displaySpokeText = `Wt: ${(spokes.weight_g * spokeCount).toFixed(0)}g`;
                }
            } else {
                // Fallback
                displaySpokeText = `Wt: ${(spokes.weight_g * spokeCount).toFixed(0)}g`;
            }
        }

        // 3. Update Spoke UI directly
        const spokeContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-image-container`);
        if (spokeContainer && displaySpokeText) {
            const weightDiv = spokeContainer.querySelector('.selected-component-weight-display');
            if (weightDiv) {
                weightDiv.innerHTML = displaySpokeText;
            }
        }

        weights[posLower] = positionWeight;
    }

    // console.groupEnd();
    weights.total = weights.front + weights.rear;
    return weights;
}

    function displayInitializationError(message) { const targetElement=document.getElementById('step-0')||builderContainer||document.body; const messageElement=targetElement.querySelector?.('.error-message'); if(messageElement){messageElement.textContent=message; targetElement.style.display='flex'; targetElement.style.flexDirection='column'; targetElement.style.alignItems='center'; document.querySelectorAll('.builder-step[data-step="1"], .builder-step[data-step="2"], .builder-step[data-step="3"]').forEach(s=>s.style.display='none'); if(summaryContainer)summaryContainer.style.display='none';}else{(builderContainer||document.body).innerHTML=`<div style="color: red; border: 1px solid red; padding: 15px; text-align: center;">${message}</div>`;} console.error("BUILDER INIT ERROR:", message); }

    // --- Function to save buildState (local storage for anonymous, customer metafields for logged in) ---
async function saveBuildState(buildId, fullStateObject) {
    if (!buildId || !fullStateObject) {
        console.error("saveBuildState: Missing buildId or fullStateObject.");
        return;
    }
  
    const stateJson = JSON.stringify(fullStateObject);
    const MAX_LOCAL_STORAGE_SIZE = 5 * 1024 * 1024; // 5MB approx
    const MAX_METAFIELD_SIZE_BYTES = 5000; // Shopify's limit for a single string metafield value is around 5KB

    if (window.customerLoggedIn && Shopify.customer.id) {
        // For logged-in users, attempt to save to a customer metafield.
        // This requires a custom metafield definition in Shopify Admin:
        // Namespace: `custom`
        // Key: `saved_builds`
        // Type: `JSON string` (or `text line` if saving multiple as a larger JSON array of objects)
        // (If individual builds are large, you might need an app or a series of metafields)

        // Simplistic approach: Just save the latest build to a single metafield.
        // More complex: Fetch existing saved_builds, add/update current, save back.
        // This example assumes saving the *most recent* build to a specific metafield for simplicity.

        // Fetch current customer metafields
        // (You'd need a backend endpoint or a Shopify App to write customer metafields securely from the frontend)
        // As writing customer metafields directly from frontend JS is not straightforward/secure in Dawn theme.
        // For now, we will save to localStorage for *all* users, and you can implement metafield saving
        // with a server-side component later if cross-device persistence for logged-in users is critical.
        
        localStorage.setItem(`loamlabs_build_${buildId}`, stateJson);

    } else {
        // For anonymous users (and as a fallback for logged-in users for now), use localStorage
        try {
            if (stateJson.length * 2 > MAX_LOCAL_STORAGE_SIZE) { // Rough size estimate for UTF-16
                console.error(`Build state for ${buildId} is too large for localStorage.`);
                alert("Your custom build is very large and could not be saved to your browser for later editing. Please contact support.");
                return;
            }
            localStorage.setItem(`loamlabs_build_${buildId}`, stateJson);
        } catch (e) {
            console.error(`[SAVE_BUILD_STATE] Error saving build "${buildId}" to localStorage:`, e);
            alert("An error occurred while trying to save your build. Please contact support.");
        }
    }
}

// --- Function to retrieve buildState (from local storage primarily) ---
function retrieveBuildState(buildId) {
    if (!buildId) { // Check if buildId is empty or null
        return null;
    }

    // Try localStorage first (for anonymous users or as primary storage for all now)
    const localStorageKey = `loamlabs_build_${buildId}`;
    const storedState = localStorage.getItem(`loamlabs_build_${buildId}`);
    
    if (storedState) {
        try {
            const parsedState = JSON.parse(storedState);
            return parsedState;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error(`[RETRIEVE_BUILD_STATE] Error PARSING stored state for buildId: "${buildId}" from localStorage. Error:`, e);
            localStorage.removeItem(localStorageKey); // Clear invalid data
            return null;
        }
    }

    // If you implement customer metafields, you'd add fetch logic here:
    // if (window.customerLoggedIn && Shopify.customer.id) {
    //     // Add logic to fetch customer metafield here, requires backend or app.
    //     // Example: Fetch from /apps/your-app/api/customer-metafield?customer_id=...
    //     // For now, this branch is effectively skipped.
    // }

    return null;
}
  
    // --- START: SAVE/LOAD FUNCTIONS ---

function getCleanBuildStateForSaving() {
    // Creates a deep copy suitable for saving.
    const stateToSave = {
        step: buildState.step,
        buildType: buildState.buildType,
        ridingStyle: buildState.ridingStyle,
        ridingStyleDisplay: buildState.ridingStyleDisplay,
        customerSupplied: { ...buildState.customerSupplied }, // <<< ADD THIS LINE
        specs: { ...buildState.specs },
        components: { ...buildState.components },
        selectedOptionalAddons: { ...buildState.selectedOptionalAddons },
        buildId: buildState.buildId,
        _ui: {
            activeVendor: buildState._ui.activeVendor,
            valveStemExplicitlyRemoved: buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved,
            step2AutoSelected: buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected || {}
        }
    };
    return stateToSave;
}

/**
 * Creates a minimal, lightweight version of the build state for analytics reporting.
 * This reduces the payload size to work reliably with navigator.sendBeacon.
 */
function getMinimalBuildStateForReporting() {
    const { buildId, buildType, ridingStyleDisplay, subtotal, components } = buildState;
    const minimalState = {
        buildId, buildType, ridingStyleDisplay, subtotal,
        components: {
            front: [],
            rear: []
        },
        visitor: buildState.visitor || null
    };

    const componentOrder = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'];
    const positions = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positions.push('front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positions.push('rear');

    positions.forEach(pos => {
        componentOrder.forEach(type => {
            const componentData = components[`${pos}${type}`];

            if (componentData && componentData.title) {
                let displayName = componentData.title; // Start with the product title

                // Use a switch statement for clarity and robustness
                switch (type) {
                    case 'Spokes':
                        // Spokes have a special 'selectedColor' property for a clean display
                        if (componentData.selectedColor) {
                            displayName += ` (${componentData.selectedColor})`;
                        }
                        break;
                    
                    // All other components can use a more generic approach based on their variant title or selected options
                    case 'Rim':
                    case 'Hub':
                    case 'Nipples':
                    case 'ValveStem':
                        // We prefer using selectedOptions for a cleaner, more reliable output
                        if (componentData.selectedOptions && componentData.selectedOptions.length > 0) {
                            const optionsString = componentData.selectedOptions
                                .map(opt => opt.value)
                                .filter(val => val && val.toLowerCase() !== 'default title' && val !== '-')
                                .join(' / ');
                            
                            if (optionsString) {
                                displayName += ` (${optionsString})`;
                            }
                        } 
                        // Fallback to the raw variantTitle if selectedOptions isn't available
                        else if (componentData.variantTitle) {
                            const variantParts = componentData.variantTitle.split(' / ').filter(part => part && part.toLowerCase() !== 'default title' && part !== '-');
                            if (variantParts.length > 0) {
                                displayName += ` (${variantParts.join(' / ')})`;
                            }
                        }
                        break;
                }
                
                minimalState.components[pos].push({
                    type: getDisplayName(type.toLowerCase()),
                    name: displayName
                });
            }
        });
    });

    return minimalState;
}

async function saveCurrentBuild() {
    console.log("saveCurrentBuild: Initiated.");
    if (buildState.step < 3 && !Object.values(buildState.components).some(c => c !== null)) {
        alert("Please select some components before saving your build.");
        return;
    }

    let buildName = prompt("Enter a name for your wheel build:", `My Build - ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}`);
    if (buildName === null) { // User pressed cancel
        console.log("Save cancelled by user.");
        return;
    }
    buildName = buildName.trim() || `Saved Build - ${Date.now()}`;

    const newBuildId = `${Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000)}`;
    const stateToSave = getCleanBuildStateForSaving();
    
    // Assign the new ID to the state object we are saving AND the main buildState
    stateToSave.buildId = newBuildId;
    buildState.buildId = newBuildId; 
    
    // Use this new ID for all subsequent operations in this function
    const currentBuildId = newBuildId;

    try {
        // Save the full build state object
        saveBuildState(currentBuildId, stateToSave); // This uses your existing function

        // Update the index
        let savedBuildsIndex = [];
        const indexJson = localStorage.getItem(SAVED_BUILDS_INDEX_KEY);
        if (indexJson) {
            try {
                savedBuildsIndex = JSON.parse(indexJson);
                if (!Array.isArray(savedBuildsIndex)) savedBuildsIndex = [];
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("Error parsing saved builds index, resetting.", e);
                savedBuildsIndex = [];
            }
        }

        const existingEntryIndex = savedBuildsIndex.findIndex(b => b.id === currentBuildId);
        if (existingEntryIndex > -1) {
            savedBuildsIndex[existingEntryIndex].name = buildName;
            savedBuildsIndex[existingEntryIndex].timestamp = Date.now();
        } else {
            savedBuildsIndex.push({
                id: currentBuildId,
                name: buildName,
                timestamp: Date.now()
            });
        }

        // Sort by timestamp, newest first
        savedBuildsIndex.sort((a, b) => b.timestamp - a.timestamp);
        localStorage.setItem(SAVED_BUILDS_INDEX_KEY, JSON.stringify(savedBuildsIndex));

        // alert(`Build "${buildName}" saved!`);
        // console.log(`Build "${buildName}" (ID: ${currentBuildId}) saved successfully.`);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error saving build:", error);
        alert("Could not save build. Check console for errors.");
    }
}

function renderSavedBuildsList() {
    if (!savedBuildsModalBody) return;
    savedBuildsModalBody.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous list

    let savedBuildsIndex = [];
    const indexJson = localStorage.getItem(SAVED_BUILDS_INDEX_KEY);
    if (indexJson) {
        try {
            savedBuildsIndex = JSON.parse(indexJson);
            if (!Array.isArray(savedBuildsIndex)) savedBuildsIndex = [];
        } catch (e) { savedBuildsIndex = []; }
    }

    if (savedBuildsIndex.length === 0) {
        savedBuildsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>No saved builds found.</p>';
        return;
    }

    const ul = document.createElement('ul');
    ul.className = 'saved-builds-list';
    savedBuildsIndex.forEach(buildEntry => {
        const li = document.createElement('li');
        li.className = 'saved-build-item';
        const dateString = new Date(buildEntry.timestamp).toLocaleString();
        li.innerHTML = `
            <div class="saved-build-info">
                <span class="saved-build-name">${buildEntry.name}</span>
                <span class="saved-build-date">Saved: ${dateString} (ID: ${buildEntry.id})</span>
            </div>
            <div class="saved-build-actions">
                <button type="button" class="button builder-button saved-build-load-btn" data-build-id="${buildEntry.id}">Load</button>
                <button type="button" class="button builder-button button--danger saved-build-delete-btn" data-build-id="${buildEntry.id}">Delete</button>
            </div>
        `;
        ul.appendChild(li);
    });
    savedBuildsModalBody.appendChild(ul);
}

async function loadBuildFromStorage(buildIdToLoad, isLastActiveResume = false) {
    const storageKey = isLastActiveResume ? LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY : `loamlabs_build_${buildIdToLoad}`;
    const retrievedStateString = localStorage.getItem(storageKey);

    if (!retrievedStateString) {
        alert("Could not find the saved build data.");
        if (isLastActiveResume) localStorage.removeItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY);
        return false;
    }

    let loadedState;
    try {
        loadedState = JSON.parse(retrievedStateString);
    } catch (e) {
        alert("Error loading build: The saved data is corrupted.");
        if (isLastActiveResume) localStorage.removeItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY);
        return false;
    }

    const loadingOverlay = document.getElementById('builder-edit-loading-overlay');
    if (loadingOverlay) loadingOverlay.style.display = 'flex';

    // Reset and merge state
    resetBuildStateToDefaults();
    Object.assign(buildState, loadedState);
    if(loadedState.specs) buildState.specs = { ...buildState.specs, ...loadedState.specs };
    if(loadedState.components) buildState.components = { ...buildState.components, ...loadedState.components };
    if(loadedState.selectedOptionalAddons) buildState.selectedOptionalAddons = { ...buildState.selectedOptionalAddons, ...loadedState.selectedOptionalAddons };
    if(loadedState._ui) buildState._ui = { ...buildState._ui, ...loadedState._ui };
    
    if(loadedState.customerSupplied) buildState.customerSupplied = { ...buildState.customerSupplied, ...loadedState.customerSupplied };

    // Ensure all promises are reset to allow re-fetching
    componentFetchPromises = { rims: null, hubs: null, spokes: null, nipples: null, valves: null, freehubs: null };

    // Update Step 1 and 2 UI immediately
    updateStep1VisualFeedback();
    validateStep1();
    renderStep2();
    updateStep2OptionsVisibility();
    updateStep2VisualFeedback();
    validateStep2();

    // Re-trigger all necessary data fetches in the background.
    triggerEarlyComponentFetches();

    // --- KEY CHANGE: REMOVED THE BLOCKING PROMISE.ALL() CALL ---
    // By calling showStep immediately, the UI for Step 3 will be rendered
    // and each component section will display its own "Loading..." message
    // while it awaits the data it needs. This eliminates the blank screen.
    await showStep(buildState.step);

    // --- Manually trigger lead time calculation after a build is loaded ---
    handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();

    // Final updates and cleanup are now handled within the showStep function
    if (isLastActiveResume) localStorage.removeItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY);
    if (savedBuildsModal?.style.display !== 'none') savedBuildsModal.style.display = 'none';
    if (lastActiveBuildPromptModal?.style.display !== 'none') lastActiveBuildPromptModal.style.display = 'none';
    if (loadingOverlay) loadingOverlay.style.display = 'none';

    return true;
}

function deleteSavedBuild(buildIdToDelete) {
    if (!buildIdToDelete) return;
        if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete build "${getBuildNameFromIndex(buildIdToDelete) || buildIdToDelete}"? This cannot be undone.`)) { // Improved prompt
            return;
        }

    localStorage.removeItem(`loamlabs_build_${buildIdToDelete}`); 
    let savedBuildsIndex = [];
    const indexJson = localStorage.getItem(SAVED_BUILDS_INDEX_KEY);
    if (indexJson) {
        try {
            savedBuildsIndex = JSON.parse(indexJson);
            if (!Array.isArray(savedBuildsIndex)) savedBuildsIndex = [];
        } catch (e) { savedBuildsIndex = []; }
    }

    const updatedIndex = savedBuildsIndex.filter(b => b.id !== buildIdToDelete);
    localStorage.setItem(SAVED_BUILDS_INDEX_KEY, JSON.stringify(updatedIndex));

    renderSavedBuildsList(); // Re-render the list in the modal
        alert(`Build "${getBuildNameFromIndex(buildIdToDelete) || buildIdToDelete}" deleted.`);
    }

    // Helper function to get build name for delete prompt (optional but nice)
    function getBuildNameFromIndex(buildId) {
        const indexJson = localStorage.getItem(SAVED_BUILDS_INDEX_KEY);
        if (indexJson) {
            try {
                const savedBuildsIndex = JSON.parse(indexJson);
                const entry = savedBuildsIndex.find(b => b.id === buildId);
                return entry ? entry.name : null;
            } catch (e) { return null; }
        }
        return null;
    }

const saveLastActiveBuild = debounce(() => {
    if (buildState.step === 1 && !buildState.buildType && !buildState.ridingStyle) {
        // Don't save an empty step 1 state
        return;
    }
    const stateToSave = getCleanBuildStateForSaving();
    // Add a display name for the "resume" prompt
    stateToSave._ui.buildNameForDisplay = `In-progress build from ${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}`;
    
    try {
        localStorage.setItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY, JSON.stringify(stateToSave));
        // console.log("Last active build progress saved.");
    } catch (e) {
        console.error("Error auto-saving last active build:", e);
    }
}, 1500); // Debounce for 1.5 seconds

async function checkForLastActiveBuildAndShowPrompt() { // Renamed and made async
        const lastActiveStateJson = localStorage.getItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY);
        if (lastActiveStateJson) {
            try {
                const lastActiveState = JSON.parse(lastActiveStateJson);
                if (lastActiveState && lastActiveState.buildId && lastActiveState.step) {
                    if (lastActiveBuildPromptModal) {
                        lastActiveBuildPromptModal.style.display = 'flex';
                        return true; // Indicate prompt was shown
                    } else {
                    }
                } else {
                    localStorage.removeItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY); 
                }
            } catch (e) {
                localStorage.removeItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY);
            }
        }
        return false; // Indicate prompt was NOT shown
    }

// --- END: SAVE/LOAD FUNCTIONS ---
  
// --- Function to load build state from URL parameters (for "Edit" functionality) ---
function loadBuildFromUrlParams() {
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    let buildIdFromUrl = urlParams.get('buildid') || urlParams.get('buildId');

    if (buildIdFromUrl && buildIdFromUrl !== "null") {
        try {
            const loadedState = retrieveBuildState(buildIdFromUrl);
            if (!loadedState) {
                console.warn(`[LOAD_FROM_URL] Build data not found for buildId: "${buildIdFromUrl}". Starting new build.`);
                return false;
            }

            // --- START: MERGE LOADED STATE and DISCOUNT STATE ---
            buildState.step = 3; // Force to step 3 for editing
            buildState.buildType = loadedState.buildType;
            
            // Restore all the saved properties
            buildState.ridingStyle = loadedState.ridingStyle;
            buildState.ridingStyleDisplay = loadedState.ridingStyleDisplay;
            buildState.specs = { ...loadedState.specs };
            buildState.buildId = loadedState.buildId;
            buildState.selectedOptionalAddons = { ...loadedState.selectedOptionalAddons };

            // Restore UI state

            // Restore UI state
            buildState._ui.activeVendor = loadedState._ui?.activeVendor || buildState._ui.activeVendor;
            buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved = loadedState._ui?.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved || buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved;
            buildState._ui.inEditMode = true; // Set edit mode flag
            buildState._ui.hasChanges = false;
            buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected = {};
            // --- END: MERGE LOADED STATE ---

            // Prune components based on the wheel type being edited
            const tempLoadedComponents = { ...loadedState.components };
            if (buildState.buildType === 'Front') {
                buildState.components = {
                    frontRim: tempLoadedComponents.frontRim, frontHub: tempLoadedComponents.frontHub,
                    frontSpokes: tempLoadedComponents.frontSpokes, frontNipples: tempLoadedComponents.frontNipples,
                    frontValveStem: tempLoadedComponents.frontValveStem,
                    rearRim: null, rearHub: null, rearSpokes: null, rearNipples: null, rearValveStem: null
                };
            } else if (buildState.buildType === 'Rear') {
                 buildState.components = {
                    rearRim: tempLoadedComponents.rearRim, rearHub: tempLoadedComponents.rearHub,
                    rearSpokes: tempLoadedComponents.rearSpokes, rearNipples: tempLoadedComponents.rearNipples,
                    rearValveStem: tempLoadedComponents.rearValveStem,
                    frontRim: null, frontHub: null, frontSpokes: null, frontNipples: null, frontValveStem: null
                };
            } else { // Wheel Set
                buildState.components = tempLoadedComponents;
            }

            // Update Step 1 visuals to reflect loaded state
            updateStep1VisualFeedback();
            validateStep1();

            // Prepare for Step 3
            buildState._ui.hasProgressedPastStep1 = true;
            triggerEarlyComponentFetches();
            handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();
            return true; // Indicate success

        } catch (e) {
            console.error('[LOAD_FROM_URL] Error processing build from URL:', e);
            return false;
        }
    }
    return false; // No buildId in URL
}

// --- Customer Supplied Modal Logic ---
let currentModalConfirmation = { component: null, position: null };

function showConsolidatedConfirmationModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal');
  const title = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-title');
  const body = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-body');
  const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-confirm-btn');
  const checkbox = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-checkbox');
  const checkboxLabel = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-checkbox-label');

  let modalBodyHtml = '';
  const providingRim = buildState.customerSupplied.front.rim || buildState.customerSupplied.rear.rim;
  const providingHub = buildState.customerSupplied.front.hub || buildState.customerSupplied.rear.hub;

  if (providingRim) {
    modalBodyHtml += `
      <div class="modal-section">
        <h4>Regarding Your Rim(s):</h4>
        <p>Please ensure your rim is new or in excellent, undamaged condition. The build lead time begins after your rim is received and inspected by LoamLabs.</p>
      </div>`;
  }

  if (providingHub) {
    modalBodyHtml += `
      <div class="modal-section">
        <h4>Regarding Your Hub(s):</h4>
        <p>To ensure a successful build, <strong>you must include the correct end caps and the complete freehub body</strong> when you send us your hub. The build lead time begins after all parts are received and inspected.</p>
      </div>`;
  }
  
  title.textContent = "Please Confirm";
  body.innerHTML = modalBodyHtml;
  checkboxLabel.textContent = "I understand and will include all necessary parts.";
  
  checkbox.checked = false;
  confirmBtn.disabled = true;
  modal.style.display = 'flex';
}

function hideConfirmationModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal');
  if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
}
  
    // --- Utility Functions ---
    // --- START: HELPER FUNCTION ---
/**
 * V5.5: Co-dependent Spoke Discovery.
 * Only generates a button if AT LEAST ONE Rim and ONE Hub exist with that count.
 */
function generateDynamicSpokeButtons(position) {
    const container = document.getElementById(`${position}-spoke-count-container`);
    if (!container) return;

    const rimCounts = new Set();
    const hubCounts = new Set();
    const posPascal = position.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + position.slice(1);

    // --- SAFETY CHECK: The "Forever" Counts ---
    const forcedCounts = ['24', '28', '32'];
    forcedCounts.forEach(c => { rimCounts.add(c); hubCounts.add(c); });

    const cleanVal = (val) => {
        if (!val) return null;
        const numeric = val.toString().replace(/\D/g, '');
        return numeric || null;
    };

    // 1. Scan Rims (Filtered by size/position)
    allRimProductsCache.forEach(product => {
        if (product.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return;
        product.variants.forEach(variant => {
            const size = buildState.specs[`${position}WheelSize`];
            const vSize = variant.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
            const sizeMatch = !size || (vSize === size || (Array.isArray(vSize) && vSize.includes(size)));
            const positionMatch = (variant.spec_position === posPascal || variant.spec_position === "Front/Rear");

            if (sizeMatch && positionMatch) {
                const c = cleanVal(variant.spec_spoke_count);
                if (c) rimCounts.add(c);
            }
        });
    });

    // 2. Scan Hubs (Filtered by position)
    allHubProductsCache.forEach(product => {
        if (product.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return;
        product.variants.forEach(variant => {
            if (variant.spec_position !== posPascal && variant.spec_position !== "Front/Rear") return;
            const positionMatch = (variant.spec_position === posPascal || variant.spec_position === "Front/Rear");
            if (positionMatch) {
                const c = cleanVal(variant.spec_spoke_count);
                if (c) hubCounts.add(c);
            }
        });
    });

    // 3. THE CO-DEPENDENCY FILTER: Only keep counts found in BOTH sets
    const discoveredCounts = Array.from(rimCounts).filter(count => hubCounts.has(count));
    const sortedCounts = discoveredCounts.sort((a, b) => parseInt(a) - parseInt(b));

    // 4. Fallback (Safety only)
    const finalCounts = sortedCounts.length > 0 ? sortedCounts : ['24', '28', '32'];

    // 5. Build Buttons
    container.innerHTML = finalCounts.map(count => {
        const valueWithH = `${count}h`;
        const isActive = buildState.specs[`${position}SpokeCount`] === valueWithH;
        return `<button type="button" class="spec-option-button builder-button ${isActive ? 'active' : ''}" data-spec-group="${position}SpokeCount" data-value="${valueWithH}" data-riding-style="both">${valueWithH}</button>`;
    }).join('');
}

function generateDynamicHubSpacingButtons(position) {
    const container = document.getElementById(`${position}-hub-spacing-container`);
    if (!container) return;

    const posPascal = position.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + position.slice(1); // "Front" or "Rear"
    const ridingStyle = buildState.ridingStyle;
    const discovered = new Set();

    // --- PHASE 1: Mapped Standards (Strictly separated by style) ---
    const standardsMap = {
        front: {
            gravelroad: ["12x100mm", "9x100mm QR"],
            mtb: ["15x110mm", "15x100mm", "20x110mm (Boost)", "20x110mm (Non-Boost)"]
        },
        rear: {
            gravelroad: ["12x142mm", "10x130mm QR"],
            mtb: ["12x148mm (Boost)", "12x142mm", "12x150mm", "12x157mm (SuperBoost)", "12x157mm (DH)"]
        }
    };

    // Add ONLY the core essentials immediately to prevent blank space without showing "ghost" buttons
const essentialStandards = {
    front: { 
        gravelroad: ["12x100mm", "9x100mm QR"], 
        mtb: ["15x110mm", "20x110mm (Boost)"] 
    },
    rear: { 
        gravelroad: ["12x142mm", "10x130mm QR"], 
        mtb: ["12x148mm (Boost)", "12x150mm", "12x157mm (SuperBoost)"] 
    }
};

if (ridingStyle === 'hybrid') {
    essentialStandards[position].gravelroad.forEach(s => discovered.add(s));
    essentialStandards[position].mtb.forEach(s => discovered.add(s));
} else if (essentialStandards[position][ridingStyle]) {
    essentialStandards[position][ridingStyle].forEach(s => discovered.add(s));
}

    // --- PHASE 2: Dynamic Discovery (Add niche ones ONLY if found in cache) ---
    if (allHubProductsCache.length > 0) {
        allHubProductsCache.forEach(product => {
            const styleMatch = ridingStyle === 'hybrid' || product.tags.some(tag => tag.includes(ridingStyle)) || product.tags.includes('style:both');
            product.variants.forEach(variant => {
                // Position Guard
if (variant.spec_position !== posPascal && variant.spec_position !== "Front/Rear") return;

const otherStyle = ridingStyle === 'mtb' ? 'gravelroad' : 'mtb';
const oppPos = position === 'front' ? 'rear' : 'front';

// 1. Block if discovery finds a spacing that actually belongs to the opposite wheel (e.g., 20x110 in Rear)
const isWrongPos = standardsMap[oppPos].mtb.includes(variant.spec_hub_spacing) || 
                   standardsMap[oppPos].gravelroad.includes(variant.spec_hub_spacing);

// 2. Block if discovery finds a spacing strictly for the other discipline (e.g., 15x110 in Gravel)
const isWrongStyle = ridingStyle !== 'hybrid' && 
                     standardsMap[position][otherStyle]?.includes(variant.spec_hub_spacing) && 
                     !standardsMap[position][ridingStyle]?.includes(variant.spec_hub_spacing);

if (styleMatch && variant.spec_hub_spacing && !isWrongPos && !isWrongStyle) {
    discovered.add(variant.spec_hub_spacing);
}
            });
        });
    }

    // --- PHASE 3: Render ---
    const sortedSpacings = Array.from(discovered).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, undefined, { numeric: true }));
    container.innerHTML = sortedSpacings.map(spacing => {
        const isActive = buildState.specs[`${position}HubSpacing`] === spacing;
        return `
            <button type="button" class="spec-option-button builder-button ${isActive ? 'active' : ''}" 
                    data-spec-group="${position}HubSpacing" data-value="${spacing}" data-riding-style="both">
                ${spacing}
                <span class="spec-count-bubble is-hub is-loading"></span>
            </button>`;
    }).join('');
}

/**
 * Gets a list of products for a given component type that are compatible with the current Step 2 spec selections.
 * @param {string} position 'Front' or 'Rear'.
 * @param {string} typePascal The component type in PascalCase (e.g., 'Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes').
 * @returns {Array} A filtered array of compatible product objects.
 */
function getCurrentlyCompatibleProducts(position, typePascal) {
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const specs = buildState.specs;
    let cacheToSearch;
    let filterFn;

    // Determine which cache and filter logic to use based on the component type
    switch (typePascal) {
        case 'Rim':
            cacheToSearch = allRimProductsCache;
            if (!specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`]) return [];
            
            filterFn = p => {
                if (p.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return true;
                return p.variants.some(v => {
                    const sizeValue = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                    const sizeMatch = (sizeValue === specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`] || (Array.isArray(sizeValue) && sizeValue.includes(specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`])));
                    const positionMatch = (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear");
                    const spokeMatch = (!specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`] || (String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`])));
                    
                    // --- THE BRAKE FILTER ENGINE ---
                    const vBrakes = v.spec_brake_interface || [];
                    let brakeMatch = false;
                    if (specs.brakeStyle === 'Rim Brake') {
                        brakeMatch = vBrakes.includes('Rim Brake');
                    } else {
                        const isDiscRim = !vBrakes.includes('Rim Brake');
                        const isRimBrakeRim = vBrakes.includes('Rim Brake');
                        brakeMatch = isDiscRim || (isRimBrakeRim && buildState._ui.showRimBrakeRims);
                    }
                    return sizeMatch && positionMatch && v.availableForSale && spokeMatch && brakeMatch;
                });
            };
            break;

        case 'Hub':
            cacheToSearch = allHubProductsCache;
            if (!specs.brakeStyle || !specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`] || !specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`] || (position === 'Rear' && !specs.freehubType)) return [];
            filterFn = p => {
                if (p.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return true;
                // For rear hubs, first perform a product-level check on available freehubs
                if (position === 'Rear' && (!p.availableFreehubs || !p.availableFreehubs.includes(specs.freehubType))) {
                    return false;
                }
                // Then check if any variant matches the rest of the specs
                return p.variants.some(v =>
        (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear") &&
        (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(specs.brakeStyle) && // This now handles "Rim Brake" correctly
        v.spec_hub_spacing === specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`] &&
        String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`]) &&
        v.availableForSale
    );
};
            break;

        case 'Spokes':
        case 'Nipples':
            // Spokes and Nipples generally don't have spec dependencies, so we return the whole cache.
            // Compatibility (e.g., with hook flange hubs) is handled visually in the UI, not by removing them from the list.
            cacheToSearch = (typePascal === 'Spokes') ? allSpokeProductsCache : allNippleProductsCache;
            filterFn = p => p.variants.some(v => v.availableForSale);
            break;
            
        case 'ValveStem':
            cacheToSearch = allValveStemProductsCache;
            const selectedRim = buildState.components[`${posLower}Rim`];
            // If no rim is selected, the section is disabled, but for completeness, we return an empty array.
            if (!selectedRim) return [];
            
            const rimDepth = selectedRim.rimDepth;
            // If the rim has no depth specified, all valves are considered compatible.
            if (rimDepth === null || typeof rimDepth === 'undefined') {
                filterFn = p => p.variants.some(v => v.availableForSale);
            } else {
                // Filter by rim depth compatibility.
                filterFn = p => p.variants.some(v => v.availableForSale && ((v.valve_min_depth === null || v.valve_max_depth === null) || (rimDepth >= v.valve_min_depth && rimDepth <= v.valve_max_depth)));
            }
            break;

        default:
            // Return an empty array for unknown types
            return [];
    }

    if (!cacheToSearch) return [];
    // Apply the determined filter function to the correct cache
    return cacheToSearch.filter(filterFn);
}
// --- END: HELPER FUNCTION ---

// --- START: UTILITY FUNCTION FOR SCROLLING ---
/**
 * Smoothly scrolls the viewport to the component subsection that was just interacted with.
 * This prevents the page from "jumping" when the selection options collapse.
 * @param {string} position 'Front' or 'Rear'.
 * @param {string} typePascal The component type in PascalCase (e.g., 'Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes').
 */
function scrollToComponentSection(position, typePascal) {
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const typeForId = typePascal.toLowerCase();
    
    const subsectionId = `${posLower}-${typeForId}-subsection`;
    const element = document.getElementById(subsectionId);

    if (element) {
        // Use a small timeout to allow the DOM to reflow after the options list collapses.
        // This makes the scroll feel smoother and more intentional.
        setTimeout(() => {
            element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
        }, 150);
    } else {
        console.warn(`scrollToComponentSection: Could not find element #${subsectionId}`);
    }
}
// --- END: UTILITY FUNCTION FOR SCROLLING ---
  
    function formatPrice(valueInCents) { const n = Number(valueInCents); return isNaN(n) ? "$0.00" : `$${(n / 100).toFixed(2)}`; }
    function debounce(func, wait) { let timeout; return function executedFunction(...args) { const later = () => { clearTimeout(timeout); func(...args); }; clearTimeout(timeout); timeout = setTimeout(later, wait); }; }
    function updateGlobalVendorLogoMap(productsArray) {
    if (!Array.isArray(productsArray)) return;
    productsArray.forEach(p => {
        const v = p.vendor;
        const l = p.vendorLogoUrl;
        if (v && (!vendorLogoMap[v] || (l && !vendorLogoMap[v].logoUrl))) {
            vendorLogoMap[v] = { name: v, logoUrl: l || null };
        }
    });
    // ADD THIS LINE: Expose the map after it's updated
    window.loamlabs = window.loamlabs || {};
    window.loamlabs.vendorLogoMap = vendorLogoMap;
}

/**
 * Initializes technical tooltips for spec labels.
 * Handles both hover (desktop) and click (mobile) states.
 */
function initializeInfoTooltips() {
    // Clean up any existing tooltips if re-initializing
    document.querySelectorAll('.info-tooltip-popup').forEach(el => el.remove());

    const triggers = document.querySelectorAll('.info-tooltip-trigger');

    triggers.forEach(trigger => {
        const text = trigger.dataset.tooltipText;
        if (!text) return;

        // Create the popup element
        const popup = document.createElement('div');
        popup.className = 'info-tooltip-popup';
        popup.textContent = text;
        document.body.appendChild(popup);

        const positionPopup = () => {
            const rect = trigger.getBoundingClientRect();
            popup.style.left = `${rect.left + (rect.width / 2)}px`;
            popup.style.top = `${rect.top - 10}px`;
        };

        // Desktop: Hover
        trigger.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
            positionPopup();
            popup.classList.add('is-visible');
        });
        trigger.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
            popup.classList.remove('is-visible');
        });

        // Mobile: Toggle on Click
        trigger.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            const wasVisible = popup.classList.contains('is-visible');
            
            // Hide all others
            document.querySelectorAll('.info-tooltip-popup').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('is-visible'));
            
            if (!wasVisible) {
                positionPopup();
                popup.classList.add('is-visible');
            }
        });
    });

    // Close tooltips when clicking anywhere else
    document.addEventListener('click', () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('.info-tooltip-popup').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('is-visible'));
    });
}

    function capitalizeFirstLetter(string) { if (!string) return ''; return string.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + string.slice(1); }
    function getDisplayName(typeLower) {
        if (typeLower === 'valvestem') return "Valve Stem";
        if (typeLower === 'nipples') return "Nipples";
        if (typeLower === 'spokes') return "Spokes";
        return capitalizeFirstLetter(typeLower);
    }
    function getNumericIdFromShopifyGid(gid) {
    if (typeof gid !== 'string') return null;
    const match = gid.match(/ProductVariant\/(\d+)/);
    return match ? parseInt(match[1]) : null;
}

function resetBuildStateToDefaults() {
    const newBuildId = `${Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000)}`;
    const defaults = {
        step: 1, buildType: null, ridingStyle: null, ridingStyleDisplay: null,
        customerSupplied: { front: { rim: false, hub: false }, rear: { rim: false, hub: false } },
        tubelessTapeInstalled: true,
        estimatedLeadTime: 0,
        specs: { frontWheelSize: null, rearWheelSize: null, frontSpokeCount: null, rearSpokeCount: null, brakeStyle: null, frontHubSpacing: null, rearHubSpacing: null, freehubType: null },
        components: { frontRim: null, rearRim: null, frontHub: null, rearHub: null, frontSpokes: null, rearSpokes: null, frontNipples: null, rearNipples: null, frontValveStem: null, rearValveStem: null, rearComponentFreehub: null },
        selectedOptionalAddons: {},
        subtotal: 0,
        buildId: newBuildId,
        _ui: {
            step2AutoSelected: {}, hasProgressedPastStep1: false,
            activeVendor: { frontRim: null, rearRim: null, frontHub: null, rearHub: null, frontSpokes: null, rearSpokes: null, frontNipples: null, rearNipples: null, frontValveStem: null, rearValveStem: null },
            isChangingComponent: null,
            valveStemExplicitlyRemoved: { front: false, rear: false },
            hasChanges: false, originalCartItemKeys: null, inEditMode: false
        }
    };

    // This is the key: Reset properties of the EXISTING object.
    Object.keys(buildState).forEach(key => delete buildState[key]);
    Object.assign(buildState, defaults);
}

async function handleAdminShareBuildClick() {
  const shareButton = document.getElementById('admin-share-build-button');
  if (!shareButton) return;

  if (!buildState || Object.keys(buildState).length === 0) {
    alert('Please configure a build before sharing.');
    return;
  }

  try {
    const buildStateJSON = JSON.stringify(buildState);
    console.log("Step 1: Original JSON Length:", buildStateJSON.length);

    const compressedData = LZString.compressToBase64(buildStateJSON);
    console.log("Step 2: Compressed Base64 Data:", compressedData);
    
    const shareableURL = `${window.location.origin}${window.location.pathname}#${compressedData}`;
    console.log("Step 3: Final URL to be copied:", shareableURL);

    // Modern "Copy to Clipboard" logic
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(shareableURL);

    // Give user feedback
    const originalButtonText = shareButton.textContent;
    shareButton.textContent = 'Copied to Clipboard!';
    shareButton.disabled = true;
    setTimeout(() => {
        shareButton.textContent = originalButtonText;
        shareButton.disabled = false;
        validateStep3(); // Re-validate to set correct disabled state
    }, 2500);

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error during link creation and copy:', error);
    alert('An error occurred while creating the share link. See console for details.');
  }
}

async function loadBuildFromShareableURL(compressedBuildData) {
    console.log("Step A: Raw data received from URL fragment:", compressedBuildData);
    
    try {
        const decodedBuildJSON = LZString.decompressFromBase64(compressedBuildData);
        console.log("Step B: Data after decompression:", decodedBuildJSON);
        
        if (!decodedBuildJSON) {
            throw new Error("Decompressed data from Base64 is null or empty.");
        }

        const loadedState = JSON.parse(decodedBuildJSON);

        // --- The rest of the function's logic remains the same ---
        const loadingOverlay = document.getElementById('builder-edit-loading-overlay');
        if (loadingOverlay) loadingOverlay.style.display = 'flex';

        resetBuildStateToDefaults();
        Object.assign(buildState, loadedState);
        if(loadedState.specs) buildState.specs = { ...buildState.specs, ...loadedState.specs };
        if(loadedState.components) buildState.components = { ...buildState.components, ...loadedState.components };
        if(loadedState.selectedOptionalAddons) buildState.selectedOptionalAddons = { ...buildState.selectedOptionalAddons, ...loadedState.selectedOptionalAddons };
        if(loadedState._ui) buildState._ui = { ...buildState._ui, ...loadedState._ui };
        if(loadedState.customerSupplied) buildState.customerSupplied = { ...buildState.customerSupplied, ...loadedState.customerSupplied };
        
        componentFetchPromises = { rims: null, hubs: null, spokes: null, nipples: null, valves: null, freehubs: null };

        updateStep1VisualFeedback();
        validateStep1();
        renderStep2();
        updateStep2OptionsVisibility();
        updateStep2VisualFeedback();
        validateStep2();
        triggerEarlyComponentFetches();

        await showStep(3);
        
        handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();

        const newUrl = window.location.protocol + "//" + window.location.host + window.location.pathname;
        window.history.pushState({ path: newUrl }, '', newUrl);

        if (loadingOverlay) loadingOverlay.style.display = 'none';
        
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[SHARE LINK] CRITICAL ERROR:', error);
        alert('The provided build link appears to be invalid or corrupt. Starting a new build.');
        resetBuildStateToDefaults();
        await showStep(1);
    }
}
  
function getSortableName(name) {
    if (typeof name !== 'string') return '';
    // Converts to lowercase and removes all non-letter/non-number characters
    return name.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '');
}
  
async function fetchAddonProductDetailsByGids(gidsArray) {
    if (!gidsArray || gidsArray.length === 0) {
        return [];
    }
    // console.log(`fetchAddonProductDetailsByGids: Fetching details for GIDs:`, gidsArray);

    const query = `
      query getAddonDetails($ids: [ID!]!) {
        nodes(ids: $ids) {
          ... on Product {
            __typename
            id
            title
            handle
            vendor
            pairingKey: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "pairing_key") { value }
            options(first: 5) { name values }
            variants(first: 50) {
              edges {
                node {
                  id
                  title
                  sku
                  availableForSale
                  price { amount currencyCode }
                  image { url(transform:{maxWidth:100, maxHeight:100}) altText }
                  selectedOptions { name value }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    `;
    try {
        const data = await storefrontApiQuery(query, { ids: gidsArray });
        if (data && data.nodes) {
            return data.nodes.filter(node => node && node.__typename === 'Product').map(p => {
                // Process variants minimally here, or do it where consumed
                const variants = p.variants.edges.map(edge => ({
                    ...edge.node,
                    price: { amount: parseFloat(edge.node.price.amount) * 100, code: edge.node.price.currencyCode }
                }));
                return {
                    id: p.id,
                    title: p.title,
                    handle: p.handle,
                    vendor: p.vendor,
                    pairingKeyValue: p.pairingKey?.value || null,
                    options: p.options,
                    variants: variants // Store processed variants
                };
            });
        }
        return [];
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error in fetchAddonProductDetailsByGids:", error, "for GIDs:", gidsArray);
        return [];
    }
}

async function applyCustomerSuppliedSelections() {
    console.log("Applying customer-supplied selections...");

    // This waits for the product data to be fetched and cached, which is correct.
    await Promise.all([
        componentFetchPromises.rims,
        componentFetchPromises.hubs
    ]);

    const positions = ['front', 'rear'];
    const componentsToProcess = [
        { type: 'Rim', cache: allRimProductsCache },
        { type: 'Hub', cache: allHubProductsCache }
    ];

    for (const position of positions) {
        for (const comp of componentsToProcess) {
            // Check if the user intended to supply this component
            if (buildState.customerSupplied[position][comp.type.toLowerCase()]) {
                const stateKey = `${position}${comp.type}`;
                const positionPascal = position.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + position.slice(1);

                // Only apply if the slot is currently empty
                if (buildState.components[stateKey]) {
                    console.log(`Skipping auto-selection for ${stateKey}, as it's already filled.`);
                    continue;
                }

                const productCache = comp.cache;
                if (productCache && productCache.length > 0) {
                    const suppliedProduct = productCache.find(p => p.vendor === 'Your Own Component');

                    if (suppliedProduct && suppliedProduct.variants.length > 0) {
                        
                        let variantToSelect = null;
                        const requiredSpokeCount = String(buildState.specs[`${position}SpokeCount`]);

                        // Logic is now different for Rims vs. Hubs
                        if (comp.type === 'Rim') {
                            const requiredWheelSize = buildState.specs[`${position}WheelSize`];
                            console.log(`[Customer Supplied Rim] Searching for variant with: Size=${requiredWheelSize}, Spokes=${requiredSpokeCount}`);
                            
                            variantToSelect = suppliedProduct.variants.find(variant => {
                                // Check for spoke count match
                                const spokeMatch = String(variant.spec_spoke_count) === requiredSpokeCount;

                                // Check for wheel size match (handles both single string and array of strings)
                                const sizeValue = variant.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                                const sizeMatch = Array.isArray(sizeValue)
                                    ? sizeValue.includes(requiredWheelSize)
                                    : sizeValue === requiredWheelSize;
                                
                                return sizeMatch && spokeMatch;
                            });

                        } else if (comp.type === 'Hub') {
                             console.log(`[Customer Supplied Hub] Searching for variant with: Spokes=${requiredSpokeCount}`);
                             variantToSelect = suppliedProduct.variants.find(variant =>
                                String(variant.spec_spoke_count) === requiredSpokeCount
                            );
                        }

                        // If no exact match is found, default to the first variant as a safe fallback.
                        if (!variantToSelect) {
                            console.warn(`Could not find a precise match for 'Your Own ${comp.type}' with the required specs. Defaulting to the first available variant.`);
                            variantToSelect = suppliedProduct.variants[0];
                        }

                        const componentData = {
                            variantId: variantToSelect.id,
                            productId: suppliedProduct.id,
                            productHandle: suppliedProduct.handle,
                            title: suppliedProduct.title,
                            variantTitle: variantToSelect.title,
                            sku: variantToSelect.sku,
                            price: variantToSelect.price.amount,
                            vendor: suppliedProduct.vendor,
                            image: variantToSelect.image,
                            pairingKey: suppliedProduct.pairingKey,
                            tags: suppliedProduct.tags || [],
                            selectedOptions: variantToSelect.selectedOptions,
                            optionalAddonProductGids: suppliedProduct.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [],
                            // Add the specific spec data to the component object for consistency
                            spec_spoke_count: variantToSelect.spec_spoke_count,
                            wheelSize: (comp.type === 'Rim') ? buildState.specs[`${position}WheelSize`] : null,
                            wheelModel: suppliedProduct.wheelModel
                        };

                        buildState.components[stateKey] = componentData;
                        console.log(`Pre-selected 'Your Own ${comp.type}' for ${position} with variant ${variantToSelect.title}.`);
                        
                        updateComponentUI(positionPascal, comp.type, componentData);
                        calculateWheelCosts(positionPascal);

                        // If we just auto-selected a Rim, we need to manually trigger the valve stem evaluation.
                        if (comp.type === 'Rim') {
                            evaluateValveStemForRimChange(positionPascal);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    // Update summary and validation after all potential changes
    updateSubtotal();
    updateBuildSummary();
    validateStep3();
}

function updateMismatchHints() {
    if (buildState.buildType !== 'Wheel Set') {
        document.querySelectorAll('.mismatch-hint, .match-pair-button--from-hint').forEach(hint => hint.remove());
        return;
    }

    const componentTypes = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'];

    const processHintForComponent = (position, type) => {
        const oppositePosition = position === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
        const posLower = position.toLowerCase();

        const currentComponent = buildState.components[`${posLower}${type}`];
        const oppositeComponent = buildState.components[`${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}${type}`];
        
        const imageContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${type.toLowerCase().replace('valvestem', 'valvestem')}-image-container`);
        const optionsContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${type.toLowerCase().replace('valvestem', 'valvestem')}-options-container`);

        imageContainer?.querySelector('.mismatch-hint')?.remove();
        optionsContainer?.querySelector('.match-pair-button--from-hint')?.remove();

        const isMatchPossible = (sourceComponent) => {
            if (!sourceComponent || !sourceComponent.pairingKey) return false;
            
            if (type === 'ValveStem') {
                const destRim = buildState.components[`${posLower}Rim`];
                return !!destRim; // Only return true if the destination rim exists
            }
            if (['Spokes', 'Nipples'].includes(type)) {
                return true;
            }

            const destSpecs = {
                wheelSize: buildState.specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`],
                spokeCount: buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`],
                brakeStyle: buildState.specs.brakeStyle,
                hubSpacing: buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`],
            };

            let cacheToSearch = type === 'Rim' ? allRimProductsCache : allHubProductsCache;
            if (type === 'Rim') {
                const sourceColor = (sourceComponent.variantTitle || '').split('/').pop().trim().toLowerCase();
                return cacheToSearch.some(p => p.pairingKey === sourceComponent.pairingKey && p.variants.some(v => {
                    const variantTitle = v.title || '';
                    return v.availableForSale &&
                        variantTitle.split('/').pop().trim().toLowerCase() === sourceColor &&
                        (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear") &&
                        String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(destSpecs.spokeCount) &&
                        (Array.isArray(v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue) ? v.spec_rim_size.parsedValue.includes(destSpecs.wheelSize) : v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue === destSpecs.wheelSize);
                }));
            } else if (type === 'Hub') {
                const sourceHubColor = sourceComponent.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value;
                return cacheToSearch.some(p => p.pairingKey === sourceComponent.pairingKey && p.variants.some(v => 
                    v.availableForSale &&
                    v.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value === sourceHubColor &&
                    (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(destSpecs.brakeStyle) &&
                    v.spec_hub_spacing === destSpecs.hubSpacing &&
                    String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(destSpecs.spokeCount)
                ));
            }
            return false;
        };

        const createHintElement = (isForOptionsContainer) => {
            const hintElement = document.createElement('button');
            hintElement.className = 'builder-button match-pair-button match-pair-button--from-hint';
            hintElement.dataset.action = 'match-from-hint'; 
            hintElement.dataset.position = position;
            hintElement.dataset.type = type;
            hintElement.textContent = `Match to ${oppositePosition} ${getDisplayName(type.toLowerCase())}`;
            
            if (isForOptionsContainer) {
                hintElement.style.marginBottom = '15px';
                hintElement.style.width = '100%';
            }
            return hintElement;
        };

        if (currentComponent && oppositeComponent) {
            let isMismatched = false;
            if (type === 'Rim') isMismatched = !areRimsPaired(currentComponent, oppositeComponent);
            else if (type === 'Hub') isMismatched = !areHubsPaired(currentComponent, oppositeComponent);
            else if (type === 'Spokes') isMismatched = !areSpokesPaired(currentComponent, oppositeComponent);
            else if (type === 'Nipples') isMismatched = !areNipplesPaired(currentComponent, oppositeComponent);
            else if (type === 'ValveStem') isMismatched = !areValveStemsPaired(currentComponent, oppositeComponent);

            if (isMismatched && isMatchPossible(oppositeComponent)) {
                const hintElement = document.createElement('div');
                hintElement.className = 'mismatch-hint';
                hintElement.dataset.action = 'match-from-hint'; 
                hintElement.dataset.position = position;
                hintElement.dataset.type = type;
                hintElement.innerHTML = `<span>Click to Match to ${oppositePosition}</span>`;
                hintElement.style.animation = 'subtleFadeIn 0.5s ease-out forwards';
                imageContainer?.appendChild(hintElement);
            }
        } else if (!currentComponent && oppositeComponent) {
            if (optionsContainer && isMatchPossible(oppositeComponent)) {
                const hint = createHintElement(true);
                optionsContainer.prepend(hint);
            }
        }
    };

    componentTypes.forEach(type => {
        processHintForComponent('Front', type);
        processHintForComponent('Rear', type);
    });
}

  
function manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(position, baseTypePascal, oldBaseVariantId, newBaseVariantId, newBaseProductOptionalAddonGids) {
    const addonKeysToProcess = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons);
    let addonsWereReassignedOrCleared = false;

    // console.log(`   New base product supports addon GIDs:`, newBaseProductOptionalAddonGids);

    for (const currentAddonKey of addonKeysToProcess) {
        const selectedAddon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[currentAddonKey];

        if (selectedAddon.baseComponentPosition === position &&
            selectedAddon.baseComponentType === baseTypePascal &&
            selectedAddon.baseComponentVariantId === oldBaseVariantId) {

            // Check if the new base variant's *product* still supports this *addon product type*
            const newBaseSupportsThisAddonProductType = newBaseProductOptionalAddonGids &&
                                                      newBaseProductOptionalAddonGids.includes(selectedAddon.addonProductId);

            if (newBaseSupportsThisAddonProductType) {
                // Addon product type IS still supported. Re-key the addon to the new base variant.
                const newAddonKey = `${position}_${baseTypePascal}_${newBaseVariantId}_${selectedAddon.addonProductId}`;
                
                // Only re-assign if the key is actually changing (it should be)
                // and to avoid issues if for some reason old and new variant ID were the same.
                if (currentAddonKey !== newAddonKey) {
                    console.log(`     from base variant ${oldBaseVariantId} to ${newBaseVariantId}.`);
                    console.log(`     Old key: ${currentAddonKey}, New key: ${newAddonKey}`);

                    // Create the new entry
                    buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[newAddonKey] = {
                        ...selectedAddon, // Copy all existing addon details
                        baseComponentVariantId: newBaseVariantId // Update the base variant ID
                    };
                    // Delete the old entry
                    delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[currentAddonKey];
                    addonsWereReassignedOrCleared = true;
                    saveLastActiveBuild();
                } else {
                }

                // Phase 1: We keep the same addon *variant*.
                // Future Phase 2 of sticky could involve re-evaluating if a *different variant* of the same addon product
                // would be more appropriate for the newBaseVariantId.

            } else {
                // Addon product type is NO LONGER supported by the new base variant's product. Clear it.
                addonsWereReassignedOrCleared = true;
                saveLastActiveBuild();
            }
        }
    }
    return addonsWereReassignedOrCleared;
}

async function attemptRevalidateComponent(position, typePascal, currentComponentData) {
    // --- Skip revalidation for Virtual Components (Integrated Wheels) ---
    if (currentComponentData && currentComponentData.isVirtual) {
        console.log(`Revalidation: Skipping Virtual Component for ${position} ${typePascal}`);
        return { ...currentComponentData, _reval_action: 'kept' };
    }
    const { productId, variantId, selectedOptions } = currentComponentData;
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();

    console.log(`Attempting revalidation for ${position} ${typePascal}... Current VariantID: ${variantId}`);

    let cacheToSearch;
    let checkCompatibilityFn;
    let newSpecs = { position: position };

    switch (typePascal) {
        case 'Rim':
            cacheToSearch = allRimProductsCache;
            checkCompatibilityFn = (productNode, variantNode, specs) => {
                if (!variantNode) return false;
                
                // --- INTEGRATED WHEEL LOGIC ---
                const isIntegrated = productNode.tags && productNode.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel');
                
                // Common Checks
                const sizeValue = variantNode.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                const sizeMatch = Array.isArray(sizeValue) ? sizeValue.includes(specs.size) : sizeValue === specs.size;
                const positionMatch = variantNode.spec_position === specs.position || variantNode.spec_position === "Front/Rear";
                const availabilityMatch = productNode.vendor === 'Your Own Component' ? true : variantNode.availableForSale;

                if (isIntegrated) {
                    // For Integrated, bypass spoke check, but check Hub Specs
                    const posLower = specs.position.toLowerCase();
                    const hubSpacing = buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];
                    const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
                    
                    const spacingMatch = variantNode.spec_hub_spacing === hubSpacing;
                    const brakeMatch = (variantNode.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle);
                    
                    // Also check Freehub if Rear
