                    let freehubMatch = true;
                    if (posLower === 'rear') {
                         const targetFreehub = buildState.specs.freehubType;
                         if (productNode.availableFreehubs && !productNode.availableFreehubs.includes(targetFreehub)) {
                             freehubMatch = false;
                         }
                    }

                    return availabilityMatch && sizeMatch && positionMatch && spacingMatch && brakeMatch && freehubMatch;
                } else {
                    // Standard Logic
                    const spokeMatch = !specs.spokeCount || (String(variantNode.spec_spoke_count) === String(specs.spokeCount));
                    return availabilityMatch && sizeMatch && positionMatch && spokeMatch;
                }
            };
            newSpecs.size = buildState.specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`];
            newSpecs.spokeCount = buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`];

            if (!newSpecs.size || !newSpecs.spokeCount) {
                console.warn(`Revalidation (${position} Rim): Wheel Size or Spoke Count is missing. Cannot validate.`);
                return null;
            }

            const originalProductInCacheRim = cacheToSearch.find(p => p.id === productId);
            if (!originalProductInCacheRim) {
                console.warn(`Revalidation: Original Product ID ${productId} not found in rim cache. Clearing selection.`);
                return null;
            }

            const currentVariantNode = originalProductInCacheRim.variants.find(v => v.id === variantId);
            if (currentVariantNode && checkCompatibilityFn(originalProductInCacheRim, currentVariantNode, newSpecs)) {
                 console.log(`Revalidation: Current ${position} Rim variant IS STILL COMPATIBLE.`);
                 return { ...currentComponentData, _reval_action: 'kept', wheelSize: newSpecs.size, spokeCount: newSpecs.spokeCount };
            }

            console.log(`Revalidation: Current ${position} Rim variant IS NO LONGER COMPATIBLE. Searching for replacement within the same product model.`);
            let replacementVariantRim = null;
            for (const variant of originalProductInCacheRim.variants) {
                if (checkCompatibilityFn(originalProductInCacheRim, variant, newSpecs)) {
                    replacementVariantRim = variant;
                    break;
                }
            }

            if (replacementVariantRim) {
                console.log(`Revalidation: Auto-replacing ${position} Rim with variant ${replacementVariantRim.title}`);
                let newComponentStateData = {
                    variantId: replacementVariantRim.id, productId: originalProductInCacheRim.id, productHandle: originalProductInCacheRim.handle,
                    title: originalProductInCacheRim.title, variantTitle: replacementVariantRim.title, sku: replacementVariantRim.sku,
                    price: replacementVariantRim.price.amount, vendor: originalProductInCacheRim.vendor, image: replacementVariantRim.image,
                    pairingKey: originalProductInCacheRim.pairingKey, selectedOptions: replacementVariantRim.selectedOptions,
                    optionalAddonProductGids: originalProductInCacheRim.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [], _reval_action: 'replaced',
                    tags: originalProductInCacheRim.tags || [],
                    wheelSize: newSpecs.size, spokeCount: newSpecs.spokeCount,
                    wheelModel: originalProductInCacheRim.wheelModel,
                    rimDepth: originalProductInCacheRim.rimDepth,
                    rim_erd: replacementVariantRim.rim_erd ?? originalProductInCacheRim.rim_erd ?? null,
                    weight_g: replacementVariantRim.weight_g ?? originalProductInCacheRim.weight_g ?? null
                };
                return newComponentStateData;
            }

            console.warn(`Revalidation: No compatible replacement Rim variant found within product "${originalProductInCacheRim.title}". Clearing selection.`);
            return null;

        case 'Hub':
            cacheToSearch = allHubProductsCache;
            checkCompatibilityFn = (productNode, variantNode, specs) => {
                if (!variantNode || !productNode) return false;
                if (specs.position === 'Rear' && productNode.vendor !== 'Your Own Component') {
                    if (!productNode.availableFreehubs || !productNode.availableFreehubs.includes(specs.freehubType)) {
                        return false;
                    }
                }
                const positionMatch = variantNode.spec_position === specs.position || variantNode.spec_position === "Front/Rear";
                const variantBrakeInterfaces = variantNode.spec_brake_interface || [];
                const brakeMatch = productNode.vendor === 'Your Own Component' ? true : variantBrakeInterfaces.includes(specs.brakeStyle);
                const spacingMatch = productNode.vendor === 'Your Own Component' ? true : variantNode.spec_hub_spacing === specs.hubSpacing;
                const spokeMatch = String(variantNode.spec_spoke_count) === String(specs.spokeCount);
                const availabilityMatch = productNode.vendor === 'Your Own Component' ? true : variantNode.availableForSale;
                return availabilityMatch && positionMatch && brakeMatch && spacingMatch && spokeMatch;
            };
            newSpecs.brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
            newSpecs.hubSpacing = buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];
            newSpecs.freehubType = (posLower === 'rear') ? buildState.specs.freehubType : null;
            newSpecs.spokeCount = buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`];

            if (!newSpecs.brakeStyle || !newSpecs.hubSpacing || (posLower === 'rear' && !newSpecs.freehubType) || !newSpecs.spokeCount) {
                console.warn(`Revalidation (${position} Hub): One or more critical hub specs missing. Cannot validate. Clearing.`);
                return null;
            }

            const originalProductInCache = cacheToSearch.find(p => p.id === productId);
            if (!originalProductInCache) {
                console.warn(`Revalidation: Original Product ID ${productId} not found in hub cache. Clearing selection.`);
                return null;
            }
            const originalWheelModel = originalProductInCache.wheelModel;
            const currentVariantNodeOriginalProduct = originalProductInCache.variants.find(v => v.id === variantId);

            if (currentVariantNodeOriginalProduct && checkCompatibilityFn(originalProductInCache, currentVariantNodeOriginalProduct, newSpecs)) {
                console.log(`Revalidation: Current ${position} Hub variant ${currentVariantNodeOriginalProduct.title} IS STILL COMPATIBLE.`);
                let updatedComponentData = { ...currentComponentData, _reval_action: 'kept' };
                if (newSpecs.position === 'Rear') {
                    updatedComponentData.spec_freehub = newSpecs.freehubType;
                }
                return updatedComponentData;
            }

            console.log(`Revalidation: Current ${position} Hub variant IS NO LONGER COMPATIBLE. Searching for replacement.`);

            // For "Your Own Component", we only search within the same product.
            const productsToSearch = (originalProductInCache.vendor === 'Your Own Component')
                ? [originalProductInCache]
                : cacheToSearch.filter(p => p.wheelModel === originalWheelModel);

            if (productsToSearch.length === 0) {
                 console.warn(`Revalidation: Original Hub has no wheelModel or no products in group. Cannot search for alternatives. Clearing.`);
                 return null;
            }

            let replacementVariant = null;
            let replacementProduct = null;
            const targetColor = selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value;
            let potentialReplacements = [];

            for (const candidateProduct of productsToSearch) {
                for (const variant of candidateProduct.variants) {
                    if (checkCompatibilityFn(candidateProduct, variant, newSpecs)) {
                        potentialReplacements.push({ variant, product: candidateProduct });
                    }
                }
            }

            if (potentialReplacements.length > 0) {
                let preferredReplacement = potentialReplacements.find(pr => pr.product.id === productId);
                if (targetColor) {
                    let colorMatchedInOriginalProduct = null;
                    if (preferredReplacement) {
                        colorMatchedInOriginalProduct = potentialReplacements.find(pr => pr.product.id === productId && pr.variant.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value === targetColor);
                    }
                    if (colorMatchedInOriginalProduct) {
                        preferredReplacement = colorMatchedInOriginalProduct;
                    }
                    const colorMatchedOverall = potentialReplacements.find(pr => pr.variant.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value === targetColor);
                    if (colorMatchedOverall) {
                        replacementVariant = colorMatchedOverall.variant;
                        replacementProduct = colorMatchedOverall.product;
                    }
                }
                if (!replacementVariant) {
                    if (preferredReplacement) {
                        replacementVariant = preferredReplacement.variant;
                        replacementProduct = preferredReplacement.product;
                    } else {
                        replacementVariant = potentialReplacements[0].variant;
                        replacementProduct = potentialReplacements[0].product;
                    }
                }
            }

            if (replacementVariant && replacementProduct) {
                console.log(`Revalidation: Auto-replacing ${position} Hub with variant ${replacementVariant.title}`);
                let productOptionalAddonGids = replacementProduct.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [];
                let newComponentStateData = {
                    variantId: replacementVariant.id, productId: replacementProduct.id, productHandle: replacementProduct.handle,
                    title: replacementProduct.title, variantTitle: replacementVariant.title, sku: replacementVariant.sku,
                    price: replacementVariant.price.amount, vendor: replacementProduct.vendor, image: replacementVariant.image,
                    pairingKey: replacementProduct.pairingKey, selectedOptions: replacementVariant.selectedOptions,
                    optionalAddonProductGids: productOptionalAddonGids, _reval_action: 'replaced',
                    tags: replacementProduct.tags || [], spec_spoke_count: String(replacementVariant.spec_spoke_count),
                    spec_brake_interface: replacementVariant.spec_brake_interface, spec_hub_spacing: replacementVariant.spec_hub_spacing,
                    wheelModel: replacementProduct.wheelModel,
                    spec_freehub: (newSpecs.position === 'Rear') ? newSpecs.freehubType : null,
                    weight_g: replacementVariant.weight_g ?? replacementProduct.weight_g ?? null
                };
                return newComponentStateData;
            }

            console.warn(`Revalidation: No compatible replacement Hub found for ${position}. Clearing selection.`);
            return null;

        default:
            console.warn(`attemptRevalidateComponent: Revalidation not configured for type ${typePascal}`);
            return {...currentComponentData, _reval_action: 'kept_no_logic'};
    }
}

async function revalidateAllStep3Selections() {
    if (buildState.step !== 3) return;
    let somethingChangedInState = false;

    const positions = [];
    if (buildState.buildType === 'Front' || buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') positions.push('Front');
    if (buildState.buildType === 'Rear' || buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') positions.push('Rear');

    for (const position of positions) {
        // --- Revalidate Rims ---
        const rimKey = `${position.toLowerCase()}Rim`;
        const currentRim = buildState.components[rimKey];
        if (currentRim) {
            const newRimData = await attemptRevalidateComponent(position, 'Rim', currentRim);
            if (newRimData === null) {
                if(clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'Rim')) somethingChangedInState = true;
                if(buildState.components[`${position.toLowerCase()}ValveStem`]) {
                    if(clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'ValveStem')) somethingChangedInState = true;
                }
                await loadAndFilterRimsForPosition(position, true);
            } else if (newRimData._reval_action === 'replaced') {
                manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(
                    position,
                    'Rim',
                    currentRim.variantId,
                    newRimData.variantId,
                    newRimData.optionalAddonProductGids
                );
                buildState.components[rimKey] = newRimData;
                updateComponentUI(position, 'Rim', newRimData);
                calculateWheelCosts(position);
                evaluateValveStemForRimChange(position);
                buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
                updateStep3ButtonText();
                somethingChangedInState = true;
            } else if (newRimData._reval_action === 'kept') {
                buildState.components[rimKey] = newRimData;
                updateComponentUI(position, 'Rim', newRimData);
                evaluateValveStemForRimChange(position);
            }
        }

        // --- Revalidate Hubs ---
        const hubKey = `${position.toLowerCase()}Hub`;
        const currentHub = buildState.components[hubKey];
        if (currentHub) {
            const newHubData = await attemptRevalidateComponent(position, 'Hub', currentHub);

            if (newHubData === null) {
                if(clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'Hub')) somethingChangedInState = true;
                if(buildState.components[`${position.toLowerCase()}Spokes`]) {
                    if(clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'Spokes')) somethingChangedInState = true;
                }
                if(buildState.components[`${position.toLowerCase()}Nipples`]) {
                    if(clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'Nipples')) somethingChangedInState = true;
                }
                await loadAndFilterHubsForPosition(position, true);
            } else if (newHubData._reval_action === 'replaced') {
                manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(
                    position, 'Hub', currentHub.variantId, newHubData.variantId,
                    newHubData.optionalAddonProductGids
                );
                buildState.components[hubKey] = newHubData;

                if (position === 'Rear') {
                    const fullProductData = allHubProductsCache.find(p => p.id === newHubData.productId);
                    if (fullProductData) {
                        setComponentFreehubForHub({ ...newHubData, freehubVariantMap: fullProductData.freehubVariantMap });
                    }
                }

                updateComponentUI(position, 'Hub', newHubData);
                calculateWheelCosts(position);
                buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
                updateStep3ButtonText();
                somethingChangedInState = true;
            } else if (newHubData._reval_action === 'kept') {
                const oldFreehub = currentHub.spec_freehub;
                const newFreehub = newHubData.spec_freehub;
                buildState.components[hubKey] = newHubData;

                if (position === 'Rear') {
                    const fullProductData = allHubProductsCache.find(p => p.id === newHubData.productId);
                    if (fullProductData) {
                        setComponentFreehubForHub({ ...newHubData, freehubVariantMap: fullProductData.freehubVariantMap });
                    }
                }

                updateComponentUI(position, 'Hub', newHubData);
                if (oldFreehub !== newFreehub) {
                    somethingChangedInState = true;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if (somethingChangedInState) {
        updateSubtotal();
        updateBuildSummary();
        updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
        validateStep3();
        saveLastActiveBuild();
    }
}
  
function triggerEarlyComponentFetches() {
    const currentRidingStyle = buildState.ridingStyle;
    if (!currentRidingStyle) return; // Wait until we know the style

    // 1. RIMS (Only fetch if not already in progress)
    if (!componentFetchPromises.rims) {
        console.log(`[Predictive] Starting Rim fetch for: ${currentRidingStyle}`);
        componentFetchPromises.rims = fetchRimProducts(currentRidingStyle).catch(err => {
            console.error("Early rim fetch failed:", err);
            componentFetchPromises.rims = null; // Allow retry
        });
    }

    // 2. HUBS (Discipline agnostic, fetch immediately)
    if (!componentFetchPromises.hubs) {
        console.log(`[Predictive] Starting Hub fetch...`);
        componentFetchPromises.hubs = fetchHubProducts().catch(err => {
            console.error("Early hub fetch failed:", err);
            componentFetchPromises.hubs = null; // Allow retry
        });
    }

    // 3. Other components (Spokes, Nipples, etc.)
    if (!componentFetchPromises.spokes) componentFetchPromises.spokes = fetchSpokeProducts();
    if (!componentFetchPromises.nipples) componentFetchPromises.nipples = fetchNippleProducts();
    if (!componentFetchPromises.valves) componentFetchPromises.valves = fetchValveStemProducts();
    if (!componentFetchPromises.freehubs) componentFetchPromises.freehubs = fetchFreehubComponentProducts();
}
  
function clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, typePascal) {
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const stateKeyBase = `${posLower}${typePascal}`; // e.g., "frontSpokes"

    const clearedBaseComponent = buildState.components[stateKeyBase];
    if (!clearedBaseComponent) {
        // console.log(`clearComponentAndItsAddons: No ${position} ${typePascal} to clear.`);
        return false; // Nothing was cleared
    }

    const baseVariantIdToClearAddonsFor = clearedBaseComponent.variantId;

    // 1. Clear base component from buildState
    buildState.components[stateKeyBase] = null;

    // 2. Clear associated optional addons for the specific cleared base component variant
    let addonsWereCleared = false;
    const addonKeysToPotentiallyRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons);
    for (const addonKey of addonKeysToPotentiallyRemove) {
        const selectedAddon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKey];
        if (selectedAddon.baseComponentPosition === position &&
            selectedAddon.baseComponentType === typePascal && // Ensure type matches (e.g., 'Spokes')
            selectedAddon.baseComponentVariantId === baseVariantIdToClearAddonsFor) {
            
            delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKey];
            addonsWereCleared = true;
            saveLastActiveBuild();
        }
    }

    // 3. Update UI for the cleared base component
    // This will also trigger updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard for the (now null) base component.
    updateComponentUI(position, typePascal, null);

    // 4. Recalculate costs, update summary, and re-validate Step 3
    // For hub/spoke incompatibility, calculateWheelCosts for the *specific wheel* might be important
    // if a hub (which determines assembly cost) was cleared.
    if (typePascal === 'Hub') { // If a hub was cleared, assembly cost might change
         calculateWheelCosts(position);
    }
    updateSubtotal();
    updateBuildSummary();
    validateStep3();
    saveLastActiveBuild();
    updateMismatchHints();
  
    return true; // Indicates that the base component (and potentially addons) were cleared
}
  
// --- BLOCK FOR ALL ADDON MODAL HELPER FUNCTIONS ---

async function fetchAndDisplayAddonDetailsInModal(addonProductGidsString) {
    if (!addonsModalBody) {
        console.error("fetchAndDisplayAddonDetailsInModal: Modal body element not found.");
        addonsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>Error: Modal body not available.</p>';
        return;
    }

    const productGids = addonProductGidsString.split(',').filter(gid => gid.trim() !== '');
    if (productGids.length === 0) {
        addonsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>No add-on GIDs provided.</p>';
        return;
    }

    addonsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>Loading add-on details...</p>';

    const query = `
      query getAddonProductsDetails($ids: [ID!]!) {
        nodes(ids: $ids) {
          ... on Product {
            __typename
            id
            title
            handle
            vendor
            pairingKey: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "pairing_key") { value } # <<< --- ADD THIS LINE ---
            options(first: 5) {
              id
              name
              values
            }
            variants(first: 50) {
              edges {
                node {
                  id
                  title
                  sku
                  availableForSale
                  price { amount currencyCode }
                  image { url(transform:{maxWidth:100, maxHeight:100}) altText }
                  selectedOptions { name value }
                }
              }
            }
            # If your addon products themselves can have 'optional_addon_gids' (unlikely for now, but if so, keep this part)
            # optionalAddonProductGids: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "optional_addon_gids") {
            #     value
            # }
          }
        }
      }
    `;

    try {
        const data = await storefrontApiQuery(query, { ids: productGids });

        if (!data || !data.nodes || data.nodes.length === 0) {
            addonsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>Could not fetch details for the add-ons.</p>';
            console.warn("fetchAndDisplayAddonDetailsInModal: No nodes returned for addon GIDs", productGids, data);
            return;
        }

        // Process the fetched products to include the pairingKey value directly
        const addonProducts = data.nodes
            .filter(node => node && node.__typename === 'Product')
            .map(productNode => {
                return {
                    ...productNode, // Spread all existing product data
                    pairingKeyValue: productNode.pairingKey?.value || null // Add pairingKeyValue for easier access
                };
            });


        if (addonProducts.length === 0) {
            addonsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>No valid add-on products found.</p>';
            return;
        }

        if (addonsModal) {
            // Store the processed products (which now include pairingKeyValue)
            addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts = JSON.stringify(addonProducts);
        }
        renderAddonProductsInModal(addonProducts);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Error fetching addon product details:", error);
        addonsModalBody.innerHTML = `<p>Error loading add-on details: ${error.message}</p>`;
    }
}

// --- START: DELEGATING HANDLER FOR MODAL ACTION BUTTONS --- // <<< This would start on line 208
function handleModalActionButtonsClick(event) {
    const addBuildButton = event.target.closest('.add-addon-to-build-btn');
    const matchButton = event.target.closest('.match-addon-btn'); // Generic class for both match buttons

    if (addBuildButton) {
        handleAddonBuildButtonClick(event); 
    } else if (matchButton) {
        handleGenericMatchButtonClick(event, matchButton);
    }
}
// --- END: DELEGATING HANDLER FOR MODAL ACTION BUTTONS ---
  
function renderAddonProductsInModal(addonProducts) {
    if (!addonsModalBody) return;
    addonsModalBody.innerHTML = ''; 

    const basePosFromModal = addonsModal.dataset.basePosition;
    const baseTypeFromModal = addonsModal.dataset.baseType;
    const currentBaseComponentVariantId = addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId;

    addonProducts.forEach(product => { 
        if (!product.variants || !product.variants.edges || product.variants.edges.length === 0) {
            console.warn(`Addon product ${product.title} has no variants or variants data is missing. Skipping.`);
            return;
        }

        const productCard = document.createElement('div');
        productCard.className = 'addon-item-card';
        productCard.dataset.addonProductId = product.id;

        let cardHTML = `
            <div class="addon-item-image">
                ${product.variants.edges[0].node.image ? `<img src="${product.variants.edges[0].node.image.url}" alt="${product.title}">` : '<div class="selected-addon-thumbnail-placeholder"></div>'}
            </div>
            <div class="addon-item-details">
                <h4>${product.title}</h4>
                <div class="addon-variant-selector" data-product-id="${product.id}"></div>
                <p class="addon-variant-price" data-product-id="${product.id}"></p>
            </div>
            <div class="addon-item-actions">
                <button type="button" class="builder-button add-addon-to-build-btn" data-product-id="${product.id}" disabled>Add to Build</button>
            </div>
        `;
        productCard.innerHTML = cardHTML;
        addonsModalBody.appendChild(productCard);

        const variantSelectorContainer = productCard.querySelector(`.addon-variant-selector[data-product-id="${product.id}"]`);
        
        let actualSelectedAddonVariantGidForThisInstance = null;
        if (basePosFromModal && baseTypeFromModal && currentBaseComponentVariantId) {
            const fullAddonKeyForLookup = `${basePosFromModal}_${baseTypeFromModal}_${currentBaseComponentVariantId}_${product.id}`;
            const selectedAddonInstanceDetails = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[fullAddonKeyForLookup];
            
            if (selectedAddonInstanceDetails) {
                actualSelectedAddonVariantGidForThisInstance = selectedAddonInstanceDetails.addonVariantId;
            }
        }

        populateAddonVariantSelector(product, variantSelectorContainer, actualSelectedAddonVariantGidForThisInstance);
        updateAddonPriceAndButtonState(product, productCard); 
    });
    
    if (basePosFromModal && baseTypeFromModal && currentBaseComponentVariantId) {
        updateAddonButtonsStateInModal(basePosFromModal, baseTypeFromModal, currentBaseComponentVariantId);
    }
    
    addonsModalBody.removeEventListener('change', handleAddonVariantChangeInModal); 
    addonsModalBody.addEventListener('change', handleAddonVariantChangeInModal);

    addonsModalBody.removeEventListener('click', handleModalActionButtonsClick); // Remove if already exists
    addonsModalBody.addEventListener('click', handleModalActionButtonsClick);
}

function populateAddonVariantSelector(product, container, currentlySelectedAddonVariantGid) {
    container.innerHTML = ''; 

    let selectedVariantNodeDetails = null;

    // Priority 1: Use the "sticky" variant already selected in the build
    if (currentlySelectedAddonVariantGid) {
        const foundEdge = product.variants.edges.find(edge => edge.node.id === currentlySelectedAddonVariantGid);
        if (foundEdge) {
            selectedVariantNodeDetails = foundEdge.node;
        }
    }

    // Priority 2: If no sticky variant (or it was removed), find the first one that is IN STOCK
    if (!selectedVariantNodeDetails) {
        const firstAvailableEdge = product.variants.edges.find(edge => edge.node.availableForSale);
        if (firstAvailableEdge) {
            selectedVariantNodeDetails = firstAvailableEdge.node;
        }
    }

    product.options.forEach(option => { 
        if (option.values.length > 0) { 
            const optionDiv = document.createElement('div');
            optionDiv.className = 'addon-option-group';
            
            const label = document.createElement('label');
            label.htmlFor = `addon-${product.id}-option-${option.name.replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`;
            label.textContent = `${option.name}:`;
            optionDiv.appendChild(label);
            
            const select = document.createElement('select');
            select.id = `addon-${product.id}-option-${option.name.replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`;
            select.dataset.optionName = option.name;
            select.dataset.productId = product.id;

            let valueToPreselect = null;
            if (selectedVariantNodeDetails && selectedVariantNodeDetails.selectedOptions) {
                const matchingSelectedOptionFromVariant = selectedVariantNodeDetails.selectedOptions.find(selOpt => selOpt.name === option.name);
                if (matchingSelectedOptionFromVariant) {
                    valueToPreselect = matchingSelectedOptionFromVariant.value;
                }
            }

            option.values.forEach(value => { 
                const opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = value;
                
                // Check if THIS specific option value is available in ANY in-stock variant
                // (This provides a hint to the user in the dropdown)
                const isPossibleInStock = product.variants.edges.some(edge => 
                    edge.node.availableForSale && 
                    edge.node.selectedOptions.some(so => so.name === option.name && so.value === value)
                );
                
                opt.textContent = isPossibleInStock ? value : `${value} (Out of Stock)`;
                if (valueToPreselect && value === valueToPreselect) {
                    opt.selected = true; 
                }
                select.appendChild(opt);
            });
            optionDiv.appendChild(select);
            container.appendChild(optionDiv);
        }
    });
}

function handleAddonVariantChangeInModal(event) {
    if (event.target.tagName === 'SELECT' && event.target.closest('.addon-variant-selector')) {
        const selectElement = event.target;
        const productId = selectElement.dataset.productId;
        const productCard = addonsModalBody.querySelector(`.addon-item-card[data-addon-product-id="${productId}"]`);
        
        const allAddonProductsData = JSON.parse(addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts || '[]');
        const productData = allAddonProductsData.find(p => p.id === productId);

        if (productData && productCard) {
            updateAddonPriceAndButtonState(productData, productCard); 
            
            const basePosFromModal = addonsModal.dataset.basePosition;
            const baseTypeFromModal = addonsModal.dataset.baseType;
            const baseVarIdFromModal = addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId;
            if (basePosFromModal && baseTypeFromModal && baseVarIdFromModal) { 
                updateAddonButtonsStateInModal(basePosFromModal, baseTypeFromModal, baseVarIdFromModal);
            }
        }
    }
}

function updateAddonPriceAndButtonState(product, productCard) {
    const selectedOptionsFromForm = [];
    const selects = productCard.querySelectorAll('.addon-variant-selector select');
    
    if (selects.length > 0) {
        selects.forEach(select => {
            selectedOptionsFromForm.push({
                name: select.dataset.optionName,
                value: select.value
            });
        });
    } else { 
        product.options.forEach(opt => {
            if (opt.values.length === 1) {
                selectedOptionsFromForm.push({ name: opt.name, value: opt.values[0] });
            }
        });
    }

    const matchingVariantEdge = product.variants.edges.find(edge => {
        const variant = edge.node;
        if (selectedOptionsFromForm.length === 0 && variant.selectedOptions.length === 0) return true;
        if (selectedOptionsFromForm.length !== variant.selectedOptions.length) return false;
        return selectedOptionsFromForm.every(selOpt => 
            variant.selectedOptions.some(vOpt => vOpt.name === selOpt.name && vOpt.value === selOpt.value)
        );
    });

    const priceElement = productCard.querySelector('.addon-variant-price');
    const addButton = productCard.querySelector('.add-addon-to-build-btn');
    const imageElement = productCard.querySelector('.addon-item-image img'); 
    const imagePlaceholder = productCard.querySelector('.addon-item-image .selected-addon-thumbnail-placeholder'); 

    if (matchingVariantEdge && matchingVariantEdge.node.availableForSale) {
        const variantNode = matchingVariantEdge.node;
        priceElement.textContent = `Price: ${formatPrice(parseFloat(variantNode.price.amount) * 100)}`;
        priceElement.classList.remove('is-unavailable-text'); // Remove red color if present
        
        // ENABLE the button
        addButton.disabled = false;
        addButton.style.opacity = "1";
        addButton.style.cursor = "pointer";

        addButton.dataset.selectedVariantId = variantNode.id; 
        addButton.dataset.selectedVariantPrice = parseFloat(variantNode.price.amount) * 100;
        
        let addonVariantDisplayTitle = product.title;
        const optionsString = variantNode.selectedOptions.map(o => o.value).join(' / ');
        if (optionsString && optionsString !== 'Default Title') {
             addonVariantDisplayTitle += ` (${optionsString})`;
        }
        addButton.dataset.selectedVariantFullTitle = addonVariantDisplayTitle;
        
        if (variantNode.image && variantNode.image.url) {
            if (imageElement) {
                imageElement.src = variantNode.image.url;
                imageElement.style.display = 'block';
                if (imagePlaceholder) imagePlaceholder.style.display = 'none';
            }
            addButton.dataset.selectedVariantImage = variantNode.image.url;
        }
    } else {
        // DISABLE the button if out of stock or variant doesn't exist
        priceElement.textContent = "Option currently unavailable";
        priceElement.classList.add('is-unavailable-text'); // Add a red styling class
        
        addButton.disabled = true;
        addButton.textContent = "Unavailable";
        addButton.style.opacity = "0.5";
        addButton.style.cursor = "not-allowed";
        
        delete addButton.dataset.selectedVariantId;
    }
}

// --- START: FUNCTION - Build Validation Summary ---
function updateValidationSummary() {
    const validationSummaryEl = document.getElementById('build-validation-summary');
    if (!validationSummaryEl) {
        return; // Do nothing if the element doesn't exist
    }

    const { buildType, components } = buildState;
    const missingFront = [];
    const missingRear = [];

    // This array defines the correct display order
    const mandatoryComponentTypes = [
        { key: 'Rim', display: 'Rim' },
        { key: 'Hub', display: 'Hub' },
        { key: 'Spokes', display: 'Spokes' },
        { key: 'Nipples', display: 'Nipples' }
    ];

    // Check for missing FRONT components
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        mandatoryComponentTypes.forEach(type => {
            if (!components[`front${type.key}`]) {
                missingFront.push({
                    name: type.display,
                    targetId: `front-${type.key.toLowerCase()}-subsection`
                });
            }
        });
    }

    // Check for missing REAR components
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        mandatoryComponentTypes.forEach(type => {
            if (!components[`rear${type.key}`]) {
                missingRear.push({
                    name: type.display,
                    targetId: `rear-${type.key.toLowerCase()}-subsection`
                });
            }
        });
    }

    // Only display the box if there's at least one missing component
    if (missingFront.length > 0 || missingRear.length > 0) {
        let html = '<h4>Build Not Complete</h4><p>Please select the following required components to proceed:</p>';
        html += '<div class="validation-columns-container">'; // Flex container for columns

        // --- Front Column ---
        if (missingFront.length > 0) {
            html += '<div class="validation-column">';
            html += '<h5>Front Wheel</h5><ul>';
            missingFront.forEach(item => {
                html += `<li><a href="#" class="validation-summary-link" data-target-id="${item.targetId}">${item.name}</a></li>`;
            });
            html += '</ul></div>';
        }

        // --- Rear Column ---
        if (missingRear.length > 0) {
            html += '<div class="validation-column">';
            html += '<h5>Rear Wheel</h5><ul>';
            missingRear.forEach(item => {
                html += `<li><a href="#" class="validation-summary-link" data-target-id="${item.targetId}">${item.name}</a></li>`;
            });
            html += '</ul></div>';
        }

        html += '</div>'; 

        validationSummaryEl.innerHTML = html;
        validationSummaryEl.style.display = 'block';
    } else {
        validationSummaryEl.innerHTML = '';
        validationSummaryEl.style.display = 'none';
    }
}
// --- END: Build Validation Summary ---
  
async function handleAddonBuildButtonClick(event) {
    const clickedButton = event.target.closest('.add-addon-to-build-btn');
    if (!clickedButton) return;
     // ... (rest of the initial variable setup: addonProductId, selectedAddonVariantId, etc.)
    event.preventDefault();
    if (clickedButton.disabled) return;
    
    const addonProductId = clickedButton.dataset.productId; // GID of the addon product being actioned
    const selectedAddonVariantId = clickedButton.dataset.selectedVariantId; // GID of its variant
    const selectedAddonPriceCents = parseInt(clickedButton.dataset.selectedVariantPrice);
    const selectedAddonFullTitle = clickedButton.dataset.selectedVariantFullTitle;
    const selectedAddonImage = clickedButton.dataset.selectedVariantImage || null;

    if (!selectedAddonVariantId || isNaN(selectedAddonPriceCents) || !selectedAddonFullTitle) {
        console.error("handleAddonBuildButtonClick: Essential data missing from button dataset.", clickedButton.dataset);
        alert("Could not add this option, data is missing.");
        return;
    }

    const basePosition = addonsModal.dataset.basePosition; 
    const baseType = addonsModal.dataset.baseType; 
    const baseComponentVariantId = addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId;

    if (!basePosition || !baseType || !baseComponentVariantId) {
        console.error("handleAddonBuildButtonClick: Base component context missing from modal dataset.");
        alert("Error: Cannot associate this addon with a base component.");
        return;
    }

    const currentAddonKey = `${basePosition}_${baseType}_${baseComponentVariantId}_${addonProductId}`;
    const isCurrentlySelectedExactVariant = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[currentAddonKey]?.addonVariantId === selectedAddonVariantId;
    
    let parentAddonProductData = null;
    try {
        const allFetchedAddonProducts = JSON.parse(addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts || '[]').map(p => ({
            ...p, 
            pairingKeyValue: p.pairingKey?.value || p.pairingKeyValue || null // Ensure pairingKeyValue is used if already processed
        }));
        parentAddonProductData = allFetchedAddonProducts.find(p => p.id === addonProductId);
    } catch (e) { console.error("handleAddonBuildButtonClick: Error parsing currentAddonProducts for handle/pairingKey:", e); }
    
    const currentAddonProductPairingKey = parentAddonProductData ? parentAddonProductData.pairingKeyValue : null;

    if (isCurrentlySelectedExactVariant) { // User is REMOVING the addon
        // --- ADVANCED DE-PAIRING (this part seemed mostly okay, ensure it covers both cases) ---
        const canHavePairedAddon = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].includes(baseType);
        if (canHavePairedAddon && buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' && currentAddonProductPairingKey) {
            const oppositePosition = basePosition === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
            const oppositeComponentStateKey = `${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}${baseType}`;
            const oppositeBaseComponent = buildState.components[oppositeComponentStateKey];

            if (oppositeBaseComponent && oppositeBaseComponent.variantId) {
                let oppositePairedAddonKeyToRemove = null;
                let oppositePairedAddonDetails = null;

                for (const key in buildState.selectedOptionalAddons) {
                    const addonEntry = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                    if (addonEntry.baseComponentPosition === oppositePosition &&
                        addonEntry.baseComponentType === baseType &&
                        addonEntry.baseComponentVariantId === oppositeBaseComponent.variantId &&
                        addonEntry.addonProductPairingKey === currentAddonProductPairingKey) {
                        
                        // Check if it's an identical item pair OR a different product pair
                        if (addonEntry.addonProductId === addonProductId) { // Identical item (e.g. valve caps)
                            if (addonEntry.addonVariantId === selectedAddonVariantId) { // Ensure variant matches too
                                oppositePairedAddonKeyToRemove = key;
                                oppositePairedAddonDetails = addonEntry;
                                break;
                            }
                        } else { // Different product with same pairing key (e.g. bearings)
                            oppositePairedAddonKeyToRemove = key;
                            oppositePairedAddonDetails = addonEntry;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (oppositePairedAddonKeyToRemove && oppositePairedAddonDetails) {
                    const oppositeDisplayName = `${oppositePosition} ${getDisplayName(baseType.toLowerCase())}`;
                    const removePairMsg = `The ${oppositeDisplayName} also has ${oppositePairedAddonDetails.addonName} selected (paired). Remove it as well?`;
                    if (confirm(removePairMsg)) {
                        delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[oppositePairedAddonKeyToRemove];
                        updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(oppositePosition, baseType, oppositeBaseComponent.variantId);
                        saveLastActiveBuild();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[currentAddonKey];
        updateSubtotal();
        buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
        updateStep3ButtonText();
        saveLastActiveBuild();

    } else { // User is ADDING/CHANGING the addon
        buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[currentAddonKey] = {
            baseComponentPosition: basePosition, baseComponentType: baseType,
            baseComponentVariantId: baseComponentVariantId, addonProductId: addonProductId,
            addonVariantId: selectedAddonVariantId, addonName: selectedAddonFullTitle,
            addonPriceCents: selectedAddonPriceCents, addonImage: selectedAddonImage,
            addonProductHandle: parentAddonProductData ? parentAddonProductData.handle : null,
            addonProductPairingKey: currentAddonProductPairingKey // Store the pairing key
        };
      updateSubtotal();
    }
        updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(basePosition, baseType, baseComponentVariantId);
    await updateAddonButtonsStateInModal(basePosition, baseType, baseComponentVariantId); 
    
    const canPairForModalUpdate = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].includes(baseType);
    if (canPairForModalUpdate && buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        const oppositePositionForModalCheck = basePosition === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
        const oppositeComponentForModalCheckKey = `${oppositePositionForModalCheck.toLowerCase()}${baseType}`;
        const oppositeBaseComponentForModalCheck = buildState.components[oppositeComponentForModalCheckKey];
        if (oppositeBaseComponentForModalCheck && oppositeBaseComponentForModalCheck.variantId) {
            if (addonsModal.style.display !== 'none' &&
                addonsModal.dataset.basePosition === oppositePositionForModalCheck &&
                addonsModal.dataset.baseType === baseType && 
                addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId === oppositeBaseComponentForModalCheck.variantId) {
                await updateAddonButtonsStateInModal(oppositePositionForModalCheck, baseType, oppositeBaseComponentForModalCheck.variantId);
            }
        }
    }
    
// Update the subtotal and summary to reflect the change immediately.
updateSubtotal();
updateBuildSummary();

// Validate Step 3 to enable/disable the "Add to Cart" button.
validateStep3();

// Save the progress.
saveLastActiveBuild();
}

function handleRemoveSelectedAddonFromCard(event) {
    const button = event.currentTarget;
    const basePos = button.dataset.basePosition;
    const baseType = button.dataset.baseType;
    const baseVarId = button.dataset.baseVariantId;
    const addonProdId = button.dataset.addonProductId;

    if (!basePos || !baseType || !baseVarId || !addonProdId) {
        console.error("Cannot remove addon from card, essential data missing from button.");
        return;
    }

    const addonKeyToRemove = `${basePos}_${baseType}_${baseVarId}_${addonProdId}`;
    if (buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKeyToRemove]) {
        console.log(`Removing addon via card 'x': Key ${addonKeyToRemove}`);
        delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKeyToRemove];
        buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
        updateStep3ButtonText();

        updateSubtotal();
        updateBuildSummary();
        updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(basePos, baseType, baseVarId);
        saveLastActiveBuild();
        
        if (addonsModal.style.display !== 'none' &&
            addonsModal.dataset.basePosition === basePos &&
            addonsModal.dataset.baseType === baseType &&
            addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId === baseVarId) {
            updateAddonButtonsStateInModal(basePos, baseType, baseVarId);
        }
        saveLastActiveBuild();
    }
}

function updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(basePosition, baseTypePascal, baseComponentVariantId) {
    const posLower = basePosition.toLowerCase();
    let typeLowerForDOM = baseTypePascal.toLowerCase();
    if (baseTypePascal === "ValveStem") typeLowerForDOM = "valvestem";
    else if (baseTypePascal === "Spokes") typeLowerForDOM = "spokes";
    else if (baseTypePascal === "Nipples") typeLowerForDOM = "nipples";

    const selectionContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-selection`);

    // **CHANGE 1: Find button from the parent subsection, not the summary span container**
    const subsectionContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-subsection`);
    if (!subsectionContainer) {
        console.warn(`updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard: Subsection container not found for ${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-subsection`);
        return;
    }
    const addonsButtonElement = subsectionContainer.querySelector('.optional-addons-btn');
    // **END CHANGE 1**

    let listContainerElement = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-selected-addons-list`);

    if (!listContainerElement || !addonsButtonElement) {
        if (addonsButtonElement) { 
             // **CHANGE 2: Simplified button text**
            addonsButtonElement.textContent = "Add Ons";
        }
        if (listContainerElement && !baseComponentVariantId) {
            listContainerElement.innerHTML = '';
            listContainerElement.style.display = 'none';
        }
        return;
    }

    listContainerElement.innerHTML = ''; 

    if (!baseComponentVariantId) { 
        addonsButtonElement.textContent = "Add Ons";
        listContainerElement.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    
    // **CHANGE 3: Simplified button text logic**
    const matchingSelectedAddons = [];
    for (const key in buildState.selectedOptionalAddons) {
        const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
        if (addon.baseComponentPosition === basePosition &&
            addon.baseComponentType === baseTypePascal &&
            addon.baseComponentVariantId === baseComponentVariantId) {
            matchingSelectedAddons.push(addon);
        }
    }

    if (matchingSelectedAddons.length > 0) {
        addonsButtonElement.textContent = `Add Ons (${matchingSelectedAddons.length} selected)`;
    } else {
        addonsButtonElement.textContent = "Add Ons";
    }
    // **END CHANGE 3**

    if (matchingSelectedAddons.length > 0) {
        listContainerElement.style.display = 'block'; 
        const ul = document.createElement('ul');
        matchingSelectedAddons.forEach(addon => {
            const li = document.createElement('li');
            
            let addonImageHtml = '';
            if (addon.addonImage) {
                addonImageHtml = `<img src="${addon.addonImage}" alt="${addon.addonName}" class="selected-addon-thumbnail">`;
            } else {
                addonImageHtml = `<div class="selected-addon-thumbnail-placeholder"></div>`;
            }

            let addonNameText = `+ ${addon.addonName}`; 
            let addonNameHtml = `<span class="selected-addon-name-text">${addonNameText}</span>`; 
            if (addon.addonProductHandle) {
                const productUrl = `/products/${addon.addonProductHandle}`;
                addonNameHtml = `<span class="selected-addon-name-text"><a href="${productUrl}" target="_blank" title="View ${addon.addonName} product page">${addonNameText}</a></span>`;
            }
            
            const removeXButtonHtml = `<button type="button" class="remove-selected-addon-btn" 
                                         data-base-position="${addon.baseComponentPosition}"
                                         data-base-type="${addon.baseComponentType}"
                                         data-base-variant-id="${addon.baseComponentVariantId}"
                                         data-addon-product-id="${addon.addonProductId}"
                                         aria-label="Remove ${addon.addonName}">×</button>`;
            
            li.innerHTML = `${addonImageHtml} ${addonNameHtml} ${removeXButtonHtml}`;
            ul.appendChild(li);
        });
        listContainerElement.appendChild(ul);

        listContainerElement.querySelectorAll('.remove-selected-addon-btn').forEach(button => {
            button.removeEventListener('click', handleRemoveSelectedAddonFromCard); 
            button.addEventListener('click', handleRemoveSelectedAddonFromCard);
        });

    } else {
        listContainerElement.style.display = 'none'; 
    }
}


// --- START: ADDONS MODAL FUNCTIONS --- (openAddonsModal, closeAddonsModal)
    function openAddonsModal(baseComponentPosition, baseComponentType, baseComponentProductId, baseComponentVariantId, optionalAddonProductGidsString) {
        if (!addonsModal || !addonsModalTitle || !addonsModalBody) {
            console.error("Addons modal elements not found.");
            return;
        }

        addonsModal.dataset.basePosition = baseComponentPosition;
        addonsModal.dataset.baseType = baseComponentType;
        addonsModal.dataset.baseProductId = baseComponentProductId;
        addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId = baseComponentVariantId;

        const cleanTypePascal = baseComponentType.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1').trim();
        let titleBase = (baseComponentType === "ValveStem") ? `${baseComponentPosition} Valve Stem` : `${baseComponentPosition} ${cleanTypePascal}`;
        addonsModalTitle.textContent = `${titleBase} Options & Upgrades`;
        
        addonsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>Loading add-on options...</p>'; 
        addonsModal.style.display = 'flex'; 

        console.log("Opening addons modal for:", {
            position: baseComponentPosition, type: baseComponentType,
            baseProductId: baseComponentProductId, baseVariantId: baseComponentVariantId,
            addonProductGids: optionalAddonProductGidsString
        });
        
        addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts = '[]'; 
        fetchAndDisplayAddonDetailsInModal(optionalAddonProductGidsString); 
    }

// --- END: ADDONS MODAL FUNCTIONS ---

// --- START: HANDLE "MATCH ADDON TO OPPOSITE" CLICKS ---
async function handleGenericMatchButtonClick(event, clickedMatchButton) {
    event.preventDefault();

    const action = clickedMatchButton.dataset.action; 
    
    let positionToApplyMatch, baseTypeToApplyMatch, addonProductToApplyId,
        sourceAddonVariantToMatchId, sourceAddonProductIdToMatch;

    if (action === "match-to") { 
        positionToApplyMatch = clickedMatchButton.dataset.targetPosition; 
        baseTypeToApplyMatch = clickedMatchButton.dataset.sourceBaseType; 
        addonProductToApplyId = clickedMatchButton.dataset.targetAddonProductId; 
        sourceAddonVariantToMatchId = clickedMatchButton.dataset.sourceAddonVariantId; 
        sourceAddonProductIdToMatch = clickedMatchButton.dataset.sourceAddonProductId; 
    } else if (action === "match-from") { 
        positionToApplyMatch = clickedMatchButton.dataset.targetPosition; 
        baseTypeToApplyMatch = clickedMatchButton.dataset.targetBaseType; 
        addonProductToApplyId = clickedMatchButton.dataset.targetAddonProductId; 
        sourceAddonVariantToMatchId = clickedMatchButton.dataset.sourceAddonVariantId; 
        sourceAddonProductIdToMatch = clickedMatchButton.dataset.sourceAddonProductId; 
    } else {
        console.error("Unknown match button action:", action);
        return;
    }

    const baseComponentToApplyOn = buildState.components[`${positionToApplyMatch.toLowerCase()}${baseTypeToApplyMatch}`];
    if (!baseComponentToApplyOn || !baseComponentToApplyOn.variantId) {
        alert(`Error: The ${positionToApplyMatch} ${getDisplayName(baseTypeToApplyMatch.toLowerCase())} is not selected.`);
        return;
    }

    const productToApplyDetailsArray = await fetchAddonProductDetailsByGids([addonProductToApplyId]);
    if (!productToApplyDetailsArray || productToApplyDetailsArray.length === 0) {
        alert("Error: Could not load details for the item to match.");
        return;
    }
    const productToApplyInfo = productToApplyDetailsArray[0];

    let variantToApply = null;
    if (productToApplyInfo.variants && productToApplyInfo.variants.length > 0) {
        if (addonProductToApplyId === sourceAddonProductIdToMatch) { 
            variantToApply = productToApplyInfo.variants.find(v => v.id === sourceAddonVariantToMatchId && v.availableForSale);
        }
        if (!variantToApply) {
            const sourceAddonFromState = Object.values(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons).find(
                sa => sa.addonVariantId === sourceAddonVariantToMatchId && sa.addonProductId === sourceAddonProductIdToMatch
            );
            const sourceNameLower = sourceAddonFromState?.addonName.toLowerCase() || "";
            if (sourceNameLower.includes("ceramic") && addonProductToApplyId !== sourceAddonProductIdToMatch) { 
                 variantToApply = productToApplyInfo.variants.find(v => v.availableForSale && (v.title.toLowerCase().includes("ceramic") || v.selectedOptions.some(so => so.value.toLowerCase().includes("ceramic"))));
            }
            if (!variantToApply) {
                variantToApply = productToApplyInfo.variants.find(v => v.availableForSale); 
            }
        }
    }

    if (!variantToApply) {
        alert(`Could not find an available option for ${productToApplyInfo.title} for the ${positionToApplyMatch} ${getDisplayName(baseTypeToApplyMatch.toLowerCase())}.`);
        return;
    }
    
    const addonKeyForBuildState = `${positionToApplyMatch}_${baseTypeToApplyMatch}_${baseComponentToApplyOn.variantId}_${addonProductToApplyId}`;
    
    let finalAddonName = productToApplyInfo.title;
    const optionsStr = variantToApply.selectedOptions.map(o => o.value).join(' / ');
    if (variantToApply.title && variantToApply.title.toLowerCase() !== 'default title') {
        if (optionsStr && variantToApply.title !== optionsStr) finalAddonName += ` (${optionsStr})`;
        else finalAddonName += ` (${variantToApply.title})`;
    } else if (optionsStr) {
        finalAddonName += ` (${optionsStr})`;
    }

    buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKeyForBuildState] = {
        baseComponentPosition: positionToApplyMatch,
        baseComponentType: baseTypeToApplyMatch,
        baseComponentVariantId: baseComponentToApplyOn.variantId,
        addonProductId: addonProductToApplyId,
        addonVariantId: variantToApply.id,
        addonName: finalAddonName,
        addonPriceCents: variantToApply.price.amount,
        addonImage: variantToApply.image ? variantToApply.image.url : null,
        addonProductHandle: productToApplyInfo.handle,
        addonProductPairingKey: productToApplyInfo.pairingKeyValue
    };

    updateSubtotal();
    updateBuildSummary();
    updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(positionToApplyMatch, baseTypeToApplyMatch, baseComponentToApplyOn.variantId);
    saveLastActiveBuild();

    // --- START: UPDATE MODAL'S DROPDOWNS ---
    // Get modal context variables ONCE here, no re-declaration
    const modalBasePos = addonsModal.dataset.basePosition;
    const modalBaseType = addonsModal.dataset.baseType;
    const modalBaseVarId = addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId;

    if (modalBasePos === positionToApplyMatch && 
        modalBaseType === baseTypeToApplyMatch && 
        modalBaseVarId === baseComponentToApplyOn.variantId) {

        const productCardInModal = addonsModalBody.querySelector(`.addon-item-card[data-addon-product-id="${addonProductToApplyId}"]`);
        if (productCardInModal) {
            const variantSelectorContainerInModal = productCardInModal.querySelector('.addon-variant-selector');
            const allAddonProductsData = JSON.parse(addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts || '[]').map(p => ({
                 ...p, // Spread existing product data from modal dataset
                 pairingKeyValue: p.pairingKey?.value || p.pairingKeyValue || null 
            }));
            const productDataForCard = allAddonProductsData.find(p => p.id === addonProductToApplyId);

            if (variantSelectorContainerInModal && productDataForCard) {
                populateAddonVariantSelector(productDataForCard, variantSelectorContainerInModal, variantToApply.id);
                updateAddonPriceAndButtonState(productDataForCard, productCardInModal);
            }
        }
    }
    // --- END: UPDATE MODAL'S DROPDOWNS ---

        // Re-evaluate all buttons in the current modal (this will now see the updated dropdowns)
    // Use the modalBasePos, etc. variables that were ALREADY DEFINED above.
    if (modalBasePos && modalBaseType && modalBaseVarId) { // These are already defined, no need for const/let
        await updateAddonButtonsStateInModal(modalBasePos, modalBaseType, modalBaseVarId);
        saveLastActiveBuild(); // MOVED INSIDE AND ON NEW LINE
    }
}
// --- END: HANDLE "MATCH ADDON TO OPPOSITE" CLICKS ---
  
// --- START: UPDATE STATE OF BUTTONS IN ADDON MODAL ---
async function updateAddonButtonsStateInModal(currentBasePositionInModal, currentBaseTypeInModal, currentBaseComponentVariantIdInModal) {
    if (!addonsModalBody) return;

    const allProductCardsInModal = addonsModalBody.querySelectorAll('.addon-item-card');

    // --- Helper function to get a concise variant descriptor ---
    const getConciseVariantName = (addonDetails) => {
        if (!addonDetails) return "Item";
        // Try to extract from selectedOptions first if available
        // Ensure selectedOptions is available on addonDetails (it should be if populated correctly in buildState)
        if (addonDetails.selectedOptions && addonDetails.selectedOptions.length > 0) {
            const colorOpt = addonDetails.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color');
            if (colorOpt) return colorOpt.value;
            const materialOpt = addonDetails.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'material');
            if (materialOpt) return materialOpt.value;
            // You might want to add more prioritized options here (e.g., 'Length', 'Size')
            return addonDetails.selectedOptions[0].value; // Fallback to first option's value
        }
        // Fallback: Try to parse from addonName like "Product (Variant)"
        const nameParts = addonDetails.addonName.match(/\(([^)]+)\)/);
        if (nameParts && nameParts[1]) {
            // Take the first part if multiple options are in parentheses like "(Option1 / Option2)"
            return nameParts[1].split(' / ')[0];
        }
        // Further fallback: first word of the addon's product title
        // This requires fetching the product title if addonDetails only has addonName
        // For simplicity, if addonName is "Product Title (Variant)", this will try to get "Product"
        const productTitleFromName = addonDetails.addonName.split('(')[0].trim();
        return productTitleFromName.split(' ')[0] || "Item"; // Fallback to "Item"
    };
    // --- End Helper ---

    await Promise.all(Array.from(allProductCardsInModal).map(async (productCard) => {
        const addonProductIdOnCard = productCard.dataset.addonProductId;
        const addButton = productCard.querySelector('.add-addon-to-build-btn');

        if (!addButton) return;

        const displayedAddonVariantIdOnCard = addButton.dataset.selectedVariantId;
        const fullAddonKeyForThisModalInstance = `${currentBasePositionInModal}_${currentBaseTypeInModal}_${currentBaseComponentVariantIdInModal}_${addonProductIdOnCard}`;
        const activeSelectedAddonInBuildState = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[fullAddonKeyForThisModalInstance];

        productCard.querySelectorAll('.match-addon-btn').forEach(btn => btn.remove());
        addButton.classList.remove('builder-button--cta');

        if (activeSelectedAddonInBuildState) {
            if (activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonVariantId === displayedAddonVariantIdOnCard) {
                let shortAddonName = getConciseVariantName(activeSelectedAddonInBuildState); // Use helper for consistency
                addButton.textContent = `Remove ${shortAddonName}`;
                addButton.classList.add('addon-added', 'remove-mode');

                const canHavePairedAddon = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].includes(currentBaseTypeInModal);
                if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' && canHavePairedAddon && activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductPairingKey) {
                    const oppositePosition = currentBasePositionInModal === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
                    const oppositeBaseComponent = buildState.components[`${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}${currentBaseTypeInModal}`];

                    if (oppositeBaseComponent && oppositeBaseComponent.variantId && oppositeBaseComponent.optionalAddonProductGids) {
                        let productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey = null;
                        
                        // Get details of the product for the current addon in the modal to compare names if needed
                        let currentModalAddonProductDetails = null;
                        const allProdsInModal = JSON.parse(addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts || '[]');
                        currentModalAddonProductDetails = allProdsInModal.find(p => p.id === activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductId);


                        const oppositeAddonCandidatesDetails = await fetchAddonProductDetailsByGids(oppositeBaseComponent.optionalAddonProductGids);
                        for (const candidate of oppositeAddonCandidatesDetails) {
                            if (candidate.pairingKeyValue === activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductPairingKey) {
                                productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey = candidate;
                                break;
                            }
                        }

                        if (productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey) {
                            const keyForPairedAddonOnOpposite = `${oppositePosition}_${currentBaseTypeInModal}_${oppositeBaseComponent.variantId}_${productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey.id}`;
                            const pairedAddonSelectedOnOpposite = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[keyForPairedAddonOnOpposite];
                            let showMatchToButton = true;
                            if (pairedAddonSelectedOnOpposite) {
                                if (productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey.id === activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductId) {
                                    if (pairedAddonSelectedOnOpposite.addonVariantId === activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonVariantId) {
                                        showMatchToButton = false;
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    showMatchToButton = false;
                                }
                            }

                            if (showMatchToButton) {
                                const matchToButton = document.createElement('button');
                                matchToButton.className = 'builder-button builder-button--secondary match-addon-btn match-addon-to-opposite-btn builder-button--cta';
                                
                                const conciseSourceName = getConciseVariantName(activeSelectedAddonInBuildState);
                                let buttonText = `Make ${oppositePosition} Match (${conciseSourceName})`;
                                // If product GIDs are different, means it's a specific pair like bearings.
                                // Use the target product's name for clarity.
                                if (productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey.id !== activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductId) {
                                    buttonText = `Make ${oppositePosition} use ${productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey.title.split(' ')[0]} (${conciseSourceName})`;
                                }
                                matchToButton.textContent = buttonText;
                                matchToButton.dataset.action = "match-to";
                                matchToButton.dataset.sourcePosition = currentBasePositionInModal;
                                matchToButton.dataset.sourceBaseType = currentBaseTypeInModal;
                                matchToButton.dataset.sourceAddonProductId = activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductId;
                                matchToButton.dataset.sourceAddonVariantId = activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonVariantId;
                                matchToButton.dataset.targetPosition = oppositePosition;
                                matchToButton.dataset.targetAddonProductId = productCandidateForOppositeSide_SamePairingKey.id;
                                productCard.querySelector('.addon-item-actions')?.appendChild(matchToButton);
                            }
                        }

                        // --- Button 2: "Adopt addon FROM Opposite side" ---
                        const addonProductOnThisCard = allProdsInModal.find(p => p.id === addonProductIdOnCard);
                        if (addonProductOnThisCard?.pairingKeyValue) {
                            let selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct = null;
                            for (const key in buildState.selectedOptionalAddons) {
                                const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                                if (addon.baseComponentPosition === oppositePosition &&
                                    addon.baseComponentType === currentBaseTypeInModal &&
                                    addon.baseComponentVariantId === oppositeBaseComponent.variantId &&
                                    addon.addonProductPairingKey === addonProductOnThisCard.pairingKeyValue) {
                                    // Now, ensure that the item selected on opposite is either the same product as this card
                                    // OR this card's product is the correct partner for what's on opposite.
                                    if (addon.addonProductId === addonProductOnThisCard.id || // Opposite has same product selected as current card
                                        (currentModalAddonProductDetails && addon.addonProductId === currentModalAddonProductDetails.id && addonProductOnThisCard.id !== currentModalAddonProductDetails.id ) // handles bearing case
                                        ) {
                                         // Check if this card's item is different from what's active on this side
                                        if (!activeSelectedAddonInBuildState || // Nothing active on this side for this card's product type OR
                                            (activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductId === addon.addonProductId && activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonVariantId !== addon.addonVariantId) || // Same product, different variant
                                            (activeSelectedAddonInBuildState.addonProductId !== addon.addonProductId) // Different products (like bearings, current is front, opposite is rear)
                                           ) {
                                                selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct = addon;
                                                break;
                                           }
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            if (selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct) {
                                const adoptFromButton = document.createElement('button');
                                adoptFromButton.className = 'builder-button builder-button--secondary match-addon-btn match-addon-from-opposite-btn builder-button--cta';
                                const conciseOppositeName = getConciseVariantName(selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct);
                                let buttonText = `Adopt from ${oppositePosition} (${conciseOppositeName})`;
                                if (selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct.addonProductId !== addonProductIdOnCard) {
                                   buttonText = `Adopt ${selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct.addonName.split(" (")[0].substring(0,15)}... (${conciseOppositeName}) from ${oppositePosition}`;
                                }
                                adoptFromButton.textContent = buttonText;
                                adoptFromButton.dataset.action = "match-from";
                                adoptFromButton.dataset.targetPosition = currentBasePositionInModal;
                                adoptFromButton.dataset.targetBaseType = currentBaseTypeInModal;
                                adoptFromButton.dataset.targetAddonProductId = addonProductIdOnCard; // Product of the current card
                                adoptFromButton.dataset.sourcePosition = oppositePosition;
                                adoptFromButton.dataset.sourceAddonProductId = selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct.addonProductId;
                                adoptFromButton.dataset.sourceAddonVariantId = selectedAddonOnOpposite_ThatPairsWithThisCardProduct.addonVariantId;
                                productCard.querySelector('.addon-item-actions')?.appendChild(adoptFromButton);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else { // Dropdowns DO NOT MATCH activeSelectedAddonInBuildState
                addButton.textContent = 'Update Selection';
                addButton.classList.remove('addon-added', 'remove-mode');
                addButton.classList.add('builder-button--cta');
            }
        } else { // No addon for this product type IS actively selected in buildState
            addButton.textContent = 'Add to Build';
            addButton.classList.remove('addon-added', 'remove-mode');
            addButton.classList.add('builder-button--cta');

            const canHavePairedAddon = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].includes(currentBaseTypeInModal);
            const currentAddonProductOnCardDetails = JSON.parse(addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts || '[]').find(p => p.id === addonProductIdOnCard);

            if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' && canHavePairedAddon && currentAddonProductOnCardDetails?.pairingKeyValue) {
                const oppositePosition = currentBasePositionInModal === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
                const oppositeBaseComponent = buildState.components[`${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}${currentBaseTypeInModal}`];

                if (oppositeBaseComponent && oppositeBaseComponent.variantId) {
                    let selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide = null;
                    for (const key in buildState.selectedOptionalAddons) {
                        const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                        if (addon.baseComponentPosition === oppositePosition &&
                            addon.baseComponentType === currentBaseTypeInModal &&
                            addon.baseComponentVariantId === oppositeBaseComponent.variantId &&
                            addon.addonProductPairingKey === currentAddonProductOnCardDetails.pairingKeyValue) {
                            selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide = addon;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide) {
                        // Check if the current card product IS the correct partner for what's on opposite
                        let isCorrectPartnerForAdopt = false;
                        if (currentAddonProductOnCardDetails.id === selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide.addonProductId) { // Same product type
                            isCorrectPartnerForAdopt = true;
                        } else if (currentAddonProductOnCardDetails.pairingKeyValue === selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide.addonProductPairingKey) {
                            // Different product types but same pairing key (e.g., bearings)
                            isCorrectPartnerForAdopt = true;
                        }


                        if (isCorrectPartnerForAdopt) {
                            const matchFromButton = document.createElement('button');
                            matchFromButton.className = 'builder-button builder-button--secondary match-addon-btn match-addon-from-opposite-btn builder-button--cta';
                            const conciseOppositeName = getConciseVariantName(selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide);
                            let buttonText = `Adopt from ${oppositePosition} (${conciseOppositeName})`;
                             if (selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide.addonProductId !== addonProductIdOnCard) { // If different product types
                                buttonText = `Adopt ${selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide.addonName.split(" (")[0].substring(0,15)}... (${conciseOppositeName}) from ${oppositePosition}`;
                            }
                            matchFromButton.textContent = buttonText;
                            matchFromButton.dataset.action = "match-from";
                            matchFromButton.dataset.targetPosition = currentBasePositionInModal;
                            matchFromButton.dataset.targetBaseType = currentBaseTypeInModal;
                            matchFromButton.dataset.targetAddonProductId = addonProductIdOnCard;
                            matchFromButton.dataset.sourcePosition = oppositePosition;
                            matchFromButton.dataset.sourceAddonProductId = selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide.addonProductId;
                            matchFromButton.dataset.sourceAddonVariantId = selectedPairedAddonOnOppositeSide.addonVariantId;
                            productCard.querySelector('.addon-item-actions')?.appendChild(matchFromButton);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }));
}
// --- END: UPDATE STATE OF BUTTONS IN ADDON MODAL ---

// --- START: updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard (RESTORES ADDON LIST) ---
function updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(basePosition, baseTypePascal, baseComponentVariantId) {
    const posLower = basePosition.toLowerCase();
    let typeLowerForDOM = baseTypePascal.toLowerCase();
    if (baseTypePascal === "ValveStem") typeLowerForDOM = "valvestem";
    else if (baseTypePascal === "Spokes") typeLowerForDOM = "spokes";
    else if (baseTypePascal === "Nipples") typeLowerForDOM = "nipples";

    // This is the container for the text "Selected Front Rim: ..."
    const selectionContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-selection`);

    const subsectionContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-subsection`);
    if (!subsectionContainer || !selectionContainer) {
        console.warn(`updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard: Critical containers not found for ${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}`);
        return;
    }
    const addonsButtonElement = subsectionContainer.querySelector('.optional-addons-btn');

    // Find the list container. We will create it if it's missing.
    let listContainerElement = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-selected-addons-list`);
    const defaultButtonText = "Add Ons";

    if (!baseComponentVariantId) {
        if (addonsButtonElement) addonsButtonElement.textContent = defaultButtonText;
        if (listContainerElement) {
            listContainerElement.innerHTML = '';
            listContainerElement.style.display = 'none';
        }
        return;
    }

    const matchingSelectedAddons = [];
    for (const key in buildState.selectedOptionalAddons) {
        const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
        if (addon.baseComponentPosition === basePosition &&
            addon.baseComponentType === baseTypePascal &&
            addon.baseComponentVariantId === baseComponentVariantId) {
            matchingSelectedAddons.push(addon);
        }
    }

// --- START: SORTING LOGIC ---
    // Get the base component from the state to find its master list of addon GIDs for sorting.
    const stateKeyForBaseComponent = `${posLower}${baseTypePascal}`;
    const baseComponent = buildState.components[stateKeyForBaseComponent];
    const masterAddonOrder = baseComponent?.optionalAddonProductGids || [];
    
    // Sort the collected addons to match the order defined in the base component's metafield.
    matchingSelectedAddons.sort((a, b) => {
        const indexA = masterAddonOrder.indexOf(a.addonProductId);
