        const indexB = masterAddonOrder.indexOf(b.addonProductId);
        // If an addon isn't found in the master list, push it to the end.
        if (indexA === -1) return 1;
        if (indexB === -1) return -1;
        return indexA - indexB;
    });
    // --- END: SORTING LOGIC ---
  
    if (addonsButtonElement) {
        if (matchingSelectedAddons.length > 0) {
            addonsButtonElement.textContent = `${defaultButtonText} (${matchingSelectedAddons.length} selected)`;
        } else {
            addonsButtonElement.textContent = defaultButtonText;
        }
    }

    if (matchingSelectedAddons.length > 0) {
        // If the list container doesn't exist, create it and append it to the right place.
        if (!listContainerElement) {
            listContainerElement = document.createElement('div');
            listContainerElement.className = 'selected-addons-list';
            listContainerElement.id = `${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-selected-addons-list`;
            // Append it to the text summary container
            selectionContainer.appendChild(listContainerElement);
        }

        listContainerElement.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous content before re-populating
        listContainerElement.style.display = 'block';

        const ul = document.createElement('ul');
        matchingSelectedAddons.forEach(addon => {
            const li = document.createElement('li');
            
            let addonImageHtml = addon.addonImage ? `<img src="${addon.addonImage}" alt="${addon.addonName}" class="selected-addon-thumbnail">` : `<div class="selected-addon-thumbnail-placeholder"></div>`;
            let addonNameText = `+ ${addon.addonName}`; 
            let addonNameHtml = `<span class="selected-addon-name-text">${addonNameText}</span>`; 
            if (addon.addonProductHandle) {
                const productUrl = `/products/${addon.addonProductHandle}`;
                addonNameHtml = `<span class="selected-addon-name-text"><a href="${productUrl}" target="_blank" title="View ${addon.addonName} product page">${addonNameText}</a></span>`;
            }
            const removeXButtonHtml = `<button type="button" class="remove-selected-addon-btn" 
                                         data-base-position="${addon.baseComponentPosition}"
                                         data-base-type="${addon.baseComponentType}"
                                         data-base-variant-id="${addon.baseComponentVariantId}"
                                         data-addon-product-id="${addon.addonProductId}"
                                         aria-label="Remove ${addon.addonName}">×</button>`;
            
            li.innerHTML = `${addonImageHtml} ${addonNameHtml} ${removeXButtonHtml}`;
            ul.appendChild(li);
        });
        listContainerElement.appendChild(ul);

        listContainerElement.querySelectorAll('.remove-selected-addon-btn').forEach(button => {
            button.removeEventListener('click', handleRemoveSelectedAddonFromCard); 
            button.addEventListener('click', handleRemoveSelectedAddonFromCard);
        });

    } else {
        if (listContainerElement) {
            listContainerElement.innerHTML = '';
            listContainerElement.style.display = 'none'; 
        }
    }
}
// --- END: updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard ---
  
// --- START: ADDONS MODAL FUNCTIONS ---
    function openAddonsModal(baseComponentPosition, baseComponentType, baseComponentProductId, baseComponentVariantId, optionalAddonProductGidsString) {
        if (!addonsModal || !addonsModalTitle || !addonsModalBody) {
            console.error("Addons modal elements not found.");
            return;
        }

        // Store context for when an addon is selected
        addonsModal.dataset.basePosition = baseComponentPosition;
        addonsModal.dataset.baseType = baseComponentType;
        addonsModal.dataset.baseProductId = baseComponentProductId;
        addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId = baseComponentVariantId;

        const cleanTypePascal = baseComponentType.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1').trim();
        let titleBase = (baseComponentType === "ValveStem") ? `${baseComponentPosition} Valve Stem` : `${baseComponentPosition} ${cleanTypePascal}`;
        addonsModalTitle.textContent = `${titleBase} Options & Upgrades`;
        
        addonsModalBody.innerHTML = '<p>Loading add-on options...</p>'; // Placeholder
        addonsModal.style.display = 'flex'; // Use flex for centering

        /* console.log("Opening addons modal for:", {
            position: baseComponentPosition,
            type: baseComponentType,
            baseProductId: baseComponentProductId,
            baseVariantId: baseComponentVariantId,
            addonProductGids: optionalAddonProductGidsString
        });
        */
        // Store the raw addon products data once fetched, so variant change handler can access it
    // This is a temporary way to make it available; a more robust state might be better long-term
    addonsModal.dataset.currentAddonProducts = '[]'; // Initialize

    fetchAndDisplayAddonDetailsInModal(optionalAddonProductGidsString); 
    }

    function closeAddonsModal() {
        if (!addonsModal) return;
        addonsModal.style.display = 'none';
        addonsModalBody.innerHTML = ''; 
        delete addonsModal.dataset.basePosition;
        delete addonsModal.dataset.baseType;
        delete addonsModal.dataset.baseProductId;
        delete addonsModal.dataset.baseVariantId;
    }
    // --- END: ADDONS MODAL FUNCTIONS ---
  
// --- START: updateVendorButtonHighlight (with Toggle UI Update) ---
function updateVendorButtonHighlight(componentKey, activeVendorName) {
    if (!componentKey) {
        console.warn("updateVendorButtonHighlight: componentKey is missing.");
        return;
    }
    let positionLc;
    let typeLcForDomId;

    if (componentKey.startsWith('front')) {
        positionLc = 'front';
        typeLcForDomId = componentKey.substring(5).toLowerCase();
    } else if (componentKey.startsWith('rear')) {
        positionLc = 'rear';
        typeLcForDomId = componentKey.substring(4).toLowerCase();
    } else {
        return;
    }

    if (componentKey.toLowerCase().endsWith("valvestem")) typeLcForDomId = "valvestem";
    if (componentKey.toLowerCase().endsWith("nipples")) typeLcForDomId = "nipples";


    const filterContainerId = `${positionLc}-${typeLcForDomId}-filters`;
    const filterContainer = document.getElementById(filterContainerId);

    if (!filterContainer) return;

    const vendorArea = filterContainer.querySelector('.vendor-filter-area');
    const dropdown = vendorArea?.querySelector('.vendor-filter-dropdown');
    if (!dropdown) {
        return;
    }
    const toggle = dropdown.querySelector('.dropdown-toggle');
    const menuButtons = dropdown.querySelectorAll('.vendor-filter-btn');

    if (toggle) {
        let newToggleContent = '';
        if (activeVendorName === null) {
            newToggleContent = '<span class="vendor-prompt"><b>Click to select a vendor</b></span>';
        } else if (activeVendorName === 'all') {
            newToggleContent = '<span class="toggle-all-vendors-button">All Vendors</span>';
        } else {
            const vendorInfo = vendorLogoMap[activeVendorName];
            const logoUrl = vendorInfo?.logoUrl;
            newToggleContent = `<span>
                                    ${logoUrl ? `<img src="${logoUrl}" alt="${activeVendorName}" class="toggle-vendor-logo">` : `<span>${activeVendorName}</span>`}
                               </span>`;
        }
        toggle.innerHTML = newToggleContent;
    }

    menuButtons.forEach(btn => {
        btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.vendor === activeVendorName);
    });
    
    // Set the state last to ensure consistency
    buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKey] = activeVendorName;
}
// --- END: updateVendorButtonHighlight ---

function updateComponentUI(position, type, componentData) {
    const pL = position.toLowerCase();

    let typePascal = type.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + type.slice(1).toLowerCase();
    if (type.toLowerCase() === "valvestem") typePascal = "ValveStem";
    else if (type.toLowerCase() === "spokes") typePascal = "Spokes";
    else if (type.toLowerCase() === "nipples") typePascal = "Nipples";

    const componentKey = `${pL}${typePascal}`;
    const tL_for_dom_id = typePascal.toLowerCase(); 

    const sub = document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL_for_dom_id}-subsection`);
    const selSpanCont = document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL_for_dom_id}-selection`); 
    const imgCont = document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL_for_dom_id}-image-container`);
    const optsCont = sub ? sub.querySelector('.component-options') : null;
    const actionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL_for_dom_id}-action-buttons`);
    const removeButton = document.getElementById(`remove-${pL}-${tL_for_dom_id}-button`);

    if (!sub || !selSpanCont || !imgCont || !optsCont || !actionButtonsContainer) {
        console.error(`updateComponentUI ABORT: Missing one or more critical UI elements for ${position} ${typePascal}.`);
        return;
    }
    const displayName = `${position} ${getDisplayName(typePascal.toLowerCase())}`;

    selSpanCont.classList.remove('no-addon-ui-present'); 

    // Clear any leftover addon UI elements before deciding to re-add them
    const existingAddonBtn = sub.querySelector('.optional-addons-btn'); 
    if (existingAddonBtn) {
        existingAddonBtn.remove();
    }
    const existingAddonList = selSpanCont.querySelector('.selected-addons-list');
    if (existingAddonList) {
        existingAddonList.remove(); 
    }

    if (componentData) { 
        const spanEl = selSpanCont.querySelector('span'); 
        const pH = componentData.productHandle;
        const url = pH ? `/products/${pH}` : '#';
        const lT = pH ? `View ${componentData.title} product page` : 'Product page link unavailable';
        const priceD = componentData.price ? ` - ${formatPrice(componentData.price)}` : '';
        let displayTitle;
        if (typePascal === 'Spokes') {
            // For spokes, construct the clean title from our new state properties
            const color = componentData.selectedColor || '';
            displayTitle = `${componentData.title} (${color})`;
        } else {
            // Original logic for all other components
            displayTitle = componentData.title;
            if (componentData.selectedOptions && Array.isArray(componentData.selectedOptions) && componentData.selectedOptions.length > 0) {
                const usefulOptions = componentData.selectedOptions.filter(opt => opt.value.toLowerCase() !== 'default title');
                if (usefulOptions.length > 0) {
                    const variantDetails = usefulOptions.map(opt => opt.value).join(', ');
                    displayTitle += ` (${variantDetails})`;
                }
            }
        }
      
        if (spanEl) {
            // Check if the component is a placeholder from "Your Own Component"
            if (componentData.vendor === 'Your Own Component') {
                // If it is, render the text without a hyperlink
                spanEl.innerHTML = `Selected ${displayName}: <strong>${displayTitle}</strong>${priceD}`;
            } else {
                // Otherwise, use the original logic to render the hyperlink
                spanEl.innerHTML = `Selected ${displayName}: <a href="${url}" target="_blank" title="${lT}"><strong>${displayTitle}</strong></a>${priceD}`;
                // This safety check remains for non-placeholder products that might be missing a handle
                if (!pH) { const lE = spanEl.querySelector('a'); if (lE) { lE.style.pointerEvents = 'none'; lE.style.textDecoration = 'none'; lE.style.color = 'inherit'; } }
            }
        }

        imgCont.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous content

// 1. Create a dedicated wrapper for the image and its weight text
const imageWrapper = document.createElement('div');
imageWrapper.className = 'selected-image-wrapper'; // New class for positioning context

// 2. Add the image to the wrapper
if (componentData.image?.url) {
    const img = document.createElement('img');
    img.src = componentData.image.url;
    img.alt = componentData.title || `${displayName} Image`;
    img.loading = 'lazy';
    img.onerror = () => { imageWrapper.innerHTML = '<p>(Image Error)</p>'; };
    imageWrapper.appendChild(img);
} else {
    imageWrapper.innerHTML = '<div class="selected-image-placeholder">No Image</div>';
}

// 3. Add the weight display to the wrapper
const weight = componentData.weight_g;

// DIAGNOSTIC LOG: Check if valves are passing weight
if (typePascal === 'ValveStem') {
    console.log(`[UI Render] Valve Stem: ${componentData.variantTitle}, Weight Data:`, weight);
}

if (weight !== null && weight !== undefined && !isNaN(weight)) {
    const weightDisplay = document.createElement('div');
    weightDisplay.className = 'selected-component-weight-display';
    
    if (typePascal === 'Spokes') {
        // Initial render for spokes (will be updated by calc function later)
        // Just show generic weight initially to prevent layout shift
        const count = buildState.specs[`${pL}SpokeCount`] || 32;
        weightDisplay.innerHTML = `Wt: ${Math.round(weight * count)}g`;
    } else {
        weightDisplay.textContent = `Wt: ${weight}g`;
    }
    
    imageWrapper.appendChild(weightDisplay);
}

// 4. Add the entire wrapper to the main image container
imgCont.appendChild(imageWrapper);
imgCont.style.display = 'flex';

        if (componentData.optionalAddonProductGids && componentData.optionalAddonProductGids.length > 0) {
            const addonsButton = document.createElement('button');
            addonsButton.type = 'button';
            addonsButton.className = 'optional-addons-btn builder-button--secondary';
            addonsButton.textContent = "Add Ons";
            addonsButton.dataset.position = position; 
            addonsButton.dataset.type = typePascal;
            addonsButton.dataset.baseComponentProductId = componentData.productId; 
            addonsButton.dataset.baseComponentVariantId = componentData.variantId;
            addonsButton.dataset.optionalAddonProductGids = componentData.optionalAddonProductGids.join(',');
            
            imgCont.appendChild(addonsButton);

            addonsButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                openAddonsModal(
                    addonsButton.dataset.position,
                    addonsButton.dataset.type,
                    addonsButton.dataset.baseComponentProductId,
                    addonsButton.dataset.baseComponentVariantId,
                    addonsButton.dataset.optionalAddonProductGids
                );
            });
            updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(position, typePascal, componentData.variantId);
        } else {
            selSpanCont.classList.add('no-addon-ui-present');
        }

        if (typePascal === "ValveStem" && imgCont && imgCont.style.display !== 'none') {
            const originalDisplay = imgCont.style.display;
            imgCont.style.display = 'none';
            imgCont.offsetHeight; 
            imgCont.style.display = originalDisplay;
        }

        optsCont.style.display = 'none';
        optsCont.innerHTML = '';

        actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'none';
        actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';

        sub.classList.add('selection-made');
        sub.classList.remove('change-in-progress');
        updateVendorButtonHighlight(componentKey, componentData.vendor);

        let filtersContainerElement = document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL_for_dom_id}-filters`);

        if (filtersContainerElement) {
            // Get the correctly filtered list of products using the new helper function.
            const compatibleProductsForFilter = getCurrentlyCompatibleProducts(position, typePascal);
            // Pass this filtered list to the function that builds the vendor UI.
            displayComponentVendorFilters(componentKey, compatibleProductsForFilter, filtersContainerElement, position);
        } else {
            console.warn(`updateComponentUI: Could not find filtersContainerElement for ${componentKey}.`);
        }
        
        const existingIcon = imgCont.querySelector('.remove-component-icon');
        if (existingIcon) {
            existingIcon.remove();
        }

        if (componentData && typePascal === "ValveStem") {
            const removeIcon = document.createElement('button');
            removeIcon.type = 'button';
            removeIcon.className = 'remove-component-icon';
            removeIcon.innerHTML = '×';
            removeIcon.title = `Remove ${position} Valve Stem`;
            removeIcon.dataset.action = 'remove-component';
            removeIcon.dataset.position = position;
            removeIcon.dataset.type = 'ValveStem';
            imgCont.appendChild(removeIcon);
            removeIcon.style.display = 'block';
        }

    } else { // No componentData (slot is empty)
        const spanEl = selSpanCont.querySelector('span');
        if (spanEl) {
            spanEl.innerHTML = `Selected ${displayName}: None`;
        }
        selSpanCont.classList.add('no-addon-ui-present');

        imgCont.innerHTML = '';
        imgCont.style.display = 'none';

        optsCont.style.display = 'flex'; 

        actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'none';
        actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';

        sub.classList.remove('selection-made', 'change-in-progress');
        updateVendorButtonHighlight(componentKey, null);

        if (removeButton) {
            removeButton.style.display = 'none';
        }
        updateSelectedAddonsDisplayOnCard(position, typePascal, null);
    }

    if (typePascal === "Rim") {
        ['Front', 'Rear'].forEach(valvePos => {
            const valveStateKey = `${valvePos.toLowerCase()}ValveStem`;
            if (buildState.components[valveStateKey]) {
                const valveImgContToReflow = document.getElementById(`${valvePos.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-image-container`);
                if (valveImgContToReflow && valveImgContToReflow.style.display !== 'none') {
                    const originalDisplay = valveImgContToReflow.style.display;
                    valveImgContToReflow.style.display = 'none';
                    valveImgContToReflow.offsetHeight;
                    valveImgContToReflow.style.display = originalDisplay;
                }
            }
        });
    }
  updateMismatchHints();
}

    function updateComponentHeaderSpecs() {

  // --- Rims ---
  const frontRimSpecEl = document.getElementById('front-rim-spec-context');
  const rearRimSpecEl = document.getElementById('rear-rim-spec-context');

  if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' || buildState.buildType === 'Front') { // Corrected: buildState.buildType directly
    if (frontRimSpecEl && buildState.specs.frontWheelSize && buildState.specs.frontSpokeCount) {
      frontRimSpecEl.textContent = `- ${buildState.specs.frontWheelSize} | ${buildState.specs.frontSpokeCount}`;
    } else if (frontRimSpecEl) {
      frontRimSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if specs not available
    }
  } else if (frontRimSpecEl) {
    frontRimSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if not applicable
  }

  if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' || buildState.buildType === 'Rear') { // Corrected: buildState.buildType directly
    if (rearRimSpecEl && buildState.specs.rearWheelSize && buildState.specs.rearSpokeCount) {
      rearRimSpecEl.textContent = `- ${buildState.specs.rearWheelSize} | ${buildState.specs.rearSpokeCount}`;
    } else if (rearRimSpecEl) {
      rearRimSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if specs not available
    }
  } else if (rearRimSpecEl) {
    rearRimSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if not applicable
  }

  // --- Hubs ---
  const frontHubSpecEl = document.getElementById('front-hub-spec-context');
  const rearHubSpecEl = document.getElementById('rear-hub-spec-context');
  const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle || ''; // Handle if brakeStyle is null/undefined

  if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' || buildState.buildType === 'Front') { // Corrected: buildState.buildType directly
    if (frontHubSpecEl && buildState.specs.frontHubSpacing && buildState.specs.frontSpokeCount) {
      frontHubSpecEl.textContent = `- ${buildState.specs.frontHubSpacing} | ${buildState.specs.frontSpokeCount} | ${brakeStyle}`;
    } else if (frontHubSpecEl) {
      frontHubSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if specs not available
    }
  } else if (frontHubSpecEl) {
    frontHubSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if not applicable
  }

  if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' || buildState.buildType === 'Rear') { // Corrected: buildState.buildType directly
    if (rearHubSpecEl && buildState.specs.rearHubSpacing && buildState.specs.rearSpokeCount && buildState.specs.freehubType) {
      rearHubSpecEl.textContent = `- ${buildState.specs.rearHubSpacing} | ${buildState.specs.rearSpokeCount} | ${brakeStyle} | ${buildState.specs.freehubType}`;
    } else if (rearHubSpecEl) {
      rearHubSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if specs not available
    }
  } else if (rearHubSpecEl) {
    rearHubSpecEl.textContent = ''; // Clear if not applicable
  }
}
    // END OF NEW updateComponentHeaderSpecs FUNCTION

    // --- START: HUB-SPOKE COMPATIBILITY HELPERS ---
function applyIncompatibleStyling(element, isCompatible, reason = '') {
    if (!element) return;
    
    if (isCompatible) {
        element.classList.remove('conditionally-incompatible');
        element.dataset.isConditionallyDisabled = 'false';
        element.removeAttribute('title'); // Remove the tooltip text when it's compatible
    } else {
        element.classList.add('conditionally-incompatible');
        element.dataset.isConditionallyDisabled = 'true';
        element.setAttribute('title', reason); // Set the native browser tooltip
    }
}
// --- END: HUB-SPOKE COMPATIBILITY HELPERS ---
  
// --- START: NEW FUNCTION - Enforce Spoke Compatibility After Programmatic Hub Selection ---
function enforceSpokeCompatibilityForHub(position, selectedHubData) {
    if (!selectedHubData) return;

    const isHookFlange = selectedHubData.tags?.includes('hub_type:hook_flange');
    if (!isHookFlange) {
        return; // Not a hook flange hub, no action needed.
    }

    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const spokeStateKey = `${posLower}Spokes`;
    const currentSpoke = buildState.components[spokeStateKey];
    const isNonBerdSpokeSelected = currentSpoke && currentSpoke.vendor?.toLowerCase() !== 'berd';

    // If a hook flange hub was just selected AND a non-Berd spoke is present, fix it.
    if (isNonBerdSpokeSelected) {
        console.log(`[Auto-Compat] Enforcing spoke compatibility for ${position} due to hook flange hub selection.`);
        
        // Clear the incompatible spokes.
        clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'Spokes');
        
        // Set the active vendor to 'Berd'.
        buildState._ui.activeVendor[spokeStateKey] = 'Berd';
        
        // Reload the spoke options UI to reflect the new filter.
        loadAndFilterSpokesForPosition(position, false);
    }
}
// --- END: NEW FUNCTION ---
  
function updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI() {
    // --- Part 1: Hub Styling based on Spoke Selection ---
    ['front', 'rear'].forEach(pos => {
        const hubOptionsContainer = document.getElementById(`${pos}-hub-options-container`);
        if (!hubOptionsContainer) return;

        const spokeData = buildState.components[`${pos}Spokes`];
        let selectedSpokeInterface = null;
        if (spokeData) {
            const spokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === spokeData.productId);
            selectedSpokeInterface = spokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface; // "J-Bend", "Straight Pull", "Hook Flange", or null/blank
        }

        hubOptionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.hub-model-card').forEach(hubCard => {
            const modelName = hubCard.querySelector('h5')?.textContent;
            if (!modelName) return;
            const productInCache = allHubProductsCache.find(p => p.wheelModel === modelName);
            const hubTags = productInCache?.tags || [];

            let isCompatible = true;
            let reason = '';

            if (selectedSpokeInterface) { // Only apply rules if a spoke is selected
                // RULE: If Spoke is explicitly "Hook Flange", Hub MUST be Hook Flange
                if (selectedSpokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && !hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) {
                    isCompatible = false;
                    reason = 'Selected spokes require a Hook Flange hub.';
                }
                // RULE: If Spoke is J-Bend, Hub cannot be Straight Pull
                else if (selectedSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) {
                    isCompatible = false;
                    reason = 'Requires Straight Pull spokes.';
                } 
                // RULE: If Spoke is Straight Pull, Hub cannot be J-Bend
                else if (selectedSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) {
                    isCompatible = false;
                    reason = 'Requires J-Bend spokes.';
                }
            }
            applyIncompatibleStyling(hubCard, isCompatible, reason);
        });
    });

    // --- Part 2: Spoke Styling based on Hub Selection ---
    ['front', 'rear'].forEach(pos => {
        const spokeOptionsContainer = document.getElementById(`${pos}-spokes-options-container`);
        if (!spokeOptionsContainer) return;

        const hubData = buildState.components[`${pos}Hub`];
        const selectedHubTags = hubData?.tags || [];

        spokeOptionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.spoke-model-card, .spoke-variant-button').forEach(spokeElement => {
            const spokeInterface = spokeElement.dataset.spokeHubInterface; // "Hook Flange", etc.

            let isCompatible = true;
            let reason = '';
            
            if (selectedHubTags.length > 0) { // Only apply rules if a hub is selected
                // RULE: If Hub is Hook Flange, allow ONLY "Hook Flange" OR "Universal/Blank" (Standard Berd)
                // This means we block J-Bend and Straight Pull steel spokes
                if (selectedHubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) {
                    if (spokeInterface === 'J-Bend' || spokeInterface === 'Straight Pull') {
                        isCompatible = false;
                        reason = 'Hook Flange hubs require Berd spokes.';
                    }
                }
                // RULE: If Hub is J-Bend/SP, block "Hook Flange" spokes (PolyLightX)
                else if (spokeInterface === 'Hook Flange') {
                    isCompatible = false;
                    reason = 'These spokes require a Hook Flange hub.';
                }
                // Standard Steel Spoke Logic
                else if (selectedHubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend') && spokeInterface === 'Straight Pull') {
                    isCompatible = false;
                    reason = 'Not compatible with selected J-Bend hub.';
                } else if (selectedHubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull') && spokeInterface === 'J-Bend') {
                    isCompatible = false;
                    reason = 'Not compatible with selected Straight Pull hub.';
                }
            }
            applyIncompatibleStyling(spokeElement, isCompatible, reason);
        });
    });
}

function applyIntegratedWheelLogic(position, variantData) {
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    
    console.group(`[Integrated Logic] Applying for ${position}`);

    // 1. Create a "Virtual" Hub
    const hubName = variantData.integrated_hub_name || "Integrated Hub";
    const virtualHub = {
        title: hubName,
        variantTitle: "Built-in (Included)",
        price: 0, 
        vendor: variantData.vendor, 
        variantId: `VIRTUAL-HUB-${position}-${Date.now()}`,
        isVirtual: true, 
        image: null,
        freehubVariantMap: variantData.freehubVariantMap,
        availableFreehubs: variantData.availableFreehubs
    };
    buildState.components[`${posLower}Hub`] = virtualHub;
    
    // Handle Freehub Swap for Rear
    if (posLower === 'rear') {
        buildState.components.rearComponentFreehub = null;
        if (virtualHub.freehubVariantMap) {
            setComponentFreehubForHub(virtualHub);
        }
    }

    updateComponentUI(position, 'Hub', virtualHub);

    // 2. Create "Virtual" Spokes & Nipples
    const virtualSpoke = { title: "Integrated Spokes", variantTitle: "N/A", price: 0, variantId: `VIRTUAL-SPOKE-${position}`, isVirtual: true, vendor: "Reserve" };
    const virtualNipple = { title: "Integrated Nipples", variantTitle: "N/A", price: 0, variantId: `VIRTUAL-NIPPLE-${position}`, isVirtual: true, vendor: "Reserve" };
    
    buildState.components[`${posLower}Spokes`] = virtualSpoke;
    buildState.components[`${posLower}Nipples`] = virtualNipple;
    updateComponentUI(position, 'Spokes', virtualSpoke);
    updateComponentUI(position, 'Nipples', virtualNipple);

    // 3. Lock the UI Sections
    ['Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].forEach(type => {
        const container = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${type.toLowerCase()}-subsection`);
        if (container) {
            container.classList.add('is-locked-integrated');
            container.style.pointerEvents = 'none'; 
            container.style.opacity = '0.6';
            const removeBtn = document.getElementById(`remove-${posLower}-${type.toLowerCase()}-button`);
            if (removeBtn) removeBtn.style.display = 'none';
        }
    });

    // 4. Auto-Select Valve (NOW AS A PAID ITEM)
    if (variantData.included_valve_variant_id) {
        const targetId = variantData.included_valve_variant_id;
        let valveVariant = null;
        let valveProduct = null;

        for (const p of allValveStemProductsCache) {
            const foundV = p.variants.find(v => v.id === targetId || v.id.endsWith(targetId.split('/').pop()));
            if (foundV) {
                valveVariant = foundV;
                valveProduct = p;
                break;
            }
        }

        if (valveVariant && valveProduct) {
            const valveComponent = {
                variantId: valveVariant.id,
                productId: valveProduct.id,
                title: valveProduct.title,
                // --- Use Real Price ---
                price: valveVariant.price.amount, 
                // ---------------------------
                variantTitle: valveVariant.title, 
                // --- Remove 'isIncluded' so it adds to cart ---
                // isIncluded: true, <--- REMOVED
                // --------------------------------------------------
                image: valveVariant.image,
                vendor: valveProduct.vendor
            };
            buildState.components[`${posLower}ValveStem`] = valveComponent;
            updateComponentUI(position, 'ValveStem', valveComponent);
        }
    }
    console.groupEnd();
}

function resetIntegratedWheelLogic(position) {
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    
    // Unlock the UI Sections (Added ValveStem)
    ['Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].forEach(type => {
        const container = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${type.toLowerCase()}-subsection`);
        if (container) {
            container.classList.remove('is-locked-integrated');
            container.style.pointerEvents = '';
            container.style.opacity = '';
        }
    });

    // Clear Virtual Items
    if (buildState.components[`${posLower}Hub`]?.isVirtual) {
        buildState.components[`${posLower}Hub`] = null;
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Hub', null);
    }
    if (buildState.components[`${posLower}Spokes`]?.isVirtual) {
        buildState.components[`${posLower}Spokes`] = null;
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Spokes', null);
    }
    if (buildState.components[`${posLower}Nipples`]?.isVirtual) {
        buildState.components[`${posLower}Nipples`] = null;
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Nipples', null);
    }
    // Clear Included Valve
    if (buildState.components[`${posLower}ValveStem`]?.isIncluded) {
        buildState.components[`${posLower}ValveStem`] = null;
        updateComponentUI(position, 'ValveStem', null);
    }
}
   
    // --- START: calculateWheelCosts FUNCTION ---
function calculateWheelCosts(wheelPosition) {
    const posLower = wheelPosition.toLowerCase();
    
    // SAFETY GUARD: Ensure the array exists
    buildState.components[`${posLower}RequiredAddons`] = buildState.components[`${posLower}RequiredAddons`] || [];

    const selectedRim = buildState.components[`${posLower}Rim`];
    // SAFETY GUARD: If no rim is selected yet, stop here to prevent errors
    if (!selectedRim) return; 

    const isIntegrated = selectedRim.tags && selectedRim.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel');

    if (isIntegrated) {
        // --- Add $20 Assembly Fee for Integrated Wheels ---
        buildState.components[`${posLower}AssemblyService`] = {
            variantGid: 'gid://shopify/ProductVariant/51777290764595', // The $20.00 Variant ID
            name: 'Assembly Service',
            price: 2000, // $20.00 in cents
            costInCents: 2000
        };
        // -------------------------------------------------------

        buildState.components[`${posLower}TubelessTape`] = null;
        // The array is already empty from the initialization above, so we don't need to null it here, 
        // but we leave it alone or empty it just to be safe.
        buildState.components[`${posLower}RequiredAddons`] = []; 
        return; 
    }

    const selectedHub = buildState.components[`${posLower}Hub`];
    const selectedSpokes = buildState.components[`${posLower}Spokes`];
    const isWheelBeingBuilt = selectedRim || selectedHub || selectedSpokes;

    if (isWheelBeingBuilt) {
        let finalAssemblyGid = null;

        // First, check the build type.
        if (buildState.buildType === 'Front' || buildState.buildType === 'Rear') {
            // Rule: If it's a single wheel build, use the flat $100 charge and ignore all other rules.
            finalAssemblyGid = SINGLE_WHEEL_ASSEMBLY_GID;

        } else {
            // Rule: If it's a Wheel Set, use the original competitive pricing logic.
            const hubVendorKey = selectedHub ? selectedHub.vendor.toLowerCase() : null;
            const hubSpecificGid = HUB_VENDOR_TO_ASSEMBLY_VARIANT_GID_MAP[hubVendorKey] || null;
            const hubPrice = hubSpecificGid ? (ASSEMBLY_SERVICE_PRICES_BY_GID[hubSpecificGid] || 0) : 0;

            const rimVendorKey = selectedRim ? selectedRim.vendor.toLowerCase() : null;
            const rimSpecificGid = RIM_VENDOR_TO_ASSEMBLY_VARIANT_GID_MAP[rimVendorKey] || null;
            const rimPrice = rimSpecificGid ? (ASSEMBLY_SERVICE_PRICES_BY_GID[rimSpecificGid] || 0) : 0;

            if (hubSpecificGid && rimSpecificGid) {
                // Both vendors have special pricing, so pick the HIGHEST of the two.
                finalAssemblyGid = (rimPrice > hubPrice) ? rimSpecificGid : hubSpecificGid;
            } else if (hubSpecificGid) {
                // Only the hub has special pricing. Use it.
                finalAssemblyGid = hubSpecificGid;
            } else if (rimSpecificGid) {
                // Only the rim has special pricing. Use it.
                finalAssemblyGid = rimSpecificGid;
            } else {
                // No vendor-specific pricing was found. Use the default for wheelsets.
                finalAssemblyGid = DEFAULT_ASSEMBLY_SERVICE_VARIANT_GID;
            }
        }

        // Get the final price based on the chosen GID.
        const finalPrice = ASSEMBLY_SERVICE_PRICES_BY_GID[finalAssemblyGid] || 0;

        // Assign the final service and cost to the build state.
        buildState.components[`${posLower}AssemblyService`] = {
            variantGid: finalAssemblyGid,
            name: "Assembly Service",
            price: finalPrice,
            costInCents: Math.round(finalPrice * 100)
        };
    }

    if (selectedRim && buildState.tubelessTapeInstalled) {
        buildState.components[`${posLower}TubelessTape`] = {
            variantGid: 'gid://shopify/ProductVariant/51561220669747',
            name: 'Tubeless Tape (Installed)',
            price: 0,
            costInCents: 0
        };
    }

    const spokeVendor = selectedSpokes ? selectedSpokes.vendor : null;
    for (const addonKey in REQUIRED_ADDONS_CONFIG) {
        const addonConfig = REQUIRED_ADDONS_CONFIG[addonKey];
        if (addonConfig.condition(selectedHub, spokeVendor)) {
            // This .push() was causing the crash because the array wasn't defined above
            buildState.components[`${posLower}RequiredAddons`].push({
                name: addonConfig.name,
                price: addonConfig.price,
                variantGid: addonConfig.variantGid,
                costInCents: Math.round(addonConfig.price * 100)
            });
        }
    }
}
// --- END: calculateWheelCosts FUNCTION ---

    // --- API Call Functions ---
    async function storefrontApiQuery(query, variables = {}) { if(!config.storefrontApiToken)throw new Error("API Token missing."); const url=`/api/2024-04/graphql.json`; try { const r=await fetch(url,{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','X-Shopify-Storefront-Access-Token':config.storefrontApiToken},body:JSON.stringify({query,variables})}); const j=await r.json(); if(j.errors||!r.ok){const e=j.errors?j.errors.map(e=>e.message).join(','):`HTTP ${r.status}`; throw new Error(`GraphQL failed: ${e}`);} if(!j.data && !j.errors) { console.warn("GraphQL query successful but no data field."); return null;} return j.data;} catch(e){console.error("API Error:",e); throw e;} }

    // --- COMPONENT LOGIC FUNCTIONS (fetchers, displayers - existing code) ---
    // ... (Keep all your existing component fetching, filtering, and display functions for Rims, Hubs, Spokes, Nipples, ValveStems here, like fetchComponentProducts, loadAndFilterRims, displayRimProductCards, etc.)
    // ... NO CHANGES TO THESE FUNCTIONS THEMSELVES, JUST THEIR CALLERS IF NEEDED
    // --- Ensure all your component selection functions correctly set:
    // --- buildState.components[key].variantId (Shopify GID string)
    // --- buildState.components[key].price (price in CENTS as a number)
    // --- buildState.components[key].vendor, etc.

async function fetchBuilderComponentProducts(tag) {
    let allProductNodes = [];
    let cursor = null;
    let hasNextPage = true;

    while (hasNextPage) {
        const query = `
            query getComponentProducts($tagQuery: String!, $first: Int = 50, $variantsFirst: Int = 250, $cursor: String) {
                products(first: $first, query: $tagQuery, after: $cursor) {
                    pageInfo { hasNextPage endCursor }
                    edges {
                        node {
                            id title handle tags vendor availableForSale productType
                            vendorLogo: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "vendor_logo") { reference { ... on MediaImage { image { url(transform:{maxWidth:100}) } } } value }
                            wheelModel: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "wheel_spec_model") { value }
                            pairingKey: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "pairing_key") { value }
                            spokeHubInterface: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "spoke_hub_interface") { value }
                            rimDepth: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "rim_depth_mm") { value }
                            leadTimeDays: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "lead_time_days") { value }
                            optionalAddonProductGids: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "optional_addon_gids") { value }
                            availableFreehubs: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "freehub") { value }
                            freehubVariantMap: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "freehub_variant_map") { value }
                            weight_g: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "weight_g") { value }
                            pre_configured_wheel_rules: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "pre_configured_wheel_rules") { value }
                            
                            rim_erd: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "rim_erd") { value }
                            hub_flange_diameter_left: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_flange_diameter_left") { value }
                            hub_flange_diameter_right: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_flange_diameter_right") { value }
                            hub_flange_offset_left: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_flange_offset_left") { value }
                            hub_flange_offset_right: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_flange_offset_right") { value }
                            hub_spoke_hole_diameter: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_diameter") { value }
                            hub_lacing_policy: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_lacing_policy") { value }

                            # --- ADDED THESE LINES FOR INTEGRATED WHEELS ---
                            integrated_hub_name: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "integrated_hub_name") { value }
                            included_valve_variant_id: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "included_valve_variant_id") { value }
                            # -----------------------------------------------

                            variants(first: $variantsFirst) {
                                edges {
                                    node {
                                        id sku title availableForSale quantityAvailable
                                        price { amount currencyCode }
                                        image { url(transform:{maxWidth:500}) altText }
                                        selectedOptions { name value }
                                        spec_position: metafield(namespace:"custom",key:"wheel_spec_position"){ value }
                                        spec_brake_interface: metafield(namespace:"custom",key:"wheel_spec_brake_interface"){ value }
                                        spec_hub_spacing: metafield(namespace:"custom",key:"wheel_spec_hub_spacing"){ value }
                                        spec_freehub: metafield(namespace:"custom",key:"wheel_spec_freehub"){ value }
                                        spec_spoke_count: metafield(namespace:"custom",key:"wheel_spec_spoke_count"){ value }
                                        spec_rim_size: metafield(namespace:"custom",key:"wheel_spec_rim_size"){ value }
                                        valve_min_depth: metafield(namespace:"custom", key:"valve_min_rim_depth_mm") { value }
                                        valve_max_depth: metafield(namespace:"custom", key:"valve_max_rim_depth_mm") { value }
                                        internal_width_mm: metafield(namespace:"custom", key:"wheel_spec_internal_width_mm"){ value }
                                        weight_g: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "weight_g") { value }
                                        rim_erd: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "rim_erd") { value }
                                        hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_left: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_left") { value }
                                        hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_right: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_right") { value }
                                        hub_manual_cross_value: metafield(namespace: "custom", key: "hub_manual_cross_value") { value }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }`;

        try {
            const data = await storefrontApiQuery(query, { tagQuery: `tag:'${tag}'`, cursor: cursor });
            if (!data?.products?.edges) { hasNextPage = false; continue; }
            const pageProducts = data.products.edges.map(edge => edge.node);
            allProductNodes.push(...pageProducts);
            hasNextPage = data.products.pageInfo.hasNextPage;
            cursor = data.products.pageInfo.endCursor;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error(`fetchBuilderComponentProducts Error for tag '${tag}': ${error.message}`);
            hasNextPage = false;
        }
    }
    
    // Helper to safely parse floats
    const safeFloat = (metafield) => {
        if (!metafield || !metafield.value || metafield.value.trim() === '') return null;
        const num = parseFloat(metafield.value);
        return isNaN(num) ? null : num;
    };

    // Helper to safely get string values
    const safeString = (metafield) => {
        if (!metafield || !metafield.value || metafield.value.trim() === '') return null;
        return metafield.value;
    };

    return allProductNodes.map(node => {
        let productOptionalAddonGids = [];
        if (node.optionalAddonProductGids && typeof node.optionalAddonProductGids.value === 'string') {
            try { productOptionalAddonGids = JSON.parse(node.optionalAddonProductGids.value); } catch (e) { productOptionalAddonGids = node.optionalAddonProductGids.value.split(',').map(gid => gid.trim()); }
            if (!Array.isArray(productOptionalAddonGids)) productOptionalAddonGids = [];
        }

        const variants = node.variants.edges.map(vEdge => {
            const vNode = vEdge.node;
            
            let processedVariant = {
                ...vNode,
                price: { amount: parseFloat(vNode.price.amount) * 100, code: vNode.price.currencyCode },
                spec_position: vNode.spec_position?.value,
                spec_brake_interface: (() => { const rawValue = vNode.spec_brake_interface?.value; if (!rawValue) return []; try { return JSON.parse(rawValue); } catch (e) { return [String(rawValue).trim()]; } })(),
                spec_hub_spacing: vNode.spec_hub_spacing?.value,
                spec_freehub: vNode.spec_freehub?.value,
                spec_spoke_count: (() => { const spokeOption = vNode.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'spoke count'); return spokeOption?.value || vNode.spec_spoke_count?.value || null; })(),
                spec_rim_size: vNode.spec_rim_size,
                valve_min_depth: vNode.valve_min_depth?.value ? parseInt(vNode.valve_min_depth.value) : null,
                valve_max_depth: vNode.valve_max_depth?.value ? parseInt(vNode.valve_max_depth.value) : null,
                internal_width_mm: vNode.internal_width_mm?.value ? parseInt(vNode.internal_width_mm.value) : null,
                weight_g: safeFloat(vNode.weight_g) !== null ? safeFloat(vNode.weight_g) : safeFloat(node.weight_g),
                rim_erd: safeString(vNode.rim_erd) !== null ? safeString(vNode.rim_erd) : safeString(node.rim_erd),
                hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_left: vNode.hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_left?.value,
                hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_right: vNode.hub_sp_offset_spoke_hole_right?.value,
                hub_manual_cross_value: vNode.hub_manual_cross_value?.value
            };
            
            if (vNode.spec_rim_size?.value) {
                try { processedVariant.spec_rim_size.parsedValue = JSON.parse(vNode.spec_rim_size.value); } catch (e) { processedVariant.spec_rim_size.parsedValue = String(vNode.spec_rim_size.value).trim(); }
            } else { processedVariant.spec_rim_size = { value: null, parsedValue: null }; }
            return processedVariant;
        });

        return {
            ...node,
            variants: variants,
            vendorLogoUrl: node.vendorLogo?.reference?.image?.url || node.vendorLogo?.value || null,
            wheelModel: node.wheelModel?.value || null,
            pairingKey: node.pairingKey?.value || null,
            spokeHubInterface: node.spokeHubInterface?.value || null,
            rimDepth: node.rimDepth?.value ? parseInt(node.rimDepth.value) : null,
            leadTimeDays: node.leadTimeDays?.value ? parseInt(node.leadTimeDays.value, 10) : 0,
            weight_g: safeFloat(node.weight_g),
            availableFreehubs: (() => { const rawValue = node.availableFreehubs?.value; if (!rawValue) return []; try { return JSON.parse(rawValue); } catch(e) { return []; } })(),
            freehubVariantMap: (() => { const rawValue = node.freehubVariantMap?.value; if (!rawValue) return {}; try { return JSON.parse(rawValue); } catch(e) { return {}; } })(),
            optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: productOptionalAddonGids,
            rim_erd: safeString(node.rim_erd),
            preconfiguredRules: (() => { 
                const rawValue = node.pre_configured_wheel_rules?.value; 
                if (!rawValue) return []; 
                try { 
                    const rules = JSON.parse(rawValue);
                    return Array.isArray(rules) ? rules.filter(r => r && r.masterVariantGid) : [];
                } catch(e) { return []; } 
            })(),
            hub_flange_diameter_left: node.hub_flange_diameter_left?.value,
            hub_flange_diameter_right: node.hub_flange_diameter_right?.value,
            hub_flange_offset_left: node.hub_flange_offset_left?.value,
            hub_flange_offset_right: node.hub_flange_offset_right?.value,
            hub_spoke_hole_diameter: node.hub_spoke_hole_diameter?.value,

            // --- ADDED MAPPING FOR INTEGRATED WHEELS ---
            integrated_hub_name: node.integrated_hub_name?.value,
            included_valve_variant_id: node.included_valve_variant_id?.value
            // -------------------------------------------
        };
    });
}
  
    async function loadAndFilterRims() {
    console.log("--- loadAndFilterRims (Combined F/R) ---");
    const buildType = buildState.buildType;
    const positionsToLoad = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Rear');
    if (positionsToLoad.length === 0) return;

    if (allRimProductsCache.length === 0) {
        console.log("Rim cache empty in loadAndFilterRims.");
        if (componentFetchPromises.rims) {
            console.log("Waiting for early rim fetch promise to complete...");
            try {
                await componentFetchPromises.rims;
                console.log("Early rim fetch completed. Cache should now be populated.");
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Error awaiting early rim fetch in loadAndFilterRims:", error);
            }
        } else {
            console.log("No early rim fetch promise found or it failed. Fetching Rims directly now...");
            const ridingStyleForDirectFetch = buildState.ridingStyle;
            if (!ridingStyleForDirectFetch) {
                console.warn("loadAndFilterRims (direct fetch): Riding style not set. Cannot fetch rims.");
                // Handle UI feedback if necessary (e.g., show error in rim sections)
                positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
                    const loader = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-rim-loading`);
                    if(loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
                    const errorEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-rim-error`);
                    if(errorEl) errorEl.textContent = `Error: Riding style not selected.`;
                     const optionsEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-rim-options-container`);
                    if(optionsEl) optionsEl.innerHTML = '<p>Please select a riding style in Step 1.</p>';
                });
                return;
            }
            try {
                // This call to fetchRimProducts will populate allRimProductsCache
                await fetchRimProducts(ridingStyleForDirectFetch);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Error fetching rim products directly in loadAndFilterRims:", error);
            }
        }
    } else {
        console.log("Using already populated/cached rim data for loadAndFilterRims.");
    }

    if (allRimProductsCache.length === 0 && buildState.ridingStyle) { // Only show critical error if style was set but fetch failed
        console.error("Rim cache is STILL empty after attempting to load/wait for fetch. Rim data loading failed.");
        positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
            const loader = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-rim-loading`);
            if(loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
            const errorEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-rim-error`);
            if(errorEl) errorEl.textContent = `Error: Rim data failed to load.`;
             const optionsEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-rim-options-container`);
            if(optionsEl) optionsEl.innerHTML = '<p>Rim data failed to load.</p>';
        });
        return;
    }

    // The rest of loadAndFilterRims (looping through positionsToLoad, calling loadAndFilterRimsForPosition) remains the same.
    for (const position of positionsToLoad) {
        await loadAndFilterRimsForPosition(position);
    }
    console.log("--- loadAndFilterRims (Combined F/R) finished ---");
}

async function loadAndFilterRimsForPosition(position, isChange = false) {
    console.log(`--- loadAndFilterRimsForPosition: ${position} ${isChange ? '(Change Mode)' : ''} ---`);
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const refs = {
        filters: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-rim-filters`),
        loading: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-rim-loading`),
        error: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-rim-error`),
        optionsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-rim-options-container`),
        selectionSpan: document.querySelector(`#${posLower}-rim-selection span`),
        imageContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-rim-image-container`),
        actionButtonsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-rim-action-buttons`)
    };

    if (!refs.optionsContainer) return;

    refs.loading.style.display = 'block';
    refs.error.style.display = 'none';
    const subsectionElement = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-rim-subsection`);
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Rim`;
    const isSelected = buildState.components[stateKey];

    // --- Restore Integrated Logic on Load ---
    if (isSelected && isSelected.tags && isSelected.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel') && !isChange) {
        console.log(`Restoring Integrated Wheel Logic for ${position}`);
        applyIntegratedWheelLogic(position, isSelected);
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Rim', isSelected);
        refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    // ---------------------------------------------

    if (isSelected && !isChange) {
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Rim', isSelected);
        refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    
    if (!isSelected) buildState._ui.activeVendor[stateKey] = null;

    refs.imageContainer.innerHTML = '';
    refs.imageContainer.style.display = 'none';
    refs.optionsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Loading options...</p>';
    if (isChange && refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    else if (refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
    if (subsectionElement && !isChange) subsectionElement.classList.remove('selection-made');

    try {
        const size = buildState.specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`];
        const spokeCountSpec = buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`];

        if (!size || !spokeCountSpec) { 
            refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Please select Wheel Size and Spoke Count in Step 2.</p>';
            refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
            displayComponentVendorFilters(stateKey, [], refs.filters, position);
            return;
        }

        if (allRimProductsCache.length === 0) {
            await loadAndFilterRims();
            if (allRimProductsCache.length === 0) {
                refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Rim data failed.</p>';
                refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }
        }
        
        // --- HELPER FOR STRICT CHECKS ---
        const checkProduct = (p, v) => {
            const isIntegrated = p.tags && p.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel');
            const sizeValue = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
            const sizeMatch = (sizeValue === size || (Array.isArray(sizeValue) && sizeValue.includes(size)));
            const positionMatch = (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear");
            const availMatch = v.availableForSale;

            // START: NEW TOGGLE-AWARE BRAKE MATCH
            let brakeMatch = false;
            const variantBrakeInterfaces = v.spec_brake_interface || [];
            const isRimBrakeRim = variantBrakeInterfaces.includes('Rim Brake');
            const toggleActive = buildState._ui.showRimBrakeRims;

            if (buildState.specs.brakeStyle === 'Rim Brake') {
                brakeMatch = isRimBrakeRim;
            } else {
                // If it's a Disc build: Show Disc Rims OR (Show Rim Brake Rims ONLY if toggle is on)
                brakeMatch = !isRimBrakeRim || (isRimBrakeRim && toggleActive);
            }
            // END: NEW TOGGLE-AWARE BRAKE MATCH

            if (isIntegrated) {
                const hubSpacing = buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];
                const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
                const spacingMatch = v.spec_hub_spacing === hubSpacing;
                const integratedBrakeMatch = (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle);
                
                // Rear Integrated Check
                if (posLower === 'rear') {
                    const targetFreehub = buildState.specs.freehubType;
                    if (!p.availableFreehubs || !p.availableFreehubs.includes(targetFreehub)) return false;
                }
                
                return sizeMatch && positionMatch && availMatch && spacingMatch && integratedBrakeMatch;
            } else {
                const spokeMatch = (String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(spokeCountSpec));
                // Ensure brakeMatch is added to the end of this return line:
                return sizeMatch && positionMatch && availMatch && spokeMatch && brakeMatch;
            }
        };

        // Filter 1: STRICTLY filtered list for the vendor dropdown.
        const strictlyCompatibleProducts = allRimProductsCache.filter(p => {
            if (p.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return true;
            return p.variants.some(v => checkProduct(p, v));
        });

        // Filter 2: LOOSELY filtered list for displaying product cards.
        const productsForDisplay = allRimProductsCache.filter(p => {
            if (p.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return true;
            return p.variants.some(v => checkProduct(p, v));
        });

        if (productsForDisplay.length === 0) {
            refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${posLower} rims available for size: ${size}.</p>`;
        }

        displayComponentVendorFilters(stateKey, strictlyCompatibleProducts, refs.filters, position);
        
        if (isChange) showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(position, 'Rim', refs.actionButtonsContainer);
        
        displayRimProductCards(position, productsForDisplay, refs.optionsContainer);

    } catch (error) {
        refs.error.textContent = `Error: ${error.message}.`;
        refs.error.style.display = 'block';
        console.error(`Error in loadAndFilterRimsForPosition(${position}):`, error);
        refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Error.</p>';
    } finally {
        refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

function generateMismatchHint(vendor, componentKey, position) {
    const { specs } = buildState;
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    
    let cacheToSearch;
    if (componentKey.endsWith('Rim')) cacheToSearch = allRimProductsCache;
    else if (componentKey.endsWith('Hub')) cacheToSearch = allHubProductsCache;
    else return `No products match your current specs`;

    const vendorProducts = cacheToSearch.filter(p => p.vendor === vendor);
    if (vendorProducts.length === 0) return `No products match your current specs`;

    // --- LOGIC FOR HUBS (with tiered hint priority) ---
    if (componentKey.endsWith('Hub')) {
        const currentBrakeStyle = specs.brakeStyle;
        const currentSpokeCount = specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`];
        const currentHubSpacing = specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];

        // --- Priority 1: Check for a "one-step fix" by changing ONLY Brake Style ---
        const possibleBrakeHints = new Set();
        for (const p of vendorProducts) {
            for (const v of p.variants) {
                if (String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(currentSpokeCount) && v.spec_hub_spacing === currentHubSpacing) {
                    (v.spec_brake_interface || []).forEach(style => {
                        if (style !== currentBrakeStyle) possibleBrakeHints.add(style);
                    });
                }
            }
        }
        if (possibleBrakeHints.size > 0) {
            return `Requires Brake Style: ${Array.from(possibleBrakeHints).join(' or ')}`;
        }

        // --- Priority 2: Check for a "one-step fix" by changing ONLY Spoke Count ---
        const possibleSpokeHints = new Set();
        for (const p of vendorProducts) {
            for (const v of p.variants) {
                if ((v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(currentBrakeStyle) && v.spec_hub_spacing === currentHubSpacing) {
                    if (String(v.spec_spoke_count) !== String(currentSpokeCount)) {
                        possibleSpokeHints.add(v.spec_spoke_count);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        if (possibleSpokeHints.size > 0) {
            const sortedCounts = Array.from(possibleSpokeHints).sort((a, b) => parseInt(a) - parseInt(b));
            return `Requires Spoke Count: ${sortedCounts.join(' or ')}`;
        }

        // --- Priority 3 (Fallback): Multiple specs are wrong. Show all available options. ---
        const allAvailableBrakeStyles = new Set();
        const allAvailableSpokeCounts = new Set();
        vendorProducts.forEach(p => {
            p.variants.forEach(v => {
                if (v.spec_hub_spacing === currentHubSpacing) { // Still respect the "hard" spec of spacing
                    (v.spec_brake_interface || []).forEach(style => allAvailableBrakeStyles.add(style));
                    if (v.spec_spoke_count) allAvailableSpokeCounts.add(v.spec_spoke_count);
                }
            });
        });

        let hints = [];
        if (allAvailableBrakeStyles.size > 0 && !allAvailableBrakeStyles.has(currentBrakeStyle)) {
            hints.push(`Brake Style: ${Array.from(allAvailableBrakeStyles).join('/')}`);
        }
        if (allAvailableSpokeCounts.size > 0 && !allAvailableSpokeCounts.has(currentSpokeCount)) {
            const sortedCounts = Array.from(allAvailableSpokeCounts).sort((a, b) => parseInt(a) - parseInt(b));
            hints.push(`Spoke Count: ${sortedCounts.join('/')}`);
        }
        if (hints.length > 0) {
            return `Requires ${hints.join(' & ')}`;
        }
    }

    // --- LOGIC FOR RIMS (Simpler, as it only has one quick-change spec) ---
    if (componentKey.endsWith('Rim')) {
        const currentSpokeCount = specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`];
        const currentWheelSize = specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`];

        const otherSpokeCounts = new Set();
        for (const p of vendorProducts) {
            for (const v of p.variants) {
                const sizeValue = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                const sizeMatch = Array.isArray(sizeValue) ? sizeValue.includes(currentWheelSize) : sizeValue === currentWheelSize;
                
                if (String(v.spec_spoke_count) !== String(currentSpokeCount) && sizeMatch) {
                    otherSpokeCounts.add(v.spec_spoke_count);
                }
            }
        }
        if (otherSpokeCounts.size > 0) {
            const sortedCounts = Array.from(otherSpokeCounts).sort((a, b) => parseInt(a) - parseInt(b));
            return `Requires Spoke Count: ${sortedCounts.join(' or ')}`;
        }
    }

    return `No products match your current specs`; // Final fallback
}

function displayComponentVendorFilters(componentKey, products, filterContainer, position) {
    if (!filterContainer) return;
    const vendorArea = filterContainer.querySelector('.vendor-filter-area');
    if (!vendorArea) {
        console.error("Missing .vendor-filter-area in", filterContainer);
        return;
    }

    let globalCacheForComponentType;
    if (componentKey.endsWith('Rim')) globalCacheForComponentType = allRimProductsCache;
    else if (componentKey.endsWith('Hub')) globalCacheForComponentType = allHubProductsCache;
    else if (componentKey.endsWith('Spokes')) globalCacheForComponentType = allSpokeProductsCache;
    else if (componentKey.endsWith('Nipples')) globalCacheForComponentType = allNippleProductsCache;
    else if (componentKey.endsWith('ValveStem')) globalCacheForComponentType = allValveStemProductsCache;
    else globalCacheForComponentType = products;

    const allPossibleVendors = [...new Set(globalCacheForComponentType.map(p => p.vendor))].sort((a, b) => {
        return getSortableName(a).localeCompare(getSortableName(b));
    });
    
    // --- Use the products list passed from the loader ---
    // The 'products' argument already contains the correctly filtered list (including Reserve Infinity).
    // We just need to check if a vendor exists in that list.
    const availableVendors = new Set(products.map(p => p.vendor));

    const currentActiveVendor = buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKey];
    let toggleContentHTML = '';

    if (currentActiveVendor === null) {
        toggleContentHTML = '<span class="vendor-prompt"><b>Click to select a vendor</b></span>';
    } else if (currentActiveVendor === 'all') {
        toggleContentHTML = '<span class="toggle-all-vendors-button">All Vendors</span>';
    } else {
        const vendorInfo = vendorLogoMap[currentActiveVendor];
        const logoUrl = vendorInfo?.logoUrl;
        toggleContentHTML = `<span>
                                ${logoUrl ? `<img src="${logoUrl}" alt="${currentActiveVendor}" class="toggle-vendor-logo">` : `<span>${currentActiveVendor}</span>`}
                             </span>`;
    }

    const hasAnyCompatibleProducts = availableVendors.size > 0;
    const allVendorsDisabledAttr = hasAnyCompatibleProducts ? '' : 'disabled';
    const allVendorsTooltip = hasAnyCompatibleProducts ? 'All Vendors' : 'No products match your current specs';

    let dropdownHTML = `
        <h4>Vendor:</h4>
        <div class="vendor-filter-dropdown" data-component-key="${componentKey}">
            <button type="button" class="dropdown-toggle">
                ${toggleContentHTML}
            </button>
            <div class="dropdown-menu">
                <div class="vendor-filter-options">
                    <button type="button" class="vendor-filter-btn ${currentActiveVendor === 'all' ? 'active' : ''}" data-vendor="all" data-position="${position}" data-component-key="${componentKey}" title="${allVendorsTooltip}" ${allVendorsDisabledAttr}>
                        <span>All</span>
                    </button>`;

    allPossibleVendors.forEach(vendor => {
        // This check now respects the "Integrated" logic because 'availableVendors' is built from the pre-filtered 'products' list
        const hasCompatibleProducts = availableVendors.has(vendor);

        // If unavailable, use hint engine
        const tooltipTitle = hasCompatibleProducts 
            ? vendor 
            : generateMismatchHint(vendor, componentKey, position);

        const vendorInfo = vendorLogoMap[vendor];
        const logoUrl = vendorInfo?.logoUrl;
        const vendorName = vendorInfo?.name || vendor;
        const activeClass = currentActiveVendor === vendorName ? 'active' : '';
        const unavailableClass = hasCompatibleProducts ? '' : 'is-unavailable';
        const disabledAttr = hasCompatibleProducts ? '' : 'disabled';

        dropdownHTML += `<button type="button" class="vendor-filter-btn ${activeClass} ${unavailableClass}" data-vendor="${vendorName.replace(/"/g, '\\"')}" data-position="${position}" data-component-key="${componentKey}" title="${tooltipTitle}" ${disabledAttr}>
                            ${logoUrl ? `<img src="${logoUrl}" alt="${vendorName}" class="vendor-logo">` : `<span>${vendorName}</span>`}
                         </button>`;
    });

    if (componentKey.endsWith('Rim')) {
        const isChecked = buildState._ui.showRimBrakeRims ? 'checked' : '';
        dropdownHTML += `
            <div class="vendor-msw-toggle-wrapper">
                <input type="checkbox" class="msw-global-checkbox" id="msw-${position}" ${isChecked}>
                <label for="msw-${position}">Include Rim Brake Options</label>
            </div>`;
    }

    dropdownHTML += `
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

    vendorArea.innerHTML = dropdownHTML;
}
  
    function checkIfModelGroupHasVariants(position, productsInGroup) { const posLower = position.toLowerCase(); const size = buildState.specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`]; const spokeCountSpec = buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`]; if (!size) return false; for (const p of productsInGroup) { for (const v of p.variants) { const sizeMatch = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue === size || (Array.isArray(v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue) && v.spec_rim_size.parsedValue.includes(size)); const positionMatch = v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear"; const spokeMatch = !spokeCountSpec || (v.spec_spoke_count && String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(spokeCountSpec)); if (v.availableForSale && positionMatch && sizeMatch && spokeMatch) return true; } } return false; }

function displayRimVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, variantContainer) {
    if (!variantContainer) return;
    variantContainer.innerHTML = ''; 

    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const size = buildState.specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`];
    const spokeCountSpec = buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`];
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Rim`;
    const selectedComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

    const getRimColor = (variantTitle) => {
        if (!variantTitle) return null;
        const parts = variantTitle.split('/').map(p => p.trim());
        const lastPart = parts[parts.length - 1];
        return isNaN(lastPart) ? lastPart.toLowerCase() : null;
    };

    let compatibleVariants = [];
    
    productsInGroup.forEach(p => {
        const productDetails = {
            productId: p.id, productTitle: p.title, productHandle: p.handle, vendor: p.vendor, pairingKey: p.pairingKey, rimDepth: p.rimDepth, optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: p.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct, leadTimeDays: p.leadTimeDays || 0, wheelModel: p.wheelModel || null, product_weight_g: p.weight_g, product_rim_erd: p.rim_erd,
            tags: p.tags, integrated_hub_name: p.integrated_hub_name, included_valve_variant_id: p.included_valve_variant_id,
            freehubVariantMap: p.freehubVariantMap, 
            availableFreehubs: p.availableFreehubs
        };

        const isIntegrated = p.tags && p.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel');

        p.variants.forEach(v => {
            const sizeValue = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
            const sizeMatch = sizeValue === size || (Array.isArray(sizeValue) && sizeValue.includes(size));
            const positionMatch = (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear");
            
            // START: TOGGLE-AWARE BRAKE MATCH
            let brakeMatch = false;
            const variantBrakeInterfaces = v.spec_brake_interface || [];
            const isRimBrakeRim = variantBrakeInterfaces.includes('Rim Brake');
            const toggleActive = buildState._ui.showRimBrakeRims;

            if (buildState.specs.brakeStyle === 'Rim Brake') {
                brakeMatch = isRimBrakeRim;
            } else {
                // Assume Disc build: Show everything except Rim Brake rims, UNLESS toggle is on.
                brakeMatch = !isRimBrakeRim || (isRimBrakeRim && toggleActive);
            }
            // END: NEW TOGGLE-AWARE BRAKE MATCH

    let spokeMatch = false;
            if (isIntegrated) {
                // Define the variables needed for the Integrated Wheel check
                const hubSpacing = buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];
                const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
                
                const spacingMatch = v.spec_hub_spacing === hubSpacing;
                const integratedBrakeMatch = (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle);
                
                let freehubMatch = true;
                if (posLower === 'rear') {
                    const targetFreehub = buildState.specs.freehubType;
                    if (p.availableFreehubs && Array.isArray(p.availableFreehubs)) {
                         if (!p.availableFreehubs.includes(targetFreehub)) {
                            freehubMatch = false;
                         }
                    } else if (targetFreehub) {
                        freehubMatch = false;
                    }
                }

                spokeMatch = spacingMatch && integratedBrakeMatch && freehubMatch;
            } else {
                // Standard Rim Logic
                spokeMatch = !spokeCountSpec || (String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(spokeCountSpec));
            }

    if (v.availableForSale && positionMatch && sizeMatch && spokeMatch && brakeMatch) {
                compatibleVariants.push({ ...v, ...productDetails });
            }
});
    });

    if (compatibleVariants.length === 0) {
        variantContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No options match Size: ${size}${spokeCountSpec ? ` & Spokes: ${spokeCountSpec}` : ''}.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    const uniqueVariants = Array.from(new Map(compatibleVariants.map(v => [v.id, v])).values())
                                .sort((a, b) => (a.productTitle || '').localeCompare(b.productTitle || ''));

    uniqueVariants.forEach(v_rim => {
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.className = 'component-variant-button rim-variant-button';
        btn.dataset.variantId = v_rim.id;
        btn.dataset.productId = v_rim.productId;
        btn.type = 'button';
        if (selectedComponent?.variantId === v_rim.id) btn.classList.add('selected');

        const weight = v_rim.weight_g ?? v_rim.product_weight_g ?? null;
        let displayTitle = v_rim.productTitle;
        const potentialColor = getRimColor(v_rim.title);
        if (potentialColor) { displayTitle += ` (${potentialColor.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + potentialColor.slice(1)})`; }

        btn.innerHTML = `
            <div class="variant-button-image-container">
                ${v_rim.image?.url ? `<img src="${v_rim.image.url}" alt="${displayTitle}" loading="lazy" class="variant-button-image">` : '<div class="variant-button-image-placeholder"></div>'}
            </div>
            <div class="variant-button-details">
                <span class="variant-details">${displayTitle}</span>
                ${v_rim.price?.amount ? `<span class="variant-price">${formatPrice(v_rim.price.amount)}</span>` : ''}
            </div>
            <div class="variant-button-stats">
                ${weight ? `<span class="stat-item">Weight: <strong>${weight}g</strong></span>` : ''}
            </div>`;

        btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const isIntegratedClick = v_rim.tags && v_rim.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel');
            if (isIntegratedClick) {
                applyIntegratedWheelLogic(position, v_rim);
            } else {
                resetIntegratedWheelLogic(position);
            }

            const selectedRimComponentData = v_rim;
            const previouslySelectedComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];
            const newSelectedVariantId = selectedRimComponentData.id;
            if (previouslySelectedComponent && previouslySelectedComponent.productId !== selectedRimComponentData.productId) {
                const addonKeysToRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons).filter(key => {
                    const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                    return addon.baseComponentPosition === position && addon.baseComponentType === 'Rim' && addon.baseComponentVariantId === previouslySelectedComponent.variantId;
                });
                addonKeysToRemove.forEach(key => { delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key]; });
                if (addonKeysToRemove.length > 0) saveLastActiveBuild();
            } else if (previouslySelectedComponent && previouslySelectedComponent.variantId !== newSelectedVariantId) {
                 manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(position, 'Rim', previouslySelectedComponent.variantId, newSelectedVariantId, selectedRimComponentData.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || []);
            }
            
            const selectedRimComponent = {
                variantId: selectedRimComponentData.id, title: selectedRimComponentData.productTitle, variantTitle: selectedRimComponentData.title, sku: selectedRimComponentData.sku,
                price: selectedRimComponentData.price.amount, vendor: selectedRimComponentData.vendor, spokeCount: String(selectedRimComponentData.spec_spoke_count),
                wheelSize: size, image: selectedRimComponentData.image, pairingKey: selectedRimComponentData.pairingKey, selectedOptions: selectedRimComponentData.selectedOptions,
                rimDepth: selectedRimComponentData.rimDepth, productId: selectedRimComponentData.productId, productHandle: selectedRimComponentData.productHandle,
                optionalAddonProductGids: selectedRimComponentData.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct,
                internal_width_mm: selectedRimComponentData.internal_width_mm,
                quantityAvailable: selectedRimComponentData.quantityAvailable, 
                leadTimeDays: selectedRimComponentData.leadTimeDays, 
                wheelModel: selectedRimComponentData.wheelModel, 
                weight_g: selectedRimComponentData.weight_g ?? selectedRimComponentData.product_weight_g ?? null,
                rim_erd: selectedRimComponentData.rim_erd ?? selectedRimComponentData.product_rim_erd ?? null,
                tags: selectedRimComponentData.tags,
                integrated_hub_name: selectedRimComponentData.integrated_hub_name,
                included_valve_variant_id: selectedRimComponentData.included_valve_variant_id,
                freehubVariantMap: selectedRimComponentData.freehubVariantMap, 
                availableFreehubs: selectedRimComponentData.availableFreehubs  
            };
