            buildState.components[stateKey] = selectedRimComponent;
            buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
            updateStep3ButtonText();
            calculateWheelCosts(position);
            updateComponentUI(position, 'Rim', selectedRimComponent);
            evaluateValveStemForRimChange(position);
            await handleAutoPairing('Rim', position, selectedRimComponent, false);
            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
            saveLastActiveBuild();
            if (buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === position && buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.type === 'Rim') { cancelComponentChange(); }
            handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();
            scrollToComponentSection(position, 'Rim');
        });
        variantContainer.appendChild(btn);
    });
}
// --- END: displayRimVariantButtonsByProduct ---

// --- START: fetchRimProducts (V4.3 - With Specific Tag Query) ---
async function fetchRimProducts(ridingStyle) {
    if (!ridingStyle) {
        console.warn("fetchRimProducts: Riding style not provided. Cannot fetch rims.");
        allRimProductsCache = []; // Ensure cache is empty if style is missing
        return;
    }
    
    let tagQuery;
    
    if (ridingStyle === 'hybrid') {
        // CORRECTION: Just pass the tag content. The fetcher wraps it in "tag:'...'"
        tagQuery = "component:rim"; 
    } else {
        // MTB/Gravel use the injection hack to add the style tag
        tagQuery = ridingStyle === 'mtb'
            ? "style:mtb' AND tag:'component:rim"
            : (ridingStyle === 'gravelroad' ? "style:gravelroad' AND tag:'component:rim" : null);
    }

    if (!tagQuery) {
        console.warn(`fetchRimProducts: Unknown ridingStyle '${ridingStyle}', cannot construct tag query for rims.`);
        allRimProductsCache = [];
        return;
    }
    
    console.log(`fetchRimProducts: Constructing query with tags: ${tagQuery}`);

    try {
        allRimProductsCache = await fetchBuilderComponentProducts(tagQuery);
        updateGlobalVendorLogoMap(allRimProductsCache);
        if (buildState.step === 2) renderStep2(); 
        console.log(`fetchRimProducts: Found and cached ${allRimProductsCache.length} rim products using query: "${tagQuery}".`);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`fetchRimProducts Error for query "${tagQuery}":`, error);
        allRimProductsCache = []; // Clear cache on error
        throw error; // Re-throw to be caught by caller
    }
}
// --- END: fetchRimProducts ---
  
// [START] fetchHubProducts
async function fetchHubProducts() {
    console.log("Fetching ALL hub products using tag: component:hub");
    const hubTag = "component:hub";
    try {
        allHubProductsCache = await fetchBuilderComponentProducts(hubTag);
        updateGlobalVendorLogoMap(allHubProductsCache);
        if (buildState.step === 2) renderStep2();
        console.log(`fetchHubProducts: Found and cached ${allHubProductsCache.length} products.`);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("fetchHubProducts Error:", error);
        allHubProductsCache = [];
        throw error;
    }
    return allHubProductsCache;
}
// [END] fetchHubProducts
  
    async function loadAndFilterHubs() { console.log("--- loadAndFilterHubs (Combined F/R) ---"); const buildType = buildState.buildType; const positionsToLoad = []; if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Front'); if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Rear'); if (positionsToLoad.length === 0) return; positionsToLoad.forEach(p => { const l=document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-hub-loading`); if(l)l.style.display='block'; const o=document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-hub-options-container`); if(o)o.innerHTML='<p>Loading hub options...</p>';}); 

        // --- START: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR HUBS ---
 if (allHubProductsCache.length === 0) {
     console.log("Hub cache empty in loadAndFilterHubs.");
     if (componentFetchPromises.hubs) {
         // console.log("Waiting for early hub fetch promise to complete...");
         try {
             await componentFetchPromises.hubs; // Wait for the early fetch
             // console.log("Early hub fetch completed. Cache should now be populated.");
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error awaiting early hub fetch in loadAndFilterHubs:", error);
             // The fetchHubProducts call itself handles setting allHubProductsCache to [] on error.
             // So, the check below will handle the error display.
         }
     } else {
         // This case means early fetch was not triggered or it failed and promise was reset.
         // console.log("No early hub fetch promise found or it failed. Fetching Hubs directly now...");
         try {
             // Crucial: Pass buildState.ridingStyle for direct fetches
             await fetchHubProducts(buildState.ridingStyle);
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error fetching hub products directly in loadAndFilterHubs:", error);
             // Error display will be handled by the check below if cache is still empty.
         }
     }
 } else {
     console.log("Using already populated/cached hub data for loadAndFilterHubs.");
 }

 // Check cache status *after* attempting to await promise or fetch directly
 if (allHubProductsCache.length === 0) {
     console.error("Hub cache is STILL empty after attempting to load/wait for fetch. Hub data loading failed.");
     positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
         const loader = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-hub-loading`);
         if(loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
         const errorEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-hub-error`);
         if(errorEl) errorEl.textContent = `Error: Hub data failed to load. Please try refreshing.`;
         const optionsEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-hub-options-container`);
         if(optionsEl) optionsEl.innerHTML = '<p>Hub data failed to load.</p>';
     });
     return; // Stop further processing for hubs if data isn't available
 }
 // --- END: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR HUBS ---
                                         
      for (const position of positionsToLoad) { await loadAndFilterHubsForPosition(position); } console.log("--- loadAndFilterHubs (Combined F/R) finished ---"); }
    
async function loadAndFilterHubsForPosition(position, isChange = false) {
    console.log(`--- loadAndFilterHubsForPosition: ${position} ${isChange ? '(Change Mode)' : ''} ---`);
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const refs = {
        filters: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-filters`),
        loading: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-loading`),
        error: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-error`),
        optionsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-options-container`),
        selectionSpan: document.querySelector(`#${posLower}-hub-selection span`),
        imageContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-image-container`),
        actionButtonsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-action-buttons`)
    };

    if (!refs.optionsContainer || !refs.filters || !refs.loading || !refs.error) {
        console.error(`Hub DOM elements missing for ${position}!`);
        return;
    }

    refs.loading.style.display = 'block';
    refs.error.style.display = 'none';
    const subsectionElement = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-subsection`);
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Hub`;
    const isSelected = buildState.components[stateKey];

// --- Handle Virtual (Integrated) Components ---
    if (isSelected && isSelected.isVirtual) {
        console.log(`Keeping Virtual Hub for ${position}`);
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Hub', isSelected);
        if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        
        // Ensure UI is locked visually
        const container = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-hub-subsection`);
        if (container) {
            container.classList.add('is-locked-integrated');
            container.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
            container.style.opacity = '0.6';
        }
        return; // STOP HERE
    }

    if (isSelected && !isChange) {
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Hub', isSelected);
        refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    
    if (!isSelected) {
        buildState._ui.activeVendor[stateKey] = null;
    }

    refs.imageContainer.innerHTML = '';
    refs.imageContainer.style.display = 'none';
    refs.optionsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Loading hub options...</p>';
    if (isChange) {
        if (refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    } else {
        if (refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
    }
    if (subsectionElement && !isChange) subsectionElement.classList.remove('selection-made');

    try {
        const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
        const hubSpacing = buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];
        const freehubType = (posLower === 'rear') ? buildState.specs.freehubType : null;
        const spokeCount = buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`]; // Get current spoke count

        let missingPrerequisites = [];
        if (!brakeStyle) missingPrerequisites.push("Brake Style");
        if (!hubSpacing) missingPrerequisites.push(`${position} Hub Spacing`);
        if (posLower === 'rear' && !freehubType) missingPrerequisites.push("Freehub Type");
        if (!spokeCount) missingPrerequisites.push(`${position} Spoke Count`); // Add spoke count to prerequisites

        if (missingPrerequisites.length > 0) {
            refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p class="selection-prompt">Please select required Step 2 specs: ${missingPrerequisites.join(', ')}.</p>`;
            refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
            displayComponentVendorFilters(stateKey, [], refs.filters, position);
            return;
        }

        if (allHubProductsCache.length === 0) {
            await fetchHubProducts();
        }

        // Filter 1: STRICTLY filtered list for the vendor dropdown.
        const strictlyCompatibleProducts = allHubProductsCache.filter(product => {
            if (product.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return true;
            if (position === 'Rear' && (!product.availableFreehubs || !product.availableFreehubs.includes(freehubType))) return false;
            return product.variants.some(variant => 
                (variant.spec_position === position || variant.spec_position === "Front/Rear") &&
                (variant.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle) &&
                variant.spec_hub_spacing === hubSpacing &&
                String(variant.spec_spoke_count) === String(spokeCount) && // Strict spoke count check
                variant.availableForSale
            );
        });

        // Filter 2: LOOSELY filtered list for displaying product cards (ignores spoke count).
        const productsForDisplay = allHubProductsCache.filter(product => {
            if (product.vendor === 'Your Own Component') return true;
            if (position === 'Rear' && (!product.availableFreehubs || !product.availableFreehubs.includes(freehubType))) return false;
            return product.variants.some(variant => 
                (variant.spec_position === position || variant.spec_position === "Front/Rear") &&
                (variant.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle) &&
                variant.spec_hub_spacing === hubSpacing &&
                variant.availableForSale
            );
        });

        if (productsForDisplay.length === 0) {
            refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No hubs match all selected specs. Please adjust your selections in Step 2.</p>`;
        }
        
        // Use the STRICT list for the vendor filter
        displayComponentVendorFilters(stateKey, strictlyCompatibleProducts, refs.filters, position);
        
        if (isChange) {
            showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(position, 'Hub', refs.actionButtonsContainer);
        }
        
        // Use the LOOSE list for the card display
        displayHubProductCards(position, productsForDisplay, refs.optionsContainer);

    } catch (error) {
        refs.error.textContent = `Error: ${error.message}.`;
        refs.error.style.display = 'block';
        console.error(`Error in loadAndFilterHubsForPosition(${position}):`, error);
    } finally {
        refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

function displayHubProductCards(position, allCompatibleProducts, optionsContainer, allowedModels = null) {
    if (!optionsContainer) return;
    const componentKeyForState = `${position.toLowerCase()}Hub`;
    const selectedVendor = buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKeyForState];

    if (selectedVendor === null) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
        return;
    }

    optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';

    const productsFilteredByVendor = selectedVendor === 'all' ? allCompatibleProducts : allCompatibleProducts.filter(p => p.vendor === selectedVendor);

    if (productsFilteredByVendor.length === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No hubs from vendor "${selectedVendor}" match your selections.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    const groupedByModel = {};
    productsFilteredByVendor.forEach(p => {
        const modelKey = p.wheelModel || 'Other';
        if (!groupedByModel[modelKey]) groupedByModel[modelKey] = [];
        groupedByModel[modelKey].push(p);
    });

    let displayedModelCount = 0;

    const selectedSpokes = buildState.components[`${position.toLowerCase()}Spokes`];
    let requiredHubTag = null;
    if (selectedSpokes) {
        const spokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === selectedSpokes.productId);
        const spokeInterface = spokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface;
        if (spokeInterface === 'J-Bend') requiredHubTag = 'hub_type:j_bend';
        if (spokeInterface === 'Straight Pull') requiredHubTag = 'hub_type:straight_pull';
    }

    const modelsToSort = allowedModels ? Object.keys(groupedByModel).filter(modelName => allowedModels.includes(modelName)) : Object.keys(groupedByModel);

    const modelsToDisplay = modelsToSort.sort((a, b) => {
        const modelAProducts = groupedByModel[a];
        const modelBProducts = groupedByModel[b];
        const tagsA = modelAProducts[0]?.tags || [];
        const tagsB = modelBProducts[0]?.tags || [];
        if (requiredHubTag) {
            const isACompatible = tagsA.includes(requiredHubTag);
            const isBCompatible = tagsB.includes(requiredHubTag);
            if (isACompatible && !isBCompatible) return -1;
            if (isBCompatible && !isACompatible) return 1;
        }
        return getSortableName(a).localeCompare(getSortableName(b));
    });

    const currentSpokeCount = buildState.specs[`${position.toLowerCase()}SpokeCount`];

    modelsToDisplay.forEach(modelName => {
        const productsInThisModelGroup = groupedByModel[modelName];
        
        const availableSpokeCounts = [...new Set(
            productsInThisModelGroup.flatMap(p => p.variants
                .filter(v => v.availableForSale && (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear"))
                .map(v => v.spec_spoke_count)
            ).filter(Boolean)
        )].sort((a, b) => a - b);
        
        if (availableSpokeCounts.length === 0) return;

        displayedModelCount++;
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'component-product-card hub-model-card';
        card.dataset.modelName = modelName; // Add model name for later reference

        const isCompatibleNow = availableSpokeCounts.includes(String(currentSpokeCount));
        if (!isCompatibleNow) {
            card.classList.add('is-spec-incompatible');
            card.dataset.targetSpec = availableSpokeCounts[0];
            card.title = `Requires ${availableSpokeCounts.join('h or ')}h spoke count. Click to change.`;
        }

        card.innerHTML = `<div class="product-card-header"><h5>${modelName}</h5></div><div class="product-card-body"><p>Click to view options...</p><div class="component-variant-options" style="display:none;"></div></div>`;

        card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.closest('.component-variant-options button')) return;

            const vc = card.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
            if (!vc) return;
            
            const isTrigger = e.target.closest('.product-card-header') || e.target.closest('.product-card-body p');
            if (!isTrigger) return;
            
            const isVisible = vc.style.display !== 'none';
            
            optionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.component-product-card.expanded').forEach(c => {
                if (c !== card) {
                    c.classList.remove('expanded');
                    const otherVc = c.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
                    if (otherVc) otherVc.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            
            vc.style.display = isVisible ? 'none' : 'block';
            card.classList.toggle('expanded', !isVisible);
            
            if (!isVisible) {
                displayHubVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInThisModelGroup, vc);
            }
        });
        optionsContainer.appendChild(card);
    });

    if (displayedModelCount === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No hub models found for the selected vendor and specifications.</p>`;
    }
    updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
}

function displayHubVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, variantContainer) {
    if (!variantContainer) return;
    variantContainer.innerHTML = 'Loading options...';

    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
    const hubSpacing = buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];
    const freehubType = (posLower === 'rear') ? buildState.specs.freehubType : null;
    const spokeCount = buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`];
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Hub`;
    const selectedComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

    let variantsForDisplay = [];
    productsInGroup.forEach(product => {
        const matchingVariants = product.variants.filter(v => {
            const isYOC = product.vendor === 'Your Own Component';
            const positionMatch = v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear";
            const brakeMatch = isYOC ? true : (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle);
            const spacingMatch = isYOC ? true : v.spec_hub_spacing === hubSpacing;
            const spokeMatch = String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(spokeCount);
            const availabilityMatch = isYOC ? true : v.availableForSale;
            return availabilityMatch && positionMatch && brakeMatch && spacingMatch && spokeMatch;
        });
        matchingVariants.forEach(variant => {
            variantsForDisplay.push({ ...variant, productId: product.id, productTitle: product.title, productHandle: product.handle, vendor: product.vendor, pairingKey: product.pairingKey, tags: product.tags || [], optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: product.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [], leadTimeDays: product.leadTimeDays || 0, wheelModel: product.wheelModel || null, availableFreehubs: product.availableFreehubs || [], freehubVariantMap: product.freehubVariantMap || {}, product_weight_g: product.weight_g });
        });
    });

    if (variantsForDisplay.length === 0) {
        variantContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No specific hub options in this model match all your Step 2 selections.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    variantsForDisplay.sort((a, b) => (a.title || '').localeCompare(b.title || ''));
    variantContainer.innerHTML = '';
    
    variantsForDisplay.forEach(v_hub => {
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.className = 'component-variant-button hub-variant-button';
        btn.dataset.variantId = v_hub.id;
        btn.dataset.productId = v_hub.productId;
        btn.type = 'button';
        btn.dataset.vendor = v_hub.vendor || '';

        if (selectedComponent?.variantId === v_hub.id) {
            btn.classList.add('selected');
        }

        // --- UPDATED COMPATIBILITY CHECK AT RENDER TIME ---
        const currentSpokes = buildState.components[`${posLower}Spokes`];
        if (currentSpokes) {
            const spokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === currentSpokes.productId);
            const spokeInterface = spokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface; // "Hook Flange", "J-Bend", etc.
            
            const hubTags = v_hub.tags || [];
            const hubIsJbend = hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend');
            const hubIsStraightPull = hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull');
            const hubIsHookFlange = hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange');

            let isRenderIncompatible = false;

            // 1. Standard Steel Logic
            if (spokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && hubIsStraightPull) isRenderIncompatible = true;
            if (spokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && hubIsJbend) isRenderIncompatible = true;

            // 2. PolyLightX (Hook Flange Spoke) Logic
            // If current spokes are Hook Flange, New Hub MUST be Hook Flange
            if (spokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && !hubIsHookFlange) isRenderIncompatible = true;

            // 3. Hook Flange Hub Logic
            // If New Hub is Hook Flange, Current Spokes cannot be J-Bend or SP
            if (hubIsHookFlange && (spokeInterface === 'J-Bend' || spokeInterface === 'Straight Pull')) isRenderIncompatible = true;

            if (isRenderIncompatible) {
                btn.classList.add('conditionally-incompatible');
                btn.dataset.isConditionallyDisabled = 'true';
                btn.setAttribute('title', `Incompatible with selected ${spokeInterface || 'current'} spokes.`);
            }
        }
        // --- END UPDATED CHECK ---

        const weight = v_hub.weight_g ?? v_hub.product_weight_g ?? null;
        let displayTitle = (v_hub.vendor === 'Your Own Component')
            ? `${v_hub.productTitle} (${v_hub.title})`
            : `${v_hub.productTitle || ''} (${v_hub.title || ''})`;
    
        btn.innerHTML = `
            <div class="variant-button-image-container">
                ${v_hub.image?.url ? `<img src="${v_hub.image.url}" alt="${displayTitle}" loading="lazy" class="variant-button-image">` : '<div class="variant-button-image-placeholder"></div>'}
            </div>
            <div class="variant-button-details">
                <span class="variant-details">${displayTitle}</span>
                ${v_hub.price?.amount ? `<span class="variant-price">${formatPrice(v_hub.price.amount)}</span>` : ''}
            </div>
            <div class="variant-button-stats">
                ${weight ? `<span class="stat-item">Weight: <strong>${weight}g</strong></span>` : ''}
            </div>`;

        btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            if (btn.dataset.isConditionallyDisabled === 'true') {
                const hubTags = v_hub.tags || [];
                let requiredSpokeType = 'Compatible';
                
                // Determine the "type" for the error message
                if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) requiredSpokeType = 'Berd (Hook Flange or Standard)';
                else if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) requiredSpokeType = 'J-Bend';
                else if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) requiredSpokeType = 'Straight Pull';

                const confirmed = confirm(`Selecting this hub requires ${requiredSpokeType} spokes and will clear your current spoke selection for this wheel. Continue?`);
                
                if (confirmed) {
                    clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'Spokes');
                    
                    // Wheelset Logic: Check if opposite wheel also needs clearing
                    if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
                        const oppositePosition = position === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
                        const oppositeSpokes = buildState.components[`${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}Spokes`];
                        if (oppositeSpokes) {
                            const oppositeSpokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === oppositeSpokes.productId);
                            const oppInterface = oppositeSpokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface;
                            
                            let oppIncompatible = false;
                            // Check Hook Flange logic on opposite side
                            if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') && (oppInterface === 'J-Bend' || oppInterface === 'Straight Pull')) oppIncompatible = true;
                            else if (!hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') && oppInterface === 'Hook Flange') oppIncompatible = true;
                            // Check J-Bend/SP logic on opposite side
                            else if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend') && oppInterface === 'Straight Pull') oppIncompatible = true;
                            else if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull') && oppInterface === 'J-Bend') oppIncompatible = true;

                            if (oppIncompatible) {
                                console.log(`Also clearing incompatible ${oppositePosition} spokes.`);
                                clearComponentAndItsAddons(oppositePosition, 'Spokes');
                            }
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    return;
                }
            }
            
            const previouslySelectedComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];
            const newSelectedVariantId = v_hub.id;
            if (previouslySelectedComponent && previouslySelectedComponent.productId !== v_hub.productId) {
                const addonKeysToRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons).filter(key => key.startsWith(`${position}_Hub_${previouslySelectedComponent.variantId}`));
                addonKeysToRemove.forEach(key => { delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key]; });
                if (addonKeysToRemove.length > 0) saveLastActiveBuild();
            } else if (previouslySelectedComponent && previouslySelectedComponent.variantId !== newSelectedVariantId) {
                manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(position, 'Hub', previouslySelectedComponent.variantId, newSelectedVariantId, v_hub.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || []);
            }
            if (position === 'Rear' && componentFetchPromises.freehubs) await componentFetchPromises.freehubs;
            const selectedHubComponent = {
                variantId: v_hub.id, productId: v_hub.productId, productHandle: v_hub.productHandle,
                title: v_hub.productTitle, variantTitle: v_hub.title, sku: v_hub.sku,
                price: v_hub.price.amount, vendor: v_hub.vendor, image: v_hub.image,
                pairingKey: v_hub.pairingKey, tags: v_hub.tags, spec_spoke_count: String(v_hub.spec_spoke_count),
                spec_brake_interface: v_hub.spec_brake_interface, spec_hub_spacing: v_hub.spec_hub_spacing,
                spec_freehub: (posLower === 'rear') ? freehubType : null, selectedOptions: v_hub.selectedOptions,
                optionalAddonProductGids: v_hub.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct, leadTimeDays: v_hub.leadTimeDays, wheelModel: v_hub.wheelModel,
                quantityAvailable: v_hub.quantityAvailable,
                leadTimeDays: v_hub.leadTimeDays,
                weight_g: v_hub.weight_g ?? v_hub.product_weight_g ?? null
            };
            buildState.components[stateKey] = selectedHubComponent;
            if (position === 'Rear') setComponentFreehubForHub(v_hub);
            buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
            updateStep3ButtonText();
            calculateWheelCosts(position);
            updateComponentUI(position, 'Hub', selectedHubComponent);
            loadAndFilterSpokesForPosition(position, false);
            updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
            saveLastActiveBuild();
            if (buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === position) cancelComponentChange();
            handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();
            await handleAutoPairing('Hub', position, selectedHubComponent, false);
            scrollToComponentSection(position, 'Hub');
        });
        
        variantContainer.appendChild(btn);
    });
}
  
function setComponentFreehubForHub(selectedHubData) {
    // This function only applies to rear hubs that have a freehub type selected in Step 2.
    if (!selectedHubData || buildState.specs.freehubType === null) {
        buildState.components.rearComponentFreehub = null;
        return;
    }

    const freehubGid = selectedHubData.freehubVariantMap[buildState.specs.freehubType];

    if (freehubGid) {
        for (const freehubProduct of allFreehubComponentProductsCache) {
            const foundVariant = freehubProduct.variants.find(v => v.id === freehubGid);
            if (foundVariant) {
                buildState.components.rearComponentFreehub = {
                    variantId: foundVariant.id,
                    productId: freehubProduct.id,
                    title: freehubProduct.title,
                    variantTitle: foundVariant.title,
                    price: foundVariant.price.amount,
                    name: `${freehubProduct.title} - ${foundVariant.title}`,
                    weight_g: foundVariant.weight_g || freehubProduct.weight_g || null
                };
                return; // Exit after finding the match
            }
        }
    }
    
    console.error(`[V3 Set Freehub] FAILURE: Could not find Component Freehub Variant for GID: ${freehubGid}.`);
    buildState.components.rearComponentFreehub = null;
}

    async function fetchSpokeProducts() { console.log("Fetching spoke products using tag: component:spoke"); const spokeTag = "component:spoke"; try { allSpokeProductsCache = await fetchBuilderComponentProducts(spokeTag); updateGlobalVendorLogoMap(allSpokeProductsCache); console.log(`fetchSpokeProducts: Found and cached ${allSpokeProductsCache.length} products.`); } catch (error) { console.error("fetchSpokeProducts Error:", error); allSpokeProductsCache = []; throw error; } return allSpokeProductsCache; }
    async function loadAndFilterSpokes() { console.log("--- loadAndFilterSpokes (Combined F/R) ---"); const buildType = buildState.buildType; const positionsToLoad = []; if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Front'); if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Rear'); if (positionsToLoad.length === 0) return; positionsToLoad.forEach(p => { const l = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-spokes-loading`); if (l) l.style.display = 'block'; const o = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-spokes-options-container`); if (o) o.innerHTML = '<p>Loading spoke options...</p>'; const e = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-spokes-error`); if (e) e.style.display = 'none'; }); 
         
                                           // --- START: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR SPOKES ---
 if (allSpokeProductsCache.length === 0) {
     // console.log("Spoke cache empty in loadAndFilterSpokes.");
     if (componentFetchPromises.spokes) {
         // console.log("Waiting for early spoke fetch promise to complete...");
         try {
             await componentFetchPromises.spokes;
             // console.log("Early spoke fetch completed.");
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error awaiting early spoke fetch in loadAndFilterSpokes:", error);
         }
     } else {
         // console.log("No early spoke fetch promise. Fetching Spokes directly now...");
         try {
             await fetchSpokeProducts();
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error fetching spoke products directly in loadAndFilterSpokes:", error);
         }
     }
 } else {
     // console.log("Using already populated/cached spoke data for loadAndFilterSpokes.");
 }

 if (allSpokeProductsCache.length === 0) {
     console.error("Spoke cache is STILL empty. Spoke data loading failed.");
     positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
         const loader = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-spokes-loading`);
         if(loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
         const errorEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-spokes-error`);
         if(errorEl) errorEl.textContent = `Error: Spoke data failed to load.`;
         const optionsEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-spokes-options-container`);
         if(optionsEl) optionsEl.innerHTML = '<p>Spoke data failed to load.</p>';
     });
     return;
 }
 // --- END: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR SPOKES ---

        for (const position of positionsToLoad) { await loadAndFilterSpokesForPosition(position); } positionsToLoad.forEach(p => { const l = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-spokes-loading`); if (l) l.style.display = 'none'; }); console.log("--- loadAndFilterSpokes (Combined F/R) finished ---"); }

async function loadAndFilterSpokesForPosition(position, isChange = false) {
    console.log(`--- loadAndFilterSpokesForPosition: ${position} ${isChange ? '(Change Mode)' : ''} ---`);
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const refs = {
        filters: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-filters`),
        loading: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-loading`),
        error: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-error`),
        optionsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-options-container`),
        selectionSpan: document.querySelector(`#${posLower}-spokes-selection span`),
        imageContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-image-container`),
        actionButtonsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-action-buttons`)
    };
    if (!refs.optionsContainer || !refs.filters || !refs.error || !refs.imageContainer || !refs.selectionSpan || !refs.actionButtonsContainer) {
        console.error(`Spoke DOM elements missing for ${position}! Check IDs:`, refs);
        if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    refs.error.style.display = 'none';
    refs.error.textContent = '';
    const subsectionElement = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-subsection`);
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Spokes`;
    const isSelected = buildState.components[stateKey];

    // --- Handle Virtual (Integrated) Components ---
    if (isSelected && isSelected.isVirtual) {
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Spokes', isSelected);
        if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        
        const container = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-spokes-subsection`);
        if (container) {
            container.classList.add('is-locked-integrated');
            container.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
            container.style.opacity = '0.6';
        }
        return;
    }

    if (isSelected && !isChange) {
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Spokes', isSelected);
        return;
    }
    
    if (!isSelected) {
        buildState._ui.activeVendor[stateKey] = null;
    }

    refs.imageContainer.innerHTML = '';
    refs.imageContainer.style.display = 'none';
    refs.optionsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
    if (isChange && refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    else if (refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
    if (subsectionElement && !isChange) {
        subsectionElement.classList.remove('selection-made');
    }

    // This section is reverted. We NO LONGER check for a hub.
    // We simply ensure the spoke cache is loaded.
    if (allSpokeProductsCache.length === 0) {
        try {
            await fetchSpokeProducts();
            if (allSpokeProductsCache.length === 0) throw new Error("Spoke data is empty after fetch.");
        } catch (error) {
            refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Error loading Spoke data.</p>';
            if (refs.error) { refs.error.textContent = `Error: ${error.message}`; refs.error.style.display = 'block'; }
            return;
        }
    }
    
    // This is the key change: We show ALL spokes and let the compatibility UI handle graying out.
    const productsToDisplay = allSpokeProductsCache;

    if (productsToDisplay.length === 0) {
        refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>No spoke products found.</p>';
    }
    
    displayComponentVendorFilters(stateKey, productsToDisplay, refs.filters, position);
    if (isChange) {
        showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(position, 'Spokes', refs.actionButtonsContainer);
    }
    displaySpokeProductCards(position, productsToDisplay, refs.optionsContainer);
    
    console.log(`--- loadAndFilterSpokesForPosition: ${position} finished ---`);
}
    
function displaySpokeProductCards(position, allCompatibleSpokes, optionsContainer) {
    if (!optionsContainer) return;
    const componentKeyForState = `${position.toLowerCase()}Spokes`;
    const selectedVendor = buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKeyForState];

    if (selectedVendor === null) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
        return;
    }

    optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
    
    const filteredProducts = selectedVendor === 'all' ? allCompatibleSpokes : allCompatibleSpokes.filter(p => p.vendor === selectedVendor);
    if (filteredProducts.length === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${position.toLowerCase()} spokes found${selectedVendor !== 'all' ? ` for vendor: ${selectedVendor}` : ''}.</p>`;
        updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
        return;
    }

    const groupedByModel = {};
    filteredProducts.forEach(p => {
        const model = p.wheelModel || 'Other';
        if (!groupedByModel[model]) groupedByModel[model] = [];
        groupedByModel[model].push(p);
    });
    
    // --- NEW SORTING LOGIC ---
    const selectedHub = buildState.components[`${position.toLowerCase()}Hub`];
    const hubTags = selectedHub?.tags || [];
    let requiredInterface = null;
    if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) requiredInterface = 'J-Bend';
    if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) requiredInterface = 'Straight Pull';

    const sortedModelNames = Object.keys(groupedByModel).sort((a, b) => {
        const modelAProducts = groupedByModel[a];
        const modelBProducts = groupedByModel[b];
        const interfaceA = modelAProducts[0]?.spokeHubInterface;
        const interfaceB = modelBProducts[0]?.spokeHubInterface;
        const vendorA = modelAProducts[0]?.vendor;
        const vendorB = modelBProducts[0]?.vendor;

        // Prioritize Berd spokes to always be at the top
        if (vendorA === 'Berd' && vendorB !== 'Berd') return -1;
        if (vendorB === 'Berd' && vendorA !== 'Berd') return 1;

        // If a required interface is set, compatible models come first
        if (requiredInterface) {
            const isACompatible = (interfaceA === requiredInterface);
            const isBCompatible = (interfaceB === requiredInterface);
            if (isACompatible && !isBCompatible) return -1;
            if (isBCompatible && !isACompatible) return 1;
        }

        // Fallback to alphabetical sorting
        return getSortableName(a).localeCompare(getSortableName(b));
    });
    // --- END NEW SORTING LOGIC ---

    let displayedModelCount = 0;
    sortedModelNames.forEach(model => { // Use the new sorted array
        const productsInGroup = groupedByModel[model];
        if (!productsInGroup.some(p => p.variants.some(v => v.availableForSale))) {
            return;
        }
        displayedModelCount++;
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'component-product-card spoke-model-card';

        const firstProductInGroup = productsInGroup[0];
        if (firstProductInGroup) {
            card.dataset.vendor = firstProductInGroup.vendor || '';
            card.dataset.spokeHubInterface = firstProductInGroup.spokeHubInterface || '';
        }
        card.dataset.position = position;

        card.innerHTML = `<div class="product-card-header"><h5>${model}</h5></div><div class="product-card-body"><p>Click to view options...</p><div class="component-variant-options" style="display:none;"></div></div>`;

        card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.closest('.component-variant-options button')) return;
            const vc = card.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
            if (!vc) return;
            const isTrigger = e.target.closest('.product-card-header') || e.target.closest('.product-card-body p');
            if (!isTrigger) return;
            const isVisible = vc.style.display !== 'none';
            optionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.component-product-card.expanded').forEach(c => {
                if (c !== card) {
                    c.classList.remove('expanded');
                    const otherVc = c.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
                    if (otherVc) otherVc.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            vc.style.display = isVisible ? 'none' : 'block';
            card.classList.toggle('expanded', !isVisible);
            if (!isVisible) {
                displaySpokeVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, vc);
            }
        });
        optionsContainer.appendChild(card);
    });

    if (displayedModelCount === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${position.toLowerCase()} spoke models found${selectedVendor !== 'all' ? ` for vendor ${selectedVendor}` : ''} with available options.</p>`;
    }
    updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
}

function displaySpokeVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, variantContainer) {
    if (!variantContainer) return;
    variantContainer.innerHTML = ''; // Clear any previous content

    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Spokes`;
    const selectedComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

    // 1. Find all "Builder Selection" variants from the product group.
    // This is the core of our new logic.
    const pricedBuilderVariants = [];
    productsInGroup.forEach(product => {
        product.variants.forEach(variant => {
            // Find the special variant where the Length option value is '-'
            const isBuilderVariant = variant.selectedOptions.some(opt => opt.name === 'Length' && opt.value === '-');
            
            if (isBuilderVariant && variant.availableForSale) {
                // Attach the parent product's info to the variant for easy access later
                pricedBuilderVariants.push({
                    ...variant, // Spread all variant properties
                    // Explicitly add parent product properties
                    productId: product.id,
                    productTitle: product.title,
                    productHandle: product.handle,
                    vendor: product.vendor,
                    pairingKey: product.pairingKey,
                    wheelModel: product.wheelModel,
                    leadTimeDays: product.leadTimeDays || 0,
                    optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: product.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [],
                    product_weight_g: product.weight_g
                });
            }
        });
    });

    if (pricedBuilderVariants.length === 0) {
        variantContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No purchaseable options found for this model. Please check product setup.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    // Sort the priced variants by their own title (which is usually the color)
    pricedBuilderVariants.sort((a, b) => (a.title || '').localeCompare(b.title || ''));

    // 2. Create a button for each "Builder Selection" variant
    pricedBuilderVariants.forEach(v_spoke => {
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.className = 'component-variant-button spoke-variant-button';
        btn.dataset.variantId = v_spoke.id;
        btn.dataset.productId = v_spoke.productId;
        btn.type = 'button';
        btn.dataset.vendor = v_spoke.vendor || '';
        btn.dataset.position = position;
        const spokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === v_spoke.productId);
        const thisSpokeInterface = spokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface || ''; // Store for logic
        btn.dataset.spokeHubInterface = thisSpokeInterface;

        if (selectedComponent?.variantId === v_spoke.id) {
            btn.classList.add('selected');
        }

        // --- UPDATED COMPATIBILITY CHECK AT RENDER TIME ---
        const currentHub = buildState.components[`${posLower}Hub`];
        if (currentHub) {
            const hubTags = currentHub.tags || [];
            let isRenderIncompatible = false;

            // 1. Standard Steel Logic
            if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend') && thisSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull') isRenderIncompatible = true;
            if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull') && thisSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend') isRenderIncompatible = true;

            // 2. Hook Flange Hub Logic
            // If Hub is Hook Flange, Spoke CANNOT be J-Bend or Straight Pull
            if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) {
                if (thisSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' || thisSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull') isRenderIncompatible = true;
            }

            // 3. PolyLightX (Hook Flange Spoke) Logic
            // If Spoke is Hook Flange, Hub MUST be Hook Flange
            if (thisSpokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && !hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) isRenderIncompatible = true;

            if (isRenderIncompatible) {
                btn.classList.add('conditionally-incompatible');
                btn.dataset.isConditionallyDisabled = 'true';
                btn.setAttribute('title', `Incompatible with selected Hub.`);
            }
        }
        // --- END UPDATED CHECK ---

        const weight = v_spoke.weight_g ?? v_spoke.product_weight_g ?? null;
        const colorOption = v_spoke.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name === 'Color');
        const displayTitleText = `${v_spoke.productTitle} (${colorOption ? colorOption.value : v_spoke.title})`;
        const priceAmount = v_spoke.price?.amount;

        btn.innerHTML = `
            <div class="variant-button-image-container">
                ${v_spoke.image?.url ? `<img src="${v_spoke.image.url}" alt="${displayTitleText}" loading="lazy" class="variant-button-image">` : '<div class="variant-button-image-placeholder"></div>'}
            </div>
            <div class="variant-button-details">
                <span class="variant-details">${displayTitleText}</span>
                ${priceAmount ? `<span class="variant-price">${formatPrice(priceAmount)}</span>` : ''}
            </div>
            <div class="variant-button-stats">
                ${weight ? `<span class="stat-item">Weight: <strong>${weight}g</strong></span>` : ''}
            </div>`;

        // 3. Attach the full, preserved event listener logic.
        btn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            // --- UPDATED BI-DIRECTIONAL ALERT FOR HOOK FLANGE ---
            if (btn.dataset.isConditionallyDisabled === 'true') {
                const hub = buildState.components[`${posLower}Hub`];
                let hubType = "selected";
                if (hub) {
                   if (hub.tags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) hubType = 'J-Bend';
                   else if (hub.tags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) hubType = 'Straight Pull';
                   else if (hub.tags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) hubType = 'Hook Flange';
                }

                const selectedSpokeInterface = btn.dataset.spokeHubInterface; // "Hook Flange", "J-Bend", etc.
                let errorMsg = `These spokes are not compatible with the selected ${hubType} hub.`;
                
                if (selectedSpokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && hubType !== 'Hook Flange') {
                    errorMsg = `PolyLightX (Hook Flange) spokes can ONLY be used with Hook Flange hubs.`;
                }

                const confirmed = confirm(`${errorMsg} Clicking OK will clear your hub selection for this wheel. Continue?`);
                
                if (confirmed) {
                    // Clear the hub for the current position first.
                    clearComponentAndItsAddons(position, 'Hub');

                    // If it's a wheelset, check and clear the opposite hub if it's also incompatible.
                    if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
                        const oppositePosition = position === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
                        const oppositeHub = buildState.components[`${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}Hub`];

                        // Check if the opposite hub is incompatible with the spokes being selected.
                        if (oppositeHub) {
                            const oppositeHubTags = oppositeHub.tags || [];
                            let isOppositeIncompatible = false;

                            // Rule: Hook Flange spokes require Hook Flange hubs
                            if (selectedSpokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && !oppositeHubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) {
                                isOppositeIncompatible = true;
                            }
                            // Rule: J-Bend/SP logic
                            else if (selectedSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && oppositeHubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) isOppositeIncompatible = true;
                            else if (selectedSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && oppositeHubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) isOppositeIncompatible = true;

                            if (isOppositeIncompatible) {
                                 console.log(`Also clearing incompatible ${oppositePosition} hub.`);
                                 clearComponentAndItsAddons(oppositePosition, 'Hub');
                            }
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    return; // Abort if user cancels
                }
            }
            // This is the combined logic from your original function.
            const previouslySelectedSpokeComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];
            const newSelectedSpokeVariantId = v_spoke.id;

            // Handle "sticky" addons if the user is changing their selection.
            if (previouslySelectedSpokeComponent && previouslySelectedSpokeComponent.variantId !== newSelectedSpokeVariantId) {
                if (previouslySelectedSpokeComponent.productId === v_spoke.productId) {
                    manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(
                        position, 'Spokes', previouslySelectedSpokeComponent.variantId,
                        newSelectedSpokeVariantId, v_spoke.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct
                    );
                } else {
                    // If the product itself is changing, clear the old addons.
                    const addonKeysToRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons).filter(key => 
                        key.startsWith(`${position}_Spokes_${previouslySelectedSpokeComponent.variantId}`)
                    );
                    addonKeysToRemove.forEach(key => delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key]);
                }
            }

            // Create the component object to save in the build state.
            const selectedSpokeComponent = {
                variantId: v_spoke.id,
                productId: v_spoke.productId,
                productHandle: v_spoke.productHandle,
                title: v_spoke.productTitle,
                variantTitle: v_spoke.title, // Will be "Black / -"
                sku: v_spoke.sku,
                price: v_spoke.price.amount,
                vendor: v_spoke.vendor,
                image: v_spoke.image,
                pairingKey: v_spoke.pairingKey,
                selectedOptions: v_spoke.selectedOptions,
                optionalAddonProductGids: v_spoke.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct,
                quantityAvailable: v_spoke.quantityAvailable,
                leadTimeDays: v_spoke.leadTimeDays,
                wheelModel: v_spoke.wheelModel,
                // Add the clean color for easy access by other functions.
                selectedColor: colorOption ? colorOption.value : null,
                weight_g: v_spoke.weight_g ?? v_spoke.product_weight_g ?? null
            };

            buildState.components[stateKey] = selectedSpokeComponent;

            // Trigger all the necessary downstream updates.
            buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
            updateStep3ButtonText();
            calculateWheelCosts(position);
            updateComponentUI(position, 'Spokes', selectedSpokeComponent);
            updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
            
            // Trigger auto-pairing for the opposite wheel.
            await handleAutoPairing('Spokes', position, selectedSpokeComponent, false);

            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
            saveLastActiveBuild();

            if (buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === position) {
                cancelComponentChange();
            }
            handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();
            scrollToComponentSection(position, 'Spokes');
        });

        variantContainer.appendChild(btn);
    });
    
    // Final UI check after rendering all buttons.
    updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
}
  
    async function fetchNippleProducts() {
    console.log("Fetching nipple products using tag: component:nipple");
    const nippleTag = "component:nipple";
    try {
        allNippleProductsCache = await fetchBuilderComponentProducts(nippleTag);
        updateGlobalVendorLogoMap(allNippleProductsCache);
        console.log(`fetchNippleProducts: Found and cached ${allNippleProductsCache.length} products.`);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("fetchNippleProducts Error:", error);
        allNippleProductsCache = [];
        throw error;
    }
    return allNippleProductsCache;
}
    async function loadAndFilterNipples() {
    console.log("--- loadAndFilterNipples (Combined F/R) ---");
    const buildType = buildState.buildType;
    const positionsToLoad = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Rear');
    if (positionsToLoad.length === 0) return;

    positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
        const l = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-nipples-loading`);
        if (l) l.style.display = 'block';
        const o = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-nipples-options-container`);
        if (o) o.innerHTML = '<p>Loading nipple options...</p>';
        const e = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-nipples-error`);
        if (e) e.style.display = 'none';
    });

    // --- START: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR NIPPLES ---
 if (allNippleProductsCache.length === 0) {
     console.log("Nipple cache empty in loadAndFilterNipples.");
     if (componentFetchPromises.nipples) {
         console.log("Waiting for early nipple fetch promise to complete...");
         try {
             await componentFetchPromises.nipples;
             console.log("Early nipple fetch completed.");
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error awaiting early nipple fetch in loadAndFilterNipples:", error);
         }
     } else {
         console.log("No early nipple fetch promise. Fetching Nipples directly now...");
         try {
             await fetchNippleProducts();
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error fetching nipple products directly in loadAndFilterNipples:", error);
         }
     }
 } else {
     console.log("Using already populated/cached nipple data for loadAndFilterNipples.");
 }

 if (allNippleProductsCache.length === 0) {
     console.error("Nipple cache is STILL empty. Nipple data loading failed.");
     positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
         const loader = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-nipples-loading`);
         if(loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
         const errorEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-nipples-error`);
         if(errorEl) errorEl.textContent = `Error: Nipple data failed to load.`;
         const optionsEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-nipples-options-container`);
         if(optionsEl) optionsEl.innerHTML = '<p>Nipple data failed to load.</p>';
     });
     return;
 }
 // --- END: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR NIPPLES ---

    for (const position of positionsToLoad) {
        await loadAndFilterNipplesForPosition(position);
    }

    positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
        const l = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-nipples-loading`);
        if (l) l.style.display = 'none';
    });
    console.log("--- loadAndFilterNipples (Combined F/R) finished ---");
}
    async function loadAndFilterNipplesForPosition(position, isChange = false) {
    console.log(`--- loadAndFilterNipplesForPosition: ${position} ${isChange ? '(Change Mode)' : ''} ---`);
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const refs = {
        filters: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-filters`),
        loading: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-loading`),
        error: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-error`),
        optionsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-options-container`),
        selectionSpan: document.querySelector(`#${posLower}-nipples-selection span`),
        imageContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-image-container`),
        actionButtonsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-action-buttons`)
    };

    if (!refs.optionsContainer || !refs.filters || !refs.error || !refs.imageContainer || !refs.selectionSpan || !refs.actionButtonsContainer) {
        console.error(`Nipple DOM elements missing for ${position}! Check IDs:`, refs);
        if(refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }

    refs.error.style.display = 'none';
    refs.error.textContent = '';

    const subsectionElement = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-subsection`);
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Nipples`;
    const isSelected = buildState.components[stateKey];

    // --- Handle Virtual (Integrated) Components ---
    if (isSelected && isSelected.isVirtual) {
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Nipples', isSelected);
        if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        
        const container = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-nipples-subsection`);
        if (container) {
            container.classList.add('is-locked-integrated');
            container.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
            container.style.opacity = '0.6';
        }
        return;
    }

    if (isSelected && !isChange) {
        updateComponentUI(position, 'Nipples', isSelected);
        return;
    }

    refs.imageContainer.innerHTML = '';
    refs.imageContainer.style.display = 'none';
    refs.optionsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
    if (isChange && refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
    else if (refs.actionButtonsContainer) refs.actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';

    if (subsectionElement && !isChange) {
        subsectionElement.classList.remove('selection-made');
    }

    if (allNippleProductsCache.length === 0) {
        console.warn(`Nipple cache empty in loadAndFilterNipplesForPosition for ${position}. Parent should have fetched.`);
        refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Nipple data not available. Please try reloading or check console.</p>';
        return;
    }

    const compatibleProducts = allNippleProductsCache;

    if (compatibleProducts.length === 0) {
        refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>No nipple products found.</p>';
        if (refs.selectionSpan) refs.selectionSpan.innerHTML = `Selected ${position} Nipples: None`;
        if (subsectionElement) subsectionElement.classList.remove('selection-made');
    } else {
        if (!isChange) {
            displayComponentVendorFilters(stateKey, compatibleProducts, refs.filters, position);
        } else {
            showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(position, 'Nipples', refs.actionButtonsContainer);
        }
        displayNippleProductCards(position, compatibleProducts, refs.optionsContainer);
    }
    console.log(`--- loadAndFilterNipplesForPosition: ${position} finished ---`);
}
   
function displayNippleProductCards(position, allCompatibleNipples, optionsContainer) {
    if (!optionsContainer) return;
    const componentKeyForState = `${position.toLowerCase()}Nipples`;
    const selectedVendor = buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKeyForState];

    // If no vendor is selected, show nothing.
    if (selectedVendor === null) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        return;
    }

    optionsContainer.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous content

    const filteredProducts = selectedVendor === 'all' ? allCompatibleNipples : allCompatibleNipples.filter(p => p.vendor === selectedVendor);

    if (filteredProducts.length === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${position.toLowerCase()} nipples found${selectedVendor !== 'all' ? ` for vendor: ${selectedVendor}` : ''}.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    const groupedByModel = {};
    filteredProducts.forEach(p => {
        const model = p.wheelModel || 'Other';
        if (!groupedByModel[model]) groupedByModel[model] = [];
        groupedByModel[model].push(p);
    });

    let displayedModelCount = 0;
    Object.keys(groupedByModel).sort((a, b) => getSortableName(a).localeCompare(getSortableName(b))).forEach(model => {
        const productsInGroup = groupedByModel[model];
        if (!productsInGroup.some(p => p.variants.some(v => v.availableForSale))) {
            return;
        }
        displayedModelCount++;
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'component-product-card nipple-model-card';
        card.innerHTML = `
            <div class="product-card-header"><h5>${model}</h5></div>
            <div class="product-card-body">
                <p>Click to view options...</p>
                <div class="component-variant-options" style="display:none;"></div>
            </div>`;
        card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.closest('.component-variant-options button')) return;
            const vc = card.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
            if (!vc) return;
            const isTrigger = e.target.closest('.product-card-header') || e.target.closest('.product-card-body p');
            if (!isTrigger) return;

            const isVisible = vc.style.display !== 'none';
            optionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.component-product-card.expanded').forEach(c => {
                if (c !== card) {
                    c.classList.remove('expanded');
                    const otherVc = c.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
                    if (otherVc) otherVc.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            vc.style.display = isVisible ? 'none' : 'block';
            card.classList.toggle('expanded', !isVisible);
            if (!isVisible) {
                displayNippleVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, vc);
            }
        });
        optionsContainer.appendChild(card);
    });

    if (displayedModelCount === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${position.toLowerCase()} nipple models found${selectedVendor !== 'all' ? ` for vendor ${selectedVendor}` : ''} with available options.</p>`;
    }
}
  
// --- START: displayNippleVariantButtonsByProduct (with lead time data) ---
function displayNippleVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, variantContainer) {
    if (!variantContainer) return;
    variantContainer.innerHTML = 'Loading options...';

    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Nipples`;
    const selectedComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

    let compatibleVariants = [];
    productsInGroup.forEach(p => {
        let p_optionalAddonProductGids = [];
        const rawGidValue = p.optionalAddonProductGids?.value;
        if (Array.isArray(rawGidValue)) {
            p_optionalAddonProductGids = rawGidValue.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
        } else if (typeof rawGidValue === 'string') {
            try {
                const parsedGids = JSON.parse(rawGidValue);
                if (Array.isArray(parsedGids)) {
                    p_optionalAddonProductGids = parsedGids.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                }
            } catch (e) {
                 if (rawGidValue.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/')) {
                       p_optionalAddonProductGids = [rawGidValue.trim()];
                 } else {
                    p_optionalAddonProductGids = rawGidValue.split(',')
                                       .map(gid => gid.trim())
                                       .filter(gid => gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                 }
            }
        }

        const productDetails = {
            productId: p.id,
            productTitle: p.title,
            productHandle: p.handle,
            vendor: p.vendor,
            pairingKey: p.pairingKey,
            optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: p_optionalAddonProductGids,
            leadTimeDays: p.leadTimeDays || 0 // <<< ADD THIS
        };
        p.variants.forEach(v => {
            if (v.availableForSale) {
                compatibleVariants.push({ ...v, ...productDetails, product_weight_g: p.weight_g, price: v.price, product_weight_g: p.weight_g });
            }
        });
    });

    if (compatibleVariants.length === 0) {
        variantContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No available nipple options in this group.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    const uniqueVariantsMap = new Map();
    compatibleVariants.forEach(v => {
        if (!uniqueVariantsMap.has(v.id)) uniqueVariantsMap.set(v.id, v);
    });
    let uniqueVariants = Array.from(uniqueVariantsMap.values()).sort((a, b) => (a.title || '').localeCompare(b.title || ''));

    variantContainer.innerHTML = '';
    uniqueVariants.forEach(v_nipple => {
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.className = 'component-variant-button nipple-variant-button';
        btn.dataset.variantId = v_nipple.id;
        btn.dataset.productId = v_nipple.productId;
        btn.type = 'button';
        if (selectedComponent?.variantId === v_nipple.id) btn.classList.add('selected');

        const imageUrl = v_nipple.image?.url;
        const displayTitleText = `${v_nipple.productTitle || 'Nipple'} (${v_nipple.title || 'Default'})`;
        const priceAmount = v_nipple.price?.amount;

        btn.innerHTML = `
            ${imageUrl ? `<img src="${imageUrl}" alt="${displayTitleText}" loading="lazy" class="variant-button-image">` : '<div class="variant-button-image-placeholder"></div>'}
            <div class="variant-button-details">
                <span class="variant-details">${displayTitleText}</span>
                ${priceAmount ? `<span class="variant-price">${formatPrice(priceAmount)}</span>` : ''}
            </div>`;

        btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const newSelectedNippleVariantId = v_nipple.id;
            const newNippleProductOptionalAddonGids = v_nipple.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [];

            const previouslySelectedNippleComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

            if (previouslySelectedNippleComponent && previouslySelectedNippleComponent.variantId !== newSelectedNippleVariantId) {
                if (previouslySelectedNippleComponent.productId === v_nipple.productId) {
                    manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(
                        position,
                        'Nipples',
                        previouslySelectedNippleComponent.variantId, 
                        newSelectedNippleVariantId,                 
                        newNippleProductOptionalAddonGids
                    );
                } else {
                    const addonKeysToPotentiallyRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons);
                    for (const addonKey of addonKeysToPotentiallyRemove) {
                        const selectedAddon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKey];
                        if (selectedAddon.baseComponentPosition === position &&
                            selectedAddon.baseComponentType === 'Nipples' &&
                            selectedAddon.baseComponentVariantId === previouslySelectedNippleComponent.variantId) {
                            delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKey];
                            saveLastActiveBuild();
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            
            const selectedNippleComponent = {
                variantId: v_nipple.id,
                productId: v_nipple.productId,
                productHandle: v_nipple.productHandle,
                title: v_nipple.productTitle,
                variantTitle: v_nipple.title,
                sku: v_nipple.sku,
                price: v_nipple.price.amount,
                vendor: v_nipple.vendor,
                image: v_nipple.image,
                pairingKey: v_nipple.pairingKey,
                selectedOptions: v_nipple.selectedOptions,
                optionalAddonProductGids: newNippleProductOptionalAddonGids,
                quantityAvailable: v_nipple.quantityAvailable,
                leadTimeDays: v_nipple.leadTimeDays,
                weight_g: v_nipple.weight_g ?? v_nipple.product_weight_g ?? null
            };

            buildState.components[stateKey] = selectedNippleComponent;
            buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
            updateStep3ButtonText();
            calculateWheelCosts(position);
            updateComponentUI(position, 'Nipples', selectedNippleComponent);

            if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
                const oppositePosition = position === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
                const oppositeStateKey = `${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}Nipples`;

                if (!buildState.components[oppositeStateKey] && selectedNippleComponent.pairingKey) {
                    const selectedColorOption = selectedNippleComponent.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color');
                    const targetColor = selectedColorOption ? selectedColorOption.value : null;

                    const pairedProducts = allNippleProductsCache.filter(p => p.pairingKey === selectedNippleComponent.pairingKey);
                    let autoSelectedPairedVariant = null;
                    let firstTechnicallyCompatibleVariant = null;
                    
                    for (const p_pair of pairedProducts) {
                        if (!p_pair || !p_pair.variants) continue;
                        let p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids = [];
                        const rawGidValuePair = p_pair.optionalAddonProductGids?.value;
                        if (Array.isArray(rawGidValuePair)) {
                            p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids = rawGidValuePair.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                        } else if (typeof rawGidValuePair === 'string') {
                             try {
                                const parsedGids = JSON.parse(rawGidValuePair);
                                if (Array.isArray(parsedGids)) p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids = parsedGids.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                            } catch (e) { /* Fallback if needed */ }
                        }

                        for (const v_pair of p_pair.variants) {
                            if (!v_pair || !v_pair.price || typeof v_pair.price.amount === 'undefined' || !v_pair.availableForSale) continue;
                            const isTechnicallyCompatible = true; 
                            if (isTechnicallyCompatible) {
                                const currentPairedVariantCandidate = { 
                                    ...v_pair, productTitle: p_pair.title, productHandle: p_pair.handle, vendor: p_pair.vendor, 
                                    productId: p_pair.id, pairingKey: p_pair.pairingKey,
                                    optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids,
                                    leadTimeDays: p_pair.leadTimeDays || 0,
                                    product_weight_g: p_pair.weight_g
                                };
                                if (!firstTechnicallyCompatibleVariant) {
                                    firstTechnicallyCompatibleVariant = currentPairedVariantCandidate;
                                }
                                const variantColorOption = v_pair.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color');
                                const variantColor = variantColorOption ? variantColorOption.value : null;
                                let colorMatch = (targetColor === variantColor);
                                if (targetColor === null) colorMatch = true;
                                if (colorMatch) {
                                    autoSelectedPairedVariant = currentPairedVariantCandidate;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        if (autoSelectedPairedVariant) break;
                    }
                    const finalVariantToSelect = autoSelectedPairedVariant || firstTechnicallyCompatibleVariant;

                    if (finalVariantToSelect) {
                        const autoSelectedNippleComponent = {
                            variantId: finalVariantToSelect.id,
                            productId: finalVariantToSelect.productId,
                            productHandle: finalVariantToSelect.productHandle,
                            title: finalVariantToSelect.productTitle,
                            variantTitle: finalVariantToSelect.title,
                            sku: finalVariantToSelect.sku,
                            price: finalVariantToSelect.price.amount,
                            vendor: finalVariantToSelect.vendor,
                            image: finalVariantToSelect.image,
                            pairingKey: finalVariantToSelect.pairingKey,
                            selectedOptions: finalVariantToSelect.selectedOptions,
                            optionalAddonProductGids: finalVariantToSelect.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct,
                            quantityAvailable: finalVariantToSelect.quantityAvailable,
                            leadTimeDays: finalVariantToSelect.leadTimeDays, 
                            weight_g: finalVariantToSelect.weight_g ?? finalVariantToSelect.product_weight_g ?? null
                        };
                        buildState.components[oppositeStateKey] = autoSelectedNippleComponent;
                        calculateWheelCosts(oppositePosition);
                        updateComponentUI(oppositePosition, 'Nipples', autoSelectedNippleComponent);
                    } else {
                        if(buildState.components[oppositeStateKey]) calculateWheelCosts(oppositePosition);
                    }
                } else if (buildState.components[oppositeStateKey]) {
                     calculateWheelCosts(oppositePosition);
                }
            }

            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
            saveLastActiveBuild();

            if (buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === position &&
                buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.type === 'Nipples') {
                cancelComponentChange();
            }
            handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();
            scrollToComponentSection(position, 'Nipples');
        });
        variantContainer.appendChild(btn);
    });
}
// --- END: displayNippleVariantButtonsByProduct ---

// [START] NEW FUNCTION - fetchFreehubComponentProducts (V3)
async function fetchFreehubComponentProducts() {
    console.log("Fetching ALL freehub component products using tag: component:freehub");
    const freehubTag = "component:freehub";
    try {
        allFreehubComponentProductsCache = await fetchBuilderComponentProducts(freehubTag);
        console.log(`fetchFreehubComponentProducts: Found and cached ${allFreehubComponentProductsCache.length} freehub component products.`);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("fetchFreehubComponentProducts Error:", error);
        allFreehubComponentProductsCache = [];
        throw error;
    }
    return allFreehubComponentProductsCache;
}
// [END] NEW FUNCTION - fetchFreehubComponentProducts (V3)
  
    async function fetchValveStemProducts() {
    console.log("Fetching valve stem products using tag: component:valvestem");
    const valveStemTag = "component:valvestem";
    try {
        allValveStemProductsCache = await fetchBuilderComponentProducts(valveStemTag);
        updateGlobalVendorLogoMap(allValveStemProductsCache);
        console.log(`fetchValveStemProducts: Found and cached ${allValveStemProductsCache.length} products.`);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("fetchValveStemProducts Error:", error);
        allValveStemProductsCache = [];
        throw error;
    }
    return allValveStemProductsCache;
}

  
    async function loadAndFilterValveStems() {
    console.log("--- loadAndFilterValveStems (Combined F/R) ---");
    if (!buildState || typeof buildState.buildType === 'undefined') {
        console.error("loadAndFilterValveStems: buildState or buildState.buildType is not defined!");
        return;
    }
    const buildType = buildState.buildType;
    const positionsToLoad = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToLoad.push('Rear');
    if (positionsToLoad.length === 0) return;

    positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
        const l = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-loading`);
        if (l) l.style.display = 'block';
        const o = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-options-container`);
        if (o) o.innerHTML = '<p>Loading valve stem options...</p>';
        const e = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-error`);
