        if (e) e.style.display = 'none';
    });

    // --- START: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR VALVESTEMS ---
 if (allValveStemProductsCache.length === 0) {
     console.log("ValveStem cache empty in loadAndFilterValveStems.");
     if (componentFetchPromises.valves) {
         console.log("Waiting for early valve stem fetch promise to complete...");
         try {
             await componentFetchPromises.valves;
             console.log("Early valve stem fetch completed.");
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error awaiting early valve stem fetch in loadAndFilterValveStems:", error);
         }
     } else {
         console.log("No early valve stem fetch promise. Fetching Valve Stems directly now...");
         try {
             await fetchValveStemProducts();
         } catch (error) {
             console.error("Error fetching valve stem products directly in loadAndFilterValveStems:", error);
         }
     }
 } else {
     console.log("Using already populated/cached valve stem data for loadAndFilterValveStems.");
 }

 if (allValveStemProductsCache.length === 0) {
     console.error("ValveStem cache is STILL empty. ValveStem data loading failed.");
     positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
         const loader = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-loading`);
         if(loader) loader.style.display = 'none';
         const errorEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-error`);
         if(errorEl) errorEl.textContent = `Error: Valve Stem data failed to load.`;
         const optionsEl = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-options-container`);
         if(optionsEl) optionsEl.innerHTML = '<p>Valve Stem data failed to load.</p>';
     });
     return;
 }
 // --- END: MODIFIED CACHE/PROMISE HANDLING FOR VALVESTEMS ---

    for (const position of positionsToLoad) {
        const stateKey = `${position.toLowerCase()}ValveStem`;
        const isAlreadySelected = !!buildState.components[stateKey];
        const isExplicitlyChangingThisOne = buildState._ui.isChangingComponent &&
                                           buildState._ui.isChangingComponent.position === position &&
                                           buildState._ui.isChangingComponent.type === 'ValveStem';

        const loadAsChangeMode = !isAlreadySelected || isExplicitlyChangingThisOne;
        await loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition(position, loadAsChangeMode);
    }

    positionsToLoad.forEach(p => {
        const l = document.getElementById(`${p.toLowerCase()}-valvestem-loading`);
        if (l) l.style.display = 'none';
    });
    console.log("--- loadAndFilterValveStems (Combined F/R) finished ---");
}
        async function loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition(position, isChange = false) {
        console.log(`--- loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition: ${position} ${isChange ? '(Change Mode)' : ''} ---`);
        const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
        const refs = {
            filters: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-valvestem-filters`),
            loading: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-valvestem-loading`),
            error: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-valvestem-error`),
            optionsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-valvestem-options-container`),
            selectionSpan: document.querySelector(`#${posLower}-valvestem-selection span`),
            imageContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-valvestem-image-container`),
            actionButtonsContainer: document.getElementById(`${posLower}-valvestem-action-buttons`),
            removeButton: document.getElementById(`remove-${posLower}-valvestem-button`)
        };

        let allRefsFound = true;
        for (const key in refs) { if (!refs[key]) { console.error(`Valve Stem DOM element missing for ${position}: ${key}`); allRefsFound = false; }}
        if (!allRefsFound) { if(refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none'; return; }

        refs.error.style.display = 'none'; refs.error.textContent = '';

        const subsectionElement = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-valvestem-subsection`);
        const stateKey = `${posLower}ValveStem`;
        const currentSelectedValve = buildState.components[stateKey];

        // If a valve is selected and we are NOT in explicit change mode, just update UI and return
        if (currentSelectedValve && !isChange) {
            console.log(`   ${position} ValveStem already selected and NOT in explicit change mode. Calling updateComponentUI.`);
            if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
            updateComponentUI(position, 'ValveStem', currentSelectedValve); // This handles remove button visibility
            
            // Ensure action buttons are hidden if a selection is displayed and not in change mode
            if (refs.actionButtonsContainer) {
                refs.actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
                refs.actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'none';
            }
            return;
        }

        // If we reach here, it means we are showing the options area for one of these reasons:
        // 1. The slot is empty (currentSelectedValve is null), regardless of isChange.
        // 2. The slot has a selection, AND isChange is true (explicitly changing).

        // --- UI Setup for showing options ---
        if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'block'; // Show loading as options will be processed/shown

        if (refs.optionsContainer) {
            refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Loading options...</p>'; // Placeholder
            refs.optionsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
        }
        if (refs.imageContainer) {
            refs.imageContainer.innerHTML = '';
            refs.imageContainer.style.display = 'none';
        }
        // Remove button should be hidden if no valve is selected OR if we are in change mode (it's handled by updateComponentUI otherwise)
        if (refs.removeButton && (!currentSelectedValve || isChange) ) {
             refs.removeButton.style.display = 'none';
        }
        
        if (subsectionElement) {
            if (isChange) { // Explicitly changing an existing selection
                subsectionElement.classList.add('change-in-progress');
                subsectionElement.classList.remove('selection-made');
            } else if (!currentSelectedValve) { // Slot is empty, and not an explicit change of a selected item
                subsectionElement.classList.remove('selection-made', 'change-in-progress');
            }
            // If currentSelectedValve exists but isChange is false, we would have returned earlier.
        }
        // --- End UI Setup for showing options ---

        // --- Manage Action Buttons (Match Pair / Cancel Change) ---
        // This should be called if options are being shown AND the prerequisite (rim) is met.
        const correspondingRimKey = `${posLower}Rim`;
        const selectedRim = buildState.components[correspondingRimKey];

        if (refs.actionButtonsContainer) {
            if (selectedRim) { // Only consider showing action buttons if rim is selected
                // showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded will handle whether it's "Match Pair" and/or "Cancel Change"
                showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(position, 'ValveStem', refs.actionButtonsContainer);
            } else {
                // If no rim, no action buttons related to valve stem pairing/changing make sense
                refs.actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = '';
                refs.actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
        // --- End Manage Action Buttons ---

        // Prerequisite: Rim must be selected to show valve stem options
        if (!selectedRim) {
            if (refs.optionsContainer) refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="selection-prompt centered-bold-prompt">Please select a Rim first to see compatible Valve Stems.</p>';
            if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
            // Action buttons are already handled above based on rim presence.
            return;
        }

        // If rim is selected, proceed to load and filter valve stems
        const selectedRimDepth = selectedRim.rimDepth;
        if (selectedRimDepth === null || typeof selectedRimDepth === 'undefined') {
             console.warn(`   Rim depth for ${selectedRim.title} is not defined. Valve stems will not be filtered by depth for ${position}.`);
        }

        if (allValveStemProductsCache.length === 0) {
            console.warn(`   Valve Stem cache empty for ${position}. Attempting fetch...`);
            try {
                await fetchValveStemProducts();
                 if (allValveStemProductsCache.length === 0) {
                    console.error(`   Valve Stem data could not be loaded after fetch.`);
                    if (refs.optionsContainer) refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Valve Stem data could not be loaded.</p>';
                    if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
                    return;
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error(`   Error fetching Valve Stem data for ${position}:`, error);
                if (refs.optionsContainer) refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Error loading Valve Stem data.</p>';
                if(refs.error) { refs.error.textContent = `Error: ${error.message}`; refs.error.style.display = 'block'; }
                if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }
        }

        const compatibleProducts = allValveStemProductsCache; // All products, filtering happens in displayValveStemProductCards

        if (compatibleProducts.length === 0) {
            if (refs.optionsContainer) refs.optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>No valve stem products found in cache.</p>';
        } else {
            // Vendor filters should be displayed if options are being shown
            // (isChange implies options are shown, !currentSelectedValve implies options are shown)
            if (isChange || !currentSelectedValve) {
                 displayComponentVendorFilters(stateKey, compatibleProducts, refs.filters, position);
            }
            displayValveStemProductCards(position, compatibleProducts, refs.optionsContainer, selectedRimDepth);
        }

        if (refs.loading) refs.loading.style.display = 'none';
        console.log(`--- loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition: ${position} finished (isChange: ${isChange}, currentSelectedValve: ${!!currentSelectedValve}) ---`);
    }
  
function displayValveStemProductCards(position, allCompatibleValveStems, optionsContainer, selectedRimDepth) {
    if (!optionsContainer) {
        console.error(`   displayValveStemProductCards: optionsContainer is null for ${position}.`);
        return;
    }
    const componentKeyForState = `${position.toLowerCase()}ValveStem`;
    const selectedVendor = buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKeyForState];

    // If no vendor is selected, show nothing.
    if (selectedVendor === null) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        return;
    }

    optionsContainer.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous content
    
    const filteredProducts = selectedVendor === 'all' ? allCompatibleValveStems : allCompatibleValveStems.filter(p => p.vendor === selectedVendor);

    if (filteredProducts.length === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${position.toLowerCase()} valve stems found${selectedVendor !== 'all' ? ` for vendor: ${selectedVendor}` : ''}.</p>`;
        return;
    }

    const groupedByModel = {};
    filteredProducts.forEach(p => {
        const model = p.wheelModel || 'Other Valve Stems';
        if (!groupedByModel[model]) groupedByModel[model] = [];
        groupedByModel[model].push(p);
    });

    let displayedModelCount = 0;
    Object.keys(groupedByModel).sort((a, b) => getSortableName(a).localeCompare(getSortableName(b))).forEach(model => {
        const productsInGroup = groupedByModel[model];

        let groupHasCompatibleVariant = false;
        if (selectedRimDepth === null || typeof selectedRimDepth === 'undefined') {
            groupHasCompatibleVariant = productsInGroup.some(p => p.variants.some(v => v.availableForSale));
        } else {
            groupHasCompatibleVariant = productsInGroup.some(p =>
                p.variants.some(v =>
                    v.availableForSale &&
                    ( (v.valve_min_depth === null || v.valve_max_depth === null) ||
                      (selectedRimDepth >= v.valve_min_depth && selectedRimDepth <= v.valve_max_depth)
                    )
                )
            );
        }

        if (!groupHasCompatibleVariant) {
            return;
        }

        displayedModelCount++;
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'component-product-card valvestem-model-card';
        card.innerHTML = `
            <div class="product-card-header"><h5>${model}</h5></div>
            <div class="product-card-body">
                <p>Click to view options...</p>
                <div class="component-variant-options" style="display:none;"></div>
            </div>`;
        card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.closest('.component-variant-options button')) return;
            const vc = card.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
            if (!vc) {
                return;
            }
            const isTrigger = e.target.closest('.product-card-header') || e.target.closest('.product-card-body p');
            if (!isTrigger) return;

            const isVisible = vc.style.display !== 'none';
            optionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.component-product-card.expanded').forEach(c => {
                if (c !== card) {
                    c.classList.remove('expanded');
                    const otherVc = c.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
                    if (otherVc) otherVc.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            vc.style.display = isVisible ? 'none' : 'block';
            card.classList.toggle('expanded', !isVisible);
            if (!isVisible) {
                displayValveStemVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, vc, selectedRimDepth);
            }
        });
        optionsContainer.appendChild(card);
    });

    if (displayedModelCount === 0) {
        let message = `No ${position.toLowerCase()} valve stem models found`;
        if (selectedVendor !== 'all') message += ` for vendor ${selectedVendor}`;
        if (selectedRimDepth !== null && typeof selectedRimDepth !== 'undefined') message += ` compatible with ${selectedRimDepth}mm rim depth`;
        message += '.';
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>${message}</p>`;
    }
}
  
// --- START: displayValveStemVariantButtonsByProduct (with lead time data) ---
function displayValveStemVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, variantContainer, selectedRimDepth) {
    if (!variantContainer) return;
    variantContainer.innerHTML = 'Loading options...';

    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const stateKey = `${posLower}ValveStem`;
    const selectedComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

    let variantsToDisplay = [];
    productsInGroup.forEach(p => {
        let p_optionalAddonProductGids = [];
        const rawGidValue = p.optionalAddonProductGids?.value;
        if (Array.isArray(rawGidValue)) {
            p_optionalAddonProductGids = rawGidValue.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
        } else if (typeof rawGidValue === 'string') {
            try {
                const parsedGids = JSON.parse(rawGidValue);
                if (Array.isArray(parsedGids)) {
                    p_optionalAddonProductGids = parsedGids.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                }
            } catch (e) {
                 if (rawGidValue.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/')) {
                       p_optionalAddonProductGids = [rawGidValue.trim()];
                 } else {
                    p_optionalAddonProductGids = rawGidValue.split(',')
                                       .map(gid => gid.trim())
                                       .filter(gid => gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                 }
            }
        }

        const productDetails = { 
            productId: p.id, productTitle: p.title, productHandle: p.handle, 
            vendor: p.vendor, pairingKey: p.pairingKey,
            optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: p_optionalAddonProductGids,
            leadTimeDays: p.leadTimeDays || 0 // <<< ADD THIS
        };
        p.variants.forEach(v => {
            if (v.availableForSale) {
                let isDepthCompatible = false;
                if (selectedRimDepth === null || typeof selectedRimDepth === 'undefined') {
                    isDepthCompatible = true;
                } else if (v.valve_min_depth === null || v.valve_max_depth === null) {
                    isDepthCompatible = true;
                } else {
                    isDepthCompatible = selectedRimDepth >= v.valve_min_depth && selectedRimDepth <= v.valve_max_depth;
                }

                if (isDepthCompatible) {
                    variantsToDisplay.push({ ...v, ...productDetails, price: v.price });
                }
            }
        });
    });

    if (variantsToDisplay.length === 0) {
        let msg = `<p>No available valve stem options in this group`;
        if (selectedRimDepth !== null && typeof selectedRimDepth !== 'undefined') {
            msg += ` compatible with ${selectedRimDepth}mm rim depth`;
        }
        msg += `.</p>`;
        variantContainer.innerHTML = msg;
        return;
    }

    const uniqueVariantsMap = new Map();
    variantsToDisplay.forEach(v => { if (!uniqueVariantsMap.has(v.id)) uniqueVariantsMap.set(v.id, v); });
    let uniqueVariants = Array.from(uniqueVariantsMap.values()).sort((a, b) => {
        const titleCompare = (a.productTitle || '').localeCompare(b.productTitle || ''); if (titleCompare !== 0) return titleCompare;
        const lengthAOpt = a.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'length');
        const lengthBOpt = b.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'length');
        const lengthA = lengthAOpt ? parseInt(lengthAOpt.value.replace(/\D/g, '')) : Infinity;
        const lengthB = lengthBOpt ? parseInt(lengthBOpt.value.replace(/\D/g, '')) : Infinity;
        return lengthA - lengthB;
    });

    variantContainer.innerHTML = '';
    uniqueVariants.forEach(v_valve => {
        const btn = document.createElement('button'); btn.className = 'component-variant-button valvestem-variant-button';
        btn.dataset.variantId = v_valve.id; btn.dataset.productId = v_valve.productId; btn.type = 'button';
        if (selectedComponent?.variantId === v_valve.id) btn.classList.add('selected');
        const imageUrl = v_valve.image?.url; let variantDisplayParts = [];
        v_valve.selectedOptions.forEach(opt => { variantDisplayParts.push(`${opt.value}`); });
        const displayTitleText = `${v_valve.productTitle || 'Valve Stem'} (${variantDisplayParts.join(', ') || v_valve.title || 'Default'})`;
        const priceAmount = v_valve.price?.amount;
        btn.innerHTML = `${imageUrl ? `<img src="${imageUrl}" alt="${displayTitleText}" loading="lazy" class="variant-button-image">` : '<div class="variant-button-image-placeholder"></div>'}<div class="variant-button-details"><span class="variant-details">${displayTitleText}</span>${priceAmount ? `<span class="variant-price">${formatPrice(priceAmount)}</span>` : ''}</div>`;

        btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const newSelectedValveVariantId = v_valve.id;
            const newValveProductOptionalAddonGids = v_valve.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [];

            const previouslySelectedValveComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

            if (previouslySelectedValveComponent && previouslySelectedValveComponent.variantId !== newSelectedValveVariantId) {
                if (previouslySelectedValveComponent.productId === v_valve.productId) {
                    manageStickyAddonsForChangedBaseVariant(
                        position,
                        'ValveStem',
                        previouslySelectedValveComponent.variantId, 
                        newSelectedValveVariantId,                 
                        newValveProductOptionalAddonGids
                    );
                } else {
                    const addonKeysToPotentiallyRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons);
                    for (const addonKey of addonKeysToPotentiallyRemove) {
                        const selectedAddon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKey];
                        if (selectedAddon.baseComponentPosition === position &&
                            selectedAddon.baseComponentType === 'ValveStem' &&
                            selectedAddon.baseComponentVariantId === previouslySelectedValveComponent.variantId) {
                            delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[addonKey];
                            saveLastActiveBuild();
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            const selectedValveComponent = {
                variantId: v_valve.id, productId: v_valve.productId, productHandle: v_valve.productHandle,
                title: v_valve.productTitle, variantTitle: v_valve.title,
                sku: v_valve.sku, price: v_valve.price.amount, vendor: v_valve.vendor,
                image: v_valve.image, pairingKey: v_valve.pairingKey,
                selectedOptions: v_valve.selectedOptions,
                selectedWithRimDepth: selectedRimDepth,
                valveMinDepth: v_valve.valve_min_depth,
                valveMaxDepth: v_valve.valve_max_depth,
                optionalAddonProductGids: newValveProductOptionalAddonGids,
                quantityAvailable: v_valve.quantityAvailable,
                leadTimeDays: v_valve.leadTimeDays,
                weight_g: v_valve.weight_g ?? v_valve.product_weight_g ?? null
            };
            buildState.components[stateKey] = selectedValveComponent;
            buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
            updateStep3ButtonText();
            buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved[posLower] = false;
            updateComponentUI(position, 'ValveStem', selectedValveComponent);

            if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
                const oppositePosition = position === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
                const oppositePosLower = oppositePosition.toLowerCase();
                const oppositeStateKey = `${oppositePosLower}ValveStem`;

                if (buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved[oppositePosLower]) {
                    // Skip auto-pair if explicitly removed
                } else if (!buildState.components[oppositeStateKey] && selectedValveComponent.pairingKey) {
                    const selectedColorOption = selectedValveComponent.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color');
                    const targetColor = selectedColorOption ? selectedColorOption.value : null;

                    const oppositeRimKey = `${oppositePosLower}Rim`;
                    const oppositeSelectedRim = buildState.components[oppositeRimKey];
                    const oppositeRimDepth = oppositeSelectedRim ? oppositeSelectedRim.rimDepth : null;
                    
                    if (!oppositeSelectedRim) {
                        // Cannot auto-pair if opposite rim not selected
                    } else {
                        const pairedProducts = allValveStemProductsCache.filter(p => p.pairingKey === selectedValveComponent.pairingKey);
                        let potentialPairedValves = [];

                        for (const p_pair of pairedProducts) {
                            if (!p_pair || !p_pair.variants) continue;
                            let p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids = [];
                            const rawGidValuePair = p_pair.optionalAddonProductGids?.value;
                            if (Array.isArray(rawGidValuePair)) {
                                p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids = rawGidValuePair.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                            } else if (typeof rawGidValuePair === 'string') {
                                try {
                                    const parsedGids = JSON.parse(rawGidValuePair);
                                    if (Array.isArray(parsedGids)) p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids = parsedGids.filter(gid => typeof gid === 'string' && gid.startsWith('gid://shopify/Product/'));
                                } catch (e) { /* Fallback if needed */ }
                            }

                            for (const v_pair of p_pair.variants) {
                                if (!v_pair.availableForSale) continue;
                                let isDepthCompatibleForPair = false;
                                if (oppositeRimDepth === null || typeof oppositeRimDepth === 'undefined') isDepthCompatibleForPair = true;
                                else if (v_pair.valve_min_depth === null || v_pair.valve_max_depth === null) isDepthCompatibleForPair = true;
                                else isDepthCompatibleForPair = oppositeRimDepth >= v_pair.valve_min_depth && oppositeRimDepth <= v_pair.valve_max_depth;
                                if (isDepthCompatibleForPair) {
                                    const variantColorOption = v_pair.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color');
                                    const variantColor = variantColorOption ? variantColorOption.value : null;
                                    let colorMatch = (targetColor === variantColor);
                                    if (targetColor === null) colorMatch = true;
                                    if (colorMatch) {
                                        potentialPairedValves.push({
                                            variant: v_pair, 
                                            product: p_pair, 
                                            optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct: p_pair_optionalAddonProductGids,
                                            leadTimeDays: p_pair.leadTimeDays || 0 // <<< ADD THIS
                                        });
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        let finalVariantToSelect = null;
                        if (potentialPairedValves.length > 0) {
                            potentialPairedValves.sort((a, b) => { /* ... existing sort ... */ });
                            finalVariantToSelect = potentialPairedValves[0]; 
                        }
                        if (finalVariantToSelect) {
                            const autoSelectedValveComponent = {
                                variantId: finalVariantToSelect.variant.id, productId: finalVariantToSelect.product.id, productHandle: finalVariantToSelect.product.handle,
                                title: finalVariantToSelect.product.title, variantTitle: finalVariantToSelect.variant.title, sku: finalVariantToSelect.variant.sku,
                                price: finalVariantToSelect.variant.price.amount, vendor: finalVariantToSelect.product.vendor, image: finalVariantToSelect.variant.image,
                                pairingKey: finalVariantToSelect.product.pairingKey, selectedOptions: finalVariantToSelect.variant.selectedOptions,
                                selectedWithRimDepth: oppositeRimDepth, valveMinDepth: finalVariantToSelect.variant.valve_min_depth, valveMaxDepth: finalVariantToSelect.variant.valve_max_depth,
                                optionalAddonProductGids: finalVariantToSelect.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct,
                                quantityAvailable: finalVariantToSelect.variant.quantityAvailable,
                                leadTimeDays: finalVariantToSelect.leadTimeDays,
                                weight_g: finalVariantToSelect.variant.weight_g ?? finalVariantToSelect.product.weight_g ?? null
                            };
                            buildState.components[oppositeStateKey] = autoSelectedValveComponent;
                            buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved[oppositePosLower] = false;
                            updateComponentUI(oppositePosition, 'ValveStem', autoSelectedValveComponent);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

                        // After auto-pairing logic, explicitly re-evaluate the opposite side's action buttons.
            // This ensures the "Match Pair" button appears if auto-pairing did not happen.
            if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
                const oppositePosition = position === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
                const oppositePosLower = oppositePosition.toLowerCase();
                const oppositeActionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${oppositePosLower}-valvestem-action-buttons`);
                
                // This is the key: We need to re-evaluate the opposite side's buttons
                // because a potential match (the one just selected) now exists.
                if (oppositeActionButtonsContainer) {
                    showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(oppositePosition, 'ValveStem', oppositeActionButtonsContainer);
                }
            }
          
            updateSubtotal(); updateBuildSummary(); validateStep3(); saveLastActiveBuild();
            if (buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === position && buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.type === 'ValveStem') cancelComponentChange();
            handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();
            scrollToComponentSection(position, 'ValveStem');
        });
        variantContainer.appendChild(btn);
    });
}
// --- END: displayValveStemVariantButtonsByProduct ---
  
    function evaluateValveStemForRimChange(rimPosition) {
        console.log(`evaluateValveStemForRimChange: Evaluating valve for ${rimPosition} Rim.`);
        const posLower = rimPosition.toLowerCase();
        const rimStateKey = `${posLower}Rim`;
        const valveStemStateKey = `${posLower}ValveStem`;

        const selectedRimComponent = buildState.components[rimStateKey];
        if (!selectedRimComponent) {
            console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: No ${rimPosition} Rim selected. Cannot evaluate valve stem.`);
            if (buildState.components[valveStemStateKey]) {
                buildState.components[valveStemStateKey] = null;
                updateComponentUI(rimPosition, 'ValveStem', null);
            }
            loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition(rimPosition, true);
            return;
        }

        const currentValveStem = buildState.components[valveStemStateKey];
        let valveStemWasCleared = false;
        let valveStemWasAutoReselected = false;
        const newRimDepth = selectedRimComponent.rimDepth;

        if (currentValveStem) {
            let isValveStillCompatible = false;
            if (newRimDepth === null || typeof newRimDepth === 'undefined') {
                isValveStillCompatible = true;
                console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: ${rimPosition} Rim has no depth. Keeping selected Valve Stem: ${currentValveStem.variantTitle}.`);
            } else if (currentValveStem.valveMinDepth === null || currentValveStem.valveMaxDepth === null) {
                isValveStillCompatible = true;
                console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: Selected ${rimPosition} Valve (${currentValveStem.variantTitle}) has no depth specs. Keeping selected Valve Stem.`);
            } else {
                isValveStillCompatible = newRimDepth >= currentValveStem.valveMinDepth && newRimDepth <= currentValveStem.valveMaxDepth;
            }

            if (!isValveStillCompatible) {
                console.warn(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: Previously selected ${rimPosition} Valve Stem (${currentValveStem.title} - ${currentValveStem.variantTitle}) NO LONGER compatible with new Rim depth (${newRimDepth}mm). Clearing.`);
                const clearedValveDetails = {
                    pairingKey: currentValveStem.pairingKey,
                    color: currentValveStem.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null,
                    originalVariantId: currentValveStem.variantId
                };
                buildState.components[valveStemStateKey] = null;
                valveStemWasCleared = true;

                if (clearedValveDetails.pairingKey && newRimDepth !== null && typeof newRimDepth !== 'undefined' && allValveStemProductsCache.length > 0) {
                    console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: Attempting auto-re-select ${rimPosition} Valve. Color: ${clearedValveDetails.color}, Key: ${clearedValveDetails.pairingKey}, Depth: ${newRimDepth}mm`);
                    let potentialNewValves = [];
                    for (const product of allValveStemProductsCache) {
                        if (product.pairingKey !== clearedValveDetails.pairingKey) continue;
                        for (const variant of product.variants) {
                            if (!variant.availableForSale || variant.id === clearedValveDetails.originalVariantId) continue;
                            let isDepthCompatibleReselect = (newRimDepth >= variant.valve_min_depth && newRimDepth <= variant.valve_max_depth);
                            if (variant.valve_min_depth === null || variant.valve_max_depth === null) isDepthCompatibleReselect = true;
                            const variantColorReselect = variant.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;
                            const isColorMatchReselect = (clearedValveDetails.color === variantColorReselect) || (clearedValveDetails.color === null);
                            if (isDepthCompatibleReselect && isColorMatchReselect) potentialNewValves.push({ variant, product });
                        }
                    }

                    if (potentialNewValves.length > 0) {
                        potentialNewValves.sort((a, b) => (parseInt(a.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity) - (parseInt(b.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity));
                        const newFoundValve = potentialNewValves[0];
                        const newValveComponent = {
                            variantId: newFoundValve.variant.id, productId: newFoundValve.product.id, productHandle: newFoundValve.product.handle,
                            title: newFoundValve.product.title, variantTitle: newFoundValve.variant.title, sku: newFoundValve.variant.sku,
                            price: newFoundValve.variant.price.amount, vendor: newFoundValve.product.vendor, image: newFoundValve.variant.image,
                            pairingKey: newFoundValve.product.pairingKey, selectedOptions: newFoundValve.variant.selectedOptions,
                            selectedWithRimDepth: newRimDepth, valveMinDepth: newFoundValve.variant.valve_min_depth, valveMaxDepth: newFoundValve.variant.valve_max_depth
                        };
                        console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: Auto-re-selected ${rimPosition} Valve:`, newValveComponent);
                        buildState.components[valveStemStateKey] = newValveComponent;
                        buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved[posLower] = false;
                        valveStemWasCleared = false;
                        valveStemWasAutoReselected = true;
                    } else {
                         console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: Could not find a valve to auto-re-select for ${rimPosition}. Slot remains cleared.`);
                    }
                }
            } else {
                buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved[posLower] = false;
                valveStemWasAutoReselected = false;
                if (newRimDepth !== null && typeof newRimDepth !== 'undefined' && allValveStemProductsCache.length > 0) {
                    console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: ${rimPosition} Valve (${currentValveStem.variantTitle}) still compatible. Checking for shorter...`);
                    let potentialShorterValves = [];
                    for (const product of allValveStemProductsCache) {
                        if (product.pairingKey !== currentValveStem.pairingKey) continue;
                        for (const variant of product.variants) {
                            if (!variant.availableForSale) continue;
                            let isDepthCompatibleShorter = (newRimDepth >= variant.valve_min_depth && newRimDepth <= variant.valve_max_depth);
                            if (variant.valve_min_depth === null || variant.valve_max_depth === null) isDepthCompatibleShorter = true;
                            const variantColorShorter = variant.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;
                            const currentColorShorter = currentValveStem.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;
                            const isColorMatchShorter = (currentColorShorter === variantColorShorter);
                            if (isDepthCompatibleShorter && isColorMatchShorter) potentialShorterValves.push({variant, product});
                        }
                    }

                    if (potentialShorterValves.length > 0) {
                        potentialShorterValves.sort((a,b) => (parseInt(a.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity) - (parseInt(b.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity));
                        const shortestCompatible = potentialShorterValves[0];
                        const currentLength = parseInt(currentValveStem.selectedOptions.find(o=>o.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,'')) || Infinity;
                        const shortestLength = parseInt(shortestCompatible.variant.selectedOptions.find(o=>o.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,'')) || Infinity;

                        if (shortestCompatible.variant.id !== currentValveStem.variantId && shortestLength < currentLength) {
                            const shorterName = `${shortestCompatible.product.title || 'Valve'} (${shortestCompatible.variant.title || shortestCompatible.variant.selectedOptions.find(o=>o.name==='Length')?.value || 'Shorter'})`;
                            if (confirm(`A shorter valve stem (${shorterName}) is available for your ${rimPosition} rim. Would you like to switch to it?`)) {
                                const newValveComponent = {
                                    variantId: shortestCompatible.variant.id, productId: shortestCompatible.product.id, productHandle: shortestCompatible.product.handle,
                                    title: shortestCompatible.product.title, variantTitle: shortestCompatible.variant.title, sku: shortestCompatible.variant.sku,
                                    price: shortestCompatible.variant.price.amount, vendor: shortestCompatible.product.vendor, image: shortestCompatible.variant.image,
                                    pairingKey: shortestCompatible.product.pairingKey, selectedOptions: shortestCompatible.variant.selectedOptions,
                                    selectedWithRimDepth: newRimDepth, valveMinDepth: shortestCompatible.variant.valve_min_depth, valveMaxDepth: shortestCompatible.variant.valve_max_depth
                                };
                                buildState.components[valveStemStateKey] = newValveComponent;
                                valveStemWasAutoReselected = true;
                            } else {
                                console.log(`   User declined shorter ${rimPosition} valve. Keeping ${currentValveStem.variantTitle}`);
                            }
                        } else {
                            console.log(`   Current ${rimPosition} valve is already shortest or only option. Keeping ${currentValveStem.variantTitle}`);
                        }
                    } else {
                        console.log(`   No other valves found to compare for shorter option for ${rimPosition} valve.`);
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
             console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: No current valve for ${rimPosition}. Will show options if rim is present.`);
            valveStemWasCleared = true;
        }

        let isNowChangingThisValve = (valveStemWasCleared && !valveStemWasAutoReselected);

        console.log(`   evaluateValveStemForRimChange: Calling loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition for ${rimPosition}. isChange (show options): ${isNowChangingThisValve}`);
        loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition(rimPosition, isNowChangingThisValve);

    // --- Set hasChanges flag only if an actual change occurred to the valve stem ---
    if (valveStemWasCleared || valveStemWasAutoReselected) {
        buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
        updateStep3ButtonText();
        saveLastActiveBuild();
    }
    // --- END ---

}
    // END OF EXISTING COMPONENT FUNCTIONS

// --- START: updateBuildSummary and updateSubtotal with Integrated Discount Logic (Plan E) ---

async function countChargeableItemsInBuild() { 
    let itemCount = 0;
    const { components, selectedOptionalAddons, buildType } = buildState;
    if (!buildType) return 0;

    const positionsToProcess = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToProcess.push('front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToProcess.push('rear');

    positionsToProcess.forEach(pos => {
        // Main components (Rims, Hubs, Spokes, Nipples, ValveStems)
        ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].forEach(type => {
            if (components[`${pos}${type}`]) {
                itemCount++;
            }
        });

        // Assembly Service
        if (components[`${pos}AssemblyService`]) {
            itemCount++;
        }

        // Required Addons (like Berd Inserts)
        if (components[`${pos}RequiredAddons`]) {
            itemCount += components[`${pos}RequiredAddons`].length;
        }
    });

    // Optional Add-ons
    if (selectedOptionalAddons) {
        itemCount += Object.keys(selectedOptionalAddons).length;
    }

    // --- START: LOGIC TO COUNT ACCESSORIES FROM CART IN EDIT MODE ---
if (buildState._ui.inEditMode === true && buildState.buildId) {
    try {
        const cartResponse = await fetch('/cart.json');
        const cartData = await cartResponse.json();
        const accessoryBundleId = `${buildState.buildId}-ACC`;
        
        cartData.items.forEach(item => {
            if (item.properties && item.properties._parent_build_id === accessoryBundleId) {
                itemCount += item.quantity;
            }
        });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error("Could not fetch cart to count accessories during edit:", e);
    }
}
// --- END: NEW LOGIC ---
  
    return itemCount;
}

/**
 * Calculates the total cost of all physical items for a pre-configured build.
 * Crucially, it ignores valve stems as they are considered an included part of the bundle.
 * @returns {number} The total cost in cents.
 */
function calculatePhysicalPreconfiguredTotal() {
    const { components, selectedOptionalAddons } = buildState;
    let total = 0;

    // IMPORTANT: Note that 'ValveStem' is excluded from this list.
    const mainComponentKeys = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples'];
    const positions = ['front', 'rear'];

    positions.forEach(pos => {
        mainComponentKeys.forEach(typeKey => {
            const component = components[`${pos}${typeKey}`];
            if (component?.price) total += component.price;
        });
        (components[`${pos}RequiredAddons`] || []).forEach(addon => {
            total += addon.costInCents;
        });
    });

    if (components.rearComponentFreehub?.price) {
        total += components.rearComponentFreehub.price;
    }

    Object.values(selectedOptionalAddons).forEach(addon => {
        total += addon.addonPriceCents;
    });

    return total;
}


function updateSubtotal() {
    let subtotalCents = 0;
    const { components, buildType, selectedOptionalAddons } = buildState;

    const mainComponentKeys = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'];
    const positionsToProcess = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToProcess.push('front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToProcess.push('rear');

    positionsToProcess.forEach(pos => {
        mainComponentKeys.forEach(typeKey => {
            const component = components[`${pos}${typeKey}`];
            if (component?.price && typeof component.price === 'number') {
                subtotalCents += component.price;
            }
        });

        const assemblyService = components[`${pos}AssemblyService`];
        if (assemblyService?.costInCents) {
            subtotalCents += assemblyService.costInCents;
        }

        const requiredAddons = components[`${pos}RequiredAddons`];
        if (requiredAddons) {
            requiredAddons.forEach(addon => {
                if (addon?.costInCents) subtotalCents += addon.costInCents;
            });
        }
    });

    if (selectedOptionalAddons) {
        Object.values(selectedOptionalAddons).forEach(addon => {
            if (addon?.addonPriceCents) subtotalCents += addon.addonPriceCents;
        });
    }

    if (components.rearComponentFreehub?.price && typeof components.rearComponentFreehub.price === 'number') {
        subtotalCents += components.rearComponentFreehub.price;
    }
    
    buildState.subtotal = subtotalCents;

    // This is now the ONLY place that calls updateBuildSummary, ensuring the flow is correct.
    updateBuildSummary();
}

// --- Inside variant-builder.js ---

/**
 * Checks if the current selection matches a pre-configured wheel rule.
 * @returns {object|null} The matching rule object (with finalPriceCents) or null if no match.
 */
function checkForPreconfiguredMatch() {

    if (buildState.buildType !== 'Wheel Set') {
        return null;
    }

    const { frontRim, rearRim, frontHub, rearHub, frontSpokes, rearSpokes } = buildState.components;

    if (!frontRim || !rearRim || !frontHub || !rearHub) {
        return null;
    }

    const frontRimProduct = allRimProductsCache.find(p => p.id === frontRim.productId);
    const rearRimProduct = allRimProductsCache.find(p => p.id === rearRim.productId);

    const rulesToCheck = [];
    // Add context to the rules so we know which product they "live" on
    if (frontRimProduct?.preconfiguredRules?.length > 0) {
        rulesToCheck.push(...frontRimProduct.preconfiguredRules.map(rule => ({ ...rule, hostProductId: frontRimProduct.id })));
    }
    if (rearRimProduct?.preconfiguredRules?.length > 0) {
        rulesToCheck.push(...rearRimProduct.preconfiguredRules.map(rule => ({ ...rule, hostProductId: rearRimProduct.id })));
    }

    if (rulesToCheck.length === 0) {
        return null;
    }

    for (const rule of rulesToCheck) {
        console.log("  - Rule requires:", {
            pairedRim: rule.pairedRimProductId,
            frontHub: rule.requiredFrontHubProductId,
            rearHub: rule.requiredRearHubProductId,
            spokes: rule.requiredSpokeProductId,
            masterVariant: rule.masterVariantGid
        });
        
        const ruleRimIds = new Set([rule.hostProductId, rule.pairedRimProductId]);
        const selectedRimIds = new Set([frontRim.productId, rearRim.productId]);
        const rimMatch = ruleRimIds.size === selectedRimIds.size && [...ruleRimIds].every(id => selectedRimIds.has(id));
        
        const hubMatch = frontHub.productId === rule.requiredFrontHubProductId && rearHub.productId === rule.requiredRearHubProductId;
        
        let spokeMatch = true;
        if (rule.requiredSpokeProductId) {
            spokeMatch = frontSpokes?.productId === rule.requiredSpokeProductId && rearSpokes?.productId === rule.requiredSpokeProductId;
        }

        console.log(`  - Match Results: rim=${rimMatch}, hub=${hubMatch}, spoke=${spokeMatch}`);

        if (rimMatch && hubMatch && spokeMatch) {
            const finalPriceCents = preconfiguredPriceCache[rule.masterVariantGid];
            if (typeof finalPriceCents === 'number') {
                return { ...rule, finalPriceCents };
            } else {
            }
        }
    }

    return null;
}

// --- START: DYNAMIC LEAD TIME FUNCTIONS ---

// Converts a number of days into a user-friendly week-based range.
function formatLeadTime(totalDays) {
    if (totalDays <= 5) return "Approx. 1 Week";
    if (totalDays <= 7) return "Approx. 1-2 Weeks";
    if (totalDays <= 12) return "Approx. 2-3 Weeks";
    if (totalDays <= 17) return "Approx. 3-4 Weeks";
    if (totalDays <= 22) return "Approx. 4-5 Weeks";
    // For anything longer, calculate weeks and add a buffer.
    const weeks = Math.ceil(totalDays / 5); // Using 5 for business days
    return `Approx. ${weeks}-${weeks + 1} Weeks`;
}

// --- START: updateLeadTime function ---
function updateLeadTime() {
    let maxLeadTime = 0;
    const { components } = buildState;

    // This new version directly inspects the selected components in the buildState,
    // which now contain all the necessary info (quantityAvailable and leadTimeDays).
    Object.values(components).forEach(component => {
        // Check if the component is a physical item with lead time info
        if (component && typeof component.quantityAvailable !== 'undefined' && typeof component.leadTimeDays !== 'undefined') {
            
            let componentLeadTime = 0;

            // If the component is out of stock, use its defined lead time.
            if (component.quantityAvailable <= 0) {
                componentLeadTime = component.leadTimeDays;
            }
            
            // Check if this component's lead time is the new maximum.
            if (componentLeadTime > maxLeadTime) {
                maxLeadTime = componentLeadTime;
            }
        }
    });

    // Add your standard in-house build time to the longest part lead time
    buildState.estimatedLeadTime = maxLeadTime + LEAD_TIME_CONFIG.BUILD_TIME_DAYS;
    
    // The display is handled by updateBuildSummary.
}
// --- END: updateLeadTime function ---

// This function needs to be called every time a component is added/removed.
// The easiest way is to add it to the functions that already run on component change.
function handleComponentChangeForLeadTime() {
    updateLeadTime();
    updateBuildSummary(); // This will re-render the summary with the new lead time.
}
// --- END: DYNAMIC LEAD TIME FUNCTIONS ---
  
// [START] updateBuildSummary (V4.4)
async function updateBuildSummary() {
    if (!summaryContainer || !subtotalValueElement || !summaryContentElement || !buildState) {
        if (summaryContentElement) summaryContentElement.innerHTML = '<p>Select options.</p>';
        if (subtotalValueElement) subtotalValueElement.textContent = formatPrice(0);
        return;
    }

    if (!buildState.buildType) {
        summaryContentElement.innerHTML = '<p>Select options.</p>';
        subtotalValueElement.textContent = formatPrice(0);
        return;
    }

    let totalCents = 0;

    const { components, buildType, selectedOptionalAddons } = buildState;
    const mainComponentKeys = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'];
    const positionsToProcess = [];
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToProcess.push('front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') positionsToProcess.push('rear');

    // 1. Calculate Totals (Include EVERYTHING in the discountable total)
    positionsToProcess.forEach(pos => {
        // Add up component costs (This includes Integrated Rims)
        mainComponentKeys.forEach(typeKey => {
            const component = components[`${pos}${typeKey}`];
            if (component?.price) {
                totalCents += component.price;
            }
        });

        const assemblyService = components[`${pos}AssemblyService`];
        if (assemblyService?.costInCents) {
            totalCents += assemblyService.costInCents;
        }

        const requiredAddons = components[`${pos}RequiredAddons`];
        if (requiredAddons) {
            requiredAddons.forEach(addon => {
                if (addon?.costInCents) totalCents += addon.costInCents;
            });
        }
    });

    if (components.rearComponentFreehub?.price) totalCents += components.rearComponentFreehub.price;
    
    Object.values(selectedOptionalAddons).forEach(addon => {
        if (addon?.addonPriceCents) totalCents += addon.addonPriceCents;
    });
    
    const grossTotal = totalCents;

    // 2. Determine Discount Eligibility
    const preconfiguredMatch = checkForPreconfiguredMatch();
    let discountInfoHtml = '';
    let finalTotal = grossTotal;

    if (preconfiguredMatch && preconfiguredMatch.masterVariantGid) {
        const finalPrice = preconfiguredMatch.finalPriceCents;
        const physicalTotal = calculatePhysicalPreconfiguredTotal();
        finalTotal = finalPrice; 
        subtotalValueElement.innerHTML = `<strike>${formatPrice(physicalTotal)}</strike> <strong>${formatPrice(finalTotal)}</strong>`;
        discountInfoHtml = `<div class="summary-discount-info">✓ LOAMLABS Discount Automatically Applied</div>`;
    } else {
        // --- CUSTOM DISCOUNT LOGIC ---
        // Calculate item count to determine eligibility for single wheels
        let itemCount = 0;
        positionsToProcess.forEach(pos => {
            ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].forEach(type => {
                const comp = components[`${pos}${type}`];
                // Only count if it exists and is not virtual. 
                // Integrated Rims count. Real Valve Stems count. Virtual Hubs do not.
                if (comp && !comp.isVirtual) {
                    itemCount++;
                }
            });
            if (components[`${pos}AssemblyService`]) itemCount++;
            if (components[`${pos}RequiredAddons`]) itemCount += components[`${pos}RequiredAddons`].length;
        });
        if (selectedOptionalAddons) itemCount += Object.keys(selectedOptionalAddons).length;
        
        let isDiscountActive = false;
        
        // Rule: Automatically active for Wheel Sets, OR if item threshold is met
        if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' && buildState.step === 3) {
             isDiscountActive = true;
        } else if (itemCount >= DISCOUNT_CONFIG.ITEM_COUNT_GOAL) { 
            isDiscountActive = true; 
        }
        
        if (isDiscountActive && totalCents > 0) { 
            discountInfoHtml = `<div class="summary-discount-info">✓ ${DISCOUNT_CONFIG.DISCOUNT_CODE} Discount Applied (10% Off)</div>`; 
            
            const discountAmount = Math.round(totalCents * (DISCOUNT_CONFIG.DISCOUNT_PERCENTAGE / 100));
            finalTotal = grossTotal - discountAmount;
            
            subtotalValueElement.innerHTML = `<strike>${formatPrice(grossTotal)}</strike> <strong>${formatPrice(finalTotal)}</strong>`;
        } else {
            finalTotal = grossTotal;
            subtotalValueElement.textContent = formatPrice(grossTotal);
        }
    }
    
    buildState.subtotal = finalTotal;
    
    let componentsHtml = '';
    if (buildState.step >= 3) {
        componentsHtml = '<h4>Components</h4><ul>';
        const componentTypes = [ { type: 'Rim', display: 'Rim' }, { type: 'Hub', display: 'Hub' }, { type: 'Spokes', display: 'Spokes' }, { type: 'Nipples', display: 'Nipples' }, { type: 'ValveStem', display: 'Valve Stem' } ];
        
        componentTypes.forEach(compTypeInfo => {
            const frontComponent = components[`front${compTypeInfo.type}`];
            const rearComponent = components[`rear${compTypeInfo.type}`];

            if (buildType === 'Wheel Set' && frontComponent && rearComponent && frontComponent.variantId === rearComponent.variantId) {
                const itemDescription = frontComponent.variantTitle ? `${frontComponent.title} (${frontComponent.variantTitle})` : frontComponent.title;
                const combinedPrice = frontComponent.price * 2;
                componentsHtml += `<li><span class="summary-item-label-column">Front/Rear ${compTypeInfo.display}:</span><span class="summary-item-description-column"><strong>(2) ${itemDescription || 'Selected'}</strong></span><span class="summary-value">(${formatPrice(combinedPrice)})</span></li>`;
            } else {
                if ((buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') && frontComponent) {
                    let itemDescription = frontComponent.variantTitle ? `${frontComponent.title} (${frontComponent.variantTitle})` : frontComponent.title;
                    componentsHtml += `<li><span class="summary-item-label-column">Front ${compTypeInfo.display}:</span><span class="summary-item-description-column"><strong>(1) ${itemDescription || 'Selected'}</strong></span> <span class="summary-value">(${formatPrice(frontComponent.price)})</span></li>`;
                }
                if ((buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') && rearComponent) {
                    let itemDescription = rearComponent.variantTitle ? `${rearComponent.title} (${rearComponent.variantTitle})` : rearComponent.title;
                    componentsHtml += `<li><span class="summary-item-label-column">Rear ${compTypeInfo.display}:</span><span class="summary-item-description-column"><strong>(1) ${itemDescription || 'Selected'}</strong></span> <span class="summary-value">(${formatPrice(rearComponent.price)})</span></li>`;
                    if (compTypeInfo.type === 'Hub') {
                        const freehubComponent = components.rearComponentFreehub;
                        if (freehubComponent) {
                            componentsHtml += `<li class="summary-item-indented"><span class="summary-item-label-column"></span><span class="summary-item-description-column"><strong>(1) ${freehubComponent.name}</strong></span><span class="summary-value">(${formatPrice(freehubComponent.price)})</span></li>`;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        componentsHtml += '</ul>';
    }

    let costsHtml = ''; 
    let hasAnyCostsOrServices = false;
    let totalAssemblyCostCents = 0;
    let frontAssemblyService, rearAssemblyService, frontTape = false, rearTape = false, frontBerdInserts, rearBerdInserts;

    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        frontAssemblyService = components.frontAssemblyService;
        if (frontAssemblyService?.costInCents) totalAssemblyCostCents += frontAssemblyService.costInCents;
        if (components.frontRim) frontTape = true;
        if (components.frontRequiredAddons?.length > 0) frontBerdInserts = components.frontRequiredAddons.find(a => a.name === 'Berd Hub Inserts');
    }
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        rearAssemblyService = components.rearAssemblyService;
        if (rearAssemblyService?.costInCents) totalAssemblyCostCents += rearAssemblyService.costInCents;
        if (components.rearRim) rearTape = true;
        if (components.rearRequiredAddons?.length > 0) rearBerdInserts = components.rearRequiredAddons.find(a => a.name === 'Berd Hub Inserts');
    }

    if (totalAssemblyCostCents > 0 || (buildState.step === 3 && (components.frontRim || components.rearRim || components.frontHub || components.rearHub))) {
        costsHtml = '<h4>Assembly & Specialized Parts</h4><ul>';
        let assemblyLabelPrefix = ""; let assemblyQty = 0;
        if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' && (frontAssemblyService || rearAssemblyService)) { assemblyLabelPrefix = "Front/Rear:"; if (frontAssemblyService) assemblyQty++; if (rearAssemblyService) assemblyQty++; }
        else if (buildState.buildType === 'Front' && frontAssemblyService) { assemblyLabelPrefix = "Front:"; assemblyQty = 1; }
        else if (buildState.buildType === 'Rear' && rearAssemblyService) { assemblyLabelPrefix = "Rear:"; assemblyQty = 1; }
        const assemblyQtyDisplay = assemblyQty > 0 ? `(${assemblyQty}) ` : '';
        costsHtml += `<li><span class="summary-item-label-column">${assemblyLabelPrefix}</span><span class="summary-item-description-column"><strong>${assemblyQtyDisplay}Assembly Service</strong></span> <span class="summary-value">${totalAssemblyCostCents > 0 ? `(${formatPrice(totalAssemblyCostCents)})` : '($0.00)'}</span></li>`;
        hasAnyCostsOrServices = true;
    }

    let tapeLabel = ""; let tapeQty = 0;
    if (buildType === 'Wheel Set' && frontTape && rearTape) { tapeLabel = "Front/Rear:"; tapeQty = 2; }
    else if (frontTape) { tapeLabel = "Front:"; tapeQty = 1; }
    else if (rearTape) { tapeLabel = "Rear:"; tapeQty = 1; }
    if (tapeQty > 0) {
        if (!costsHtml) costsHtml = '<h4>Assembly & Specialized Parts</h4><ul>';
        const isChecked = buildState.tubelessTapeInstalled ? 'checked' : '';
        const isUncheckedClass = buildState.tubelessTapeInstalled ? '' : 'is-not-included';
        const TAPE_WEIGHT_DISPLAY = tapeQty * 10;
        const tapeDescription = `(${tapeQty}) Tubeless Tape (Installed) - Wt: ${TAPE_WEIGHT_DISPLAY}g`;
        const tapeDescriptionHtml = buildState.tubelessTapeInstalled ? `<strong>${tapeDescription}</strong>` : tapeDescription;
        const tapeHtml = `<li class="${isUncheckedClass}"><span class="summary-item-label-column">${tapeLabel}</span><span class="summary-item-description-column"><label for="tubeless-tape-toggle-checkbox" style="cursor: pointer; display: inline-flex; align-items: center; user-select: none;"><span>${tapeDescriptionHtml}</span><input type="checkbox" id="tubeless-tape-toggle-checkbox" ${isChecked} style="margin-left: 10px; flex-shrink: 0;"></label></span><span class="summary-value">($0.00)</span></li>`;
        costsHtml += tapeHtml;
        hasAnyCostsOrServices = true;
    }

    let berdLabel = ""; let berdDescription = ""; let berdPriceCents = 0;
    if (buildType === 'Wheel Set' && frontBerdInserts && rearBerdInserts) { berdLabel = "Front/Rear:"; berdDescription = "<strong>(2) Berd hub inserts (Required)</strong>"; berdPriceCents = frontBerdInserts.costInCents + rearBerdInserts.costInCents; }
    else if (frontBerdInserts) { berdLabel = "Front:"; berdDescription = "<strong>(1) Berd hub inserts (Required)</strong>"; berdPriceCents = frontBerdInserts.costInCents; }
    else if (rearBerdInserts) { berdLabel = "Rear:"; berdDescription = "<strong>(1) Berd hub inserts (Required)</strong>"; berdPriceCents = rearBerdInserts.costInCents; }
    if (berdDescription) {
        if (!costsHtml) costsHtml = '<h4>Assembly & Specialized Parts</h4><ul>';
        costsHtml += `<li><span class="summary-item-label-column">${berdLabel}</span><span class="summary-item-description-column">${berdDescription}</span> <span class="summary-value">(${formatPrice(berdPriceCents)})</span></li>`;
        hasAnyCostsOrServices = true;
    }
    if (hasAnyCostsOrServices) { costsHtml += '</ul>'; } else { costsHtml = ''; }
    
    let optionalAddonsHtml = '';
    if (selectedOptionalAddons && Object.keys(selectedOptionalAddons).length > 0) {
        optionalAddonsHtml = '<h4>Optional Add-ons</h4><ul>';
        const consolidatedAddons = {};
        Object.values(selectedOptionalAddons).forEach(addon => {
            const key = addon.addonVariantId; if (!key) return;
            if (!consolidatedAddons[key]) {
                consolidatedAddons[key] = { name: addon.addonName, price: addon.addonPriceCents, baseComponentType: addon.baseComponentType, positions: new Set(), count: 0 };
            }
            consolidatedAddons[key].count++; consolidatedAddons[key].positions.add(addon.baseComponentPosition);
        });
        const sortedConsolidatedAddons = Object.values(consolidatedAddons).sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
        sortedConsolidatedAddons.forEach(item => {
            const positionsArray = Array.from(item.positions); let positionLabelText = (positionsArray.length > 1) ? "Front/Rear" : positionsArray[0];
            const baseTypeDisplayName = getDisplayName(item.baseComponentType.toLowerCase()); const fullLabel = `${positionLabelText} ${baseTypeDisplayName}:`;
            const itemDescription = item.name; const quantityDisplay = `(${item.count})`; const totalCost = item.price * item.count;
            optionalAddonsHtml += `<li class="summary-item-indented"><span class="summary-item-label-column">${fullLabel}</span><span class="summary-item-description-column"><strong>${quantityDisplay} ${itemDescription}</strong></span><span class="summary-value">(${formatPrice(totalCost)})</span></li>`;
        });
        optionalAddonsHtml += '</ul>';
    }

    let leadTimeHtml = '';
    if (buildState.step === 3 && buildState.estimatedLeadTime > 0) {
        leadTimeHtml = `<div class="summary-lead-time-info">Estimated Build Time: <strong>${formatLeadTime(buildState.estimatedLeadTime)}</strong></div>`;
    }

    summaryContentElement.innerHTML = '' + componentsHtml + costsHtml + optionalAddonsHtml + leadTimeHtml;

    const buildSummaryElement = document.getElementById('build-summary');
    if (buildSummaryElement) {
        let discountContainer = buildSummaryElement.querySelector('.summary-discount-container');
        if (!discountContainer) {
            discountContainer = document.createElement('div');
            discountContainer.className = 'summary-discount-container';
            buildSummaryElement.appendChild(discountContainer);
        }
        discountContainer.innerHTML = discountInfoHtml;
    }

    const estimatedWeightValueElement = document.getElementById('estimated-weight-value');
    if (estimatedWeightValueElement) {
        const calculatedWeights = calculateTotalEstimatedWeight();
        if (calculatedWeights.total > 0) {
            let weightHtml = `<strong>${Math.round(calculatedWeights.total)} g</strong>`;
            if (buildType === 'Wheel Set' && calculatedWeights.front > 0 && calculatedWeights.rear > 0) {
                weightHtml += `<div style="font-size: 0.85em; font-style: italic; color: #666; margin-top: 2px;">(Front: ${Math.round(calculatedWeights.front)}g | Rear: ${Math.round(calculatedWeights.rear)}g)</div>`;
            }
            estimatedWeightValueElement.innerHTML = weightHtml;
        } else {
            estimatedWeightValueElement.textContent = '-- g';
        }
    }
}
// [END] updateBuildSummary

async function showStep(stepNumber, options = {}) {
    console.log(`--> showStep Function Entered. Requested step: ${stepNumber}`);
    if (!builderContainer) { console.error("showStep: Builder container missing!"); return; }
    buildState.step = stepNumber;

    // --- NAVIGATION VISIBILITY RESET ---
    const nav1 = document.querySelector('.nav-step-1');
    const nav23 = document.querySelector('.nav-step-2-3');
    const navBottom3 = document.querySelector('.nav-bottom-step3');
    
    if (nav1) nav1.style.display = 'none';
    if (nav23) nav23.style.display = 'none';
    if (navBottom3) navBottom3.style.display = 'none';

    builderContainer.querySelectorAll('.builder-step').forEach(step => { step.style.display = 'none'; });
    const targetStepElement = document.getElementById(`step-${stepNumber}`);
    
    if (targetStepElement) {
        targetStepElement.style.display = 'flex';
        
        // Show correct Nav Bar
        if (stepNumber === 1 && nav1) nav1.style.display = 'flex';
        if (stepNumber === 2 && nav23) nav23.style.display = 'flex';

        const stepHeader = targetStepElement.querySelector('h2');
        if (stepHeader && !options.skipScroll) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                stepHeader.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
            }, 50);
        }
    } else {
        console.error(`showStep: Step element step-${stepNumber} not found!`);
        return;
    }

    if (stepNumber !== 3 && buildState._ui.isChangingComponent) {
        cancelComponentChange();
    }
    if (stepNumber > 1) {
        buildState._ui.hasProgressedPastStep1 = true;
    }
    const step1ResetBtn = document.getElementById('step-1-reset-button');
    if (step1ResetBtn) {
        step1ResetBtn.style.display = (buildState._ui.hasProgressedPastStep1 && stepNumber === 1) ? '' : 'none';
    }

    try {
        if (stepNumber === 1) {
            updateStep1VisualFeedback();
            validateStep1();
        } else if (stepNumber === 2) {
            renderStep2();
            updateStep2OptionsVisibility();
            updateStep2VisualFeedback();
            validateStep2();

            // Dynamic Discovery Update
            Promise.all([componentFetchPromises.rims, componentFetchPromises.hubs]).then(() => {
                if (buildState.step === 2) {
                    console.log("[Data Ready] Re-rendering Step 2 Discovery.");
                    renderStep2();
                }
            });
        } else if (stepNumber === 3) {
            console.log("showStep(3): Starting sequential build of Step 3 content.");
            
            // UI Controls Visibility
            if (builderSaveLoadControls) builderSaveLoadControls.style.display = 'flex';
            if (navBottom3) navBottom3.style.display = 'flex';

            // Full Screen Overlay Logic
            if (step3RefreshOverlay) {
    if (!options.isRefreshing) {
        step3RefreshOverlay.style.display = 'flex';
    } else {
        step3RefreshOverlay.style.display = 'none';
    }
}
           
            renderStep3();
            renderQuickSpecAdjusters();
            updateComponentHeaderSpecs();

            // Fetch and Filter All Categories
            await loadAndFilterRims();
            await cachePreconfiguredPrices();
            await loadAndFilterHubs();
            await loadAndFilterSpokes();
            await loadAndFilterNipples();
            await loadAndFilterValveStems();

            if (!options.skipRevalidation) {
                await revalidateAllStep3Selections();
            }

            // --- START: PRODUCT PAGE FUNNEL LOGIC (STARTCOMPONENT) ---
            if (buildState.startComponent && !buildState.startComponent.processed) {
              const { variantId, type } = buildState.startComponent;
              let { position } = buildState.startComponent;
              let productCache = type === 'hub' ? allHubProductsCache : allRimProductsCache;
              const originalProduct = productCache?.find(p => p.variants.some(v => v.id === variantId));

              if (originalProduct) {
                if (position === 'front/rear') position = 'front';
                const positionsToSelectIn = (type === 'rim' && buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') ? ['Front', 'Rear'] : [position.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + position.slice(1)];
                
                positionsToSelectIn.forEach(pos => {
                  const posLower = pos.toLowerCase();
                  const currentSpecs = {
                      spokeCount: buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`],
                      wheelSize: buildState.specs[`${posLower}WheelSize`],
                      hubSpacing: buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`],
                      brakeStyle: buildState.specs.brakeStyle
                  };

                  let variantToClickId = null;
                  const isVariantCompatible = (v) => {
                      if (!v || !v.availableForSale) return false;
                      if (type === 'rim') {
                          const sizeVal = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                          const sizeMatch = Array.isArray(sizeVal) ? sizeVal.includes(currentSpecs.wheelSize) : sizeVal === currentSpecs.wheelSize;
                          return String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(currentSpecs.spokeCount) && sizeMatch;
                      }
                      return String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(currentSpecs.spokeCount) && v.spec_hub_spacing === currentSpecs.hubSpacing && (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(currentSpecs.brakeStyle);
                  };

                  const originalVariantNode = originalProduct.variants.find(v => v.id === variantId);
                  if (isVariantCompatible(originalVariantNode)) variantToClickId = variantId;
                  else {
                      const originalColor = originalVariantNode?.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value;
                      let fallback = originalProduct.variants.find(v => isVariantCompatible(v) && v.selectedOptions.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value === originalColor);
                      if (!fallback) fallback = originalProduct.variants.find(isVariantCompatible);
                      if (fallback) variantToClickId = fallback.id;
                  }

                  if (variantToClickId) {
                      const vendorButton = document.querySelector(`.vendor-filter-btn[data-position="${pos}"][data-vendor="${originalProduct.vendor}"]`);
                      if (vendorButton) {
                          vendorButton.click();
                          setTimeout(() => {
                              const modelCard = document.querySelector(`#${posLower}-${type}-options-container .component-product-card[data-model-name="${originalProduct.wheelModel}"]`);
                              if (modelCard) modelCard.querySelector('.product-card-header')?.click();
                              setTimeout(() => {
                                  document.querySelector(`.component-variant-button[data-variant-id="${variantToClickId}"]`)?.click();
                              }, 150);
                          }, 150);
                      }
                  }
                });
              }
              buildState.startComponent.processed = true;
            }
            // --- END: FUNNEL LOGIC ---

            await applyCustomerSuppliedSelections();

            if (buildState.buildType === 'Front' || buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') calculateWheelCosts('Front');
            if (buildState.buildType === 'Rear' || buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') calculateWheelCosts('Rear');

            validateStep3();
            updateStep3ButtonText();
            updateBuildSummary();
            if (step3RefreshOverlay) step3RefreshOverlay.style.display = 'none';
        }

        if (stepNumber > 1) {
            saveLastActiveBuild();
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`showStep: Error during setup for step ${stepNumber}:`, error);
        displayInitializationError(`Runtime Error during step ${stepNumber} setup: ${error.message}`);
    }
  
    console.log(`<-- showStep Function Exited for step ${stepNumber}.`);
}
  
    function updateStep1VisualFeedback(gT=null, selB=null){ console.log(`updateStep1VisualFeedback called. GroupType: ${gT}, SelectedButton provided: ${!!selB}`); const c=document.getElementById('step-1'); if(!c) { console.error("updateStep1VisualFeedback: Step 1 container not found."); return; } if(gT && selB){ c.querySelectorAll(`button[data-selection-type="${gT}"]`).forEach(b => { const isActive = b === selB; b.classList.toggle('active', isActive); }); } else { console.log("  - Updating all Step 1 buttons based on current buildState."); c.querySelectorAll('button[data-selection-type]').forEach(b => { const type = b.dataset.selectionType; const value = b.dataset.value; const isActive = buildState[type] === value; b.classList.toggle('active', isActive); }); } }
    function validateStep1(){ const ridingStyleSelected = !!buildState.ridingStyle; const buildTypeSelected = !!buildState.buildType; const isValid = ridingStyleSelected && buildTypeSelected; console.log(`validateStep1: Riding Style = ${buildState.ridingStyle}, Build Type = ${buildState.buildType}, isValid = ${isValid}`); if(step1NextButton) { step1NextButton.disabled = !isValid; } else { console.warn("validateStep1: step1NextButton not found."); } return isValid; }

function updateCustomerSuppliedCheckboxesVisibility() {
  const section = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-section');
  if (!section) {
    // This guard is important. If the section isn't in the DOM yet, do nothing.
    return;
  }

  // Part 1: Handle the enabled/disabled state.
  const isEnabled = buildState.ridingStyle && buildState.buildType;
  section.classList.toggle('is-disabled', !isEnabled);

  // Part 2: Handle showing/hiding individual labels based on build type.
  // This logic now correctly handles the case where buildType is null (show all).
  const showFront = !buildState.buildType || buildState.buildType.includes('Front') || buildState.buildType.includes('Set');
  const showRear = !buildState.buildType || buildState.buildType.includes('Rear') || buildState.buildType.includes('Set');

  // Use safer queries that check for element existence before trying to set style.
  const frontRimLabel = section.querySelector('.customer-supplied-checkbox[data-position="front"][data-component="rim"]')?.parentElement;
  if (frontRimLabel) frontRimLabel.style.display = showFront ? '' : 'none';

  const frontHubLabel = section.querySelector('.customer-supplied-checkbox[data-position="front"][data-component="hub"]')?.parentElement;
  if (frontHubLabel) frontHubLabel.style.display = showFront ? '' : 'none';

  const rearRimLabel = section.querySelector('.customer-supplied-checkbox[data-position="rear"][data-component="rim"]')?.parentElement;
  if (rearRimLabel) rearRimLabel.style.display = showRear ? '' : 'none';

  const rearHubLabel = section.querySelector('.customer-supplied-checkbox[data-position="rear"][data-component="hub"]')?.parentElement;
  if (rearHubLabel) rearHubLabel.style.display = showRear ? '' : 'none';
}
  
    function updateMtbWheelSizeCompatibility() {
    const c = document.getElementById('step-2');
    if (!c) return;
    c.querySelectorAll('.spec-option-button').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('is-incompatible'));
    if (buildState.ridingStyle !== 'mtb' || buildState.buildType !== 'Wheel Set') return;

    const frontSize = buildState.specs.frontWheelSize;
    const rearSize = buildState.specs.rearWheelSize;

    // Use double-escaped backslashes for the inch symbol
    const f27Btn = c.querySelector('button[data-spec-group="frontWheelSize"][data-value="27.5\\""]');
    const r29Btn = c.querySelector('button[data-spec-group="rearWheelSize"][data-value="29\\""]');

    if (frontSize === '27.5"') r29Btn?.classList.add('is-incompatible');
    if (rearSize === '29"') f27Btn?.classList.add('is-incompatible');
}
    function updateStep2VisualFeedback() {
    const c = document.getElementById('step-2');
    if (!c) return;

    c.querySelectorAll('.spec-group.selection-row:not([style*="display: none"])').forEach(row => {
        const stateSpecKey = row.dataset.specName;
        if (!stateSpecKey) return;
