        row.querySelectorAll('button.spec-option-button').forEach(btn => {
            const btnValue = btn.dataset.value;
            const currentValueInState = buildState.specs[stateSpecKey];
            
            // Highlight the button if it matches the current state
            btn.classList.toggle('active', btnValue === currentValueInState);
        });
    });
}
    
    function renderStep2() {
    const sC = document.getElementById('step-2-spec-container');
    if (!sC || !buildState.buildType) return;
    const bT = buildState.buildType;

    // Handle Row Visibility
    sC.querySelectorAll('.spec-group.selection-row').forEach(g => {
        const f = g.dataset.buildTypeFilter;
        let s = f ? f.split('|').includes(bT) : true;
        g.style.display = s ? 'flex' : 'none';
    });

    // Populate Buttons (Standard ones show immediately, niche ones show after cache fills)
    if (bT === 'Front' || bT === 'Wheel Set') {
        generateDynamicSpokeButtons('front');
        generateDynamicHubSpacingButtons('front');
    }
    if (bT === 'Rear' || bT === 'Wheel Set') {
        generateDynamicSpokeButtons('rear');
        generateDynamicHubSpacingButtons('rear');
    }

    validateStep2();
    updateSpecAvailabilityCounters(); // This fills the loading bubbles with numbers
}

function updateStep2OptionsVisibility() {
    const step2Container = document.getElementById('step-2');
    const ridingStyle = buildState.ridingStyle;
    if (!step2Container || !ridingStyle) {
        return;
    }
    let stateChanged = false;

    step2Container.querySelectorAll('.spec-group.selection-row:not([style*="display: none"])').forEach(groupElement => {
        const optionButtons = groupElement.querySelectorAll('button[data-spec-group][data-riding-style]');
        if (optionButtons.length === 0) return;

        const stateSpecKey = groupElement.dataset.specName;
        if (!stateSpecKey) return;

        let visibleOptions = [];
        optionButtons.forEach(buttonElement => {
            const supportedStyles = buttonElement.dataset.ridingStyle.split('|');
            
            // If ridingStyle is 'hybrid', force visibility (isVisible = true).
            // Otherwise, check if the button's supported styles include the current style.
            const isVisible = ridingStyle === 'hybrid' || supportedStyles.includes(ridingStyle) || supportedStyles.includes('both');

            buttonElement.style.display = isVisible ? '' : 'none';
            if (isVisible) {
                visibleOptions.push(buttonElement);
            } else if (buildState.specs[stateSpecKey] === buttonElement.dataset.value) {
                // If the currently selected option becomes invisible (e.g. switching from Hybrid back to MTB), clear it.
                buildState.specs[stateSpecKey] = null;
                if (buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected[stateSpecKey] === buttonElement.dataset.value) {
                    delete buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected[stateSpecKey];
                }
                stateChanged = true;
            }
        });

        // Auto-selection logic
        if (visibleOptions.length === 1 && buildState.specs[stateSpecKey] === null) {
            const singleButton = visibleOptions[0];
            const singleValue = singleButton.dataset.value;

            console.log(`Auto-selecting for ${stateSpecKey}: ${singleValue}`);
            buildState.specs[stateSpecKey] = singleValue;
            buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected[stateSpecKey] = singleValue;
            stateChanged = true;

            // We only auto-sync wheel size for gravel/road wheelsets. Hub spacing is ALWAYS independent.
            if (buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set' && buildState.ridingStyle === 'gravelroad') {
                const isWheelSize = stateSpecKey === 'frontWheelSize' || stateSpecKey === 'rearWheelSize';
                if (isWheelSize) {
                    const oppositeKey = stateSpecKey === 'frontWheelSize' ? 'rearWheelSize' : 'frontWheelSize';
                    if(buildState.specs[oppositeKey] === null) {
                        buildState.specs[oppositeKey] = singleValue;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    });

    if (ridingStyle === 'mtb') {
        updateMtbWheelSizeCompatibility();
    }
    if (stateChanged) {
        updateStep2VisualFeedback();
        validateStep2();
        updateBuildSummary();
        saveLastActiveBuild();
    }
}

function validateStep2() {
    let isValid = true;
    const { specs, buildType } = buildState;
    if (!specs || !buildType) return false;

    // 1. Check all selections exist
    if ((buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') && (!specs.frontWheelSize || !specs.frontSpokeCount || !specs.frontHubSpacing)) isValid = false;
    if ((buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') && (!specs.rearWheelSize || !specs.rearSpokeCount || !specs.rearHubSpacing || !specs.freehubType)) isValid = false;
    if (!specs.brakeStyle) isValid = false;

    // 2. CRITICAL SAFETY GATE: Block "Next" if current build results in 0 components
    if (isValid) {
        const activeBubbles = document.querySelectorAll('button.spec-option-button.active .spec-count-bubble');
        activeBubbles.forEach(bbl => {
            if (bbl.classList.contains('is-zero')) {
                isValid = false;
                console.log(`[Validation] Blocking Next: Selection resulted in 0 availability.`);
            }
        });
    }

    if (step2NextButton) step2NextButton.disabled = !isValid;
    return isValid;
}

/**
 * V5.1: Path-Aware Counting with String Normalization.
 * Fixes "Zero-out" bug and implements Freehub gray-out logic.
 */
function updateSpecAvailabilityCounters() {
    const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('button.spec-option-button[data-spec-group]');
    const { specs } = buildState;
    const clean = (val) => val ? String(val).replace(/\D/g, '') : "";

    buttons.forEach(btn => {
        const group = btn.dataset.specGroup;
        const value = btn.dataset.value;
        const pos = group.startsWith('rear') ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
        const posL = pos.toLowerCase();
        const hubsLoaded = allHubProductsCache.length > 0;
        const rimsLoaded = allRimProductsCache.length > 0;

        let count = null;
        let bubbleClass = '';

        // --- RIMS (Size Discovery) ---
        if (group.toLowerCase().includes('size')) {
            bubbleClass = 'is-rim';
            if (!rimsLoaded) count = "loading";
            else {
                count = allRimProductsCache.filter(p => p.variants.some(v => {
                    // Position Guard
                    if (v.spec_position !== pos && v.spec_position !== "Front/Rear") return false;
                    const sizeVal = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                    const sizeMatch = (sizeVal === value || (Array.isArray(sizeVal) && sizeVal.includes(value)));
                    const spokeMatch = !specs[`${posL}SpokeCount`] || clean(v.spec_spoke_count) === clean(specs[`${posL}SpokeCount`]);
                    let brakeMatch = specs.brakeStyle === 'Rim Brake' ? (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes('Rim Brake') : !(v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes('Rim Brake');
                    return v.availableForSale && sizeMatch && spokeMatch && brakeMatch;
                })).length;
            }
        }

        // --- HUBS (Spacing Discovery) ---
        else if (group.includes('HubSpacing')) {
            bubbleClass = 'is-hub';
            if (!hubsLoaded) count = "loading";
            else {
                count = allHubProductsCache.filter(p => p.variants.some(v => {
                    // 1. Strict Position Match
                    if (v.spec_position !== pos && v.spec_position !== "Front/Rear") return false;
                    
                    // 2. String Match
                    if (normalizeSpacing(v.spec_hub_spacing) !== normalizeSpacing(value)) return false;

                    // 3. Spoke Count Match
                    const spokeMatch = !specs[`${posL}SpokeCount`] || clean(v.spec_spoke_count) === clean(specs[`${posL}SpokeCount`]);
                    
                    // 4. Brake Style Match
                    const brakeMatch = !specs.brakeStyle || (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(specs.brakeStyle);
                    
                    // 5. Freehub Match (Rear Only)
                    if (pos === 'Rear' && specs.freehubType) {
                        if (!p.availableFreehubs || !p.availableFreehubs.includes(specs.freehubType)) return false;
                    }

                    return v.availableForSale && brakeMatch && spokeMatch;
                })).length;
            }

            // Gray out instead of hiding
if (hubsLoaded) {
    btn.classList.toggle('is-unavailable', count === 0);
    btn.style.display = ''; // Ensure it stays visible
}
        }

        // --- FREEHUBS (Gray-out Logic) ---
        else if (group === 'freehubType' || group === 'freehub') {
            if (hubsLoaded) {
                const possible = allHubProductsCache.some(p => {
                    const offersFreehub = p.availableFreehubs && p.availableFreehubs.includes(value);
                    if (!offersFreehub) return false;
                    return p.variants.some(v => {
                        const brakeMatch = !specs.brakeStyle || (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(specs.brakeStyle);
                        const spacingMatch = !specs.rearHubSpacing || v.spec_hub_spacing === specs.rearHubSpacing;
                        const spokeMatch = !specs.rearSpokeCount || clean(v.spec_spoke_count) === clean(specs.rearSpokeCount);
                        return v.availableForSale && (v.spec_position === 'Rear' || v.spec_position === 'Front/Rear') && brakeMatch && spacingMatch && spokeMatch;
                    });
                });
                btn.classList.toggle('is-unavailable', !possible);
            }
        }

        // --- UI DRAWING ---
        let bbl = btn.querySelector('.spec-count-bubble');
        if (count !== null) {
            if (!bbl) { 
                bbl = document.createElement('span'); 
                btn.appendChild(bbl); 
            }
            if (count === "loading") {
                bbl.className = 'spec-count-bubble is-loading';
                bbl.textContent = '';
            } else {
                bbl.className = `spec-count-bubble ${bubbleClass}`;
                bbl.textContent = count;
                bbl.classList.toggle('is-zero', count === 0);
            }
        } else if (bbl) {
            bbl.remove();
        }
    });

    validateStep2();
}


/**
 * Helper to manage individual bubble elements
 */
function updateSingleBubble(parentBtn, type, count) {
    const className = `spec-count-${type}`;
    let bubble = parentBtn.querySelector(`.${className}`);
    
    if (count === null) {
        if (bubble) bubble.remove();
        return;
    }

    if (!bubble) {
        bubble = document.createElement('span');
        bubble.className = `spec-count-bubble ${className}`;
        parentBtn.appendChild(bubble);
    }
    
    bubble.textContent = count;
    bubble.classList.toggle('is-zero', count === 0);
}
  
function renderQuickSpecAdjusters() {
    const sectionContainer = document.getElementById('spec-adjuster-section');
    if (!sectionContainer) return;

    const frontColumn = document.getElementById('front-spec-adjusters');
    const rearColumn = document.getElementById('rear-spec-adjusters');
    const centerColumn = document.getElementById('center-spec-adjusters');
    const wrapper = document.getElementById('spec-adjuster-wrapper');

    if (!frontColumn || !rearColumn || !centerColumn || !wrapper) return;

    const { buildType, specs } = buildState;
    let frontHtml = '';
    let rearHtml = '';
    let centerHtml = '';

    const createButtonGroup = (position, specKey, displayName) => {
        const specValue = specs[specKey];
        if (specValue === null) return '';
        const options = ['24h', '28h', '32h', '36h']; // Added 36h to adjuster
        let buttonsHtml = options.map(opt =>
            `<button type="button" class="builder-button spec-option-button ${specValue === opt ? 'active' : ''}" data-position="${position}" data-spec-key="${specKey}" data-value="${opt}">${opt}</button>`
        ).join('');
        return `<div class="quick-spec-group"><label>${displayName}</label><div class="spec-adjuster-options">${buttonsHtml}</div></div>`;
    };

    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') frontHtml = createButtonGroup('Front', 'frontSpokeCount', 'Front Spoke Count');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') rearHtml = createButtonGroup('Rear', 'rearSpokeCount', 'Rear Spoke Count');

    // CENTER COLUMN LOGIC (Brake Style)
    // We only show this if it's NOT a Rim Brake build. 
    // Switching from Rim Brake to Disc requires an axle change, which is best handled in Step 2.
    if (buildType !== null && specs.brakeStyle !== 'Rim Brake') { 
        const brakeStyleValue = specs.brakeStyle;
        const brakeOptions = ['6-Bolt', 'Centerlock']; 
        let brakeButtonsHtml = brakeOptions.map(opt =>
            `<button type="button" class="builder-button spec-option-button ${brakeStyleValue === opt ? 'active' : ''}" data-position="Both" data-spec-key="brakeStyle" data-value="${opt}">${opt}</button>`
        ).join('');
        
        centerHtml = `
            <div class="quick-spec-group">
                <label>Brake Style</label>
                <div class="spec-adjuster-options">${brakeButtonsHtml}</div>
            </div>`;
    }

    frontColumn.innerHTML = frontHtml;
    rearColumn.innerHTML = rearHtml;
    centerColumn.innerHTML = centerHtml;
    
    frontColumn.style.display = frontHtml ? 'flex' : 'none';
    rearColumn.style.display = rearHtml ? 'flex' : 'none';
    centerColumn.style.display = centerHtml ? 'flex' : 'none';

    wrapper.classList.toggle('build-type-wheel-set', buildType === 'Wheel Set');
    wrapper.classList.toggle('build-type-single', buildType !== 'Wheel Set');
    sectionContainer.style.display = (frontHtml || rearHtml || centerHtml) ? 'block' : 'none';
}

function showSpecChangeModal(position, componentType, targetSpecValue, actionInfo = null) {
    if (!specChangeModal || !specChangeModalTitle || !specChangeModalBody) return;

    // --- Add the vendor of the component being cleared to our action plan ---
    const componentStateKey = `${position.toLowerCase()}${componentType}`;
    const componentToClear = buildState.components[componentStateKey];
    if (actionInfo && componentToClear) {
        actionInfo.vendorToSelect = componentToClear.vendor;
    }
    _tempActionAfterSpecChange = actionInfo;
    // --- END  ---

    specChangeModalTitle.textContent = `Update Spoke Count?`;
    const componentTypeLower = componentType.toLowerCase();
    const cleanTargetSpecValue = targetSpecValue.replace(/h/g, '') + 'h';
    const modelName = actionInfo?.modelToExpand || null;

    let messageHtml = modelName ?
        `<p>Components in the <strong>${modelName}</strong> model group require a <strong>${cleanTargetSpecValue}</strong> spoke count.</p>
         <p>This will clear your current ${position.toLowerCase()} ${componentTypeLower} selection. Would you like to proceed?</p>` :
        `<p>This ${componentTypeLower} requires a <strong>${cleanTargetSpecValue}</strong> spoke count.</p>
         <p>Would you like to update your ${position} wheel to use a ${cleanTargetSpecValue} configuration?</p>`;

    specChangeModalBody.innerHTML = messageHtml;

    const oldBtn = specChangeModalConfirmBtn;
    const newBtn = oldBtn.cloneNode(true);
    oldBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newBtn, oldBtn);
    specChangeModalConfirmBtn = newBtn;

    specChangeModalConfirmBtn.onclick = () => {
        specChangeModal.style.display = 'none';

        if (componentToClear) {
            buildState.components[componentStateKey] = null;
        }

        const specKey = `${position.toLowerCase()}SpokeCount`;
        updateSpecAndRefreshStep3({
            [specKey]: cleanTargetSpecValue
        });
    };

    specChangeModal.style.display = 'flex';
}

function getHubBaseModelName(title) {
    if (!title) return '';
    
    // Convert to lowercase and remove brake-specific terms and extra spaces
    let cleanTitle = title.toLowerCase()
        .replace(/6-bolt|centerlock/g, '') // Remove brake types
        .replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim(); // Collapse multiple spaces into one and trim ends
        
    return cleanTitle;
}

async function attemptSmartHubSwap(position, newBrakeStyle) {
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const stateKey = `${posLower}Hub`;
    const currentComponent = buildState.components[stateKey];

    if (!currentComponent || !currentComponent.title) {
        return; // Nothing to swap if there's no title
    }

    console.log(`%c[Smart Swap] Attempting for ${position} Hub. Target Brake Style: ${newBrakeStyle}`, "color: #007bff; font-weight: bold;");

    const originalBaseModel = getHubBaseModelName(currentComponent.title);
    const originalColor = currentComponent.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;

    console.log(`[Smart Swap] Original Base Model Key: "${originalBaseModel}"`);
    console.log(`[Smart Swap] Original Color: ${originalColor}`);

    let bestMatch = null;

    // Search the entire hub cache for a product with a matching base name
    for (const candidateProduct of allHubProductsCache) {
        const candidateBaseModel = getHubBaseModelName(candidateProduct.title);

        if (candidateBaseModel === originalBaseModel) {
            // Found a product with the same base name, now check its variants
            for (const variant of candidateProduct.variants) {
                const positionMatch = variant.spec_position === position || variant.spec_position === "Front/Rear";
                const brakeMatch = (variant.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(newBrakeStyle);
                const spacingMatch = normalizeSpacing(variant.spec_hub_spacing) === normalizeSpacing(buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`]);
                const spokeMatch = String(variant.spec_spoke_count) === String(buildState.specs[`${posLower}SpokeCount`]);
                
                if (variant.availableForSale && positionMatch && brakeMatch && spacingMatch && spokeMatch) {
                    const variantColor = variant.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;
                    if (variantColor === originalColor) {
                        bestMatch = { variant, product: candidateProduct };
                        console.log(`%c[Smart Swap] Found perfect match!`, "color: green;", bestMatch);
                        break; // Found the best possible match
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        if (bestMatch) break;
    }

    if (bestMatch) {
        const { variant, product } = bestMatch;

        const newHubComponent = {
            variantId: variant.id, productId: product.id, productHandle: product.handle, title: product.title,
            variantTitle: variant.title, sku: variant.sku, price: variant.price.amount, vendor: product.vendor,
            image: variant.image, pairingKey: product.pairingKey, tags: product.tags,
            selectedOptions: variant.selectedOptions, optionalAddonProductGids: product.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [],
            quantityAvailable: variant.quantityAvailable, leadTimeDays: product.leadTimeDays, wheelModel: product.wheelModel,
            spec_spoke_count: String(variant.spec_spoke_count), spec_brake_interface: variant.spec_brake_interface, 
            spec_hub_spacing: variant.spec_hub_spacing, 
            spec_freehub: (position === 'Rear') ? buildState.specs.freehubType : null,
            weight_g: variant.weight_g ?? product.weight_g ?? null
        };

        buildState.components[stateKey] = newHubComponent;
    } else {
        console.log(`%c[Smart Swap] No compatible replacement found for ${position} Hub. Selection will be cleared.`, "color: #dc3545;");
    }
}

/**
 * Core engine for updating specs from within Step 3.
 * Passes an 'isRefreshing' flag to showStep to prevent full-screen blinking.
 */
async function updateSpecAndRefreshStep3(specUpdates) {
    
    let stateWasChanged = false;
    for (const key in specUpdates) {
        if (buildState.specs[key] !== specUpdates[key]) {
            buildState.specs[key] = specUpdates[key];
            stateWasChanged = true;
        }
    }

    // Always run if state changed, or if called with an empty object (like the toggle)
    if (stateWasChanged || Object.keys(specUpdates).length === 0) {
        // We pass the option 'isRefreshing: true' to suppress the blink
        await showStep(3, { isRefreshing: true });

        if (_tempActionAfterSpecChange) {
            // ... (keep the existing post-change logic for vendor/model expansion) ...
            const { modelToExpand, vendorToSelect } = _tempActionAfterSpecChange;
            const updatedSpecKey = Object.keys(specUpdates)[0];
            let position;
            if (updatedSpecKey?.startsWith('rear')) position = 'Rear';
            else if (updatedSpecKey?.startsWith('front')) position = 'Front';

            if (position && vendorToSelect) {
                const vendorButton = document.querySelector(`.vendor-filter-btn[data-position="${position}"][data-vendor="${vendorToSelect}"]`);
                if (vendorButton) vendorButton.click();
            }

            if (modelToExpand) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    const cardToExpand = document.querySelector(`.component-product-card[data-model-name="${modelToExpand}"]`);
                    if (cardToExpand) {
                        const header = cardToExpand.querySelector('.product-card-header');
                        if (header) {
                            header.click();
                            setTimeout(() => { cardToExpand.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); }, 150);
                        }
                    }
                }, 100);
            }
            _tempActionAfterSpecChange = null;
        }
    }
}

function renderStep3() {
    const s3C = document.getElementById('step-3');
    if (!s3C) return;
    const bT = buildState.buildType;
    const sF = bT === 'Front' || bT === 'Wheel Set'; // showFront
    const sR = bT === 'Rear' || bT === 'Wheel Set';  // showRear
    let sCl = false; // stateCleared

    ['rim', 'hub', 'spokes', 'nipples', 'valvestem'].forEach(t => { // t is component type lowercase
        let sId; // sectionId (e.g., component-section-rims)
        if (t === 'valvestem') sId = 'component-section-valvestems';
        else if (t === 'spokes' || t === 'nipples') sId = `component-section-${t}`;
        else sId = `component-section-${t}s`;

        const sE = s3C.querySelector(`#${sId}`); // The main section for this component type (e.g., #component-section-rims)
        if (!sE) return;

        const w = sE.querySelector('.component-position-wrapper'); // The container for front/rear subsections (e.g., for rims)
        if (!w) return;

        // Helper to manage individual front/rear subsections
        const managePositionSubsection = (positionName, showSubsection) => {
            const subSecEl = w.querySelector(`#${positionName.toLowerCase()}-${t}-subsection`);
            if (!subSecEl) return;

            subSecEl.style.display = showSubsection ? '' : 'none';

            if (bT === 'Wheel Set') {
                // If it's a wheel set, prevent subsections from stretching to match sibling height.
                // This assumes .component-position-wrapper.build-type-wheel-set is display: flex (row).
                subSecEl.style.alignSelf = 'flex-start';
            } else {
                // Reset for single builds if necessary (though likely not an issue if not flex row)
                subSecEl.style.alignSelf = '';
            }

            if (!showSubsection) { // If hiding, clear relevant state
                let typePascal = t.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + t.slice(1);
                if (t === 'valvestem') typePascal = 'ValveStem';
                else if (t === 'nipples') typePascal = 'Nipples';
                else if (t === 'spokes') typePascal = 'Spokes';

                const stateKey = `${positionName.toLowerCase()}${typePascal}`;
                if (buildState.components[stateKey]) {
                    buildState.components[stateKey] = null;
                    sCl = true; // Mark that state was cleared

                    // Also clear any selected optional addons for this cleared base component
                    const addonKeysToRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons).filter(key => {
                        const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                        return addon.baseComponentPosition === positionName && addon.baseComponentType === typePascal;
                    });
                    addonKeysToRemove.forEach(key => delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key]);
                    saveLastActiveBuild();
                }
            }
        };

        managePositionSubsection('Front', sF);
        managePositionSubsection('Rear', sR);

        // Adjust classes on the position wrapper for overall layout styling
        if (bT === 'Wheel Set') {
            w.classList.add('build-type-wheel-set');
            w.classList.remove('build-type-single');
        } else {
            w.classList.remove('build-type-wheel-set');
            w.classList.add('build-type-single');
        }
        sE.style.setProperty('display', ''); // Ensure the main component section is visible
    });

    if (sCl) { // If any component state was cleared
        updateBuildSummary();
        updateSubtotal();
        validateStep3(); // Re-validate if components were removed
        saveLastActiveBuild();
    }
}

function clearStep3UI() { const s3=document.getElementById('step-3'); if(s3){['rim','hub','spokes','nipples','valvestem'].forEach(t=>{['front','rear'].forEach(p=>{const fE=document.getElementById(`${p}-${t}-filters`); const oE=document.getElementById(`${p}-${t}-options-container`); const iE=document.getElementById(`${p}-${t}-image-container`); const sE=document.querySelector(`#${p}-${t}-selection span`); const ssE=document.getElementById(`${p}-${t}-subsection`); const actionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${p}-${t}-action-buttons`); const removeBtn = document.getElementById(`remove-${p}-${t}-button`); if(fE){const vA=fE.querySelector('.vendor-filter-area'); if(vA)vA.innerHTML='';} if(actionButtonsContainer) actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = ''; if(oE)oE.innerHTML='<p>Select dependencies.</p>'; if(iE){iE.innerHTML='';iE.style.display='none';} if(sE){let typePascal = t.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + t.slice(1); if (t === 'valvestem') typePascal = 'ValveStem'; else if (t === 'nipples') typePascal = 'Nipples'; else if (t === 'spokes') typePascal = 'Spokes'; let l=`${p[0].toUpperCase()+p.slice(1)} ${typePascal}`;sE.innerHTML=`Selected ${l}: None`;} if(ssE)ssE.classList.remove('selection-made','change-in-progress'); if(removeBtn) removeBtn.style.display = 'none'; });});}}
    function resetComponentSelectionUI(position, typePascal) { const pL=position.toLowerCase(); const tL = typePascal.toLowerCase(); const sS=document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL}-subsection`); const iC=document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL}-image-container`); const oC=document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL}-options-container`); const actionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${pL}-${tL}-action-buttons`); const sSpan=document.querySelector(`#${pL}-${tL}-selection span`); const removeBtn = document.getElementById(`remove-${pL}-${tL}-button`); if(iC){iC.style.display='none';iC.innerHTML='';} if(oC){oC.innerHTML='<p>Select options...</p>';oC.style.display='flex';} if(actionButtonsContainer) actionButtonsContainer.innerHTML = ''; if(sSpan){ let l=`${position} ${typePascal.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + typePascal.slice(1)}`;sSpan.innerHTML=`Selected ${l}: None`;} if(sS)sS.classList.remove('selection-made','change-in-progress'); if(removeBtn) removeBtn.style.display = 'none'; if(buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position===position&&buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.type===typePascal)cancelComponentChange(); }
    
    function areRimsPaired(rim1, rim2) {
    if (!rim1 || !rim2) return false;

    // 1. They must have the same pairing key. If not, they can't be a pair.
    if (rim1.pairingKey !== rim2.pairingKey) {
        return false;
    }

    // 2. Extract the color from each rim's variantTitle.
    const getColorFromTitle = (rim) => {
        if (!rim || !rim.variantTitle) return null;
        const parts = rim.variantTitle.split('/').map(part => part.trim());
        const color = parts[parts.length - 1];
        // Return the color only if it's a word, not a number, otherwise null.
        return isNaN(color) ? color.toLowerCase() : null;
    };

    const color1 = getColorFromTitle(rim1);
    const color2 = getColorFromTitle(rim2);

    // 3. Compare the colors. They must be identical.
    return color1 === color2;
}
  
    function areHubsPaired(hub1, hub2) { if (!hub1 || !hub2) return false; if (hub1.pairingKey !== hub2.pairingKey) return false; const getColor = (hub) => { if (!hub || !hub.selectedOptions) return null; const colorOption = hub.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color'); return colorOption ? colorOption.value : null; }; const color1 = getColor(hub1); const color2 = getColor(hub2); return color1 === color2; }
    function handleSelectedImageClick(e, imageContainer) { e.preventDefault(); if (buildState._ui.isChangingComponent) return; const componentType = imageContainer.dataset.componentType; const position = imageContainer.dataset.position; if (!componentType || !position) { console.error("handleSelectedImageClick: Missing data-component-type or data-position on image container."); return; } console.log(`handleSelectedImageClick: Initiating change for ${position} ${componentType}`); const posLower = position.toLowerCase(); const typeLower = componentType.toLowerCase(); const subsection = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLower}-subsection`); const optionsContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLower}-options-container`); const actionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLower}-action-buttons`); if (!subsection || !optionsContainer || !actionButtonsContainer) { console.error("handleSelectedImageClick: Critical UI elements missing for component change.", { subsection, optionsContainer, actionButtonsContainer }); return; } imageContainer.style.display = 'none'; optionsContainer.style.display = 'flex'; optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Loading options...</p>'; actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'flex'; /* <<< Ensure action buttons are visible */ showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(position, componentType, actionButtonsContainer); subsection.classList.add('change-in-progress'); buildState._ui.isChangingComponent = { position: position, type: componentType }; if (typeLower === 'rim') loadAndFilterRimsForPosition(position, true); else if (typeLower === 'hub') loadAndFilterHubsForPosition(position, true); else if (typeLower === 'spokes') loadAndFilterSpokesForPosition(position, true); else if (typeLower === 'nipples') loadAndFilterNipplesForPosition(position, true); else if (typeLower === 'valvestem') loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition(position, true); else { optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Error: Unknown component type.</p>'; } document.addEventListener('click', handleClickAway, true); }
    function handleClickAway(e) {
    const cI = buildState._ui.isChangingComponent;
    if (!cI) {
        document.removeEventListener('click', handleClickAway, true);
        return;
    }

    const cSS = document.getElementById(`${cI.position.toLowerCase()}-${cI.type.toLowerCase()}-subsection`);
    
    const isClickInsideSpecModal = specChangeModal && specChangeModal.contains(e.target);

    // Only cancel the change if the click is outside BOTH the component's subsection AND the spec change modal.
    if (cSS && !cSS.contains(e.target) && !isClickInsideSpecModal) {
        // console.log(`handleClickAway: Clicked outside ${cI.position} ${cI.type} subsection. Cancelling change.`);
        e.stopPropagation();
        e.preventDefault();
        cancelComponentChange();
    }
}

    function cancelComponentChange() {
        const cI = buildState._ui.isChangingComponent;
        if (!cI) return;

        // console.log(`cancelComponentChange: For ${cI.position} ${cI.type}`);
        const posLower = cI.position.toLowerCase();
        let typePascal = cI.type;
        const typeLowerForDOM = typePascal.toLowerCase() === 'valvestem' ? 'valvestem' : typePascal.toLowerCase();

        const subsection = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}-subsection`);

        if (subsection) {
            subsection.classList.remove('change-in-progress');
        } else {
            console.warn(`cancelComponentChange: Subsection not found for ${posLower}-${typeLowerForDOM}`);
        }

        const stateKey = `${posLower}${typePascal}`;
        const currentComponentData = buildState.components[stateKey];

        updateComponentUI(cI.position, typePascal, currentComponentData);

        buildState._ui.isChangingComponent = null;
        document.removeEventListener('click', handleClickAway, true);
        // console.log(`cancelComponentChange: Change cancelled for ${cI.position} ${cI.type}. UI should be fully restored.`);
    }

function displayRimProductCards(position, allCompatibleProducts, optionsContainer, allowedModels = null) {
    if (!optionsContainer) return;
    const componentKeyForState = `${position.toLowerCase()}Rim`;
    const selectedVendor = buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKeyForState];

    if (selectedVendor === null) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        return;
    }

    optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';

    // --- DEBUG 1: Vendor Filtering ---
    console.group(`[CardGen Debug] Displaying Rims for ${position}`);
    console.log(`Selected Vendor: "${selectedVendor}"`);
    
    // Find the infinity wheel in the raw input
    const infinityRaw = allCompatibleProducts.find(p => p.title.toLowerCase().includes('infinity'));
    if (infinityRaw) {
        console.log(`✅ Infinity Wheel FOUND in input list.`);
        console.log(`   - Vendor: "${infinityRaw.vendor}"`);
        console.log(`   - Model Metafield: "${infinityRaw.wheelModel}"`);
        console.log(`   - Vendor Match? ${infinityRaw.vendor === selectedVendor}`);
    } else {
        console.error(`❌ Infinity Wheel MISSING from input list (Loader issue?).`);
    }

    const productsFilteredByVendor = selectedVendor === 'all' ? allCompatibleProducts : allCompatibleProducts.filter(p => p.vendor === selectedVendor);

    if (productsFilteredByVendor.length === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${position.toLowerCase()} rims for vendor: ${selectedVendor} matching specs.</p>`;
        console.log("No products match vendor.");
        console.groupEnd();
        return;
    }

    // --- DEBUG 2: Grouping ---
    const groupedByModel = {};
    productsFilteredByVendor.forEach(p => {
        const model = p.wheelModel || 'Other';
        if (!groupedByModel[model]) groupedByModel[model] = [];
        groupedByModel[model].push(p);
    });

    console.log("Model Groups Created:", Object.keys(groupedByModel));
    
    // Check where Infinity ended up
    Object.keys(groupedByModel).forEach(key => {
        const hasInfinity = groupedByModel[key].some(p => p.title.toLowerCase().includes('infinity'));
        if (hasInfinity) console.log(`👉 Reserve Infinity is inside group: "${key}"`);
    });

    let displayedModelCount = 0;
    const modelsToDisplay = allowedModels ? Object.keys(groupedByModel).filter(modelName => allowedModels.includes(modelName)) : Object.keys(groupedByModel).sort((a, b) => getSortableName(a).localeCompare(getSortableName(b)));
    
    const currentSpokeCount = buildState.specs[`${position.toLowerCase()}SpokeCount`];

    modelsToDisplay.forEach(model => {
        const productsInGroup = groupedByModel[model];
        
        // CHECK IF INTEGRATED
        const isIntegratedGroup = productsInGroup.some(p => p.tags && p.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel'));

        const availableSpokeCounts = [...new Set(
            productsInGroup.flatMap(p => p.variants
                .filter(v => v.availableForSale && (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear"))
                .map(v => v.spec_spoke_count)
            ).filter(Boolean)
        )].sort((a, b) => a - b);

        // --- FILTER CHECK ---
        if (availableSpokeCounts.length === 0 && !isIntegratedGroup) {
            console.log(`Skipping Group "${model}": No spokes & Not integrated.`);
            return;
        }

        displayedModelCount++;
        console.log(`Rendering Card: "${model}"`);

        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'component-product-card rim-model-card';
        card.dataset.modelName = model;

        if (!isIntegratedGroup) {
            const isCompatibleNow = availableSpokeCounts.includes(String(currentSpokeCount));
            if (!isCompatibleNow) {
                card.classList.add('is-spec-incompatible');
                card.dataset.targetSpec = availableSpokeCounts[0];
                card.title = `Requires ${availableSpokeCounts.join('h or ')}h spoke count. Click to change.`;
            }
        }
        
        card.innerHTML = `<div class="product-card-header"><h5>${model}</h5></div><div class="product-card-body"><p>Click to view options...</p><div class="component-variant-options" style="display:none;"></div></div>`;
        
        card.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.closest('.component-variant-options button')) return;

            if (card.classList.contains('is-spec-incompatible')) {
                const targetSpokeCount = card.dataset.targetSpec + 'h';
                showSpecChangeModal(position, 'Rim', targetSpokeCount, { modelToExpand: model });
                return;
            }

            const vc = card.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
            if (!vc) return;
            const isTrigger = e.target.closest('.product-card-header') || e.target.closest('.product-card-body p');
            if (!isTrigger) return;

            const isVisible = vc.style.display !== 'none';

            optionsContainer.querySelectorAll('.component-product-card.expanded').forEach(c => {
                if (c !== card) {
                    c.classList.remove('expanded');
                    const ovc = c.querySelector('.component-variant-options');
                    if (ovc) ovc.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            
            vc.style.display = isVisible ? 'none' : 'block';
            card.classList.toggle('expanded', !isVisible);
            
            if (!isVisible) {
                displayRimVariantButtonsByProduct(position, productsInGroup, vc);
            }
        });
        optionsContainer.appendChild(card);
    });

    console.groupEnd();

    if (displayedModelCount === 0) {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>No ${position.toLowerCase()} rim models for vendor ${selectedVendor} match specs.</p>`;
    }
}

  
// --- START: handleAutoPairing ---
async function handleAutoPairing(componentType, position, selectedComponent, isExplicitMatchClick = false) {
    if (buildState.buildType !== 'Wheel Set') return 'not_applicable';

    const oppositePosition = position === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
    const oppPosLower = oppositePosition.toLowerCase();
    const oppositeStateKey = `${oppPosLower}${componentType}`;

    const componentToBeReplaced = buildState.components[oppositeStateKey];

    if (componentToBeReplaced && !isExplicitMatchClick) return 'opposite_filled';

    const selectedPairingKey = selectedComponent.pairingKey;
    if (!selectedPairingKey) return 'no_pairing_key';
    
    let cacheToSearch;
    switch (componentType) {
        case 'Hub': cacheToSearch = allHubProductsCache; break;
        case 'Rim': cacheToSearch = allRimProductsCache; break;
        case 'Spokes': cacheToSearch = allSpokeProductsCache; break;
        case 'Nipples': cacheToSearch = allNippleProductsCache; break;
        case 'ValveStem': cacheToSearch = allValveStemProductsCache; break;
        default: return 'unsupported_type';
    }

    const oppSpecs = {
        brakeStyle: buildState.specs.brakeStyle,
        wheelSize: buildState.specs[`${oppPosLower}WheelSize`],
        spokeCount: buildState.specs[`${oppPosLower}SpokeCount`],
        hubSpacing: buildState.specs[`${oppPosLower}HubSpacing`],
        freehubType: (oppositePosition === 'Rear') ? buildState.specs.freehubType : null,
        rimDepth: buildState.components[`${oppPosLower}Rim`]?.rimDepth
    };

    const pairedProducts = cacheToSearch.filter(p => p.pairingKey === selectedPairingKey);
    const targetColor = selectedComponent.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;

    let perfectMatches = [];
    for (const p_pair of pairedProducts) {
        for (const v_pair of p_pair.variants) {
            if (!v_pair.availableForSale) continue;
            let isMatch = false;
            switch (componentType) {
                case 'Hub':
                    if (oppositePosition === 'Rear' && (!p_pair.availableFreehubs || !p_pair.availableFreehubs.includes(oppSpecs.freehubType))) continue;
                    isMatch = (v_pair.spec_position === oppositePosition || v_pair.spec_position === "Front/Rear") && (v_pair.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(oppSpecs.brakeStyle) && v_pair.spec_hub_spacing === oppSpecs.hubSpacing && String(v_pair.spec_spoke_count) === String(oppSpecs.spokeCount);
                    break;
                case 'Rim':
                    const sizeValue = v_pair.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                    const sizeMatch = Array.isArray(sizeValue) ? sizeValue.includes(oppSpecs.wheelSize) : sizeValue === oppSpecs.wheelSize;
                    isMatch = (v_pair.spec_position === oppositePosition || v_pair.spec_position === "Front/Rear") && sizeMatch && String(v_pair.spec_spoke_count) === String(oppSpecs.spokeCount);
                    break;
                case 'ValveStem':
                    if (typeof oppSpecs.rimDepth !== 'number') continue; 
                    isMatch = (oppSpecs.rimDepth >= v_pair.valve_min_depth && oppSpecs.rimDepth <= v_pair.valve_max_depth) || (v_pair.valve_min_depth === null || v_pair.valve_max_depth === null);
                    break;
                case 'Spokes':
                    const sourceSpokeColor = selectedComponent.selectedColor;
                    const isBuilderVariant = v_pair.selectedOptions.some(o => o.name === 'Length' && o.value === '-');
                    if (!isBuilderVariant) { isMatch = false; continue; }
                    const targetSpokeColor = v_pair.selectedOptions.find(o => o.name === 'Color')?.value;
                    isMatch = (sourceSpokeColor === targetSpokeColor);
                    break;
                case 'Nipples':
                    const sourceNippleColor = selectedComponent.selectedOptions.find(o => o.name === 'Color')?.value;
                    const targetNippleColor = v_pair.selectedOptions.find(o => o.name === 'Color')?.value;
                    isMatch = (sourceNippleColor === targetNippleColor);
                    break;
            }
            if (isMatch) {
                perfectMatches.push({ variant: v_pair, product: p_pair });
            }
        }
    }

    let finalVariantsToConsider = perfectMatches;
    if (perfectMatches.length > 1 && targetColor) {
        const colorMatchedVariants = perfectMatches.filter(match => {
            const variantColor = match.variant.selectedOptions?.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;
            return variantColor === targetColor;
        });
        if (colorMatchedVariants.length > 0) {
            finalVariantsToConsider = colorMatchedVariants;
        }
    }
    
    if (componentType === 'ValveStem' && finalVariantsToConsider.length > 1) {
        finalVariantsToConsider.sort((a,b) => (parseInt(a.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity) - (parseInt(b.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity));
    }

    if (finalVariantsToConsider.length === 1 || (['Spokes', 'Nipples', 'ValveStem'].includes(componentType) && finalVariantsToConsider.length > 0)) {
        const bestMatch = finalVariantsToConsider[0];
        const { variant, product } = bestMatch;

        if (componentType === 'Spokes') {
            const oppositeHub = buildState.components[`${oppPosLower}Hub`];
            if (oppositeHub) {
                const bestMatchSpokeInterface = product.spokeHubInterface;
                const oppositeHubTags = oppositeHub.tags || [];
                
                let isAutoPairIncompatible = false;
                // Standard Checks
                if ((bestMatchSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && oppositeHubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) ||
                    (bestMatchSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && oppositeHubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend'))) isAutoPairIncompatible = true;
                
                // --- NEW HOOK FLANGE CHECKS ---
                if (oppositeHubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') && (bestMatchSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' || bestMatchSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull')) isAutoPairIncompatible = true;
                if (bestMatchSpokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && !oppositeHubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) isAutoPairIncompatible = true;

                if (isAutoPairIncompatible) {
                    const actionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${oppPosLower}-spokes-action-buttons`);
                    if (actionButtonsContainer) showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(oppositePosition, 'Spokes', actionButtonsContainer);
                    return 'cancelled_incompatible';
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (componentType === 'Hub') {
            const oppositeSpokes = buildState.components[`${oppPosLower}Spokes`];
            if (oppositeSpokes) {
                const bestMatchHubTags = product.tags || [];
                const oppositeSpokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === oppositeSpokes.productId);
                const oppositeSpokeInterface = oppositeSpokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface;
                
                let isAutoPairIncompatible = false;
                // Standard Checks
                if ((oppositeSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && bestMatchHubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) ||
                    (oppositeSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && bestMatchHubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend'))) isAutoPairIncompatible = true;

                // --- NEW HOOK FLANGE CHECKS ---
                if (bestMatchHubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') && (oppositeSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' || oppositeSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull')) isAutoPairIncompatible = true;
                if (oppositeSpokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && !bestMatchHubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) isAutoPairIncompatible = true;

                if (isAutoPairIncompatible) {
                    const actionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${oppPosLower}-hub-action-buttons`);
                    if (actionButtonsContainer) showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(oppositePosition, 'Hub', actionButtonsContainer);
                    return 'cancelled_incompatible';
                }
            }
        }

        if (componentToBeReplaced && componentToBeReplaced.productId !== product.id) {
            const addonKeysToRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons).filter(key => {
                const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                return addon.baseComponentPosition === oppositePosition && addon.baseComponentType === componentType && addon.baseComponentVariantId === componentToBeReplaced.variantId;
            });
            addonKeysToRemove.forEach(key => delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key]);
            if (addonKeysToRemove.length > 0) saveLastActiveBuild();
        }

        // --- CONSTRUCT COMPONENT OBJECT ---
        // Ensure we grab the weight from the variant, or fallback to product
        const safeWeight = variant.weight_g !== undefined ? variant.weight_g : (product.weight_g !== undefined ? product.weight_g : null);

        const autoSelectedComponent = {
            variantId: variant.id, productId: product.id, productHandle: product.handle, title: product.title,
            variantTitle: variant.title, sku: variant.sku, price: variant.price.amount, vendor: product.vendor,
            image: variant.image, pairingKey: product.pairingKey, tags: product.tags,
            selectedOptions: variant.selectedOptions, optionalAddonProductGids: product.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [],
            quantityAvailable: variant.quantityAvailable, leadTimeDays: product.leadTimeDays, wheelModel: product.wheelModel,
            
            // --- Ensure weight is assigned ---
            weight_g: safeWeight
        };
        
        switch (componentType) {
            case 'Hub':
                Object.assign(autoSelectedComponent, { spec_spoke_count: String(variant.spec_spoke_count), spec_brake_interface: variant.spec_brake_interface, spec_hub_spacing: variant.spec_hub_spacing, spec_freehub: oppSpecs.freehubType });
                if (oppositePosition === 'Rear') setComponentFreehubForHub({ ...variant, freehubVariantMap: product.freehubVariantMap });
                break;
            case 'Rim':
                Object.assign(autoSelectedComponent, { spokeCount: String(variant.spec_spoke_count), wheelSize: oppSpecs.wheelSize, rimDepth: product.rimDepth, internal_width_mm: variant.internal_width_mm });
                // Ensure ERD is passed
                if (variant.rim_erd) autoSelectedComponent.rim_erd = variant.rim_erd;
                else if (product.rim_erd) autoSelectedComponent.rim_erd = product.rim_erd;
                break;
            case 'Spokes':
                const colorOption = variant.selectedOptions.find(o => o.name.toLowerCase() === 'color');
                if (colorOption) autoSelectedComponent.selectedColor = colorOption.value;
                break;
        }

        buildState.components[oppositeStateKey] = autoSelectedComponent;
        if (componentType === 'Rim') {
            const isIntegrated = autoSelectedComponent.tags && autoSelectedComponent.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel');
            if (isIntegrated) {
                applyIntegratedWheelLogic(oppositePosition, autoSelectedComponent);
            } else {
                // If we matched to a standard rim, we MUST unlock the hub/spokes/nipples
                resetIntegratedWheelLogic(oppositePosition);
            }
        }
        buildState._ui.activeVendor[oppositeStateKey] = autoSelectedComponent.vendor;
        updateVendorButtonHighlight(oppositeStateKey, autoSelectedComponent.vendor);
        calculateWheelCosts(oppositePosition);
        
        // Update the UI, which will now see the weight_g we just assigned
        updateComponentUI(oppositePosition, componentType, autoSelectedComponent);
        
        switch (componentType) {
            case 'Hub':
            case 'Spokes':
                updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
                break;
            case 'Rim':
                evaluateValveStemForRimChange(oppositePosition);
                break;
        }

        updateSubtotal();
        updateBuildSummary();
        validateStep3();
        saveLastActiveBuild();
        updateMismatchHints();
        return 'single_match_selected';

    } else if (finalVariantsToConsider.length > 1) {
        if (buildState.components[oppositeStateKey]) {
            clearComponentAndItsAddons(oppositePosition, componentType);
            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
        }
        const oppOptionsContainer = document.getElementById(`${oppPosLower}-${componentType.toLowerCase()}-options-container`);
        if (oppOptionsContainer) {
            const vendorOfMatchingModels = finalVariantsToConsider[0].product.vendor;
            buildState._ui.activeVendor[oppositeStateKey] = vendorOfMatchingModels;
            updateVendorButtonHighlight(oppositeStateKey, vendorOfMatchingModels);
            
            const allowedModelNames = [...new Set(finalVariantsToConsider.map(match => match.product.wheelModel))];
            if (componentType === 'Hub') displayHubProductCards(oppositePosition, pairedProducts, oppOptionsContainer, allowedModelNames);
            else if (componentType === 'Rim') displayRimProductCards(oppositePosition, pairedProducts, oppOptionsContainer, allowedModelNames);
        }
        return 'multiple_matches_shown';
    }

    return 'no_match_found';
}
// --- END: handleAutoPairing ---
  
    // --- START: Contextual Mismatch Notification Display (Task 6.13) ---
function displayMismatchNotification(position, componentType, failedSpecName, requestedSpecValue, availableSpecValues) {
    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
    const typeLower = componentType.toLowerCase();
    const optionsContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLower}-options-container`);

    if (!optionsContainer) {
        console.error(`displayMismatchNotification: Could not find options container for ${position} ${componentType}`);
        return;
    }

    // Ensure availableSpecValues is sorted numerically for a clean "24h or 28h" display
    const sortedAvailable = availableSpecValues.sort((a, b) => parseInt(a) - parseInt(b));
    const availableSpecsString = sortedAvailable.map(s => `<strong>${s}</strong>`).join(' or ');

    const messageHtml = `
        <div class="mismatch-notification">
            <p>No <strong>${requestedSpecValue}</strong> ${getDisplayName(typeLower).toLowerCase()} was found for this model.</p>
            <p>However, compatible ${availableSpecsString} options are available.</p>
            <p>To select one, please return to Step 2 and adjust the <strong>${failedSpecName}</strong> for the <strong>${position}</strong> wheel.</p>
        </div>
    `;

    optionsContainer.innerHTML = messageHtml;

    // Also clear the vendor filters for that section to avoid confusion and an inconsistent UI state
    const filterContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLower}-filters`);
    if (filterContainer) {
        const vendorArea = filterContainer.querySelector('.vendor-filter-area');
        if (vendorArea) vendorArea.innerHTML = '';
    }
}
// --- END: Contextual Mismatch Notification Display (Task 6.13) ---
  
    function handleVendorFilterClick(event, vendorButton) {
    event.preventDefault();
    const componentKeyFromButton = vendorButton.dataset.componentKey;
    const position = vendorButton.dataset.position;
    const clickedVendor = vendorButton.dataset.vendor;

    const dropdown = vendorButton.closest('.vendor-filter-dropdown');
    if (dropdown) {
        const toggle = dropdown.querySelector('.dropdown-toggle');
        if (toggle) {
            let newToggleContent = ''; // Start empty

            if (clickedVendor === 'all') {
                newToggleContent = '<span class="toggle-all-vendors-button">All Vendors</span>';
            } else {
                const vendorInfo = vendorLogoMap[clickedVendor];
                const logoUrl = vendorInfo?.logoUrl;
                newToggleContent = `<span>
                                        ${logoUrl ? `<img src="${logoUrl}" alt="${clickedVendor}" class="toggle-vendor-logo">` : `<span>${clickedVendor}</span>`}
                                   </span>`;
            }

            toggle.innerHTML = newToggleContent;
        }
        dropdown.classList.remove('is-open');
    }

    let derivedComponentTypePascal = "";
    if (componentKeyFromButton && position && componentKeyFromButton.toLowerCase().startsWith(position.toLowerCase())) {
        derivedComponentTypePascal = componentKeyFromButton.substring(position.length);
    } else {
        console.error(`handleVendorFilterClick: Cannot derive component type from componentKey "${componentKeyFromButton}" and position "${position}"`);
        return;
    }
    if (derivedComponentTypePascal.toLowerCase() === "valvestem") derivedComponentTypePascal = "ValveStem";

    const componentTypeLower = derivedComponentTypePascal.toLowerCase();
    buildState._ui.activeVendor[componentKeyFromButton] = clickedVendor;

    const menuOptions = dropdown?.querySelector('.vendor-filter-options');
    if(menuOptions){
        menuOptions.querySelectorAll('.vendor-filter-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
        vendorButton.classList.add('active');
    }

    const isComponentSelectedInState = !!buildState.components[componentKeyFromButton];
    const isCurrentlyChangingThisSlot = buildState._ui.isChangingComponent &&
                                    buildState._ui.isChangingComponent.position === position &&
                                    buildState._ui.isChangingComponent.type === derivedComponentTypePascal;

    if (isComponentSelectedInState && !isCurrentlyChangingThisSlot) {
        const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
        const typeLowerForDomId = componentTypeLower;
        const imageContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDomId}-image-container`);
        const optionsContainerForChange = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDomId}-options-container`);
        const subsection = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDomId}-subsection`);
        const actionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${posLower}-${typeLowerForDomId}-action-buttons`);
        if (imageContainer && optionsContainerForChange && subsection && actionButtonsContainer) {
            imageContainer.style.display = 'none';
            optionsContainerForChange.style.display = 'flex';
            actionButtonsContainer.style.display = 'flex';
            showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(position, derivedComponentTypePascal, actionButtonsContainer);
            subsection.classList.add('change-in-progress');
            buildState._ui.isChangingComponent = { position: position, type: derivedComponentTypePascal };
            document.addEventListener('click', handleClickAway, true);
        } else {
            console.error(`handleVendorFilterClick: Missing UI elements for initiating change mode for ${position} ${derivedComponentTypePascal}. Check DOM IDs like ${posLower}-${typeLowerForDomId}-image-container`);
        }
    }

    const optionsContainer = document.getElementById(`${position.toLowerCase()}-${componentTypeLower}-options-container`);
    if (!optionsContainer) {
        return;
    }
    optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Filtering options...</p>';

    if (componentTypeLower === 'rim') {
        const cachedProducts = allRimProductsCache;
        const size = position === 'Front' ? buildState.specs.frontWheelSize : buildState.specs.rearWheelSize;
        const spokeCount = position === 'Front' ? buildState.specs.frontSpokeCount : buildState.specs.rearSpokeCount;
        
        if (!size) {
            optionsContainer.innerHTML = '<p>Select Wheel Size in Step 2 to see Rim options.</p>'; return;
        }

        const compatibleProducts = cachedProducts.filter(p => {
            // CHECK FOR INTEGRATED WHEEL
            const isIntegrated = p.tags && p.tags.includes('type:integrated_wheel');

            return p.variants.some(v => {
                // Common Checks
                const sizeValue = v.spec_rim_size?.parsedValue;
                const sizeMatch = (sizeValue === size || (Array.isArray(sizeValue) && sizeValue.includes(size)));
                const positionMatch = (v.spec_position === position || v.spec_position === "Front/Rear");
                const availMatch = v.availableForSale;

                if (isIntegrated) {
                    // --- NEW LOGIC for Vendor Click: Bypass Spoke Count ---
                    const posLower = position.toLowerCase();
                    const hubSpacing = buildState.specs[`${posLower}HubSpacing`];
                    const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
                    
                    const spacingMatch = v.spec_hub_spacing === hubSpacing;
                    const brakeMatch = (v.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle);
                    
                    return sizeMatch && positionMatch && availMatch && spacingMatch && brakeMatch;
                } else {
                    // --- STANDARD LOGIC ---
                    const spokeMatch = (!spokeCount || (String(v.spec_spoke_count) === String(spokeCount)));
                    return sizeMatch && positionMatch && availMatch && spokeMatch;
                }
            });
        });
        displayRimProductCards(position, compatibleProducts, optionsContainer);
    } else if (componentTypeLower === 'hub') {
        const cachedProducts = allHubProductsCache;
        const brakeStyle = buildState.specs.brakeStyle;
        const hubSpacing = position === 'Front' ? buildState.specs.frontHubSpacing : buildState.specs.rearHubSpacing;
        const freehubType = position === 'Rear' ? buildState.specs.freehubType : null;
        const spokeCount = buildState.specs[`${position.toLowerCase()}SpokeCount`];
        
        const compatibleProducts = cachedProducts.filter(product => {
            // Wildcard exception for customer-supplied parts
            if (product.vendor === 'Your Own Component') {
                return true;
            }

            // Product-level check for rear hubs
            if (position === 'Rear') {
                if (!product.availableFreehubs || !product.availableFreehubs.includes(freehubType)) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
            
            // Variant-level check: Verify the hub matches your specific selections
            return product.variants.some(variant => {
                const positionMatch = variant.spec_position === position || variant.spec_position === "Front/Rear";
                const brakeMatch = (variant.spec_brake_interface || []).includes(brakeStyle);
                const spacingMatch = normalizeSpacing(variant.spec_hub_spacing) === normalizeSpacing(hubSpacing);
                const spokeMatch = String(variant.spec_spoke_count) === String(spokeCount);
                
                return variant.availableForSale && positionMatch && brakeMatch && spacingMatch && spokeMatch;
            });
        });

        displayHubProductCards(position, compatibleProducts, optionsContainer);
    } else if (componentTypeLower === 'spokes') {
        const cachedSpokes = allSpokeProductsCache;
        displaySpokeProductCards(position, cachedSpokes, optionsContainer);
    } else if (componentTypeLower === 'nipples') {
        const cachedNipples = allNippleProductsCache;
        displayNippleProductCards(position, cachedNipples, optionsContainer);
    } else if (componentTypeLower === 'valvestem') {
        const cachedValveStems = allValveStemProductsCache;
        const currentRimKey = `${position.toLowerCase()}Rim`;
        const currentSelectedRim = buildState.components[currentRimKey];
        const currentRimDepth = currentSelectedRim ? currentSelectedRim.rimDepth : null;
        displayValveStemProductCards(position, cachedValveStems, optionsContainer, currentRimDepth);
    } else {
        optionsContainer.innerHTML = `<p>Options for ${derivedComponentTypePascal} from vendor '${clickedVendor}' coming soon.</p>`;
    }
    updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
}

function handleStep3Clicks(event) {
    const mswCheckbox = event.target.closest('.msw-global-checkbox');
    if (mswCheckbox) {
        // 1. Identify which dropdown is currently open so we can restore it
        const openDropdown = document.querySelector('.vendor-filter-dropdown.is-open');
        const openPosition = openDropdown ? openDropdown.closest('.position-subsection')?.dataset.position : null;

        // 2. Update global state
        buildState._ui.showRimBrakeRims = mswCheckbox.checked;
        
        // 3. Refresh Rims
        const refreshPromises = [];
        if (buildState.buildType === 'Front' || buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
            refreshPromises.push(loadAndFilterRimsForPosition('Front', buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === 'Front'));
        }
        if (buildState.buildType === 'Rear' || buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
            refreshPromises.push(loadAndFilterRimsForPosition('Rear', buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === 'Rear'));
        }

        // 4. Once refreshed, re-open the dropdown if it was open
        Promise.all(refreshPromises).then(() => {
            if (openPosition) {
                const newDropdown = document.querySelector(`.position-subsection[data-position="${openPosition}"] .vendor-filter-dropdown`);
                if (newDropdown) newDropdown.classList.add('is-open');
            }
        });
        
        return; 
    }
    // This now looks for EITHER the old hint class OR the new button class.
    const mismatchHint = event.target.closest('.mismatch-hint, .match-pair-button--from-hint');

    if (mismatchHint) {
        const positionToChange = mismatchHint.dataset.position;
        const typeToChange = mismatchHint.dataset.type;

        if (positionToChange && typeToChange) {
            event.preventDefault();
            event.stopPropagation();
            
            const oppositePosition = positionToChange === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
            const oppositeComponentStateKey = `${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}${typeToChange}`;
            const oppositeComponent = buildState.components[oppositeComponentStateKey];

            if (oppositeComponent) {
                console.log(`Matching ${positionToChange} ${typeToChange} from a valid hint click.`);
                handleAutoPairing(typeToChange, oppositePosition, oppositeComponent, true);
            }
            return;
        }
    }

    const removeComponentIcon = event.target.closest('[data-action="remove-component"]');
    const imageContainer = event.target.closest('.component-selected-image');
    const vendorButton = event.target.closest('.vendor-filter-btn');
    const dropdownToggle = event.target.closest('.vendor-filter-dropdown .dropdown-toggle');

    if (removeComponentIcon) {
        const positionFromButton = removeComponentIcon.dataset.position;
        if (positionFromButton) {
            const posPascal = positionFromButton.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + positionFromButton.slice(1);
            const posLower = positionFromButton.toLowerCase();
            const stateKeyForValveInComponents = `${posLower}ValveStem`;
            const baseComponentTypeForAddonCheck = 'ValveStem';
            const valveBeingRemoved = buildState.components[stateKeyForValveInComponents];

            if (valveBeingRemoved && valveBeingRemoved.variantId) {
                const removedValveVariantId = valveBeingRemoved.variantId;
                const addonKeysToRemove = Object.keys(buildState.selectedOptionalAddons).filter(key => {
                    const addon = buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                    return addon.baseComponentPosition === posPascal &&
                           addon.baseComponentType === baseComponentTypeForAddonCheck &&
                           addon.baseComponentVariantId === removedValveVariantId;
                });
                addonKeysToRemove.forEach(key => {
                    delete buildState.selectedOptionalAddons[key];
                });
            }

            buildState.components[stateKeyForValveInComponents] = null;
            buildState._ui.hasChanges = true;
            updateStep3ButtonText();
            buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved[posLower] = true;
            
            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
            saveLastActiveBuild();

            const correspondingRimKeyForCheck = `${posLower}Rim`;
            if (buildState.components[correspondingRimKeyForCheck]) {
                updateComponentUI(posPascal, baseComponentTypeForAddonCheck, null);
                loadAndFilterValveStemsForPosition(posPascal, true);
            } else {
                updateComponentUI(posPascal, baseComponentTypeForAddonCheck, null);
            }
            
            const otherPosition = positionFromButton === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
            const otherPosLower = otherPosition.toLowerCase();
            const otherActionButtonsContainer = document.getElementById(`${otherPosLower}-valvestem-action-buttons`);

            const isOtherSlotInOptionsView = !buildState.components[`${otherPosLower}ValveStem`] || 
                                           (buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.position === otherPosition && 
                                            buildState._ui.isChangingComponent?.type === 'ValveStem');

            if (otherActionButtonsContainer && isOtherSlotInOptionsView) {
                showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(otherPosition, 'ValveStem', otherActionButtonsContainer);
            }
        }
    } else if (imageContainer) {
        if (!event.target.closest('.optional-addons-btn') && !event.target.closest('.mismatch-hint')) {
            handleSelectedImageClick(event, imageContainer);
        }
    } else if (vendorButton) {
        handleVendorFilterClick(event, vendorButton);
    } else if (dropdownToggle) {
        const dropdown = dropdownToggle.closest('.vendor-filter-dropdown');
        const currentlyOpen = dropdown.classList.contains('is-open');
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.vendor-filter-dropdown.is-open').forEach(d => {
            d.classList.remove('is-open');
        });

        if (!currentlyOpen) {
            dropdown.classList.add('is-open');
        }
    } else if (!event.target.closest('.vendor-filter-dropdown')) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.vendor-filter-dropdown.is-open').forEach(d => {
            d.classList.remove('is-open');
        });
    }
}
  
function validateStep3() {
    let isSelectionComplete = true;
    const buildType = buildState.buildType;
    const components = buildState.components;
    const mandatoryComponentTypes = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples'];

    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        mandatoryComponentTypes.forEach(type => { if (!components[`front${type}`]) isSelectionComplete = false; });
    }
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        mandatoryComponentTypes.forEach(type => { if (!components[`rear${type}`]) isSelectionComplete = false; });
    }
    
    // Update all relevant Add to Cart buttons
    document.querySelectorAll('#step-3-add-to-cart-button, #step-3-add-to-cart-button-bottom').forEach(btn => {
        btn.disabled = !isSelectionComplete;
    });
    
    // Also manage the state of the admin-only share button
    const adminShareButton = document.getElementById('admin-share-build-button');
    if (adminShareButton) {
        adminShareButton.disabled = !isSelectionComplete;
    }
  
    updateValidationSummary();

    return isSelectionComplete;
}

// [START] packageBuildDataForCart - Updated V2
function packageBuildDataForCart() {
    const { buildType, components, buildId, selectedOptionalAddons, estimatedLeadTime, customerSupplied } = buildState;
    
    // 1. Define Base Properties
    const baseItemProperties = { "_BuildID": buildId, "_bundle_id": buildId };

    // 2. Helper: Add Item to Raw List (Defined here to capture scope)
    const rawItems = [];
    const addRawItem = (position, componentType, componentData) => {
        if (!componentData) return;
        if (componentData.isVirtual) return; // Skip virtual hubs/spokes
        if (componentData.isIncluded) return; // Skip the free valve

        const componentGid = componentData.variantId || componentData.variantGid;
        if (componentGid) {
            const itemProps = { ...baseItemProperties, "Wheel": position };
            
            // Pass Freehub selection to the Hub Line Item
            if (componentType === 'Hub' && position === 'Rear' && componentData.spec_freehub) {
                itemProps["_Freehub_Type"] = componentData.spec_freehub;
            }
            
            rawItems.push({
                id: getNumericIdFromShopifyGid(componentGid),
                quantity: 1,
                properties: itemProps
            });
        }
    };

    // 3. Clean State for Saving (Remove Virtual Items from JSON)
    const cleanStateForSaving = getCleanBuildStateForSaving();
    const stateForCart = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(cleanStateForSaving));
    
    if (stateForCart.components) {
        Object.keys(stateForCart.components).forEach(key => {
            const comp = stateForCart.components[key];
            if (comp) {
                if (comp.isVirtual) {
                    stateForCart.components[key] = null;
                } else {
                    delete comp.image; delete comp.tags; delete comp.pairingKey;
                    delete comp.productHandle; delete comp.productId; delete comp.optionalAddonProductGids;
                }
            }
        });
    }
    saveBuildState(buildId, cleanStateForSaving);

    // 4. Check for Pre-configured Match
    const preconfiguredMatch = checkForPreconfiguredMatch();

    if (preconfiguredMatch && preconfiguredMatch.masterVariantGid) {
        // === PATH A: PRE-CONFIGURED MATCH ===
        console.log(`[Cart] Adding Pre-configured Match: ${preconfiguredMatch.name}`);
        const masterVariantId = getNumericIdFromShopifyGid(preconfiguredMatch.masterVariantGid);

        const readableSpecs = {};
        const addSpec = (label, comp) => {
            if (comp) {
                let val = comp.title;
                if (comp.selectedOptions) {
                    const details = comp.selectedOptions.map(o => o.value).filter(v => v !== 'Default Title').join(' / ');
                    if (details) val += ` (${details})`;
                } else if (comp.variantTitle && comp.variantTitle !== 'Default Title') {
                    val += ` (${comp.variantTitle})`;
                }
                readableSpecs[label] = val;
            }
        };

        if (buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
            addSpec('Front Rim', components.frontRim);
            addSpec('Rear Rim', components.rearRim);
            addSpec('Front Hub', components.frontHub);
            addSpec('Rear Hub', components.rearHub);
            if (components.rearHub && components.rearHub.spec_freehub) readableSpecs['Freehub Body'] = components.rearHub.spec_freehub;
            else if (components.rearComponentFreehub) addSpec('Freehub Component', components.rearComponentFreehub);
            addSpec('Front Spokes', components.frontSpokes);
            addSpec('Rear Spokes', components.rearSpokes);
            addSpec('Front Nipples', components.frontNipples);
            addSpec('Rear Nipples', components.rearNipples);
        }

        rawItems.push({
            id: masterVariantId,
            quantity: 1,
            properties: {
                ...baseItemProperties,
                ...readableSpecs,
                "_is_custom_wheel_build": "true",
                "_EstLeadTime": formatLeadTime(estimatedLeadTime),
                "_build": JSON.stringify(stateForCart),
                "_Preconfigured_Rule": preconfiguredMatch.name
            }
        });

        if (selectedOptionalAddons) {
            Object.values(selectedOptionalAddons).forEach(addon => {
                if (addon?.addonVariantId) {
                    rawItems.push({
                        id: getNumericIdFromShopifyGid(addon.addonVariantId),
                        quantity: 1,
                        properties: { ...baseItemProperties, "Wheel": addon.baseComponentPosition, "_AttachedTo": `${addon.baseComponentType} Add-on` }
                    });
                }
            });
        }

    } else {
        // === PATH B: CUSTOM BUILD (Standard & Integrated) ===
        
        if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
            addRawItem('Front', 'Rim', components.frontRim);
            addRawItem('Front', 'Hub', components.frontHub);
            addRawItem('Front', 'Spokes', components.frontSpokes);
            addRawItem('Front', 'Nipples', components.frontNipples);
            addRawItem('Front', 'ValveStem', components.frontValveStem);
            addRawItem('Front', 'AssemblyService', components.frontAssemblyService);
            addRawItem('Front', 'TubelessTape', components.frontTubelessTape);
            (components.frontRequiredAddons || []).forEach(addon => addRawItem('Front', 'RequiredAddon', addon));
        }

        if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
            addRawItem('Rear', 'Rim', components.rearRim);
            addRawItem('Rear', 'Hub', components.rearHub);
            addRawItem('Rear', 'Spokes', components.rearSpokes);
            addRawItem('Rear', 'Nipples', components.rearNipples);
            addRawItem('Rear', 'ValveStem', components.rearValveStem);
            addRawItem('Rear', 'AssemblyService', components.rearAssemblyService);
            addRawItem('Rear', 'TubelessTape', components.rearTubelessTape);
            (components.rearRequiredAddons || []).forEach(addon => addRawItem('Rear', 'RequiredAddon', addon));
        }

        if (components.rearComponentFreehub?.variantId) {
            rawItems.push({
                id: getNumericIdFromShopifyGid(components.rearComponentFreehub.variantId),
                quantity: 1,
                properties: { ...baseItemProperties, "Wheel": "Rear", "Component": "Freehub" }
            });
        }

        if (selectedOptionalAddons) {
            Object.values(selectedOptionalAddons).forEach(addon => {
                if (addon?.addonVariantId) {
                    rawItems.push({
                        id: getNumericIdFromShopifyGid(addon.addonVariantId),
                        quantity: 1,
                        properties: { ...baseItemProperties, "Wheel": addon.baseComponentPosition, "_AttachedTo": `${addon.baseComponentType} Add-on` }
                    });
                }
            });
        }

        const isSupplyingOwnParts = Object.values(customerSupplied.front).some(v => v) || Object.values(customerSupplied.rear).some(v => v);
        const placeholderProperties = {
            ...baseItemProperties,
            "_is_custom_wheel_build": "true",
            "_EstLeadTime": formatLeadTime(estimatedLeadTime),
            "_build": JSON.stringify(stateForCart)
        };
        if (isSupplyingOwnParts) placeholderProperties['_Customer_Parts_Confirmed'] = 'true';

        rawItems.unshift({
            id: getNumericIdFromShopifyGid(PLACEHOLDER_PRODUCT_VARIANT_ID),
            quantity: 1,
            properties: placeholderProperties
        });
    }

    // 5. Consolidate duplicates (e.g. tape)
