    const consolidatedItems = {};
    for (const item of rawItems) {
        if (!item.id) continue;
        if (consolidatedItems[item.id]) {
            consolidatedItems[item.id].quantity += item.quantity;
            if (consolidatedItems[item.id].properties.Wheel && item.properties.Wheel && consolidatedItems[item.id].properties.Wheel !== item.properties.Wheel) {
                 consolidatedItems[item.id].properties.Wheel = 'Front/Rear';
            }
        } else {
            consolidatedItems[item.id] = item;
        }
    }

    return { itemsForShopifyCart: Object.values(consolidatedItems) };
}
// [END] packageBuildDataForCart

/**
 * V4.5 Build Check Engine: Pairing-Aware
 * Only warns about add-ons if the base components are a pair AND the addon is pairable.
 */
function performBuildCheck() {
    const warnings = [];
    const { buildType, components, selectedOptionalAddons } = buildState;

    if (buildType !== 'Wheel Set') return warnings;

    // --- Check 1: Valve Stem Mismatch ---
    // Rule: Warn if one is selected but not the other, provided BOTH rims are present.
    if (components.frontRim && components.rearRim) {
        const fValve = components.frontValveStem;
        const rValve = components.rearValveStem;
        if ((fValve && !rValve) || (!fValve && rValve)) {
            warnings.push({
                type: 'ValveStem',
                message: 'Only one wheel has a Valve Stem selected.',
                targetId: !fValve ? 'front-valvestem-subsection' : 'rear-valvestem-subsection'
            });
        }
    }

    // --- Check 2: Paired Add-on Mismatch ---
    const addonKeys = Object.keys(selectedOptionalAddons);
    const checkedPairingKeys = new Set();

    addonKeys.forEach(key => {
        const addon = selectedOptionalAddons[key];
        const pKey = addon.addonProductPairingKey;
        const compType = addon.baseComponentType; // e.g. 'Hub' or 'Rim'
        const pos = addon.baseComponentPosition; // 'Front' or 'Rear'
        const oppPos = pos === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';

        // 1. Only process if the addon is actually intended to be paired (has a pairing_key)
        if (pKey && !checkedPairingKeys.has(pKey)) {
            
            const currentBase = components[`${pos.toLowerCase()}${compType}`];
            const partnerBase = components[`${oppPos.toLowerCase()}${compType}`];

            // 2. Only warn if the components themselves are a match (e.g. both are DT 350 Hubs)
            // If the Rear is a DT 350 and the Front is a Chris King, we don't warn about 
            // a bearing mismatch because the products are fundamentally different.
            const isBaseComponentPair = currentBase && partnerBase && 
                                        currentBase.pairingKey === partnerBase.pairingKey;

            if (isBaseComponentPair) {
                // 3. Search for a partner addon on the opposite wheel with the same pairing key
                const hasPartner = addonKeys.some(otherKey => {
                    const otherAddon = selectedOptionalAddons[otherKey];
                    return otherAddon.baseComponentPosition === oppPos &&
                           otherAddon.baseComponentType === compType &&
                           otherAddon.addonProductPairingKey === pKey;
                });

                if (!hasPartner) {
                    warnings.push({
                        type: 'Addon',
                        message: `The ${pos} ${getDisplayName(compType.toLowerCase())} has the "${addon.addonName}" upgrade, but the ${oppPos} does not.`,
                        targetId: `${oppPos.toLowerCase()}-${compType.toLowerCase()}-subsection`
                    });
                    checkedPairingKeys.add(pKey);
                }
            }
        }
    });

    return warnings;
}

/**
 * Displays the Build Warning Modal.
 * @param {Array} warnings - The list of warnings from performBuildCheck.
 * @param {Function} onContinue - Callback if user clicks "Continue Anyway".
 */
function showBuildWarningModal(warnings, onContinue) {
    // We will reuse the spec-change-confirm-modal structure to keep CSS lean
    const modal = document.getElementById('spec-change-confirm-modal');
    const title = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-title');
    const body = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-body');
    const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-confirm-btn');
    const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-cancel-btn');

    if (!modal || !body) return;

    title.textContent = "Review Your Build";
    
    let warningHtml = `<p>We noticed a few things you might want to double-check before proceeding:</p><ul class="build-check-list">`;
    warnings.forEach(w => {
        warningHtml += `<li><strong>${w.message}</strong></li>`;
    });
    warningHtml += `</ul><p>Would you like to go back and fix these, or continue to checkout?</p>`;
    
    body.innerHTML = warningHtml;

    confirmBtn.textContent = "Continue to Checkout";
    cancelBtn.textContent = "Go Back & Fix";

    // Setup "Continue" action
    confirmBtn.onclick = () => {
        modal.style.display = 'none';
        onContinue();
    };

    // Setup "Go Back" action (Snapping to the first issue)
    cancelBtn.onclick = () => {
        modal.style.display = 'none';
        const firstWarning = warnings[0];
        const targetElement = document.getElementById(firstWarning.targetId);
        if (targetElement) {
            targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
            targetElement.classList.add('flash-highlight');
            setTimeout(() => targetElement.classList.remove('flash-highlight'), 2000);
        }
    };

    modal.style.display = 'flex';
}



// [START] addToCart logic with Build Check
async function addToCart() {
    console.log("%c[Action] addToCart logic started", "background: #222; color: #bada55; padding: 2px;");
    
    const { buildType } = buildState;

    // 1. Standard completion check
    if (!validateStep3()) {
        alert("Please complete all component selections.");
        return;
    }

    // --- NEW: Perform Inconsistency Check ---
    // We skip this check if the user is in "Edit Mode" to avoid annoying them 
    // unless they specifically made changes.
    if (!buildState._ui.inEditMode || buildState._ui.hasChanges) {
        const warnings = performBuildCheck();
        if (warnings.length > 0) {
            showBuildWarningModal(warnings, () => proceedWithAddToCart());
            return; // Halt execution until user clicks "Continue"
        }
    }

    // If no warnings, proceed immediately
    proceedWithAddToCart();
}

/**
 * The actual cart submission logic, isolated so it can be called after a warning is acknowledged.
 */
async function proceedWithAddToCart() {
    const { buildType } = buildState;

    // 1. Run final cost/engineering calculations
    if (buildType === 'Front' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') calculateWheelCosts('Front');
    if (buildType === 'Rear' || buildType === 'Wheel Set') calculateWheelCosts('Rear');
    updateSubtotal();

    // 2. Package the build data
    const { itemsForShopifyCart } = packageBuildDataForCart();
    const validItems = itemsForShopifyCart.filter(item => item.id);

    // 3. UI Feedback
    const isEditMode = buildState._ui.inEditMode === true;
    const allCartButtons = document.querySelectorAll('#step-3-add-to-cart-button, #step-3-add-to-cart-button-bottom');
    allCartButtons.forEach(btn => {
        btn.disabled = true;
        btn.textContent = isEditMode ? 'Updating Cart...' : 'Adding to Cart...';
    });

    try {
        if (isEditMode) {
            const cartRes = await fetch('/cart.js');
            const cartData = await cartRes.json();
            const others = cartData.items.filter(item => !item.properties || item.properties._BuildID !== buildState.buildId);
            await fetch('/cart/clear.js', { method: 'POST' });
            const itemsToReAdd = [...others.map(i => ({ id: i.variant_id, quantity: i.quantity, properties: i.properties })), ...validItems];
            await fetch('/cart/add.js', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ items: itemsToReAdd }) });
        } else {
            await fetch('/cart/add.js', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ items: validItems }) });
        }

        if (isEditMode) {
            sessionStorage.setItem(`ll_main_build_edited_${buildState.buildId}`, 'true');
            window.location.href = '/cart';
        } else {
            window.location.href = `/pages/accessories?build_id=${buildState.buildId}`;
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Cart Error] addToCart failed:', error);
        alert("An error occurred while adding to cart.");
        allCartButtons.forEach(btn => btn.disabled = false);
        updateStep3ButtonText(); 
    }
}
// [END] addToCart logic

    // --- Listener Setup Functions (Keep existing, ensure step3 listener calls new addToCart) ---
    function setupStep1Listeners() {
    const step1Element = document.getElementById('step-1');
    if (!step1Element) {
        console.error("setupStep1Listeners: Step 1 element not found.");
        return;
    }
    step1Element.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        const targetButton = e.target.closest('button.selection-button');
        if (!targetButton || targetButton.id === 'step-1-next-button') return;
        const selectionType = targetButton.dataset.selectionType;
        const value = targetButton.dataset.value;
        const displayText = targetButton.textContent.trim();
        if (!selectionType || !value) {
            console.warn("Step 1 button clicked without type/value", targetButton);
            return;
        }
        if (buildState[selectionType] !== value) {
            const previousRidingStyle = buildState.ridingStyle;
            buildState[selectionType] = value;
            if (selectionType === 'ridingStyle') {
                buildState.ridingStyleDisplay = displayText;
            }
            updateStep1VisualFeedback(selectionType, targetButton);
            validateStep1();
            if (selectionType === 'buildType') {
                let specsCleared = false;
                const specsToClear = [];
                if (value === 'Front') specsToClear.push('rearWheelSize', 'rearSpokeCount', 'rearHubSpacing', 'freehubType');
                else if (value === 'Rear') specsToClear.push('frontWheelSize', 'frontSpokeCount', 'frontHubSpacing');
                specsToClear.forEach(key => {
                    if (buildState.specs[key] !== null) {
                        buildState.specs[key] = null;
                        specsCleared = true;
                        if (buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected[key]) delete buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected[key];
                    }
                });
                if (specsCleared) updateBuildSummary();
                updateCustomerSuppliedCheckboxesVisibility(); 
            } else if (selectionType === 'ridingStyle') {
                if (previousRidingStyle !== null && previousRidingStyle !== value) {
                    console.log(`Riding style changed from ${previousRidingStyle} to ${value}. Resetting build while preserving edit state.`);
                    const preservedUiState = buildState._ui;
                    const preservedBuildId = buildState.buildId;
                    Object.keys(buildState.specs).forEach(k => buildState.specs[k] = null);
                    Object.keys(buildState.components).forEach(k => buildState.components[k] = null);
                    buildState.selectedOptionalAddons = {};
                    buildState._ui = preservedUiState;
                    buildState.buildId = preservedBuildId;
                    buildState._ui.step2AutoSelected = {};
                    allRimProductsCache = [];
                    allHubProductsCache = [];
                    componentFetchPromises.rims = null;
                    componentFetchPromises.hubs = null;
                    clearStep3UI();
                    updateBuildSummary();
                    saveLastActiveBuild();
                    if (buildState.step >= 2) {
                        renderStep2();
                        updateStep2OptionsVisibility();
                        updateStep2VisualFeedback();
                        validateStep2();
                    }
                }
                
                triggerEarlyComponentFetches();
                updateBuildSummary();
                updateCustomerSuppliedCheckboxesVisibility();
            }
            updateBuildSummary();
        }
    });

    const customerSuppliedSection = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-section');
    if (customerSuppliedSection) {
        customerSuppliedSection.addEventListener('change', event => {
            const checkbox = event.target;
            if (!checkbox || !checkbox.matches('.customer-supplied-checkbox')) {
                return;
            }
            const position = checkbox.dataset.position;
            const component = checkbox.dataset.component;
            if (buildState && buildState.customerSupplied && buildState.customerSupplied[position] && typeof buildState.customerSupplied[position][component] !== 'undefined') {
                buildState.customerSupplied[position][component] = checkbox.checked;
            } else {
                console.error('State is not ready for customer supplied input. Aborting.', {
                    state: buildState,
                    position: position,
                    component: component
                });
            }
        });
    }
}
      
function setupStep2Listeners() {
    const step2Element = document.getElementById('step-2');
    if (!step2Element) return;

    step2Element.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        const button = e.target.closest('button.spec-option-button');
        if (!button) return;

        const specGroupDiv = button.closest('.spec-group');
        const domSpecKey = specGroupDiv.dataset.specName;
        const specValue = button.dataset.value;
        let stateChanged = false;

        if (buildState.specs[domSpecKey] !== specValue) {
            
            // --- 1. FORCED COMPATIBILITY LOGIC (Mullet / Inverted Mullet) ---
            if (button.classList.contains('is-incompatible')) {
                if (domSpecKey === 'frontWheelSize' && specValue === '27.5"') {
                    buildState.specs.rearWheelSize = '27.5"'; // Force Rear to 27.5 if user forces 27.5 Front
                } else if (domSpecKey === 'rearWheelSize' && specValue === '29"') {
                    buildState.specs.frontWheelSize = '29"'; // Force Front to 29 if user forces 29 Rear
                }
            }

            buildState.specs[domSpecKey] = specValue;
            stateChanged = true;

            // --- 2. GRAVEL/ROAD SMART SYNC (V5.4 - Using letter "x") ---
            if (buildState.ridingStyle === 'gravelroad' && buildState.buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
                
                // Sync Wheel Sizes (Always matching for Gravel/Road)
                if (domSpecKey === 'frontWheelSize' || domSpecKey === 'rearWheelSize') {
                    buildState.specs.frontWheelSize = specValue;
                    buildState.specs.rearWheelSize = specValue;
                }

                // Sync Brake Style -> Axles
                if (domSpecKey === 'brakeStyle') {
                    if (specValue === 'Rim Brake') {
                        buildState.specs.frontHubSpacing = "9x100mm QR";
                        buildState.specs.rearHubSpacing = "10x130mm QR";
                    } else if (specValue === '6-Bolt' || specValue === 'Centerlock') {
                        buildState.specs.frontHubSpacing = "12x100mm";
                        buildState.specs.rearHubSpacing = "12x142mm";
                    }
                }

                // Sync Axles -> Brake Style & Partner Axle
                if (domSpecKey === 'frontHubSpacing' || domSpecKey === 'rearHubSpacing') {
                    if (specValue.includes('QR')) {
                        buildState.specs.brakeStyle = "Rim Brake";
                        buildState.specs.frontHubSpacing = "9x100mm QR";
                        buildState.specs.rearHubSpacing = "10x130mm QR";
                    } else if (specValue === "12x100mm" || specValue === "12x142mm") {
                        buildState.specs.frontHubSpacing = "12x100mm";
                        buildState.specs.rearHubSpacing = "12x142mm";
                        if (buildState.specs.brakeStyle === "Rim Brake") {
                            buildState.specs.brakeStyle = null;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (stateChanged) {
            updateMtbWheelSizeCompatibility(); // Refreshes gray-out states
            updateStep2VisualFeedback();      // Highlights active buttons
            updateSpecAvailabilityCounters(); // Updates bubbles and dynamic discovery
            validateStep2();                 // Checks if "Next" should be enabled
            saveLastActiveBuild();           // Persists session
        }
    });
}
function setupNavigationListeners() {
    step1NextButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (!step1NextButton.disabled) {
            const hasCustomerSupplied = Object.values(buildState.customerSupplied.front).some(v => v) || Object.values(buildState.customerSupplied.rear).some(v => v);

            if (hasCustomerSupplied) {
                // If user is supplying parts, show the consolidated modal first.
                // The modal's confirm button will then trigger the move to Step 2.
                showConsolidatedConfirmationModal();
            } else {
                // If not supplying parts, proceed directly to Step 2.
                triggerEarlyComponentFetches();
                showStep(2);
            }
        }
    });

    step2NextButton?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        if (!step2NextButton.disabled) {
            step2NextButton.disabled = true;
            step2NextButton.textContent = 'Building...';
            try {
                await showStep(3);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Error during Step 3 build process:", error);
                alert("An error occurred while preparing the next step. Please try again.");
            } finally {
                step2NextButton.disabled = false;
                step2NextButton.textContent = 'Next: Components';
                validateStep2();
            }
        }
    });

    // Back button logic remains the same
    document.getElementById('step-2-back-button')?.addEventListener('click', () => showStep(1));
    document.querySelectorAll('#step-3-back-button-TOP, #step-3-back-button, #step-3-back-button-bottom').forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', () => showStep(2));
    });
}

/**
 * Generates a simple Version 4 UUID for anonymous user tracking.
 * @returns {string} A unique identifier string.
 */
function generateUUID() {
  return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
    var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c == 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
    return v.toString(16);
  });
}

/**
 * Determines the visitor's identity for tracking purposes.
 * It prioritizes the server-rendered customer data object.
 * @returns {object} An object containing visitor identification data.
 */
function getVisitorIdentifier() {
    // Priority 1: Check for our custom, server-rendered customer object.
    if (window._loamlabs_customer_data && window._loamlabs_customer_data.isLoggedIn) {
        const customer = window._loamlabs_customer_data;
        return {
            isLoggedIn: true,
            customerId: customer.id,
            email: customer.email,
            firstName: customer.first_name,
            lastName: customer.last_name
        };
    }

    // Fallback to anonymous tracking using localStorage
    const anonymousIdKey = 'loamlabs_visitor_id';
    let visitorId = localStorage.getItem(anonymousIdKey);

    if (!visitorId) {
        // Assuming generateUUID() function exists elsewhere in this file
        visitorId = generateUUID(); 
        localStorage.setItem(anonymousIdKey, visitorId);
    }

    return {
        isLoggedIn: false,
        anonymousId: visitorId
    };
}

/**
 * Checks if the current build is "significant" enough to be logged as an abandonment.
 * A significant build is defined as one in Step 3 with all mandatory components selected
 * for the given build type.
 * @returns {boolean} True if the build is significant.
 */
function isBuildSignificant() {
    // A build is never significant if we're not on the component selection step.
    if (buildState.step !== 3) {
        return false;
    }

    const { buildType, components } = buildState;
    const mandatoryComponentTypes = ['Rim', 'Hub', 'Spokes', 'Nipples'];

    if (buildType === 'Front') {
        // For a Front wheel, every mandatory front component must exist.
        return mandatoryComponentTypes.every(type => components[`front${type}`]);
    }
    
    if (buildType === 'Rear') {
        // For a Rear wheel, every mandatory rear component must exist.
        return mandatoryComponentTypes.every(type => components[`rear${type}`]);
    }
    
    if (buildType === 'Wheel Set') {
        // For a Wheel Set, every mandatory component for BOTH front and rear must exist.
        const isFrontComplete = mandatoryComponentTypes.every(type => components[`front${type}`]);
        const isRearComplete = mandatoryComponentTypes.every(type => components[`rear${type}`]);
        return isFrontComplete && isRearComplete;
    }

    // If the buildType is not one of the above, it's not a significant build.
    return false;
}

/**
 * Sets up a listener to report significant builds that are abandoned.
 * This fires when the user navigates away from or closes the page.
 */
function setupAbandonmentTracking() {
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
        if (isBuildSignificant()) {

            // --- START: EXCLUSION LOGIC ---
            // First, check if the visitor is a staff member.
            const customerData = window._loamlabs_customer_data || {};
            if (customerData.isLoggedIn && customerData.tags && customerData.tags.includes('staff_builder')) {
                console.log("Abandonment report skipped for staff_builder account.");
                return; // Exit the function immediately, preventing the report from being sent.
            }
            // --- END: EXCLUSION LOGIC ---

            console.log("Attempting to report significant abandoned build for a customer/anonymous user...");
            const stateToReport = getMinimalBuildStateForReporting();
            
            // Add the visitor identification data to our report
            stateToReport.visitor = getVisitorIdentifier();

            const reportUrl = 'https://loamlabs-ops-dashboard.vercel.app/api/log-abandoned-build';

            console.log("FINAL DATA PACKET TO BE SENT:", JSON.stringify(stateToReport));

            try {
              // Use fetch with the keepalive flag.
              fetch(reportUrl, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(stateToReport),
                keepalive: true 
              });
              console.log("Abandoned build report sent via fetch(keepalive).", stateToReport);
            } catch (e) {
              console.error("Failed to send abandoned build report:", e);
            }
        }
    });
}

    // --- Function to update the Add to Cart / Update Cart / Back to Cart button text ---
function updateStep3ButtonText() {
    const allAddToCartButtons = document.querySelectorAll('#step-3-add-to-cart-button, #step-3-add-to-cart-button-bottom');
    if (allAddToCartButtons.length === 0) return;

    const isEditMode = !!buildState._ui.originalCartItemKeys;
    const hasChanges = buildState._ui.hasChanges;
    const isComplete = validateStep3();

    const backToCartButton = document.getElementById('step-3-back-to-cart-button'); // This is a separate button for the "no changes" state

    if (isEditMode) {
        if (hasChanges) {
            allAddToCartButtons.forEach(btn => {
                btn.textContent = 'Update Cart';
                btn.disabled = !isComplete;
                btn.style.display = '';
            });
            if (backToCartButton) backToCartButton.style.display = 'none';
        } else {
            allAddToCartButtons.forEach(btn => { btn.style.display = 'none'; });
            if (backToCartButton) {
                backToCartButton.style.display = '';
                backToCartButton.disabled = false;
            }
        }
    } else {
        allAddToCartButtons.forEach(btn => {
            btn.textContent = 'Add Build to Cart';
            btn.disabled = !isComplete;
            btn.style.display = '';
        });
        if (backToCartButton) backToCartButton.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

// Helper for "Back to Cart"
function redirectToCart() {
    window.location.href = '/cart';
}
      
function setupStep3Listeners() {
    const step3Container = document.getElementById('step-3');
    if (!step3Container) return;

    console.log("Step 3 Listeners Initializing...");

    // Event Delegation: Listen for clicks on the document to handle cart and validation links.
    // This ensures buttons work even after they are refreshed via AJAX.
    document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
        // A. Detect "Add to Cart" Clicks
        const isCartClick = event.target.closest('#step-3-add-to-cart-button-bottom') || 
                           event.target.closest('#step-3-add-to-cart-button') ||
                           event.target.closest('.add-to-cart-button');

        if (isCartClick) {
            console.log("%c[Click] Add to Cart Button Detected", "color: green; font-weight: bold;");
            event.preventDefault();
            event.stopPropagation();
            addToCart();
            return;
        }

        // B. Detect Validation Summary Links (The "Flash" effect)
        const validationLink = event.target.closest('.validation-summary-link');
        if (validationLink) {
            event.preventDefault();
            const targetId = validationLink.dataset.targetId;
            const targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId);
            if (targetElement) {
                targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                targetElement.classList.add('flash-highlight');
                setTimeout(() => targetElement.classList.remove('flash-highlight'), 1500);
            }
        }
    });

    // Handle standard Step 3 component clicks (Vendors, Images, etc)
    step3Container.addEventListener('click', handleStep3Clicks);
    
    updateStep3ButtonText(); 
}
      
function setupResetButtonListeners() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.reset-build-button').forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to reset your custom wheel build? All selections will be lost.')) {
                
                // Use our new, safe reset function
                resetBuildStateToDefaults();

                // Disable navigation buttons
                if (step1NextButton) step1NextButton.disabled = true;
                if (step2NextButton) step2NextButton.disabled = true;
                if (step3AddToCartButton) step3AddToCartButton.disabled = true;

                // Clear data caches and promises
                allRimProductsCache = []; allHubProductsCache = []; allSpokeProductsCache = []; allNippleProductsCache = []; allValveStemProductsCache = []; vendorLogoMap = {};
                componentFetchPromises = { rims: null, hubs: null, spokes: null, nipples: null, valves: null, freehubs: null };
                step3PreRenderPromise = null;

                // Update the UI
                showStep(1);
                clearStep3UI();
                updateBuildSummary();
                cancelComponentChange();
                updateCustomerSuppliedCheckboxesVisibility(); // Also call it here for safety
                console.log("Build state reset complete.");
            }
        });
    });
}

    function areSpokesPaired(spoke1, spoke2) {
    if (!spoke1 || !spoke2) return false;
    if (spoke1.pairingKey !== spoke2.pairingKey) return false;
    const getColor = (spoke) => { if (!spoke || !spoke.selectedOptions) return null; const colorOption = spoke.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color'); return colorOption ? colorOption.value : null; };
    const color1 = getColor(spoke1); const color2 = getColor(spoke2);
    if ((color1 === null && color2 !== null) || (color1 !== null && color2 === null)) return false;
    if (color1 !== null && color2 !== null && color1 !== color2) return false;
    return true;
}
    function areNipplesPaired(nipple1, nipple2) {
    if (!nipple1 || !nipple2) return false;
    if (nipple1.pairingKey !== nipple2.pairingKey) return false;
    const getColor = (nipple) => { if (!nipple || !nipple.selectedOptions) return null; const colorOption = nipple.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color'); return colorOption ? colorOption.value : null; };
    const color1 = getColor(nipple1); const color2 = getColor(nipple2);
    if ((color1 === null && color2 !== null) || (color1 !== null && color2 === null)) return false;
    if (color1 !== null && color2 !== null && color1 !== color2) return false;
    return true;
}
    function areValveStemsPaired(valve1, valve2) {
    if (!valve1 || !valve2) return false;
    if (valve1.pairingKey !== valve2.pairingKey) return false;
    const getColor = (valve) => { if (!valve || !valve.selectedOptions) return null; const colorOption = valve.selectedOptions.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color'); return colorOption ? colorOption.value : null; };
    const color1 = getColor(valve1); const color2 = getColor(valve2);
    if (color1 !== null && color2 !== null && color1 !== color2) return false;
    return true;
}
    function showCancelChangeButtonIfNeeded(positionBeingChanged, typeBeingChanged, actionButtonsContainerElement) {
    if (!actionButtonsContainerElement) return;

    actionButtonsContainerElement.innerHTML = ''; // Always start fresh
    actionButtonsContainerElement.style.display = 'none';

    let typePascal = typeBeingChanged.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + typeBeingChanged.slice(1).toLowerCase();
    if (typeBeingChanged.toLowerCase() === "valvestem") typePascal = "ValveStem";
    else if (typeBeingChanged.toLowerCase() === "spokes") typePascal = "Spokes";
    else if (typeBeingChanged.toLowerCase() === "nipples") typePascal = "Nipples";

    const isTrulyChanging = buildState._ui.isChangingComponent &&
                           buildState._ui.isChangingComponent.position === positionBeingChanged &&
                           buildState._ui.isChangingComponent.type === typePascal;

    if (isTrulyChanging) {
        const cancelButton = document.createElement('button');
        cancelButton.type = 'button';
        cancelButton.className = 'builder-button cancel-change-button button--link-style';
        cancelButton.textContent = 'Cancel Change';
        cancelButton.addEventListener('click', (e) => { e.preventDefault(); cancelComponentChange(); });
        actionButtonsContainerElement.appendChild(cancelButton);
        actionButtonsContainerElement.style.display = 'flex';
    }
}

async function handleMatchPairButtonClick(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    event.stopPropagation(); // Stop the click from triggering handleClickAway.

    const button = event.currentTarget;
    const positionToChange = button.dataset.positionToChange;
    const typeToChangePascal = button.dataset.typeToChange;
    const posLowerToChange = positionToChange.toLowerCase();
    const stateKeyToChange = `${posLowerToChange}${typeToChangePascal}`;

    if (!positionToChange || !typeToChangePascal) return;

    const oppositePosition = positionToChange === 'Front' ? 'Rear' : 'Front';
    const stateKeyOppositeComponent = `${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}${typeToChangePascal}`;
    const oppositeComponent = buildState.components[stateKeyOppositeComponent];

    // --- START: SYMMETRICAL PRE-FLIGHT CHECK (UPDATED V2.19) ---
    if (typeToChangePascal === 'Spokes') {
        const hubOnSideToChange = buildState.components[`${posLowerToChange}Hub`];
        if (hubOnSideToChange && oppositeComponent) { 
            const sourceSpokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === oppositeComponent.productId);
            const sourceSpokeInterface = sourceSpokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface; 
            const hubTags = hubOnSideToChange.tags || [];

            let isIncompatible = false;
            let errorMsg = "";

            // 1. Standard Steel Logic
            if (sourceSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) { isIncompatible = true; errorMsg = "J-Bend spokes are not compatible with Straight Pull hubs."; }
            if (sourceSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) { isIncompatible = true; errorMsg = "Straight Pull spokes are not compatible with J-Bend hubs."; }

            // 2. Hook Flange Hub Logic (Steel Spokes vs Hook Flange Hub)
            if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') && (sourceSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' || sourceSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull')) {
                isIncompatible = true; 
                errorMsg = "Steel spokes are not compatible with Hook Flange hubs.";
            }

            // 3. PolyLightX Logic (Hook Flange Spoke vs Standard Hub)
            if (sourceSpokeInterface === 'Hook Flange' && !hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange')) {
                isIncompatible = true;
                errorMsg = "Hook Flange spokes are not compatible with this hub.";
            }

            if (isIncompatible) {
                const confirmed = confirm(`${errorMsg} Clicking OK will clear the ${positionToChange} Hub to continue.`);
                if (confirmed) {
                    clearComponentAndItsAddons(positionToChange, 'Hub');
                } else {
                    if(buildState._ui.isChangingComponent) cancelComponentChange();
                    return; // ABORT THE MATCH
                }
            }
        }
    } else if (typeToChangePascal === 'Hub') {
        const spokesOnSideToChange = buildState.components[`${posLowerToChange}Spokes`];
        if (spokesOnSideToChange && oppositeComponent) { 
            const spokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === spokesOnSideToChange.productId);
            const spokeInterface = spokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface;
            
            // Find the tags of the hub we are ABOUT to match to
            const potentialMatchProduct = allHubProductsCache.find(p => p.pairingKey === oppositeComponent.pairingKey && p.id !== oppositeComponent.productId);
            const hubSourceProduct = potentialMatchProduct || allHubProductsCache.find(p => p.id === oppositeComponent.productId);
            const hubTags = hubSourceProduct?.tags || [];

            let isIncompatible = false;
            let errorMsg = "";

            // 1. Standard Steel Logic
            if (spokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && hubTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) { isIncompatible = true; errorMsg = "Current J-Bend spokes not compatible with Straight Pull hub."; }
            if (spokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && hubTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) { isIncompatible = true; errorMsg = "Current Straight Pull spokes not compatible with J-Bend hub."; }

            // 2. Hook Flange Hub Logic (Hook Flange Hub vs Steel Spokes)
            if (hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') && (spokeInterface === 'J-Bend' || spokeInterface === 'Straight Pull')) {
                isIncompatible = true;
                errorMsg = "Hook Flange hubs require Berd spokes. Current spokes are steel.";
            }

            // 3. PolyLightX Logic (Standard Hub vs Hook Flange Spokes)
            if (!hubTags.includes('hub_type:hook_flange') && spokeInterface === 'Hook Flange') {
                isIncompatible = true;
                errorMsg = "Current Hook Flange spokes require a Hook Flange hub.";
            }

            if (isIncompatible) {
                const confirmed = confirm(`${errorMsg} This will clear your current ${positionToChange} spoke selection. Continue?`);
                if (confirmed) {
                    clearComponentAndItsAddons(positionToChange, 'Spokes');
                } else {
                    if(buildState._ui.isChangingComponent) cancelComponentChange();
                    return; // ABORT THE MATCH
                }
            }
        }
    }
    // --- END: SYMMETRICAL PRE-FLIGHT CHECK ---
    // --- END: SYMMETRICAL PRE-FLIGHT CHECK ---

    if (typeToChangePascal === 'Hub' || typeToChangePascal === 'Rim') {

        // --- START: PRE-FLIGHT CHECK ---
        const componentToBeReplaced = buildState.components[stateKeyToChange]; // The hub slot we are about to fill
        const oppositeSpokes = buildState.components[`${oppositePosition.toLowerCase()}Spokes`]; // The spokes on the OTHER wheel
        
        if (typeToChangePascal === 'Hub' && oppositeSpokes && !componentToBeReplaced) {
            const oppositeSpokeProduct = allSpokeProductsCache.find(p => p.id === oppositeSpokes.productId);
            const oppositeSpokeInterface = oppositeSpokeProduct?.spokeHubInterface;

            // Find the tags of the hub that WILL be matched
            const potentialMatchProduct = allHubProductsCache.find(p => p.pairingKey === oppositeComponent.pairingKey);
            const potentialMatchTags = potentialMatchProduct?.tags || [];
            
            let isMatchIncompatible = false;
            if (oppositeSpokeInterface === 'J-Bend' && potentialMatchTags.includes('hub_type:straight_pull')) isMatchIncompatible = true;
            if (oppositeSpokeInterface === 'Straight Pull' && potentialMatchTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) isMatchIncompatible = true;

            if (isMatchIncompatible) {
                const requiredHubType = (potentialMatchTags.includes('hub_type:j_bend')) ? 'J-Bend' : 'Straight Pull';
                const confirmed = confirm(`The selected ${oppositePosition} spokes are not compatible with this ${requiredHubType} hub. Clicking OK will clear the ${oppositePosition} spokes to continue.`);
                if (confirmed) {
                    clearComponentAndItsAddons(oppositePosition, 'Spokes');
                } else {
                    cancelComponentChange();
                    return; // Abort
                }
            }
        }
        // --- END: PRE-FLIGHT CHECK ---

        const result = await handleAutoPairing(typeToChangePascal, oppositePosition, oppositeComponent, true);

        // If multiple matches were shown, the UI is now waiting for user input.
        // We should NOT cancel the change mode in this case.
        if (result !== 'multiple_matches_shown') {
            cancelComponentChange();
            updateMismatchHints();
        }

    } else if (typeToChangePascal === 'Spokes' || typeToChangePascal === 'Nipples') {
        // This logic handles simpler components that auto-select without presenting multiple model options.
        const cacheToSearch = (typeToChangePascal === 'Spokes') ? allSpokeProductsCache : allNippleProductsCache;
        const targetColor = oppositeComponent.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;

        const pairedProducts = cacheToSearch.filter(p => p.pairingKey === oppositeComponent.pairingKey);
        let potentialMatches = [];

        for (const p_pair of pairedProducts) {
            for (const v_pair of p_pair.variants) {
                if (!v_pair.availableForSale) continue;
                
                const variantColor = v_pair.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;
                if (variantColor === targetColor) {
                    potentialMatches.push({ variant: v_pair, product: p_pair });
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (potentialMatches.length > 0) {
            const bestMatch = potentialMatches[0];

            const newComponent = {
                variantId: bestMatch.variant.id, productId: bestMatch.product.id, productHandle: bestMatch.product.handle,
                title: bestMatch.product.title, variantTitle: bestMatch.variant.title, sku: bestMatch.variant.sku,
                price: bestMatch.variant.price.amount, vendor: bestMatch.product.vendor, image: bestMatch.variant.image,
                pairingKey: bestMatch.product.pairingKey, selectedOptions: bestMatch.variant.selectedOptions,
                optionalAddonProductGids: bestMatch.product.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [],
                quantityAvailable: bestMatch.variant.quantityAvailable, leadTimeDays: bestMatch.product.leadTimeDays || 0,
                weight_g: bestMatch.variant.weight_g ?? bestMatch.product.weight_g ?? null
            };

            buildState.components[stateKeyToChange] = newComponent;
            
            updateComponentUI(positionToChange, typeToChangePascal, newComponent);
            calculateWheelCosts(positionToChange);
            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
            if (typeToChangePascal === 'Spokes') {
                updateHubSpokeCompatibilityUI();
            }
            cancelComponentChange();
            saveLastActiveBuild();
            updateMismatchHints();

        } else {
            alert(`Could not find a matching ${getDisplayName(typeToChangePascal.toLowerCase())}.`);
            cancelComponentChange();
        }

    } else if (typeToChangePascal === 'ValveStem') {
        // Logic for Valve Stems
        const targetRim = buildState.components[`${posLowerToChange}Rim`];
        if (!targetRim) {
            alert(`Please select a ${positionToChange} Rim before matching the Valve Stem.`);
            cancelComponentChange();
            return;
        }
        const targetRimDepth = targetRim.rimDepth;
        const targetColor = oppositeComponent.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;

        const pairedProducts = allValveStemProductsCache.filter(p => p.pairingKey === oppositeComponent.pairingKey);
        let potentialMatches = [];

        for (const p_pair of pairedProducts) {
            for (const v_pair of p_pair.variants) {
                if (!v_pair.availableForSale) continue;

                let isDepthCompatible = false;
                if (targetRimDepth === null || typeof targetRimDepth === 'undefined' || v_pair.valve_min_depth === null || v_pair.valve_max_depth === null) {
                    isDepthCompatible = true;
                } else {
                    isDepthCompatible = targetRimDepth >= v_pair.valve_min_depth && targetRimDepth <= v_pair.valve_max_depth;
                }

                if (isDepthCompatible) {
                    const variantColor = v_pair.selectedOptions?.find(opt => opt.name.toLowerCase() === 'color')?.value || null;
                    if (variantColor === targetColor) {
                        potentialMatches.push({ variant: v_pair, product: p_pair });
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (potentialMatches.length > 0) {
            potentialMatches.sort((a, b) => (parseInt(a.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity) - (parseInt(b.variant.selectedOptions.find(opt=>opt.name==='Length')?.value.replace(/\D/g,''))||Infinity));
            const bestMatch = potentialMatches[0];

            const newComponent = {
                variantId: bestMatch.variant.id, productId: bestMatch.product.id, productHandle: bestMatch.product.handle,
                title: bestMatch.product.title, variantTitle: bestMatch.variant.title, sku: bestMatch.variant.sku,
                price: bestMatch.variant.price.amount, vendor: bestMatch.product.vendor, image: bestMatch.variant.image,
                pairingKey: bestMatch.product.pairingKey, selectedOptions: bestMatch.variant.selectedOptions,
                selectedWithRimDepth: targetRimDepth, valveMinDepth: bestMatch.variant.valve_min_depth, valveMaxDepth: bestMatch.variant.valve_max_depth,
                optionalAddonProductGids: bestMatch.product.optionalAddonProductGidsFromProduct || [],
                quantityAvailable: bestMatch.variant.quantityAvailable, leadTimeDays: bestMatch.product.leadTimeDays || 0,
                weight_g: bestMatch.variant.weight_g ?? bestMatch.product.weight_g ?? null
            };

            buildState.components[stateKeyToChange] = newComponent;
            buildState._ui.valveStemExplicitlyRemoved[posLowerToChange] = false;
            
            updateComponentUI(positionToChange, typeToChangePascal, newComponent);
            updateSubtotal();
            updateBuildSummary();
            validateStep3();
            cancelComponentChange();
            saveLastActiveBuild();
            updateMismatchHints();

        } else {
            alert(`Could not find a compatible matching ${getDisplayName(typeToChangePascal.toLowerCase())}. Please check rim depth or color compatibility.`);
            cancelComponentChange();
        }
    }
}

// --- START: FUNCTION to initialize the Step 1 Image Slider ---
function initializeStep1Slider() {
    const sliderContainer = document.querySelector('#step-1 .image-slider-container');
    if (!sliderContainer) return;

    const slides = sliderContainer.querySelectorAll('.slider-image-item');
    if (slides.length <= 1) {
        if (slides[0]) slides[0].classList.add('active');
        return;
    }

    let currentIndex = 0; // Always start with the first image (index 0)
    let shuffledPlaylist = [];
    const slideInterval = 5000;

    // A modern and reliable shuffle algorithm
    const shuffleArray = (array) => {
        for (let i = array.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
            const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
            [array[i], array[j]] = [array[j], array[i]]; // Swap elements
        }
    };

    const createShuffledPlaylist = () => {
        // Create an array of indices for all images *except* the first one
        const otherImageIndices = Array.from({ length: slides.length - 1 }, (_, i) => i + 1);
        shuffleArray(otherImageIndices);
        shuffledPlaylist = otherImageIndices;
        console.log("New shuffled playlist created:", shuffledPlaylist);
    };

    const showNextSlide = () => {
        // Hide the current slide
        slides[currentIndex].classList.remove('active');

        // Check if our playlist is empty
        if (shuffledPlaylist.length === 0) {
            // If the playlist is empty, it means we've shown all the other images.
            // It's time to show the main image (index 0) and then create a new playlist.
            currentIndex = 0;
            createShuffledPlaylist(); // Create a new random order for the next cycle
        } else {
            // If the playlist is not empty, pull the next image index from the front of the list
            currentIndex = shuffledPlaylist.shift(); // .shift() removes and returns the first item
        }

        // Show the new slide
        slides[currentIndex].classList.add('active');
    };

    // --- Initial Setup ---
    // Immediately show the first slide (the main logo)
    slides[currentIndex].classList.add('active');
    // Immediately create the first shuffled playlist for the other images
    createShuffledPlaylist();
    // Start the interval to begin the rotation after the first image has been displayed
    setInterval(showNextSlide, slideInterval);
}
  
// --- Initialization on DOM Load ---
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
    // --- STEP 1: ALWAYS assign DOM element variables first ---
    builderContainer = document.getElementById('variant-builder-container');
    if (!builderContainer) {
        console.error("CRITICAL INIT ERROR: Builder container #variant-builder-container not found.");
        return;

    step1NextButton = document.getElementById('step-1-next-button');
    step2NextButton = document.getElementById('step-2-next-button');
    step3AddToCartButton = document.getElementById('step-3-add-to-cart-button');
    summaryContainer = document.getElementById('build-summary');

    summaryContentElement = document.getElementById('summary-content');
    frontRimFilters = document.getElementById('front-rim-filters'); frontRimLoading = document.getElementById('front-rim-loading'); frontRimError = document.getElementById('front-rim-error'); frontRimOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('front-rim-options-container'); frontRimImageContainer = document.getElementById('front-rim-image-container');

    frontHubFilters = document.getElementById('front-hub-filters'); frontHubLoading = document.getElementById('front-hub-loading'); frontHubError = document.getElementById('front-hub-error'); frontHubOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('front-hub-options-container'); frontHubImageContainer = document.getElementById('front-hub-image-container');
    rearHubFilters = document.getElementById('rear-hub-filters'); rearHubLoading = document.getElementById('rear-hub-loading'); rearHubError = document.getElementById('rear-hub-error'); rearHubOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('rear-hub-options-container'); rearHubImageContainer = document.getElementById('rear-hub-image-container');
    frontSpokesFilters = document.getElementById('front-spokes-filters'); frontSpokesLoading = document.getElementById('front-spokes-loading'); frontSpokesError = document.getElementById('front-spokes-error'); frontSpokesOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('front-spokes-options-container'); frontSpokesImageContainer = document.getElementById('front-spokes-image-container');
    rearSpokesFilters = document.getElementById('rear-spokes-filters'); rearSpokesLoading = document.getElementById('rear-spokes-loading'); rearSpokesError = document.getElementById('rear-spokes-error'); rearSpokesOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('rear-spokes-options-container'); rearSpokesImageContainer = document.getElementById('rear-spokes-image-container');
    frontNipplesFilters = document.getElementById('front-nipples-filters'); frontNipplesLoading = document.getElementById('front-nipples-loading'); frontNipplesError = document.getElementById('front-nipples-error'); frontNipplesOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('front-nipples-options-container'); frontNipplesImageContainer = document.getElementById('front-nipples-image-container');
    rearNipplesFilters = document.getElementById('rear-nipples-filters'); rearNipplesLoading = document.getElementById('rear-nipples-loading'); rearNipplesError = document.getElementById('rear-nipples-error'); rearNipplesOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('rear-nipples-options-container'); rearNipplesImageContainer = document.getElementById('rear-nipples-image-container');
    frontValveStemFilters = document.getElementById('front-valvestem-filters'); frontValveStemLoading = document.getElementById('front-valvestem-loading'); frontValveStemError = document.getElementById('front-valvestem-error'); frontValveStemOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('front-valvestem-options-container'); frontValveStemImageContainer = document.getElementById('front-valvestem-image-container'); removeFrontValveStemButton = document.getElementById('remove-front-valvestem-button');
    rearValveStemFilters = document.getElementById('rear-valvestem-filters'); rearValveStemLoading = document.getElementById('rear-valvestem-loading'); rearValveStemError = document.getElementById('rear-valvestem-error'); rearValveStemOptionsContainer = document.getElementById('rear-valvestem-options-container'); rearValveStemImageContainer = document.getElementById('rear-valvestem-image-container'); removeRearValveStemButton = document.getElementById('remove-rear-valvestem-button');
    addonsModal = document.getElementById('addons-modal');
    addonsModalTitle = document.getElementById('addons-modal-title');
    addonsModalBody = document.getElementById('addons-modal-body');
    addonsModalCloseBtn = document.querySelector('.addons-modal-close-btn');
    addonsModalDoneBtn = document.getElementById('addons-modal-done-btn');
    builderSaveLoadControls = document.getElementById('builder-save-load-controls');
    saveCurrentBuildBtn = document.getElementById('save-current-build-btn');
    mySavedBuildsBtn = document.getElementById('my-saved-builds-btn');
    savedBuildsModal = document.getElementById('saved-builds-modal');
    savedBuildsModalTitle = document.getElementById('saved-builds-modal-title');
    savedBuildsModalBody = document.getElementById('saved-builds-modal-body');
    savedBuildsModalCloseBtn = document.getElementById('saved-builds-modal-close-btn');
    savedBuildsModalDoneBtn = document.getElementById('saved-builds-modal-done-btn');
    lastActiveBuildPromptModal = document.getElementById('last-active-build-prompt-modal');
    resumeLastActiveBtn = document.getElementById('resume-last-active-btn');
    startNewActiveBtn = document.getElementById('start-new-active-btn');
    quickSpecAdjustersContainer = document.getElementById('quick-spec-adjusters-container');
    step3RefreshOverlay = document.getElementById('builder-step3-refresh-overlay');
    specChangeModal = document.getElementById('spec-change-confirm-modal');
    specChangeModalTitle = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-title');
    specChangeModalBody = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-body');
    specChangeModalCloseBtn = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-close-btn');
    specChangeModalCancelBtn = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-cancel-btn');
    specChangeModalConfirmBtn = document.getElementById('spec-change-modal-confirm-btn');

    // --- STEP 2: ALWAYS initialize the API token configuration ---
    try {
        if (window.loamlabs?.builderConfig?.storefrontApiToken) {
            config.storefrontApiToken = window.loamlabs.builderConfig.storefrontApiToken;
        } else {
            throw new Error("Storefront API Token missing!");
        }
    } catch (error) {
        displayInitializationError(`Configuration Error: ${error.message}`);
        return;
    }

    // --- STEP 3: ALWAYS set up all event listeners to make the page interactive ---
    if (step1NextButton) step1NextButton.disabled = true;
    if (step2NextButton) step2NextButton.disabled = true;
    if (step3AddToCartButton) step3AddToCartButton.disabled = true;

    setupStep1Listeners();
    setupStep2Listeners();
    setupNavigationListeners();
    setupStep3Listeners();
    setupResetButtonListeners();
    initializeStep1Slider();
    initializeInfoTooltips();
    updateCustomerSuppliedCheckboxesVisibility();
    setupAbandonmentTracking();

    if (specChangeModal) {
        specChangeModal.addEventListener('click', (event) => { if (event.target === specChangeModal) specChangeModal.style.display = 'none'; });
    }
    if (specChangeModalCloseBtn) specChangeModalCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => specChangeModal.style.display = 'none');
    if (specChangeModalCancelBtn) specChangeModalCancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => specChangeModal.style.display = 'none');
    const specAdjusterSection = document.getElementById('spec-adjuster-section');
    if (specAdjusterSection) {
        // 1. Handle Button Clicks (Spoke Counts / Brake Style)
        specAdjusterSection.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            const button = e.target.closest('button.spec-option-button');
            // Ensure it's one of the adjuster buttons and isn't already the active one
            if (!button || !button.closest('.quick-spec-group') || button.classList.contains('active')) return;

            const specKey = button.dataset.specKey;
            const value = button.dataset.value;
            
            console.log(`[Quick Adjuster] Button Clicked: Setting ${specKey} to ${value}`);
            updateSpecAndRefreshStep3({ [specKey]: value });
        });

        // 2. Handle Checkbox Changes (Rim Brake Toggle)
        specAdjusterSection.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            if (e.target.id === 'global-msw-toggle') {
                buildState._ui.showRimBrakeRims = e.target.checked;
                console.log(`[Global Toggle] MSW Checkbox Changed: ${e.target.checked}`);
                // Refresh Step 3 to apply new filters
                updateSpecAndRefreshStep3({}); 
            }
        });
    }
    const adminShareButton = document.getElementById('admin-share-build-button');
    if (adminShareButton) {
      adminShareButton.addEventListener('click', handleAdminShareBuildClick);
    }
    if (addonsModalCloseBtn) addonsModalCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', closeAddonsModal);
    if (addonsModalDoneBtn) addonsModalDoneBtn.addEventListener('click', closeAddonsModal);
    if (addonsModal) { addonsModal.addEventListener('click', (event) => { if (event.target === addonsModal) closeAddonsModal(); }); }
    const csModalCloseBtn = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-close-btn');
    if (csModalCloseBtn) {
        csModalCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const { component, position } = currentModalConfirmation;
            const checkboxToUncheck = document.querySelector(`.customer-supplied-checkbox[data-component='${component}'][data-position='${position}']`);
            if (checkboxToUncheck) {
                checkboxToUncheck.checked = false;
                buildState.customerSupplied[position][component] = false;
            }
            hideConfirmationModal();
        });
    }
    const csModalCheckbox = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-checkbox');
    if (csModalCheckbox) {
        csModalCheckbox.addEventListener('change', event => {
            const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-confirm-btn');
            if(confirmBtn) confirmBtn.disabled = !event.target.checked;
        });
    }
    const csModalConfirmBtn = document.getElementById('customer-supplied-modal-confirm-btn');
    if (csModalConfirmBtn) {
        csModalConfirmBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            hideConfirmationModal();
            triggerEarlyComponentFetches();
            showStep(2);
        });
    }
    saveCurrentBuildBtn?.addEventListener('click', saveCurrentBuild);
    mySavedBuildsBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => { renderSavedBuildsList(); if (savedBuildsModal) savedBuildsModal.style.display = 'flex'; });
    savedBuildsModalCloseBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => { if (savedBuildsModal) savedBuildsModal.style.display = 'none'; });
    savedBuildsModalDoneBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => { if (savedBuildsModal) savedBuildsModal.style.display = 'none'; });
    savedBuildsModal?.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
        if (event.target === savedBuildsModal) savedBuildsModal.style.display = 'none';
        const loadBtn = event.target.closest('.saved-build-load-btn'); const deleteBtn = event.target.closest('.saved-build-delete-btn');
        if (loadBtn) { const buildId = loadBtn.dataset.buildId; if (buildId) loadBuildFromStorage(buildId); }
        else if (deleteBtn) { const deleteBuildIdVal = deleteBtn.dataset.buildId; if (deleteBuildIdVal) deleteSavedBuild(deleteBuildIdVal); }
    });
    resumeLastActiveBtn?.addEventListener('click', async () => { if (lastActiveBuildPromptModal) lastActiveBuildPromptModal.style.display = 'none'; await loadBuildFromStorage(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY, true); });
    startNewActiveBtn?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        if (lastActiveBuildPromptModal) lastActiveBuildPromptModal.style.display = 'none';
        localStorage.removeItem(LAST_ACTIVE_BUILD_KEY);
        resetBuildStateToDefaults();
        clearStep3UI();
        await showStep(1);
        updateCustomerSuppliedCheckboxesVisibility();
        updateSubtotal();
        updateBuildSummary();
    });

    // --- STEP 4: Now that the page is "live", decide which build to show ---
    try {
        console.log('[Builder] Entering final loading sequence.');
        
        // --- START: CORRECTED INITIALIZATION LOGIC ---
        const prebuildHandled = handlePrebuildState(); // First, try to handle a #prebuild= link.

        if (!prebuildHandled) {
            // If it was NOT a prebuild link, then check for other types of links or states.
            const hash = window.location.hash.substring(1);
            if (hash) {
                // If there's any other hash, assume it's a shareable link.
                await loadBuildFromShareableURL(hash);
            } else {
                // If there's no hash at all, check for an edit link or a saved session.
                let buildLoadedFromUrlForEdit = loadBuildFromUrlParams();
                if (buildLoadedFromUrlForEdit) {
                    await showStep(3);
                } else {
                    const promptShown = await checkForLastActiveBuildAndShowPrompt();
                    if (!promptShown) {
                        await showStep(1); // Normal fresh start.
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            // If the prebuild link WAS handled successfully, we just need to show Step 1.
            await showStep(1);
        }
        
        // Final updates
        updateSubtotal();

        // FINAL RE-SYNC AFTER DATA IS CACHED
        // This ensures bubbles update from "0" to real numbers once the download finishes
        Promise.all([componentFetchPromises.rims, componentFetchPromises.hubs]).then(() => {
            console.log("[Bubbles] Data caches ready, running initial count.");
            updateSpecAvailabilityCounters();
        });

        updateBuildSummary();
        handleComponentChangeForLeadTime();
        saveLastActiveBuild();

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('%c[Builder] CRITICAL ERROR during final build loading sequence:', 'color: red; font-weight: bold;', error);
        displayInitializationError(`Error during build loading: ${error.message}`);
    }
});

 
} // End of Execution Guard 'else' block
